UWA TA GARI - Prolong - Wattpad
Jawahir yarinya ce 'yar kimanin shekara sha takwas wacce take tsananin son mahaifinta kwatankwacin yanda take kin mahaifiyarta
Bata shakkar nuna soyayyarta ga mahaifinta a gaban kowa ciki kuwa harda mahaifiyarta dukda tanada masaniyar cewar mahaifanta sun dade da rabuwa
Zata zauna hannun matar uba wacce zata gana mata azaba irin na matan uba wanda imani ta musu karanci
Mahaifiyarta me sonta zata ceceta ba tareda tayi fushi akan halin da 'yarta ke nuna mata ba

UWA TA GARI - 1 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Gidane haddade wanda kallo daya zaka mishi ka gane gidane na masu hannu da shuni, gabadaya gidan fentin shi farine se roofing din daya kasance blue, haka zalika gate din gidan ma blue ne
Karamin gidane ba wani girma ne dashi ba, three bedroom flat ne ko wani daki da bathroom se parlour da kitchen da dinning se dan karamin balcony daketa waje wanda daga wurin kana iya hango gate din gidan
Wata matace wacce bazata wuce shekaru talatin da biyar ba zaune a kayataccen parlourn gidan wanda yaji kayan alatu da furnitures na zamani, laptop ne kirar apple a gabanta idanunta sanye da medical glasses ta kurawa system din ido da gani wani muhimmin abu takeyi duba da yadda tabada hankalinta gabadaya ga system din
Kofan daya daga cikin dakunan aka bude inda yarinya 'yar kimanin shekara sha takwas ta fito jikinta sanye da red pencil jeans da white top a jiki an rubuta 'ride or die' da red ink, kanta ba dankwali se kananun kiso kalaba daya zubo har kafadunta
Karasowa tayi gaban matar fuskanta dauke da tsananin farin ciki ta karaso gaban mahaifiyarta tareda cewa "Mamah guess what?", ba tareda da wacce aka kira da Mamah ta dago ba tace "Jawahir go straight to the point, nayi busy yanzu", rolling idanuwanta wacce aka kira da Jawahir tayi tareda da hararan mamah ta gefen ido sannan tace "fine, dama zamuje hiking dasu Zahra da wasu course mates dina ne gobe, shine nazo na fada miki", bata jira cewar Mamah ba ta juya zata wuce daga sama taji Mamah tace "ba inda zaki"
Juyowa tayi a 360 tareda kallon Mamah tace "banji me kikace ba", ba tareda nuna damuwa koh wani abu ba Mamah tace "cewa nayi ba idan zaki", ta karashe maganan tana dagowa for the first time, Masha Allah shine abinda nace saboda ganin tsantsar kyawu irin na wannan mata sannan ga photocopy dinta tsaye ta hade rai kaman hadarin gabas ta kankance ido tana kallon mahaifiyarta tace "Mamah banazo karban permission bane, na fada miki ne saboda Dada yace i should always inform you before going out for safety purpose, saboda haka bakida right dinda zacike naje ko kar naje"
Murmushi Mamah tayi tareda ajiye laptop din da ke kan cinyarta ta kalli Jawahir da kyau sannan tace "ni kuwa keda right akanki Jawahir, dan haka tunda nace ba inda zaki toh ba inda zakije din, it's better you find something useful to do with your precious time, banga abinda zakijeyi a wurin hiking ba in banda risking life dinki a banza, kuma
", bata karashe ba Jawahir ta katse ta tareda cewa "risking life dina as if you care", sannan ta wuce ta kom daki ba tareda ta jira cewar Mamah ba
Girgiza kai Mamah tayi tareda jingina kanta kan kujera yayinda wasu hawaye suka zubo mata tasa hannu ta share tareda lumshe ido tana tunanin metayiwa Jawahir a rayuwa da take kinta kaman ba mahaifiyarta ba
Kafadarta taji an dafa ta bude ido tareda gyara zama sanin cewar ba kowa bane illa Baba Salamatu wacce take zaune dasu tsawon shekaru kenan tanayi musu aiki
"Hakuri zakiyi hajiya, komai me wucewa ne a rayuwa, wata rana se labari, kici gaba dayi mata addu'a Allah ya shirya miki ita", girgiza kai Mamah tayi wasu dumammun hawaye na zubo mata ta goge tareda cewa "Baba Salamatu na rasa me nayi a rayuwa da Allah ya zabi ya hukuntani ta wannan hanyar, ace 'yar cikina bata ganin girma na balle taji magana ta", sake dafata Baba Salamatu tayi tace "akul, kar na sake jin haka a bakinki, wannan jarabawace daga Allah wanda shi kadai yasan dalilinshi nayin haka, ki cigaba da hakuri kaman yadda kika saba kodan kici wannan jarabawar, wata rana da kanta zata kawo kanta gareki a yadda kike muradin son ganinta inshallahu", murmushi Mamah tayi tareda jinjina kai sannan tace "nagode Baba Salamatu da shawarwarin da kike bani, kuma inshallahu zanci gaba da addu'a Allah ya shirya min ita", mikewa Baba Salamatu tayi tareda cewa "ameen, bari na duba abinda na dora kan wuta", sannan ta wuce kitchen tabar Mamah tana kokarin tashi itama
Bangaren Jawahir kuwa tana shiga daki ta zauna kan gadonta wanda yakenan kaman na mutane shida tana Jan tagwayen tsaki tareda gunguni tana cewa "ni wallahi matar nan tana shiga rayuwata dayawa, shiyasa nafison na zauna wurin Dada amma ya tashi yayi tafiya a lokacinda nafi bukatan shi mtswww", taja sabon tsaki tana daukan wayarta dake ringing, Zahra aka rubuta akan screen din tayi pick tareda cewa "babe ya akayi?", daga dayan bagaren Zahra tace "hope kin shirya ma fitan gobe, zamuje da wuri saboda mu dawo da wuri kinsan gobe Friday zuwa 1 hanya ze matse saboda masu zuwa masallaci", wani tsakin Jawahir ta kuma ja tace "kedai zan fito da wuri karki damu, I will be with you guys by 7am", "good, se goben", Zahra tace tareda katse waya
Kwantawa tayi tana kallon ceiling tareda tunanin yanda za'ayi ta samu hanyar fita dan Mamah ta gargadi me gadinsu akan cewar idan ba school Jawahir zataba kar a bari ta fita, gashi gateman din yasan hutu sukeyi
Tashi tayi ta dauko wani peach school bag tasa abubuwan da tasan zata bukata wurin hiking din ta ajiye gefe a daidai lokacin da aka fara kiran sallan magrib
Zama tayi kan gado tareda dauko phone dinta ta fara danne danne ba tareda tayi tunanin tashi yin sallah ba
Wuraren 7:30pm Mamah ta leko dakin dan ganin koh Jawahir tayi sallah dan tasan halin kayanta, da sallama ta shiga dakin taga Jawahir kwance se zuba murmushi takeyi da gani kasan chatting takeyi Mamah tace "Jawahir kinyi sallah?", ba tareda ta dago ba tace "nayi", girgiza kai Mamah tayi tace "tashi kije kiyi sallah lokaci na tafiya", rai bace ta dago tareda cewa "Mamah nace miki nayi, kodan ba'a rubuta a goshina ba shiyasa kike gani kaman banyi ba?", cike da takaici Mamah ta girgiza kai tareda cewa"Allah ya baki hakuri", sannan taja kofan ta fita zuciyarta na kuna
Alhamdullilah ga first page nan na typo muku da izinin Allah
Nasan dayawa suna mamakin halin Jawahir da kuma dalilin da yasa Mamah bata iya hukunta ta, ku cigaba da bina sannan a hankali zan warware muku komai
Yawan comment dinku shi zesa nayi typing next page da wuri, tell me your points of view, ya kukaga labarin, tell me what you think about the story, the more you comment the more I update
Don't forget to vote, comment and share

UWA TA GARI - 2 - Page 4 - Wattpad
Koda Mamah ta koma daki zama tayi kan abin sallarta taci gaba da addu'o'inta tana me rokawa Jawahir gafara wurin ubangiji
Jawahir kuwa bin kofan da Mamah taja tayi da harara tareda tashi ta wuce bathroom tayi alwallah tazo ta duddungura sallanta ta tashi ta koma kan gado dan dai kar ace batayi sallan ba
Sau biyu Baba Salamatu na lekowa akan tazo taci abinci amma tace bataci, haka duk suka kyaleta suka kwanta ba tareda wani ya sake mata magana ba
Se wuraren 12am ta tashi ta canza kayan jikinta zuwa kayan bacci ta fito ta shiga kitchen saboda cikinta dake kururuwar yunwa
Meatpie dinda Mamah ta ajiye a fridge ta dauko tasa a oven tayi heating dinshi sannan ta dau coke ta wuce daki, seda ta gamaci sannan tasa alarm da wayanta saboda tanaso ta riga kowa tashi dan kar aga fitanta, kwanciya tayi bayan ta kashe fitilun dakin ta kunna side lamp
4:30am ta tashi tayi wanka tayi shirinta sannan ta dauko babban hijabi har kasa tasa ta shimfida sallaya ta zauna kai tana jiran shigowar Mamah dan tasan dole Mamah tazo tashinta sallan asuba
Wuraren 5:10am Mamah ta shigo dakin da sallama a tunaninta zataga Jawahir kwance amma ga mamakinta seta ganta zaune kan sallaya tana azkar kaman da gaske, da murmushi a fuskar Mamah tace "Ashe kin tashi, bari naje nima nayi raka'tainil fajr kafin a kira sallah, Allah ya karba", da fadan haka ta fita tareda rufe kofan
Wani murmushi Jawahir tayi sannan ta mike da saurinta ta dau jakan da tasa kaya ciki da wayanta ta fita
Ta kitchen tabi saboda kar a ganta zuwa backyard din gidan, ladder dinda ke ajiye a wurin ta gyarama tsayuwa sannan ta hau ta haura fence tayi ficewarta ana kiran sallan asuba
Gudu ta fara saboda ganin garin ba wani haske ne dashi ba ga tsoro duk ya kamata lokaci daya, seda takai wurin masallacin juma'an unguwarsu sannan ta samu wuri ta tsaya tana jira gari ya gama wayewa ta wuce abinta
Tana zaune wurin har past 6 sannan Zahra ta kirata a waya dan taji koh zata samu fitowa, bata dauka ba seda call din ya katse sannan ta turawa Zahra text cewar zatazo saboda yadda takejin gabanta na faduwa bata ganin zata iya magana
6:30 lokacin gari yayi haske sosai ta tsayar da me adaidaita ta shige tareda fada mishi inda ze kaita, har gaban hiking center din ya ajiyeta ta biyashi kudinshi sannan ya tafi, hijab din jikinta ta cire tasa a jaka tareda ciro face cap tasa akai sannan ta ciro socks da shoes tasa ta hakimce kan wani dutse tana jiran isowan su Zahra, yanda ta zauna hankali kwance bazakace gudowa tayi ba
Takai kusan awa daya zaune a wurin sannan suka karaso cikin wani bus maza da mata sunkai su bakwai, da murmushi ta tashi ta karasa wurinsu tana cewa "you guys kept me waiting, ku kalli lokaci yanzu", wani gaye ne a cikinsu ya kalleta da murmushi tareda cewa "my baby tin yaushe kike nan", harara ta watsa mishi sannan tace "7", ciki ciki kaman bataso yayi murmushi tareda cewa "da gani guduwa kikayi dan kowa nan yasan halinki, a komai ke kike zuwa karshe amma idan wurin satan hanya ne kina riga kuwa zuwa", bata tankashi ba ta kalli Zahra tareda cewa "why did you bring this asshole here?", daga kafada Zahra tayi sannan tace "shiya kawo kanshi bani na kawoshi ba", bata kulasu ba ta koma ta zauna yayinda ko wannensu ke kokarin canzawa zuwa something comfortable
Daya daga cikin en matan ne taje kusa da Jawahir tareda zama gefenta tace "Jawahir hope ba guduwa kikayi daga gida ba?", ajiyar zuciya Jawahir tayi ba tareda ta kalli yarinyar ba tace "I don't have a choice Rumana", girgiza kai Rumana tayi tace "Jawahir banason yadda kike leaving rayuwarki, you need to change for the better girl, wlh da nice akace kar na fito bazan fito ba saboda neman albarkar iyaye amma ke tsalleka maganan Mamah a wurinki ba komai bane", dagowa Jawahir tayi ta kalli Rumana tareda cewa "albarkan Dada kawai ma ya isheni", cikeda mamaki Rumana ta zaro ido waje tana kallon Jawahir kafin tace "ai albarkan iyaye bata isa, koda kuwa kin tsufane balle ma bazaki taba comparing albarkar mahaifiya dana mahaifi ba, ko manzon Allah seda yace kabi uwa, kabi uwa, kabi uwa sannan kabi uba", cikeda rashin nuna kulawa Jawahir ta mike ganin sauran sun gama shiri sannan ta kalli Rumana tace "toh uztaziya nagode da tunatarwa", sannan ta kara gaba ba tareda ta jira cewar Rumana ba
Girgiza kai Rumana tayi sannan tace "Allah ya shirye ki Jawahir", sannan itama tabi bayansu
Gabadaynsu tsayawa sukayi suna kallon gaint rock dinda ke gabansu, basuda burin da ya wuce su haura saman rock din, Zahra data kasance itace kan gaba ta kallesu tareda cewa "who will go first?", gayen da yama Jawahir magana dazu yace "I will", da sauri wani daka cikinsu yace "wait Bash, let's make this a competition", gabadaya kallon shi sukayi suna jiran karin bayani, ya gyara tsayuwa tareda cewa "it won't be fun if we just climb up and back again, mu ajiye kudi ko something expensive, se mu hau a tare, duk wanda ya riga kaiwa gets the price", "I love that idea Isma'il", cewar wata wacce duk ta fisu kankanta a wurin, bata hannu yayi sukayi high five tareda cewa "dats my girl", ba tareda bata lokaci ba suka hada 25k nan take a wurin sannan ko wannensu ya fara shirin hawa dutse
Sosai sukayi nisa wurin hawa Jawahir ta tsaya hutawa dan kuwa sunayi suna hutawa ne ba tareda sun bari kafansu ya zame ba, sosai take maida numfashi dan kuwa ba karamin aiki bane hawa wannan dutsen, lumshe ido tayi tana shakar kamshin dutsen taji motsi ta wurin hannunta, bude ido tayi inda tayi ido hudu da tsaka ba shiri ta saki wani kara tareda cire hannunta wanda yazo da tsautsayi ta zame, "Jawahir!!!", kusan ko wannensu a wurin seda sukayi ihun kiran sunanta amma inaaa tuni Jawahir tayi kasa batama jinsu, a hankali suka fara saukowa ko wanne hankali tashi musamman Rumana dahar ta fara tunanin me zasuce cewa Mamah
Mamah kuwa tana idar da sallolinta ta koma ta kwanta saboda ta samu bacci kadan kafin lokacin zuwa aiki yayi amma sam ta kasa baccin saboda murnar ganin Jawahir kan sallaya da tayi tana azkar, duk a tunaninta Jawahir ta fara shiryuwa ne, ganin baccin ba zuwa zeyi ba ta mike ta shiga wanka, bata dau lokaci ba ta fito ta shirya cikin bakin jallabiya da blue veil, sosai tayi kyau dan idan ka ganka bazakace ita ta haifi Jawahir ba
Jakanta ta dauka tareda laptop da phone dinta sannan ta fito ta ajiyesu kan center table ta karasa kitchen inda Baba Salamatu ke aikin breakfast
"Assalamu alaikum, Baba Salamatu ina kwana", "ameen wa alaikumul salaman, hajiya Hindu kin tashi lfy", "lfy lau Baba", Mamah ta amsa mata da murmushi dauke a fuskarta, Baba Salamatu tace "hajiya yau kin kammala da wuri ince dai lfy", murmushi Mamah tayi tace "lfy lau Baba, ai yau farin cikin ganin Jawahir na sallah ne ya hanani komawa bacci, shine kawai na shirya na fito", kayataccen murmushi Baba Salamatu tayi sannan tace "masha Allah diyata haka nakeso ki kasance cikin farin ciki akoda yaushe, ita kuma Jawahir Allah ya kara shirya miki ita", "ameen", Mamah ta amsa mata dashi tana kokarin bude fridge
Tea ta hadawa kanta sannan ta dau soyayyen kwan da Baba Salamatu ta soya ta koma kan dinning tana karyawa hankalinta kwance yau ta fara ganin changes akan Jawahir
Seda ta gama duk abinda zatayi sannan ta leka dakin Jawahir saboda ta mata sallama
Ganinta tayi kwance tana sharar baccinta, harta juya se kuma ta dawo dan tasan cewar Jawahir bata lulluba da zani har kai, sosai ta karewa figure dinda ke kwance kan gado kallo sannan ta girgiza kai ta karasa tareda yaye comforter din, sosai taji gabanta ya fadi ganin an jera pillow an lulluba musu zani ba Jawahir, kanta daya fara sara mata ta rike tareda zama kan gadon tana karanto addu'o'i, ta dade zaune kafin ta mike jiki ba kwari ta fita zuwa wurin Baba Salamatu dake zaune parlour tana kallon labarai
"Lfy na ganki haka", zama Mamah tayi tana tare kwallan da ke kokarin zubowa tace "Baba Salamatu Jawahir bata gidan", Baba Salamatu batayi mamaki ba, dan ba yau Jawahir ta fara satan hanya ba, se ajiyar zuciya data sauke sannan ta kalli Mamah tace "karki tada hankalinki, ki mata addu'a Allah ya tsareta a duk inda take", cike da takaici Mamah tace "yanzu har Jawahir tayi wayonda zata iya fooling dina saboda ta fita ba tareda na sani, ko ba'a fadamin ba nasan wurin hiking din nan taje, gashi wannan sport din is very risky, idan wani abu ya sameta me nasan zan fadawa mahaifinta wanda a koda yaushe nice mai laifi akan Jawahir", cike da tausayawa Baba Salamatu tace "ki kwantar da hankalinki, zata dawo lfy lau, idan ta dawo seki ja mata kunne ko kuma ki hukunta ta", girgiza kai Mamah tayi tace "hankalina be kwanta da wurin bane, kuma kinsan cewar bazan iya hukunta Jawahir ba, ko yatsa na daga kan Jawahir se kotu ta shiga tsakani, shiyasa nake taka tsantasan wurin ganin bana dukanta dukda kuwa kullum cikin yin abin dukan take", Mamah ta karashe zancenta cikin sheshekar kuka
Wannan karon Baba Salamatu bata hanata kukan ba dan tasan shi kadai ne ze ragewa Mamah radadin da takeji a zuciyarta, seda tayi me isarta sannan ta mike ta shiga toilet dinda ke parlour ta wanko fuskarta sannan ta dawo ta dauki jakanta tayiwa Baba sallama ta fice daga gidan ganin tana neman makara
Tuni ko wannensu ya karaso Zahra har gurjewa tayi a gwiwa tsabar sauri duk suka zagaye Jawahir dake kwance a kasa unconscious, tuni duk suka rude barin ma matan da har sun fara hawaye ganin halin da take ciki
Mazajen ne sukayi karfin halin daukarta sukasa a bus dinda sukazo dashi, kowa ya tattara kayanshi sukayi ciki dan su samu su kaita asibiti
A mota daya daga cikinsu wanda suke kira da Sadiq ya dau waya ya kira mahaifinshi tareda sanar dashi abinda ya faru kasancewar mahaifinshi likita ne
Koda suka kai hospital din already su ake jira, da sauri suka fito nurses din suka dorata kan gado tareda turata zuwa emergency room
Sosai likitocin suka dau lokacin yayinda su Zahra ko wannensu ke safa da marwa sun kasa zaune sun kasa tsaye, daga masu nadama se masu dana sanin fitowa
Rai bace mahaifin Sadiq ya fito tareda karasowa wurin da yaran suke yace "can someone explain to me what exactly happened??", cikin rawar murya Sadiq ya fara labartawa mahaifinshi ai be kai karshe ba yaji saukan tagwayen mari a fuskarta, dafe kuncinshi yayi yayinda mahaifinshi yacigaba da musu fada ta inda yake shiga ba ta nan yake fita ba "yanzu fisabilillahi ku har kunsan kuje wani hiking, ina ku ina hawa kan dutse in banda rigima irin naku, kai Sadiq ubanwa ka fada zaka fita, ni na baro gida thinking kana daki kana bacci ashe bamaka cikin gidan, yanzu dalilin rashin hankalinku gashi kuna nema ku janyowa 'yar mutane matsala, wannan wani irin jidali ne?", gabadayansu shiru sukayi bame cewa kala gashi reception din duk su ake kallo
Ciki da bacin rai yace "ku bani numbern wani wanda zan kira a gidansu", jiki na rawa Zahra ta bada na Mamah aka kira yayta ringing amma bata dauka seta bada na Dada wanda shi ringing daya ya dauka ba tareda ya duba wanda ke kiran ba
Sallaman da yaji an mishi ne yasashi duba number din inda yaga bakon number ya mayar da wayan kunne tareda amsa sallaman suka gaisa cikin mutunci sannan mahaifin Sadiq yace "kai ne mahaifin Jawahir?", seda gabanshi ya fadi jin tambayar da aka mai a hankali yace "eh nine", ba bata lokaci mahaifin Sadiq yace "muna bukatan ku yanzu dan anyi admitting dinta a Sir Yahaya Memorial Hospital", cike da tashin hankali Dada yace "innalillahi wa inna ilaihi raji'un, meyasami Mamana?", "kwantar da hankalinka alhaji ba wani abin daga hankali bane, idan kazo sena maka bayani", cikin rawar murya Dada yace "toh shikenan, bana gari ne ina Abuja amma yanzu zan taho, keep me updated pls", "toh shikenan, Allah ya kawoka lfy" ciki ciki ya amsa da "ameen" tareda kashe wayan
Nan da nan ya fara shirin komawa Birnin Kebbi dan ganin 'yarshi kwaya daya tal da Allah ya azurtashi da ita
Mamah kuwa koda takai wurin aikinta bata bi takan wayanta ba se wuraren sha biyu yayarta ta kirata, daukan wayar tayi tareda sallama ta daya bangaren aka amsa mata sallaman ta, "Yaya Aysha ina kwana", "lfy lau Hindu, kin tashi lfy?", "lfy lau Yaya Aysha", "ya Jawahir,hope ana samun improvement a kanta", ajiyar zuciya Mamah tayi sannan tace "wani improvement Yaya Aysha, yanzu hakama fita tayi wai taje hiking batareda izini na ba, jira kawai nakeyi mahaifinta ya dawo daga tafiyan da yayi ta koma wurinshi dan wallahi hankalina yafi kwanciya idan tana chan", girgiza kai Yaya Aysha tayi sannan tace "toh Allah dai ya shiryeta", "ameen", Mamah ta amsa, "dama na kira ne na fada miki yau Najib ze dawo daga Canada, alhamdullilah ya gama karatunshi", cike da murna Mamah tace "Masha Allah, amma na tayashi murna, Allah ya dawo dashi lfy, Inshallah idan na taso aiki zan biyo", "toh se na ganki, bye", da haka suka ajiye waya inda se'a lokacin Mamah ta lura da miss call dinda aka mata
Ganin bakon number ne seta share amma kuma se hankalinta ya kasa kwanciya ta dau waya tareda kiran number din, mahaifin Sadiq ya gane numbern dan haka dugu biyu ya daga tareda sallama inda ta amsa sannan suka gaisa yake sanar da ita halin da ake ciki
Banda salati ba abinda takeyi dan ta tabbata shikenan nata ya kare a wurin Dada saboda ta riga tasan cewar kasheta ne kawai bazeyi ba akan accident dinda Jawahir ta samu
Jiki na bari ta dauki car keys dinta ta fito hankali tashe ko kallon ma'aikatan dake gaisheta batayi dan kuwa batada burin da ya wuce taje taga halin da Jawahir ke ciki
Har yanzu dai ban kai ga warware muku wannan chakwakiya dake tsakanin Mamah da Jawahir ba, amma sannu a hankali zan warware komai, kudai cigaba da bina har mu karshe
My watsapp readers jiya naji dadin comments dinku sosai Allah ya barmu tare, I love you wujiga wujiga
Don't forget to vote, comment & share

UWA TA GARI - 3 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Dada na ajiye waya ya shirya ya fita, be tsaya ko ina ba se Nnamdi Azikwe International Airport, direct counter yaje, yaci sa'a akwai jirgin da ze tashi zuwa kebbi, ticket ya siya ya koma yana zaman jira, cikin kankanin lokaci suka gama shiryawa jirgi ya tashi
Basu dau lokaci me tsayi ba suka sauka daga airport yayi charter din taxi dan gani yake idan yace ze tsaya jiran driver dinshi ma bata lokaci ne
A gaban hospital din aka ajiyeshi ya biya sannan ya shiga ciki, a reception ya tsaya yana tambayan dakin da aka kwantar da Jawahir, wata nurse ce ta mishi jagora har cikin dakin sannan ta fito dan ta kira mishi doctor
Cike da tausayawa yake kallon Jawahir harya karasa gaban gadon inda take kwance an mata dauri a kafa da hannu daya sannan dayan hannun kuma ana mata karin ruwa ga goshinta ga katon plaster da alama dai ciwo taji a wurin
Hannunta wanda aka ma dauri ya riko tareda shafa kanta da dayan hannunshi a hankali yace "what the hell happened to my princess?", ba me bashi amsa dan haka yaja kujera ya zauna ba tareda ya sake hannun nata ba yaci gaba da kallonta yana me nadamar barinta wurin Mamah da yayi da zai yi tafiya
Mahaifin Sadiq ne ya shigo da sallama tareda karasawa kusa da Dada ya mika masa hannu tareda cewa "I'm Dr Kabir, u must be her father?", kada kai Dada yayi yace "yes", gyara tsayuwa Dr Kabir yayi sannan yace "Good, karka tada hankalinka dan ba wani babban matsala aka samu ba, karaya ta samu a hannun hagu da kafa, se kuma goshinta daya buge da dutse ta samu rauni"
Cike da mamaki Dada yace "dutse kuma, waishin ya akayi ta samu duka wannan raunikan?", kallonshi Dr Kabir yayi yace "da alama baka da labarin cewar ta fita hiking itada kawayenta da abokanta wanda tsautsayi yasa ta fado daga kan dutsen", da sauri Dada yace "subhanallahi, wannan wani irin kasada ne", dafa kafadarshi Dr Kabir yayi ganin Dada ya shiga tunani yace "mu godewa Allah da abin yazo da sauki bezo da karan kwana ba, nan da anjima kadan zata tashi, idan ta tashi ina consultation room 4", kada kai kawai Dada yayi dan beda bakin magana
A haka Dr Kabir ya fita yaja musu kofa
Mamah hankali tashe ta karasa cikin hospital din itama tana tambayar dakin da Jawahir take, har gaban dakin aka kaita sannan nurse din ta juya, gabanta ne ke mummunan faduwa saboda ko ba'a gaya mata ba tasan Osama mahaifin Jawahir na ciki dan kuwa ta jiyo kamshin turarenshi
Lumshe ido tayi sannan ta bude tana sauke ajiyar zuciya, handle din kofan ta kama ta bude sannan ta shiga da sallama, amsa mata sallaman yayi ba tareda ya dago ba har seda ta karaso gaban gadon, bata kai ga riko hannun Jawahir ba taji muryarshi na cewa "i regret leaving her under your care", cak Mamah ta tsaya tana kallonshi bakinta se motsi yake alamar tanaso tayi magana amma maganan yaki fitowa
Dagowa yayi da idanunshi dasuka kada sukayi ja saboda bacin rai yace "meyasa idan Jawahir na wurinki ba'a sati take shiga matsala, meyasa bakya kula da ita yanda ya dace, for goodness sake she is your daughter as well as mine, kidena bari kiyayyar da kikemin na shafanta dan duk abinda ya faru a baya batada masaniya akanshi, keda kanki kika kaini kotu akan na karbe miki 'yarki batayi wayo ba akace na baki 'yarki harse ta shekara bakwai sannan se mu fara rabawa tana zuwa wurina sometimes kuma wurinki amma gabadaya kin kasa kula da Jawahir", shiru yayi daga masifan da yake yayinda Mamah ke tsaye guri daya banda hawaye ba abinda takeyi
A haka yaci gaba da cewa "yanzu kalleta, just look at her, kalli yanda ta dawo kaman ba princess dina ba, she looks pale dan ba haka na tafi na barta ba, amma cikin kwana uku kalli yadda ta dawo", girgiza mai kawai Mamah keyi sannan a hankali tace "Allah ya baku hakuri kai da Jawahir ya huci zuciyarku, kuma inshallah daga rana irin ta yau baza'a kara samun matsala ba dan kuwa na yafema Jawahir har abada kayi duk abinda kaga dama da ita, nima yanzu zan samu kwanciyar hankali Allah ya kawomin wani mijin nayi aure, idan ta tashi kace mata ina mata sannu", tana fadar haka ta fice tana goge hawayen kan fuskarta
Shikuwa Dada sokoko ya tsaya yana kallo harta fita sannan a zuciyarshi yace "lallai ma matar nan, wato maganan da nayi ne ya bata mata rai har take cewa ta yafe Jawahir, toh me take nufi, kenan bataza kara hulda da Jawahir ba kome
", kiranshi dayaji anyi ne yasa ya juyo yana kallon Jawahir wacce take nan idanunta biyu yayinda hawaye ke zuba tace "Dada ka kyaleta ai dama chan ba sona takeyi ba, kuma nima banason ta, tinda Dada na nasona ai shikenan bazan kara zuwa inda take ba", tausayin Jawahir ne yasa hawaye zubo mishi yasa hannu ya gogesu sannan ya shiga gogewa Jawahir nata hawaye yana cewa "uhmm, inshallah your Dada will never disappoint you, I promise to give you both mother and father's love, base da Hindu zaki iya yin rayuwa ba, ko babu ita a rayuwarki life still moves on", murmushi tayi sannan tace "thank you Dada I love you", "I love you too princess", a haka Dr Kabir ya shigo ya samesu, murmushi yayi tareda karasa danya duba Jawahir
Mamah kuwa tana fita ta shiga mota bata tsaya ko ina ba se a gidan Yaya Aysha wacce suke uwa daya uba daya, Allah ne ya kaita gidan lafiya dan kuwa kuka take tana tuki ba sosai take ganin hanya
Horn tayi gateman ya bude mata ta shiga ko tsayawa gyara parking batayi ba ta fito da dan saurinta ta karasa cikin gida, a parlour ta tarar da Yaya Aysha da Najib wanda keta faman zuba mata shagwaba wai tunda yau ya dawo ita zata bashi abinci a baki, se Adil dake zaune gefe yana musu dariya
Da sauri ta karasa wurin Yaya Aysha ta fada kanta tareda sakin wani gunjin kuka, gabadayansu nutsuwa sukayi suna kallonta ba kaman Najib da har kwalla ta taru mishi a ido dan kwatakwata bayason ganin antynshi cikin kunci ko bakin ciki, a hankali Yaya Aysha ta fara bubbuga bayanta yayinda Najib kuma ya matso yana buga kafadarta
Seda sukaga ta tsagaita kukan sannan Yaya Aysha ta kalli Adil tace "babana daukomin ruwa", tashi yayi jiki a mace ya dauko ruwa a fridge da cup ya kawo, Mamah seda ta kusa shanye gora daya sannan ta ajiye tareda sakin ajiyar zuciya tana maida kwallanta
Kallon tsaf Yaya Aysha ta mata sannan tace "lafiya Hindu na ganki haka", girgiza kai Mamah tayi tace "Yaya Aysha Jawahir da mahaifinta nema suke su kasheni, waishin wani laifi nayi ake hukuntani ta wannan hanyan, nayi auren wuri banji dadin auren ba, a haka na lallaba harna haifi Jawahir amma ace yau itace bata ganin kimata da darajata, ita tamin rashin mutunci mahaifinta yazo ya kara da nashi, bakiji irin maganganun da ya gaya min ba akan Jawahir yau", "meyafaru fadamin", cewar Yaya Aysha data maida hankalinta gabadaya kan Mamah, a hankali Mamah ta fara koro mata abinda ya faru tun daga yanda sukayi da Jawahir akan zuwa hiking har zuwa yanzu datasha bakar magana a wurin Dada, tana karashe zance ta karasa da cewa "kuma abinda yafi kona min rai shine koh tambayata ya akayi ya akayi beyi ba, se fada daya rufeni dashi kaman nice najiwa Jawahir din ciwo, fisabilillahi ba rashin jinta bane ya jawo mata ba? da ace taji maganata danace kartaje ai da duk haka baze faru ba", ta karashe zancenta hawaye na ambaliya a fuskarta
Tashi Najib yayi yaja hannun Adil ba tareda sunce komai ba suka fita yayinda Yaya Aysha ta maida hankalinta gabadaya kan Mamah ta riko hannunta tana matsawa cikin nata itama idanunta cike da kwalla tace "hakuri Hindu, hakuri, shine kawai abinda zan cigaba dace miki, nasan bakiji dadin zama da Osama ba kamar yadda bakyajin dadin zama da Jawahir yanzu, amma inaso kisan abu daya, Jawahir gudan jininku ce unlike Osama wanda shi mijinki ne ada, zaki iya canzashi amma koda ace sama da kasa zasu hade bazaki bata iya canza Jawahir a matsayin 'yarki ba, ke kika tsugunna kika haife ta dan haka karki bari bacin rai ko maganganun Osama susa kizo kiyi abinda zakiyi danasani nan gaba, hannunka baya rubewa ka yanke kayar, inaso ki nutsu kisan me kikeso a yanzu, babu wanda ya isa ya rabaki da Jawahir kuma hakkin tarbiyantar da ita na kanki, yanzu da kikace kin yafeta wa kike tunanin ze bata tarbiya me kyau?", girgiza kai Mamah tayi Yaya Aysha tace "babu, sai ke, dan na tabbata rabi da kwatan lalacewar Jawahir Osama ne sila, yanzu da kika barta a hannunshi gabadaya me kike tunanin Jawahir zata zama nan gaba?, inaso ki zauna kiyi tunanin abinda kikeso a rayuwa dan bazeyu ki zauna haka ba, bacin ran yau daban na gobe daban"
A hankali Mamah tace "Yaya Aysha na riga da na yanke hukunci, a yanzu babu abinda nakeso kaman ganin nayi aure, kila idan nayi na samu kwanciyar hankali, sannan Jawahir kuma 'yata ce, komin daren dadewa zata nemeni a duk inda nake dan nasan tabbas duniya zata koya mata hankali"
Murmushi Yaya Aysha tayi tace "Masha Allah Hindu, abinda na dade ina son ji kenan daga bakinki, Allah ya baki miji na gari, me nagarta, me tunani da sanin ya kamata ba irinsu Osama ba, ita kuma Jawahir Allah ya ganar da ita", da murmushi Mamah tace "ameen", tana kwanciya kan kafadar Yaya Aysha yayinda Yaya Aysha kuma ke shafa kanta tana addu'ar Allah ya inganta rayuwar kanwarta
Bangarensu su Najib kuwa karban makullin motar Adil yayi tareda cewa "muje ka rakani", da mamaki Adil yace "Yaya ina zamu?", dan yaga alamun bacin rai a fuskar Najib, Najib be kulashi ba se karasawa da yayi gaban motan ya bude ya shiga cike yayi horn aka bude mishi gate ba shiri Adil ma ya fada motan suka fita inda Najib ke sharara gudu cike da kwarewa yana tuna abinda Mamah ta labarta musu
A compound din hospital dinda Jawahir take yayi parking suka fito shidai Adil ba bakin magana se kallon ikon Allah yakeyi, juyawa Najib yayi ya kalleshi yace "zaka shigo ne ko zaka jirani a nan", kada kai Adil yayi yace "muje", a reception suka tsaya tambayan dakin da take aka musu kwatance suka karasa, da sallama suka shiga wani ajiyar zuciya Najib ya sauke ganin Dada na ciki dan dama wurinshi yazo, ko kallon inda Jawahir take beyi ba sema zubawa gadon harara da yayi sannan ya kalli Dada yace "Alhaji wurinka nazo", ba tareda Dada yayi tunanin komai ba yace "bakaga 'yar uwarka bane, batada lafiya", shiru Najib yayi Adil ne yayi kokarin cewa "Jawahir sannu ya jiki?", kai kawai ta kada mishi dan ita burinta shine Najib ya kalleta tareda yi mata sannu, shikuwa ba tareda ya kalleta ba yace "Allah ya kara lafiya", sannan ya fita waje Dada ya tashi yabi bayanshi shikuma Adil ya karasa ciki ya zauna batareda yace da ita komai ba, itama lumshe ido tayi ta shiga duniyar tunani yau kuma meke samun Najib dayaki kulata haka
A waje suka tsaya Najib ya kalli Dada yace "I'm very disappointed in you Alhaji Osama, gaka a ido kaman wani babban mutum amma a zuci ba haka bane, ita Jawahir bata laifi ne a rayuwa dazaka dauki laifinta ka dorawa Anty", se a lokacin Dada ya fahimci inda maganan ta dosa dan Mamah suke kira da Anty, a zuciyarshi yace "wato harta kai kara", katse mishi zancen zuci Najib yayi da cewa "meyasa baka tsaya ka tambaya ba'asin yanda akayi Jawahir ta fita da sunan hiking ba ka tashi ka dauki fushi ka dorawa Anty, ance maka ita Anty batada zuciya ne?, banzo dan mu tsaya kace nace ba, nazo baka warning ne akan antyna daga yau ko a hanya ka ganta karka nuna kasanta dan baze ace tana tareda kai bataji dadi ba yanzu kuma da bakwa tare still zanin ba canza ba, no, baze yiwu ba, ka dauki Jawahir kayi yanda kakeso da ita muddin bazaka shiga gonar antyna ba, idan har anty bata kula da Jawahir zaka gani idan kuma tana kula da ita zaka gani", yana gama fadar haka ya juya yabar ward din yayinda ya dau waya ya kira Adil, Adil na ganin kiranshi ya taso ya fito ba tareda ya kara kallon Jawahir ba har yazo ya wuce Dada, Dada besani ba dan tunaninshi ya riga yayi zurfi, tabbas yayi kuskure da be tsaya jin ya akayi hakan ta faru ba tinda yasan cewar babu uwar da zata tura 'yarta ga halaka, girgiza kai yayi dan kwatakwata beson yayi wani positive tunani akan Mamah, yafison yata ganin laifinta na ba gaira ba dalili, da wannan ya kawar da tunanin ya koma dakin Jawahir

UWA TA GARI - 4 - Wattpad
ASALIN LABARI
Alhaji Hussain da Alhaji Ahmad wanda akafi sani da A2 aminan juna ne wanda abotansu ya wuce a kirasu da aminai se 'yan uwan juna, duk inda kaga Hussain toh zakaga A2, tun suna yara suke tare sakamakon tasowa da sukayi a unguwa daya, tare sukayi wasan kasa tun sunasa napkin, wannan amintan nasu yasa iyayensu ma suke zumunci
Akwana a tashi Hussain da A2 suka zama matasa wanda a duk fadin unguwarsu ansansu matasa ne su da sukeji da kyau, sosai en mata ke crushing musu sedai su ba wannan ke gabansu ba, lokacin da suka samu admission an samu an biyawa A2 kudin registration inda Hussain kuma iyayenshi ke buga buga ba dare ba rana dan ganin sun samu shima sun mishi nashi registration din amma abu yakici kasancewar iyayensa ba masu hali bane, sosai A2 yasawa iyayenshi daru akan idan basu biyawa Hussain kudin registration ba shima bazashi ba, haka suka kokarta suka biyawa Hussain dukda cewar suma ba wani kudi ne dasu ba
A haka suka fara karatu inda suke karantar mathematics a Kebbi state university, sosai kansu ke ja dan kuwa ba'a competing dasu, cikin ikon Allah suka dinga pass da distinction har suka gama inda gabadayansu suka fita da first class, school authorities din sosai sukaji dadin hikima da kwazo irin na Hussain da A2 gashi mata basa gabansu, abinda ya kawosu shi sukeyi wanda wannan yasa school din da kansu sukayi advertising certificate nasu
Cikin kankanin lokaci aka fara neman su dan a basu aiki, sosai iyayensu sukaji dadi ganin aiki ne ke nemansu basu ke neman aiki ba, sun ma rasa a ina zasuyi aikin dan companies da dama sunaso su basu aiki haka ma gwamnati wanda daga karshe suka zabi suyi aiki a karkashin gwamnatin jihar Kebbi state din saboda sunji dadin garin dansu asalinsu en garin kogi ne, sunada yare (igbira)
A nan Kebbi state university din aka basu lecturing su biyun gabadaya inda a wata suke daukan 250k albashi, sannan kuma aka basu apartment a cikin staff quarters, shekara biyu da fara lecturing sukace zasu dora masters iyayensu suka basu go ahead ba bata lokaci suka fara karatun masters dinsu at the same time suna lecturing kasancewar ba koda yaushe sukada class ba sunmafi karatu weekend
Cikin ikon Allah suka gama lafiya wanda suna gamawa aka kara musu matsayi aka kuma kara musu salary dinsu
Nan iyayensu suka fara musu maganan aure tin suna kaucewa hardai daga karshe suka fito sukace su basu da en mata amma a basu lokaci zasu nema
A cikin students dinsu A2 yaga wata bafullatanan maiduguri wanda ya yaba da nutsuwarta me suna Shaukiyya yace yanaso wanda ta karbeshi hannu bibbiyu kasancewar shima ba bayaba wurin kyau
Hussain kuwa har yanzu ya kasa samun wacce ze aura hardai aka kai kudin gaisuwar A2 yana nan yana neman tashi rabon, a haka akasa ranan A2 da zumar idan Hussain ya samu budurwa ko daga bayane anyi nashi dukda A2 beso hakan ba amma kowa da tashi qaddarar saboda haka ya hakura har Allah ya kawosu lokacin auren, a wurin yinin bikin A2 Hussain ya samo budurwa wacce ta kasance 'yar asalin garin kaduna kuma kawa ga Shaukiyya
Shima ba'a wani bata lokaci ba aka kai kudin gaisuwa Kaduna tareda sa rana inda iyayenta sukace seta gama 200level dinta za'ayi auren dan itama karatu takeyi a Kaduna state university
A kwana a tashi ba wuya har anyi wata bakwai da auren A2 da Shaukiyya wanda a lokacin ma tana dauke da cikin wata shida akayi auren Hussain da amaryarsa Naja'atu
A kwana a tashi ba wuya Shaukiyya ta haifi 'yarta kyakyawa ba inda ta baro mahaifinta sukasa mata suna Aysha sunan mahaifiyar A2 a lokacin kuma Naja'atu na da cikin wata biyu da en sattina, Aysha nada wata goma Allah ya azurta Naja'atu da samun a namiji inda suka rada mishi suna Osama sunan mahaifin Hussain din, Aysha da Osama sun taso kusan kan su aya saboda girman jiki da Osama ke dashi ita kuwa Aysha Allah yayita da karamin jiki
Tin wannan lokacin Allah be kara azurtasu da aa ba, sukan je kogi ziyara tareda yaransu inda iyayensu ke matukar jin dadi amma sunfiso ace yaransu sun dawo kusa dasu sukuma sukace se Kebbi dan gaba-daya ma sun rikie sun koma hausawan Kebbi
Watarana suna zaune aka bugu musu inda aka shaida musu Allah yayiwa mahaifin Hussain rasuwa sakamakon ciwon ciki da yayi fama dashi na kwana aya, sunji mutuwar nan a ransu amma haka suka dangana sukaje kogi akayi zaman gaisuwa dasu harseda akayi bakwai sannan suka dawo da zumar idan za'ayi arba'in zasu dawo sedai ko kafin arba'in din shima mahaifin A2 yace ga garinku
Sunji mutuwar mahaifansu sosai sedai Allahn da yabasu fisu sonsu, koda akayi arba'in se sukace zasu tafi da uwayensu Kebbi amma duk suka ki yarda haka dai suka hakaru suka kyale su
Shekara uku da rasuwan mahaifansu mahaifiyar A2 itama ta kwanta jinya, seda tayi jinyar shekara daya sannan Allah ya karbi ranta, wannan mutuwa ya jijjiga mahaifiyar Hussain dan kuwa gani take itama ai lokacin ta yayi
Bayan rasuwan da shekara daya Allah ya azurta Shaukiyya da samun wani cikin wanda a lokacin Aysha da Osama suna shekara biyar biyar, tare suke zuwa makaranta tare suke dawowa komai tare suke idan ka gansu se kace en biyu ne
A lokacin da Shaukiyya ta zamu ciki yazo mata da laulayi sosai wanda wannan yasa mahaifiyar Hussain zuwa zama dasu danta kula da Shaukiyya saboda a yanzu itace uwarsu itace ubansu dan kuwa basuda wanda ya wuce ita din
A haka cikin ikon Allah Shaukiyya ta sauka lafiya inda ta haifa mace sedai ta samu matsala dole aka cire mahaifarta saboda ya lalace
Tasha kukan bakin ciki sosai kafin ta dangana ganin kukan ba inda ze kaita
Ranar suna baby taci suna Hindu sunan mahaifiyar Hussain saboda su mata kara
Hindu yarinya ce da batada haniya kaman mahaifiyar ta dan kuwa komai na mahaifiyarta ta dauko hatta kamannin, tinda aka haifi Hindu Osama beda abokiyar wasa se ita, tuni ya watsar da Aysha gefe, idan kuwa yaji kukan Hindu ya dinga mata wasa yana lallashin ta kenan harse tayi shiru, idan kuma yaje school ko islamiyya seya siyo mata kayan zaki a hanya tun ana hanashi saboda batakai sha ba har aka hakura aka kyale shi
Ana haka Hussain da A2 suka hada kudi sukayi gini a nan cikin birnin Kebbi din inda sukayi flat uku daya na Hussain daya na A2 se karamin ciki na Hajiya Hindu wacce ta dawo wurinsu da zama
Ganin sun tara dukiya suka ajiye aikin gwamnati inda suka bude Company din kayan mai suka zuba ma'aikata cikin kankanin lokaci sukayi fice duniya tasan da zaman su
Osama nada shekara sha takwas ya samu admission a BUK inda yake karantar business administration saboda ya taimakawa iyayenshi idan ya gama
A wannan shekara Aysha tayi aure duk da anso taci gaba da karatunta ta nuna ita aure take so suka mata ba tareda sun tauye mata hakki ba wanda a wannan lokacin Hindu nada shekara goma sha uku inda take jss 1
Auren Aysha da Yusuf da shekara daya ta haifi danta kyakkyawa inda suka sa mishi Nijib, Hindu na matukar son Najib kaman ita ta haifeshi saboda kama da akace sunayi shima bayan mahaifiyar shi da mahaifinshi baya yarda da kowa se ita
BAKAR RANA

UWA TA GARI - 5 - Page 3 - Wattpad
BAKAR RANA
Yau ya kasance ranar juma'a saboda haka da wuri aka tashi school Hindu ta dawo gida tayi wanka ta canza kayan jikinta zuwa jallabiya sannan ta shige dakin mahaifiyarta, da sallama ta shiga taga mahaifiyarta kwance hannunta rike da carbi da alama lazumi takeyi
"Sunnu Ammi", dagowa tayi ta kalli Hindu tareda cewa "yauwa daughter se ina haka", murmushi tayi tace "zanje gidan Yaya Aysha ne in dauko Najib yazo ya mana weekend", gyara kwanciya Shaukiyya tayi tace "kinsan dai bata yayeshi ba, dan haka bazaiyu yazo ya kwana ba, ki daije ki gaishesu amma karkiyi dare saboda kisan hanya ba kyau, biyar nayi ki bar gidan ki dawo", a hankali cikin sanyinta tace "toh Ammi"
Fita tayi a compound taga Osama na shirin shiga mota zashi masallaci dayake suna hutu ta karasa wurinshi da dan saurinta tace "ina wuni Ya Osama", murmushi yayi ya dago yana kallonta yace "sweetsis se ina haka kika dau wanka", murmushi tayi tace "gidan Yaya Aysha zani", ada kai yayi yace "shigo muje na saukeki tinda duk hanya ne, amma fa kinyi kyau", ya karasa fada yana mata wink, hannu tasa ta rufe fuskar ta alamar kunya ta zagaya ta shige motar shikuwa karamar dariya yayi ya tada motar suka bar gidan
Duk abinda sukeyi akan idon Hussain da A2 wanda suka fito daga angaren Hajiya Hindu dan zuwa masallacin, murmushi sukayi Hussain yace "kaga Abinda nake fada maka koh, hada Osama da Hindu aure shine kwanciyar hankalinmu dan kuwa shine kadai mukeda tabbacin ze kula da ita koda bayan ran mu ne", murmushi A2 yayi yace "wannan haka yake amma inaga mu farawa Osama magana saboda kar mu danne mishi hakki", tsaki Hussain yaja yace "idan mun isa dashi bazeki bin maganar mu ba", a haka suka shiga mota suna kara tautauna maganar
A gaban gidan Yaya Aysha ya sauketa sannan yace "idan kin tashi tafiya gida ki kirani da wayan Aysha inzo in daukeki, banson kina bin hanya ke kadai", "toh Ya Osama zan kiraka Inshallah", gada kai yayi tareda cewa "ki gaisheta", sannan yaja motar yayi gaba
Kwankwasa gate tayi me gadi ya bude mata ta gaisheshi cikeda ladabi ya amsa sannan ta karasa ciki, da sallama ta shiga parlourn gidan inda taga Najib kwance a kujera shikadai se shure shure yakeyi irin nasu na jarirai yanasa hannu baki alamar yunwa, ya bata fuska yanaso yayi kuka, da sauri ta karasa wurinshi ta daukeshi tana jijjigashi tareda cewa "oh my baby boy, ina momma ta tafi ta barka uhm", tsit yayi kaman yasan itace ta daukeshi ta juya zata shiga bedroom din Yaya Aysha ta ganta ta fito daga kitchen, dawowa tayi tace " Yaya Aysha ina wuni, dama kina kitchen?", Amsa gaisuwarta tayi tace "ina ciki kawoshi inda bashi abinci", mika shi tayi suka zauna suna hira yayinda Yaya Aysha ke bashi nono
Har yamma tana gidan tana wasa da Najib, seda aka mishi wanka taga yayi bacci sannan ta dau wayan Yaya Aysha ta kira Osama ya dauka yana yacewa "gani kofar gida dan ko kinyi niyyar kira yanzu inada niyyar shida nayi zanzo", murmushi tayi tana kashe wayar Yaya Aysha dake tsaye tace "wasa wasa Osama akwai masifa shima din", murmushi kawai ta sake yi ta mike tana cewa "toh ni na wuce", "yauwa Hindu, ki gaida gida, kicewa Ammi zanzo gobe", tana yafa mayafi tace "toh Allah ya kaimu", tareda karban dari biyar dinda Yaya Aysha ke mika mata tayi godiya sannan ta fita
Gaisheshi tayi sanda ta shiga motar ya amsa mata yana cewa "wato da bakida niyyar dawowa da wuri koh?", girgiza kai tayi tace "wlh bansan lokaci ya wuce haka ba", shiru yayi bece komai ba har suka karasa gida yayi parking tareda cewa "shiga ciki, ni fita zanyi se anjima zan dawo", fita tayi tace "a dawo lafiya", yace "ameen" tareda jan motar
Misalin arfe biyun dare A2 na kwance yana aiki a laptop dinshi beyi barci ba yaji durowar mutane cikin gidan, sosai gabanshi ya fadi ya tashi a hankali ya leka ta window inda yaga mutane sun kai biyar ko wannensu da mask a fuskar shi , a hankali ya koma ya dauki wayanshi tareda kiran Hussain amma ina yayi nisa da bacci wanda hakan ya hanashi daga waya sema shiga voicemail da kiran keyi, kashe wayan yayi yay dail din number police cikin kankanin lokaci suka dauka ya sanar dasu halin da ake ciki sukayi alkawarin zuwa yanzu
Ajiye wayan yayi sannan ya fara haa duk wasu important documents dinshi wuri aya wanda Allah ya taimakesu daga document din Hussain har nashi hae suke wuri aya, buya ta musamman ya musu sannan ya koma ya kwanta kaman besan da bakin dari a gidan ba ya barwa Allah ikon shi
Rabuwa sukayi biyu suka shiga bangaren A2 biyu kuma suka shiga bangaren Hussain aya ya tsaya a compound yana busa sigari, gabadayansu tasosu akayi aka taso keyarsu da bindiga suka kwanta a compound din gidan amma banda Hindu wacce da alama basu san da ita ba
Wanda ke tsaye a compound din gidan ne ya kalli sauran yaran yace "a lissafina su goma ne a gidan hae da me gadi da masu aikinsu amma tinda mun samu wa'anda mukazo wurinsu shikenan, juyawa yayi ya kalli su A2 dake kwance a matukar tsorace yace "hadin kai zaku bamu, idan kunason mu rabu lafiya, ko wannenku ze mana jagora zuwa inda kukasan zamu samu abinda mukazo nema ba tareda gardama ba", a hankali A2 yace "Inshallah zamuyi abinda kukeso", yayinda Hussain cikin bacin rai yace "No way!", dukan kanshi sukayi da bayan bindiga yayinda Naja'atu da Shaukiyya sukasa ihu suma duk aka bisu aka mammake saboda suyi shiru wanda duka abinda ke faruwa a kan idon Hindu wacce take kallo ta windown dakin mahaifinta dan motsinsu ne ya tasheta ta shige dakin A2 saboda ta tabbata tanan ne zataga komai duk da tasan cewar ba iya taimakonsu zatayi ba
A2 da Hussain aka dago inda mutane biyu biyu suka musu jagora zuwa nashi bangaren, tuni Hindu ta boye karkashin gado hawaye na zubo mata saboda tsoro amma ko kadan bata bari kukanta ya fito waje ba
Save A2 ya bude musu suka diba kudi sun ransu sannan suka juya, sheshekar da na karshen su yaji ne yasashi tsayawa saboda yaji daga ina kukan ke fitowa, a hankali ya taka har tsakiyar dakin dan ya lura daga karkashin gado ne ya tsugunna sannan yasa hannu ya janyo ta yana dariyar mugunta yayinda ita kuma tasa wani razanniyar kara wanda yasa duk wani mahaluki dake gidan sannin cewa an samu matsala, amma kowa lamo yayi saboda son kai banda Hajiya Hindu da tayi karfin halin fitowa amma cak ta tsaya ganin abinda ke faruwa saboda ko ina da wuta, fito da ita yayi yayinda daya cikinsu ya janyo Hajiya Hindu itama haka ta kwanta kasa ba tareda sun tausayawa mata ba
Har gaban ogansu ya kawo ta jikinta se kakkarwa yakeyi tana kuka sosai, tsayawa kallonta ogansu yayi sanye take da farin sleeping dress zuwa gwiwa, tsayawa raya kyau irin nata yayi a zuciyarshi yana raya kyawun hallita da za'ayi idan ta kara girma nan gaba
Hannu yasa yana shafa fuskarta da sauri Osama ya tashi cikin tsananin bacin rai yace "don't you dare lay a finger on her", mari aya daga cikinsu ya sauke mishi amma Osama koh gezau, A2 da Hussain ma zuciyarsu tafarfasa yakeyi sosai haka zalika Naja'atu, Hajiya Hindu da Shaukiyya ba karamin bugawa yake ba
Sake tabata yayi Osama ya matsa ze tunkaroshi cikin wata irin murya yace "taku daya idan ya kara ku harbe minshi", cak Osama ya tsaya yayinda ogansu ya kalli su A2 da suka koma suka kwanta yace "zan baku daman rufe ido saboda abinda zan aikata yanzu nasan har karshen rayuwarku bazaku manta ba sannan kuma kai
", ya fada yana kallon Osama yace "idan ka kuskura ka rufe koda ido daya ne sena harbe tsohuwar ka", gabadayansu gabansu faduwa yakeyi ba kaman Shaukiyya da banda addu'a ba abinda takeyi dan ko kadan bata don su taba mata yarinya
A gaban idon Osama ya cire wandoshi wanda yasa Hindu saurin runtse ido da sakin wani karan saboda ganin abinda bata taba gani ba tana kuka me tsuma zuciya, ja daya yama 'yar rigar dake jikinta ya yage da sauri Osama yace "yanzu me zakaci a jikin yarinya karama, me kake tunanin aikatawa?, nasan tabbas idan baka da yarinya kamarta kanada kanwa, ka tausaya mata karka lalata mata rayuwa", wani dariya ya bushe dashi sannan ya kalli Osama yace "tabbas bakayi karya inada kanwa wacce bazata wuce wannan ba amma kasan wani abu, ta dade da rasuwa ta wannan hanyar itama, a gabana aka mata fyade wanda wannan yasa na dau alwashin sena bari mutane sama da dari sun dadi ciwo da radadin da na dandana", yana fadar haka ya kwantar da Hindu akan lafiyayyar kwalta din gidan ya cire mata pant tana kuka tana tureshi amma kaman ma bashi take turewa ba
Shaukiyya, Naja'atu da Hajiya Hindu banda kuka ba abinda sukeyi yayinda Hussain da A2 kuwa tuni hawayen bakin ciki ya wanke musu fuska, wannan wata irin addara ce ace a gabanka a ma 'yar cikinka fyade kanaji kana gani ba yanda ka iya, Osama kyam idonshi akan Hindu ko kyaftawa bayayi tuni idonshi ya bushe ba alamun kwalla a ciki, ihun Hindu da kukanta har cikin kwakwalwar shi yakeji, sunaji suna gani Hindu ta rasa budurcinta a gabansu, seda suka kammala suka fice ta gate suda suka hauro ta fence sannan aka fara jin jiniyan en sanda
Da sauri Shaukiyya tayi kan Hindu wacce ta dade da suma ta rungume ta tana kuka me tsuma zuciya, Osama kuwa ko motsin kirki baya iyayi inda yake nan yake ko motsawa bayayi
Hajiya Hindu ce cikin muryanta daya riga ya dishe tace "Ahmadi dauketa ku kaita ciki, karku bari en sanda susan da wannan saboda ta haka ne kawai zamu iya rufawa kanmu asiri", A2 be musa ba ya dauki Hindu a hannu yayi ciki da ita idonshi cike da kwalla, shigowar en sandan yasa Hussain share kwallarshi ze fara musu bayani A2 ya fito yace "karka yarda kace musu wani abu akan wannan case din, dan ko ka fada a banza, saboda kusan awa daya kenan danayi kiransu amma seda suka daidaici an gama komai sannan suka zo", haka en sanda suka sasu gaba amma basu samu wani information daga mutanen gidan ba, haka suka hakura suka juya suka wuce cike da kunya da takaici
Da safe aka kira doctor yazo ya duba Hindu wacce har lokacin bata tashi ba, gwaje-gwaje ya mata sannan ya mata allurai tareda mata arin ruwa sannan ya juya ga familyn yace "dogon suma tayi saboda ta tsorata amma Inshallah zata farfao, sedai seta samu lafiya zamu sani whether she's stable or not, amma for now dai na mata allurai wanda ze kara mata karfin jiki"
Gabadayansu ada kai kawai sukayi jiki a sanyaye yayinda Hussain yayi karfin halin masa godiya tareda cewa "dan Allah munaso wannan abin yazama sirri, kasan generation dinnan damuke ciki, yanzu se society su hanata shan iska me dadi", ada kai doctor yayi sannan yace "na fahimce ku Alhaji amma kuma inaga gwara duniya su sani kuma a kokarta a kwatar mata 'yancin ta saboda gaba, shirun da kuke shirin yi shi yakesa cases irin wannan kara yalwata a cikin al'umma"
Ba tareda A2 ya kalleshi ba yace "bazan yaa 'ata ga idon duniya ba, na barwa Allah komai, Inshallah se Allah ya shiga tsakaninmu da wannan azzaluman", fahimtar basuda niyyar daukar mataki yasa ya musu sallama tareda cewa idan ta tashi su kirashi
Yana fita Yaya Aysha na shigowa da sallama, Hajiya Hindu ce kawai tayi karfin amsa mata sallama dan Shaukiyya ma bebiya ta zama, ido kawai ta zubawa Hindu ta lula duniyar tunanin da ita kadai tasan me take tunani, cike da fargaba Yaya Aysha ta gaishesu duk ciki ciki suka amsa mata, wurin Naja'atu dake zaune gefen gado ta zuba tagumi ta nufa a hankali tace "anty lafiya kuwa, ko Hindu ce ba lafiya", hawaye ne ya gangarowa Naja'atu yayinda ta shiga labartawa Yaya Aysha abinda ya faru, kuka sosai takeyi tareda tsinewa wannan bawan Allah da yayi nasarar lalatawa kanwarta rayuwa
Mikewa Osama yayi ya bar dakin, dakin shi ya wuce ya kwanta tareda lumshe ido, babu abinda yake gani se lokacin azzalumin nan yayi nasarar tura joystick dinshi a gaban Hindu, da sauri ya bude ido hawaye na gangarowa, hasbunallahu wa ni'imal wakil ya dinga maimaita harsai da yaji zuciyar shi tayi mishi sanyi sannan ya tashi ya shige bathroom saboda watsa ruwa

UWA TA GARI - 6 - Page 4 - Wattpad
Kwana biyu kenan da faruwan mummunar abinda ya auku akan Hindu, gaba-daya ta canza bata magana, bata tashi daga inda take, abinci ma se anyi da gaske take ci, a takaice ma dai dura ake mata
Osama kuwa be kara zuwa inda take ba tin daga ranar, idan ya tashi da safe ya fita baya dawowa se goma na dare, yana dawowa kuma ze kwanta koh lekata bayayi
Wannan abin sosai ya canza rayuwar mutanen gidan ba kaman Hindu, Osama da Shaukiyya wacce tafi kowa sanin ciwon 'arta, ganin haka ne yasa Hajiya Hindu cewa zata dauki Hindu su koma Kogi a canza mata makaranta a chan kila ta dan sake amma Hindu tace ba inda zata, ba yanda ba'ayi da ita ba taki tafiya
Ganin iyayenta na shiga damuwa yasa ta fara sakewa tana fitowa amma abinda ke matukar bata mamaki shine rashin ganin Osama, tayi tunanin ya koma makaranta ne shiyasa bata wani damu sosai
BAYAN SHEKARA DAYA
Gabadayansu sun dangana sun maida komai ba komai ba sunci gaba da rayuwarsu kaman ba wani abu daya taa faruwa
A halin yanzu Hindu nada shekaru goma sha biyar, sosai ta zama budurwa dan har an fara samun masu zuwa cewa suna sonta
Ganin haka yasa su Hussain tsaida ranar aurenta da Osama saboda kar asamu wanda ze hure mata kai idan sukace sun mata miji taki amince ba tareda sun sanar da yaran cewar an musu baiko ba
A ranar da Osama ya dawo daga school aka zaunar dasu gaba-dayansu Hussain yayi gyaran murya tareda cewa "Osama kai ana ne, nasan kanada masaniyar cewa bazan taa cutar da kai ba, Hindu kanwarka ce, mun dade da muku baiko tsakaninku, saboda haka yau nake maka albishir da cewar nan da wata daya me zuwa zamu aura maka Hindu a matsayin matarka duk da musan cewar bawai ka kai ka rike mata bane"
Osama ji yayi kaman ya dora hannu a kai ya fasa ihu, tuni zufa ya wanke mishi fuska yasa handkerchief ya goge yana mamakin meyasa iyayensa suka masa haka, a rasa wacce za'a aura masa se Hindu, yarinyar da aka lalata mata rayuwa a gabanshi, da wani idon ze kalleta? wani irin rayuwar aure ze shimfida da ita bayan har yanzu ya kasa cire abinda ya faru ranar a kanshi, ba komai yasa yake guje mata ba sedan duk sanda ze ganta se ya tuna da wannan mummunar ranar, yanzu a haka akeso ya aure ta? Ina bazai yiwu ba
Tunani kala kala yakeyi ya kasa dagowa ya kalli iyayenshi balle su san halin da yake ciki, ita kuwa Hindu rakuewa tayi jikin kujera hawaye na silala a kumatunta dan ta tabbata Osama ba sonta yakeyi ba, a rayuwa batada da burin da ya wuce tayi auren soyayya, ta auri wanda take so kuma yake sonta amma koda ace tanajin son Osama a zuciyarta ta tabbata shi baya sonta
A2 ne yayi karfin halin cewa "Osama idan kaga banason Hindu zamu janye maganar mu", murmushin da yafi kuka ciwo Osama yayi a hankali yace "Abba na isa ince banason jinin ka, aiko bana sonta muddin kukace na aureta zan kokarta na koyawa zuciyata sonta, saboda haka Abba na amince da zabinku Allah yasa yakan shine mafi alkhairi", gabadayansu sunji dadin abinda yace, da murmushi kan fuskar ko wannensu Hussain yace "Masha Allah, haka akeso a nagari ya kasance, Allah ya muku albarka gabadayanku", da ameen suka amsa sannan duk suka mike suka fita
Tun daga ranar Ammi ta fara gyara 'yarta, dama ta dade tana gyarata orawa tayi daga inda ta tsaya, Hindu ta zuba ido ta gani ko Osama ze zo su fuskanci juna amma har aka fara shirye shiryen biki dangin su suka fara zuwa batasa Osama a ido ba
Wannan kawai ya tabbatar mata da lallai Osama baya sonta
Shikuwa tin daga ranar yabar gidan ya tare gidan wani abokinshi sedai yazo ya gaida iyayensa ya koma
Duk wani hidima na aure wanda akasan namiji keyi su A2 da Hussain ne sukayi dan kuwa Osama bemada kudin hada lefe balle na kama gida, yanzu yake final year dinsa a University
Rana bata karya a yau aka sheda daurin auren Osama Hussain Osama da matarsa kuma kanwarsa Hindu Ahmad akan sadaki Naira dubu talatin saboda albarkan dake ciki ake nema
A ranar ta tare gidanta wanda aka siya musu halak malak dinsu, karfe 9 ango ya shigo wurin amaryarshi saboda ko kadan bayaso ya tauye mata hakki inba haka ba da bazezo ba
Da sallama ya shiga dakinta inda ta amsa a sanyaye cikin disasshiyar murya alamar taci kuka ta koshi, a hankali ya karasa ya zauna kan gadon tareda zuba mata ido, rasa me zaice mata yayi, a haka suka dauki sama da minti goma kafin yayi ta maza yace "Hindu tashi muyi sallah", a hankali tace "nayi sallah", murmushi yayi be takurata ba yace "toh tashi kici abinci ga kaza na kawo miki", bata musa ba tashi ta sauko daga kan gadon ta yaye mayafinta ta zauna kasa shima cire babban riganshi yayi ya dawo kasa ya zauna tareda bude mata yace ta faraci yana zuwa
Kitchen ya shiga ya dauko cup ya dawo ya juye mata lemun fanta dinda ya siyo ciki ya zauna yana kallonta tanaci, seda ta gama sannan yace tayi wanka ta kwanta, haka kuwa akayi seda yaga bacci ya dauketa sannan shima yaci sauran da ta rage shima ya watsa ruwa yazo ya kwanta gefenta tareda zuba mata ido, a haka har bacci ya daukeshi
Haka suka kwashi tsawon sati daya daga gaisuwa se hira sama sama se kuma idan ze tambaye ta ko tanason wani abu, wannan al'amarin ya dami Hindu sosai saboda haka tayiwa kanta alkawarin tambayansa dalilinshi na yawan shareta, yau koda ta gama abinda takeyi batayi bacci ba ta zauna zaman jiranshi ya dawo, da sallama ya shigo ta amsa mishi sallaman shi, sosai yayi mamakin ganinta zaune saboda yasan tana saurin bacci, cikin sanyin jiki ya karasa ciki dakin yana cewa "bakiyi bacci ba?", ada kai tayi tace "banyi ba", basu kara cewa komai ba tana kallonshi ya watsa ruwa yayi abinda zeyi yazo ya kwanta yana cewa "ki kwanta, sha daya fah yanzu", shiru tayi ta rasa ta yanda zata fara mishi magana, juyowa yayi ya kalleta jin shiru seya tashi zauna yana fuskantar ta yace "koda wani abu ne?", share guntun hawayenta tayi cikin sanyinta tace "dama ina so ne in tambayeka meyasa baka jana a jiki sosai, meyasa baka zama sosai, bakason mun magana??", shiru yayi na en dakiku yana kallonta, be taba tunanin yarinya kamarta zata damu da rashin kulawarshi gareta ba amma se gashi da bakinta take tambaya
Kallon gefe yayi sannan yace "banda kwakkwaran hujja Hindu, amma ki yafemin idan na tauye miki hakki", girgiza kai tayi tace "bakamin komai ba", ranar farko kenan daya janyo ta jikinshi sukeyi bacci rungume da juna duk da karfin hali yakeyi saboda ko yaya ya motsa yajita jikinshi seya tunota a hannun wannan azzalumin
Washegari Yaya Aysha tazo ziyartar su, bayan sun gaisa da Osama sun dan taba hira taja Hindu daki, cikin salo ta gano cewar babu abinda ya shiga tsakanin Osama da Hindu sakamakon tambayoyin da tayiwa Hindu din
Data tashi tafiya taja Osama gefe ta mishi wa'azi akan hakkin mata akan mijinta da kuma hakkin miji akan matarsa tareda fahimtar dashi ya kamata ya kokarta ya sauke hakkin dake kanshi, seda taga ta daidaita komai sannan ta musu sallama ta wuce
A daren ranar Osama yaso karban hakkin shi wurin Hindu dan yaji wa'azin da Yaya Aysha ta mishi sosai amma sam ya kasa, sosai ya dinga playing nata tun tana tureshi har ta hakura ta bada kai bori ya hau, sedai Osama na kaiwa kofan wambai yaga baze iya shiga ba saboda tsananin kishin wani ya rigashi, haka ya hakura ya sauka daga kanta kasancewar dama chan kuka take mishi, bathroom ya shiga ya barta kwance wurin itakuwa hamdala tayi dan a ganinta tausayinta yaji ya kyaleta
Haka suka kwashi kwana hudu suna abu daya, amma Osama ya kasa dangana ya barwa Allah komai, ita kuwa Hindu baiwar Allah bata dauka hakan a bakin komai ba duk da kuwa idan ya barta takanji feelings na taso mata amma gani take da ta sake jin irin azabar da taji ranar nan gwara ta hakura yata wasa da jikinta kawai dukda ta tabbata komai daren dadewa seya karba hakkinshi tinda ita ba jahila bace
BAYAN KWANA BIYU
Yau Osama se shirye shirye yakeyi kasancewar washegari ze koma school, yana gama shirya kayanshi ya kalli Hindu dake zaune gefe ta zuba tagumi tana kallonshi dan kuwa dan zamansu dinnan yasa wata irin shakuwa ta shiga tsakaninsu dukda ba wani jan juna sukeyi a jiki sosai ba, murmushi yayi dan ya harbo jikinta yazo kusa da ita ya zauna tareda dagata ya dorata kan ciyarshi yana jan kumatunta yace "Matar Osama yada tagumi", kwantar da kanta tayi kan kirjinta shikuma ya dinga shafa gashinta yana jiran amsa, jin shiru yasa ya kara tambayar ta a hankali tace "ni karka tafi, bazan iya zama nan ni kadai ba, tsoro nake ji", murmushi yayi yace "kodai zakiyi missing dina ne hmm", boye fuskarta tayi a kirjinshi tana daga mishi kai alama "eh", yayi 'yar dariya tareda cewa "karki damu idan na tafi wannan karon three months zanyi na dawo, kuma bazan barki a nan ke kadai ba, gida zan kaiki ki zauna a chan harse na dawo"
Murmushi tayi tareda kara shigewa jikinshi, shidai harga Allah nutsuwa da kunyar Hindu na birgeshi, kissing din gashinta yayi yana shafawa tareda kissing din wuyanta yana mata wasannin da ya saba, tun tana nokewa hardai ta saki jiki itama ta biye mishi ya samu ya kashe arna, yau dai Allah yayi Osama ya kai zuciya nisa ya barki hakkinshi wurin Hindu dukda kuwa kukan da taci, sosai yasha mamakin ganin ba yanda yayi tunanin ze jita ba haka ya jita ba, duk a tunaninshi bazesha wahala wurin samun hanya ba tinda yasan already hanya a bude take sedai inaa, abu yasha bambam dan kuwa a kulle yaji wurin saboda tsananin gyaran da tasha a gida dukda baza'a hadata da mace virgin ba amma itama kam Alhamdullilah yaji dadi yanda ya sameta
Da kanshi ya gyara mata jiki ya mata wanka tazo ta kwanta saboda gajiya, a wannan ranar love akasha tsakanin Osama da Hindu inda washegari ma be barta ba seda ya kashe arna sannan ya dauketa ya kaita gidansu, wannan karon wurin Naja'atu zata zauna taci gaba da zuwa school harya dawo sannan ta koma gidanta
Ganin yanda yake rawar jiki a kanta yasa Naja'atu fahimtar wani abu, murmushi tayi a zuciyarta tace "lallai Hindu zakisha gyara a wurina kodan na dinga ganin irin wannan annurin a fuskar a aya tilo da Allah ya bani", seda ya zagaya gabadaya gidan ya musu sallama sannan ya wuce cike da kewar amaryarsa
A gurguje
Alhamdullilah Osama ya gama karatunshi lfy inda yace baya bukatan yin service saboda a company din iyayenshi zeyi aiki, sun bashi maganer inda ya dauki aikinshi seriously, kullum seya sauke Hindu a school sannan yake wucewa wurin aiki, 2pm lokacin da suke lunch break zeje ya dauketa ya maida ita gida
Tuni dukkansu sunyi wani kyau sunyi jiki saboda kwanciyar hankali dan tsakaninshi da Hindu ko chachar baki basayi saboda biyayya irin nata, a kwana a tashi ba wuya Hindu ta gama secondary inda a lokacin tanada 17yrs, ta kara kyau sosai, boobs, hips, bum sedai ka alla kace Masha Allah dan kuwa Hindu Allah ya azurtata da kyau da diri
Kwana biyu kenan Hindu na fama da zazzai, tin batason zuwa asibiti hardai ta yarda Osama ya kaita dan a dubata, bayan en gwaje gwaje aka tabbatar musu da ciki ne da ita harna tsawon wata uku da en kwanaki ma, sosai sukayi murna ba kaman Osama daya dauki son duniya ya dorawa cikin
Tinda akace Hindu nada ciki ta fara ganin canji wurin Osama dan motsi kadan idan tayi zece "hankali karki mun asara", wannan kalaman na matukar bata mata rai amma sedai ta hadiye bata cewa komai, sannan tinda ta samu ciki Osama be sake kusantarta ba ita har tunani takeyi kodai kyamarta yakeyi amma data tambayeshi yace ba haka bane kawai dai beson ya takurawa babynshi ne, tayi hakuri idan ta haihu he's all hers
Hindu tayi kukan bakin ciki ranar da Osama ya mata wannan maganar amma haka ta hakura dukda kuwa tsananin bukatar mijinta dake taso mata, taso danne damuwar ta amma sam ta kasa, cikin kankanin lokaci ta rame ta zama wani iri se ido da dogon wuya da katon ciki, babu wanda ya kawo wani abu a ranshi dan duk tunaninsu laulayi ne ya maida ita haka nan basu san cewar damuwa ne ya sata gaba ba
Lokacin da cikin ta ya shiga wata bakwai sukaje gwaji asibiti doctor yata fada kan an barta ba'a kula da ita har gashi jininta ya hau
Osama hakuri ya dinga bawa likita a haka suka karba magunguna suka dawo gida, suna zuwa gida yasata gaba da fada inda yake shiga ba nan yake fita akan tana nema ta halaka mishi baby, idan ita batason babyn toh shi yanason kayanshi dan haka ta kula karta kuskura tayi abinda zesa babynshi ya samu matsala
A ranar Hindu ba karamin kuka tasha ba, wato shi bama ta ita yakeyi ba babynshi ne ya dameshi, a haka nakuda ya sameta gadan gadan ba tareda ta shirya ba, kiran wayanshi takeyi amma bata shiga, sosai ta galabaita ta rasa inda zata kanta, cikin ikon Allah Yaya Aysha ta diro gidan da sallaman ta itama da nata katon ciki wanda haihuwa yau ko gobe, sosai tashiga tashin hankalin ganin halin da Hindu ke ciki dan tuni ruwa ya alle mata, da kyar ta samu ta daga Hindu suka fita ta samu napep suka shiga ya kaisu asibiti, seda taga an shiga da Hindu labour room sannan ta kira Osama cikin sa'a kuwa ya kunna wayarshi dama suna meeting ne shiyasa ya kashe
Seda yaje gida ya dauko kayan haihuwa sannan ya dawo asibiti cikin rawar jiki, yana karasowa doctor na zuwa, kallon Osama yayi sannan yace "I'm sorry to say amma matarka bazata iya haihuwa da kanta ba saboda hanyar ta matse dayawa kuma wannan laifinka ne a matsayin ka na mijinta, dole muyi gaggawar yi mata cs saboda ceto ran jaririn dake cikinta idan ba haka ba zamu iya rasasu gaba-daya"
Sharce gumi Osama yayi sannan ya karba file dinda nurse ke mika mishi yasa hannu aka shiga da Hindu theater room dan ceto ranta
Da mamaki Yaya Aysha ke kallon Osama a hankali tace "Osama idan na fahimce abinda doctor ya fada ka dade baka sadu da Hindu ba kenan bayan kasan ciki ne da ita, dat's wat she needs the most", gumi ne ya zubo kan goshinshi yasa handkerchief ya goge idonshi cike da hawaye yace "I'm sorry", babu wanda ya sake magana cikinsu se zaman jiran tsammani har seda doctor ya fito
Da sauri suka karasa gabanshi Osama yace "How's the baby
", yayinda a tare itakuma Yaya Aysha tace "How's Hindatu
", gabadayansu kallon Osama sukayi jin abinda ya fito bakinshi, wato babynshi ce a gabanshi ba matarshi ba, cike da kunya yace "How's my wife doing?", girgiza kai doctor yayi yace "Alhamdullilah da cs was successful your wife is stable and your baby is also healthy sedai tana samun difficulty wurin numfashi which is possible kasancewar da dade tana kokarin fitowa ba hanya, amma Inshallah wannan ba problem bane zamu kula da ita, yanzu zamuje asa babyn a incubator tinda bakwaini ce while the mother kuma zamu bata daki"
Dadi kashe Osama ance masa babynshi is alright, cike da murna yace "thank you doctor can i see them", murmushi doctor din yayi yace "sure, amma se an gama gyarasu"
Tuni labari har ya isa gida Hindu ta haihu ta haifi mace dan Yaya Aysha bata ata lokaci ba ta kira ta sanar dasu, shi kuwa Osama Allah Allah yakeyi yaga yarinyar shi, tun a lokacin Yaya Aysha tasan cewar da matsala tsakanin Hindu da Osama wanda koh ita Hindu yanzu aka tambaye me matsalan batada amsa dan kuwa tasan zaman lafiya sukeyi da Osama amma kaman kar ace ta samu ciki ya canza kuma yanason cikin jikinta bawai beso ba
Readers kuna ganin Osama ya kyautawa Hindu kuwa??

Gaskiya Osama baiyi amana ba
UWA TA GARI - 7 - Page 3 - Wattpad
Seda sukayi kusan sati daya a hospital sannan aka sallame su, gida ta koma saboda jego, sosai take samun kulawa ta kowani bangare har gurin Osama kuwa inda kullum seyazo dubasu ita da babynta wacce suka sawa suna Jawahir, Jawahir ba inda ta baro Hindu wurin kamanni, komai na mahaifiyarta ta dauko
Watansu biyu cif suka koma gida, Hindu ta ciko tayi kyau tayi bulbul abinta, tinda ta dawo suka koma zaman da sukeyi da Osama, be rageta da komai ba, duk abinda takeso ze siyo ya kawo mata haka zalika yana kokarin sauke mata hakkin ta amma da zaran yaji kukan Jawahir ya fara rawar jiki kenan harsai Hindu tabar duk wani abinda takeyi ta kulata
Yau tinda ya dawo yakejin kukan Jawahir kuma kuka takeyi bana wasa ba, cike da wasu wasin ina Hindu take ya shigo dakin amma batanan se Jawahir daya gani kwance se kuka takeyi, daukanta yayi ya fara jijjiga ta amma takiyin shiru, daga bathroom Hindu ta fito daure da towel ta kalleshi tareda cewa "sanda dawowa Abban Jawahir", kallon da ya mata yasa hanjin cikinta kadawa, cike da tsananin bacin rai yace "kinsan Allah akan Jawahir zamu bata dake, dan banga dalilin da zesa kebarmin yarinya tana kuka ba kuma bazaki kulata ba", kallonshi tayi tace "wanka fa nakeyi, zan bar abinda nakeyi ne na fito bayan nasan ba yunwa takeji ba tinda seda na bata nono sannan na shiga wankan", harara ya watsa mata yace "ai kuwa daga yau koh fitsari kikeyi kikaji kukanta dole ki barshi kizo ki kulata dan bazan lazumci jin kukanta koda yaushe ba", baki sake take kallonshi amma ya murtuke fuska tareda cewa "karbeta ki bata nono", bata kulashi tayi hanyar dressing mirror tareda cewa "cigaba da lallashin ta ba yunwa takeji ba, rigima ce kawai"
Ji yayi kaman ya maketa amma ya share tareda fita ya bar mata dakin, ranar a hannun Osama Jawahir ta kwana dan kin yarda Hindu ta dauketa yayi, duk yadda taso karban yarinyar kodan ta bata nono yaki yarda, washegari ma da dabara ta kare ta a hannunshi kafin ya wuce office
Abu fa se abinda yayi gaba dan Hindu cin mutunci take gani kala kala akan Jawahir se kace wata 'yar gwal, tun tana rikewa har dai taga bazata iya ba ta fadawa Yaya Aysha halin da ake ciki, Aysha tasha mamaki dan haka washegari tazo gidan tareda danta wanda Jawahir nada sati uku ta haifeshi me suna Adil, sosai tayiwa Osama fada kuma ta nuna mishi bacin ranta yayinda yayita bata hakuri akan cewar Inshallah ze canza, tare ta hadasu ta musu fada tareda basu shawarwari akan zamantakewar aure
BAYAN SHEKARA BIYAR
Jawahir ta girma se kiriniya da rashin kunya da tasa gaba, baga babba ba baga yaro ba wanda halin nata yasa kwata kwata basa shiri da Najib, Hindu tana iya kokarinta wurin ganin Jawahir ta canza hali amma abu ya gagara dan koyaya ta hukunta Jawahir mahaifinta ze tsaya mata yaciwa Hindu mutunci a gabanta wanda wannan yasa kwata kwata Jawahir bata ganin girman Hindu, tsaki, harara, murgua baki da turo baki gaba ba wanda Jawahir batawa Hindu, kuma ba dama tace zata daketa
Yau da rigima Jawahir ta tashi kasancewar ranar asabar ne yasa Hindu ko kulata batayi ba, Osama ne yayi kokarin mata wanka ya shirya ta sannan ya kawo ta dinning dan taci abinci, indomie ne Hindu ta dafa mata da kwai amma kirikiri Jawahir tace ita bataci abincin be mata dadi ba, Hindu dake zaune parlour tana kallo tace "dan gidanku aise ki tashi kije ki dafa wani marar kunya kawai", turo baki tayi tana kallon mahaifinta idonta cike da kwalla tana jira taji mezai ce
Kallon inda Hindu ke zaune yayi yace "my princess me zaki ci", "Oat" ta fada a takaice, kallon Hindu yayi yace "zoki hada mata Oat din", banza tayi dashi kaman bada ita yake ba yace "ko bakiji bane" kai tsaye tace "bazan iya ba", tasowa yayi daga dinning din Jawahir na bayanshi rike da rigarshi ya karaso gabanta yace "karki bari raina ya aci tashi kije ki hada mata", ba tare da ta kalleshi ba tace "na riga na fada maka bazan yi ba, idan bazataci indomie din ba ta barshi, danni ba baiwar ta bace da zanyi girki tace min ita girkin be mata ba"
Lekowa Jawahir tayi daga bayan Osama tace "Dada ai kasan Mamah bata iya abinci me dadi ba koh?", takaici ne ya kama Hindu ta janyo Jawahir daga bayanshi ta mareta tareda cewa "dan uwarki aise kije ki dafa tinda ni ban iya ba, dan
", bata karasa fadan abinda takeso tace ba Osama ya bata mari itama wanda seda yasa tayi tsayuwar hucin gadi kafin ta farfao ta kalleshi idonta jajir tace "yau ni ka mara akan na daketa", ada kai yayi yace " idan kika kuma tabata sena miki wanda yafi wannan", kallon Jawahir tayi wacce ke goge hawayenta tana mata gwalo tinda an rama mata, takaici yasa ta riko ta ta wanke ta marika biyu masu rai da lafiya sannan ta dago ta kalli Osama dake kallonta baki sake tace "na daketa seka rama mata"
Be kulata ba yace "kije gida se nazo anjima", yana fadar haka ya dauki Jawahir suka fita ya bar Hindu wurin tana juya maganar shi, zama tayi kan kujera tana hawayen bakin cikin Osama da Jawahir, wannan wace irin rayuwar aure ne da za'ace kaje gida dan kawai ka hukunta 'yar cikinka
Girgiza kanta tayi tareda mikewa ta dau mayafinta ta fita, gidan Yaya Aysha ta tafi dan tasan ita kadai zata iya fadawa matsalar ta, koda ta isa gidan ta korowa Yaya Aysha ce mata tayi suje gida a kirashi aji dalilinshi na akaita abinda yayi
A gidan gabadayansu suna zaune a parlour suna jiran zuwan Osama, be bata lokaci ba ya karaso inda ya shigo parlourn da sallama tareda neman wuri ya zauna ya kwantar da Jawahir kan cinyarsa kasancewar tayi bacci
Hussain ne ya dago cike da kunya zeyi magana Osama ya dakatar dashi ta hanyar mika mishi paper dinda ke hannunshi, da mamaki kuwa ke kallon Osama cikin nutsuwa yace "ku gafarceni nasan ban kyauta muku ba kasancewar na sallamo Hindu sedai bazan iya zama da macen da bazata iya kularmin da 'yata ba", shiru sukayi kafin A2 yace "Osama ka taba ganin inda uwa ta haifa kuma ta kasa kula da abinda ta haifa, me laifin Hindu dan ta hukunta Jawahir akan laifin da tayi", kanshi kasa yace "ni ban hanata hukunta Jawahir ba amma dukane banaso shiyasa na kawo takardar ta dan bazan lazumci duka ba"
Gabadayansu kallon shi sukayi Naja'atu cike da takaici ta kalleta tace "yanzu kanaso ka cemin ka saki Hindu dan kawai ta mari Jawahir", be dago ya kallesu ba, Hussain yayi karfin halin bude takardar da Osama ya mika mishi ai kuwa saki daya ya rubuta mata wanda beda wani kwakwaran dalili sena ana dukan Jawahir, cike da bacin rai Hussain yayo kanshi A2 yayi saurin dakatar dashi tareda cewa "haba Hussain, karkayi haka mana, ka kyaleshi, kila bayan wannan yanada wata hujjar ne amma na tabbata Osama bazai saki Hindu dan kawai ta daki Jawahir ba", kasa magana Hussain yayi saboda kunyar abinda Osama ya aikata, Hindu kuwa tana rakue gefe se sharar hawaye takiyi, duk da ba wani jin dadin zama da Osama takeyi ba amma bazata so ace aurenta ya mutu ba
Kallon Osama Hussain yayi cikin bacin rai yace "ka sani nan gaba se kayi dana sani wannan abin daka aikata, sannan kuma ina so ka sani Jawahir 'yar Hindu ce dan haka baka isa ka rabasu ba, ko kanaso ko bakaso dole kabarwa Hindu Jawahir ko saboda tarbiyyar ta sannan ban yarda ka dawo da sunan cewar kazo maida Hindu ba, tinda bakasan darajar ta ba banga dalilin da zaisa ta koma maka ba"
Osama be musa ba, yana gani A2 da Hussain suka fice yayinda shikuma ya tashi yaje gaban mahaifiyarshi ya dora mata Jawahir kan cinya sannan ya fice, wato dai baze bawa Hindu Jawahir ba, duk shiru sukayi Naja'atu kuwa kunya duk ta kamata, tashi tayi zata mikawa Hindu Jawahir Shaukiyya tace "barta a hannun ki, tinda ke ya zaba ki rike masa 'yarsa toh ki riketa, ai damu dake duk daya ne balle kuma ana cikin gida daya, karki damu kanki jeki shimfide ta", jiki a sanyaye Naja'atu ta fita
Kallon Hindu Shaukiyya tayi sannan tace "karki tada hankalin ki Hindu, inaso ki sani komai ya faru da bawa a duniyar nan toh mukaddari ne, ki sani addara bata wuce ranar ta, kiyi addu'a Allah yasa abin nan daya faru shine mafi alkhairi", fashewa tayi kuka tana kara shigewa jikin Yaya Aysha wacce ta kasa koda motsin kirki saboda tsananin tausayin kanwarta, amma tabbas Osama be rike amana ba
Zaman gidan ya dawowa Hindu sabo duk da tafi jin dadin zaman gidan akan gidan Osama, tana yawan ganin Jawahir amma kota kirata bata zuwa sedai ta murguda mata baki ta gudu, kuma takan ga Osama sedai koh gaisuwa bata hadasu
Tana gama iddarta tayi jamb Allah yasa ta samu result me kyau, ba jimawa aka bata admission inda take karantar theater art
A shekaran da ta samu admission a shekarar Shaukiyya, A2, da Hussaini sukayi hatsarin jirgi a hanyarsu ta dawowa daga umrah wanda gabadayansu suka amsa kiran Ubangiji, sosai wannnan rasuwa ya jijjiga su dan a halin yanzu basu da wani katanga se Naja'atu wacce bata samu zuwa ba dan Hajiya Hindu ma ta dade rasuwa bayan doguwar jinya da tayi
Haka suka lallaba sukaci gaba da rayuwarsu da dadi ba dadi har dai Allah yasa Jawahir ta shekara takwas, a lokacin da Jawahir ta shekara takwas lokacin Osama yasa zafi shi se karbeta daga hannun Naja'atu, bata musa ba ta bashi ita duk da tasan ba iya kula da ita zeyi ba
Wannan al'amarin sosai ya tadawa Hindu hankali dan kuwa Jawahir kawai take gani takejin dadi duk da kuwa Jawahir din bawai ta damu da ita bane, har gida tabi Osama kan ya bata Jawahir amma fir yaki, bata gaji ba tace toh su dinga raba kwana, idan tayi sati a wurinshi se tayi sati a wurinta amma nan ma yaki yarda, ba irin rokon da batayi ba amma yakiji saboda a ganinshi bazata kula da Jawahir sosai ba
Da kukanta ta wuce gidan Yaya Aysha ta koro mata yanda sukayi inda Yaya Aysha tace why not su kai kara court, haka kuwa akayi suka shigar da kara inda aka aika mishi da sammaci, be damu ba dan aganinshi shine me gaskiya
A ranar suka zauna court alkali ya nemi sannin dalilin da yasa Osama ke nema ya raba Jawahir da mahaifiyarta, ba tareda shakkar komai ba yace "saboda bazata iya kula da ita ba, bata kula da ita yadda ya dace sannan bata shakkar muzgunawa Jawahir ta hanyar dukanta, nasan yara suna laifi amma duka ba shine hanyar da uwa zatabi da sunan gyara ba", ada kai alkali yayi alamar ya fahimci Osama sannan ya kalli Hindu yace "toh ke kinji abinda yace, shin haka ne", kanta a kasa tace "ya mai girma mai shari'a Jawahir 'yata ce, babu uwar da zata haifi yarinya kuma ta kasa kula da ita, tsananin soyayyar da yakewa Jawahir yasa kome aka mata yake gani kaman ba'ayi daidai ba, hukunci kuma inagani uwa ita takeda damar yiwa yaro duk hukuncin da taga ya dace dashi idan yayi laifi", ada kai alkali ya sakeyi yace "haka ne, kina da gaskiya, ko wannenku na gane inda kuka dosa sedai inaso ku sani cewar wannan abin da kukeyi baze amfani ita yarinyar taku ba, dan haka nakeso ku dinga raba kwana, idan satin nan tana wurin mahaifinta wani satin ya zamana tana wurin mahaifiyarta kaman yadda ita uwar ta bukata, amma sedai ke Hindu inaso ki kiyaye, tinda mahaifinta ya nuna beson duka toh karki daketa, dan muddin kika daketa ze iya shigar da kara akan hakan wanda wannan ze iya saki a matsala"
Da haka alkali ya kawo karshen rikicin su, sedai Jawahir tafison zama da mahaifinta dan kome takeso tana samu har bataso satin da zata koma wurin Hindu ya matso saboda ba laifi Hindu na tsawatar mata daidai gwargwado, sedai bata dukanta gudun kar tayi laifi duk da kuwa Jawahir na yin abin dukan
Cikin gidajen gadonta ta gyara daya ta koma inda ta samu wata mata wanda a girme ta girme ta nisa ba kusa shiyasa take bata respect sosai tana tayata da aikin da baza'a rasa ba yayinda taci gaba da karatun ta har ta samu ta gama lafiya, bata nemi aiki karkashin kowa ba sema bude nata fashion business din da tayi tana designing kaya da kanta inda ta samu wasu suna mata modelling
Haka rayuwa taci gaba da tafiyar musu har Allah ya kawosu wannan rana da Hindu ta shaidawa Osama cewar ta yafe mishi Jawahir
Wannan shine asalin labarin abinda ya faru tsakanin Osama da Hindu da kuma dalilin da yasa Hindu bata yiwa Jawahir wani kwakwaran hukunci
Yanzu zamu cigaba daga inda muka tsaya a next page
