UWA TA GARI - 8 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Satin Jawahir daya hospital aka sallame ta, su Zahra da Rumana duk sunzo sun gaisheta kafin a sallame ta, koda ta koma gida seda ta sake sati daya sannan ta koma school inda take karantar Mass Communication
Da wuri yau ta tashi saboda tanada lecture 9am, wanka tayi ta shirya cikin black straight pencil skirt da grey shirt sannan ta dauko black veil ta daura a kanta, half cover shoe tasa ta dau bag tasa writing materials dinta ciki ta dau phone dinta ta fito
Koda ta fito Dada ya riga ya wuce office dan haka cornflakes kawai ta haa da sha sannan ta fita, a daidaita ta tsayar ya kaita har gate din school
A gaban department dinsu ta hadu da Zahra da Rumana, da dan saurinta ta karasa wurinsu tareda hadasu su biyu ta rungume tana cewa "I missed you guys alot", dariya sukayi a tare sukace "we missed you too", Zahra ta kara da cewa "yanzu ne school ze mana dadi tinda our babe is back", murmushi tayi dan a rayuwa tanaso taga ana fifita ta a komai ace itace a gaba
Rumana ce ta mika mata notebook hardcover tace "ga note dinki, nayi completing nashi, so u won't have a problem", sannan ta mika mata wani booklet tace "wannan kuma English assignment ne, i did it for you, yau zamuyi submit", rungume Rumana tayi tace "tnx babe, u are the best", a haka suka karasa lecture hall suna hira tsakaninsu
A gaba suka zauna dan Jawahir bata zaman ko ina se gaba, shiyasa idan tasan tanada lectures toh da wuri zatazo, koda lecturer ya shigo yana musu lectures nutsuwa tayi tana sauraronshi kaman ba ita ba
A haka har suka gama ta fito sannan suka koma next lecture, se 3pm suka gama lectures gabadaya ita dasu Zahra suka wuce hostel din Zahra saboda ta volunteer zata musu girki
A hostel ne ta nemi wuri ta zauna tana danne dannen waya har Rumana tayi sallah tana nan zaune, da Rumana ta idar ta kalleta tace "Jawahir bazakiyi sallah bane?", a takaice tace "I'm off", girgiza kai Rumana tayi tace "Jawahir ki dai ji tsoron Allah", Jawahir bata kulata ba, se Zahra dake gyara kayan miya tace "ke ma dai Rumana da neman magana, tace miki tana off ba shikenan ba", harara Rumana ta watsa wa Zahra tace "dadi na dake daurewa karya gindi, amma ni dake da ita duk musan karya take sanda tace she's off"
Duk tsayawa suka suna kallonta Zahra ta nuna kanta da wukan dake hannunta tace "ni kike gayawa haka", Rumana ta kalleta tace "ai kema kinsan gaskiya na fada, kuma kina kare mata ne saboda ke kanki bayi zakiyi ba, idan bazaki mata wa'azi ba kidena condemning dina idan ina kokarin dorata kan hanya", Zahra zatayi magana Jawahir tayi saurin dakatar da ita ta hanyar cewa "girls, girls, calm down, me haka kukeyi ne, haba, se kace wasu yara kanana", duk shiru sukayi suna hararan juna Jawahir taja tsaki tareda cewa "Rumana inaso ki sani I know what I'm doing, I'm no longer a kid, banajin magana, nasani, amma wannan bashi ze baki daman samin ido ba, sallahn nan da kike damuna aka i know it's worth na san muhimmancin sallah, so you don't have to tell what to do, idan kikaga banyi sallah ba ki kyaleni, kabarinmu ba daya ba, dey ur dey make I dey my dey, kowa yayi abinda ya kawoshi kawai karki kara samin ido, sallahn nan idan nayi ma kaina idan banyi bama ma kaina dan haka kowa ya kama gabanshi"
Tana gama fadan haka ya dauki kayanta ta fice, Zahra ta juya ta kalli Rumana tace "yanzu ai hankalinki ya kwanta?", zama Rumana tayi tace "is it a crime to just try to change my friend, kawai dan inason ta da alkhairi shikenan seta dau fushi dani? naga ai kawaye suna fadawa junansu gaskiya", haka sukaci gaba da zanjen yayin da Zahra ta ajiye aikin girkin gefe dan dukkansu babu me nutsuwar zama yaci koda an gama
Jawahir kuwa tana fita ta dau wayanta ta kira Jarood, bugu daya aka daga tace "hello Jarood where are you", Jarood yace "ina within the school premises around social center ya akayi", a shagwabe tace "I need you", miskilin murmushi yayi yace "kina ina", inda take ta fada mishi yace "will be there soon", kashe wayan tayi ta nemi wuri ta zauna tana tunanin sabanin da suka samu da Rumana, ta sani Rumana kawai so take ta gyara halinta amma kuma she knows Rumana batabi right way daya dace ba, saboda Rumana nason nuna tafisu son ibada alhali shi tsoron Allah a zuci yake ba'a fili ba, base ka fito ka nuna kai me tsoron Allah bane za'a san kana tsoronshi
Good and fine tasan hanyar da ta daukowa kanta bame bullewa bane amma she choose this way, this is how she wants to leave her life, toh meyasa baza'a kyaleta ba?
"Penny for your thoughts", muryan Jarood ya dawo da ita daga duniyar tunanin data lula, ajiyar zuciya ta sauke ya riko hannunta tareda kallonta yace "you don't seem happy, hope all is well?", girgiza kai tayi tana wasa da yatsunshi tace "I'm bad", da mamaki ya kalleta yace "why did you say so?", idanunta cike da hawaye tace "i scolded Rumana dan kawai tamin maganan sallah", murmushi yayi dan yasan halin Jawahir dama base an fada mishi ba, she's more like a sister to him
Gyara zaman shi yayi yace "toh kema meyasa bakiyi ba?", a hankali tace "ina jira ne ayi la'asar se in hada inyi", murmushi yayi yace "meyasa bazakiyi ba se kin hada da la'asar?", "ai naga it's almost time ne shiyasa, kuma yunwa nake ji i thought of eating before praying", ba tareda ya dauki maganar da zafi ba yace "next time if you don't want to fight with your friends kiyi abinda sukeso that's the best solution", ada mishi kai tayi sannan yace "yanzu me zakici?", "anything", ta fada a takaice, "muje muci abinci toh sena kaiki gida", mikewa tayi tabi bayanshi yana gaba
WAYE JAROOD
Jarood dan wani hamshaqin attajiri ne wanda su biyu ne a wurin iyayensu su, daga shi se kanwarshi wacce bazata wuce shekara sha biyar ba, Jarood El Muaz Jega shine asalin sunanshi, mahaifinshi haifaffen dan garin Kebbi ne under Jega local government, mahaifiyarshi Hajiya Turai kuma 'yar asalin garin Niger ce, buzuwa ce wanda a wurinta Jarood da kanwarshi Sofiyyah suka gado kyau da gashi, Jarood tun suna yara yake tareda Jawahir dan tare sukayi school sedai yayi senior dinta da two classes dan ko a age ma ya bata shekara biyu, shima kaman Jawahir din ba wani tarbiyya isassa ya samu ba saboda mahaifansu basu da lokacin su, harkan business dinsu suka sa gaba, El Muaz Jega idan ya tashi tafiye tafiyen shi yakeyi na siyasa ita kuwa Hajiya Turai business dinta na siyar da kayan lace tasa a gaba, amma duk da haka ya danfi Jawahir natsuwa duk da wasu rashin jin nata ma dasa hannunshi a ciki, shima a nan uni din yake karantar physiology, yana year three dinshi, babu maganar wanda Jawahir keji kaman na Jarood se kuma Najib da take tsananin tsoron shi
Wannan kenan 
Restaurant ya kaita dan taci abinci, se janta da hira yakeyi amma gaba-daya hankalinta na wani wurin daban, kallon inda take kallo yayi inda yaga Najib tareda wasu en 400level tsaye jikin mota suna hira se murmushi yakeyi
Take mood din Jarood ya canza yana kokarin janta su bar wurin amma Jawahir ko motsawa, a hankali Najib ya dago suka ido da Jawahir ta sakar mishi murmushi shikuma ya bata rai yana kallon hannunta wanda ke cikin na Jarood, ganin yayi focus kan hannunta yasa a hankali ta zare nata sannan ta fara tafiya zata tunkaroshi yama abokanshi sallama ya juya ya shige mota
Ji tayi kaman ya zuba mata ruwan zafi a jiki saboda yanda yayi kaman besan Allah yayi ruwanta a wurin ba, shikuwa Jarood murmushi yayi yace "let's go babe", a hankali taci gaba da binshi har suka kai restaurant din suka zauna, an ajiye mata abinci a gaban ta amma kwata kwata ta kasa ci dan tunanin Najib ne yamata kaka gida a zuciyarta, ta rasa meyasa Najib baya sake mata fuska
Da kyar Jarood ya samu taci abinci kadan sannan suka wuce, inda yayi parking din mota suka karasa ya bude mata ta shiga sannan ya zagaya ya shiga, seda suka hau titi sannan yace "U should forget about him since he doesn't care about you", shiru tayi dan tasan koda wa yake, ganin she's not in the mood to talk to him yasa ya kama bakinshi yayi shiru
A gaban gidan yayi parking duk suka zauna bame magana a cikinsu, se bayan kaman five minutes yace "we are home, ki shiga ciki", girgiza kai tayi tace "ko na shiga ma ni kadaice Dada be dawo ba", shiru yayi kafin daga baya yace "there's a party this evening, na wani abokina zakije?", Da murmushi tace "why not", yace "ok, get ready, zanzo na daukeki anjima", girgiza mishi kai tayi yayi pecking dinta a kumatu kafin ta fice, inda sabo ta saba dan haka murmushi kawai tayi ta fita tana waving hannunta har ya wuce sannan ta shige gida

Wanka Jawahir tayi tayi alwallah ta fito ta haa azahar da la'asar sannan ta tashi ta nufi gaban dressing mirror ta fara kwaliyya, simple make up tama kanta wanda ya karbi fuskanta tayi kyau sosai musamman ma da tasa nude lipstick, tashi tayi ta nufi wardrobe dinta wanda Dada ya cika mata da kaya ta dauko wani maroon material gown tasa, A shape gown ne wanda bayanshi ya sauka kasa sosai amma gaban a dage yake ba kaman bayan ba
Milk veil ta dauko ta daura a kanta bayan tasa rigan sannan tama kanta wanka da turare tana wakan 'she looks so perfect by 5 seconds of summer' saboda duniya tai mata dadi, black gucci bag ta dauko wanda yazo da takalminshi shima black tasa sannan ta dauko wayanta ta fara snapchat kafin Jarood yazo
Sosai ta bata lokaci tana abu daya dan batada aikin yi, karfe shida da en mintuna Jarood ya kira wayanta cewar yana kofan gida, kara kallon kanta tayi a mirror ta kara fesa turare sannan ta fice abinta, masu aikin gidan duk binta da ido sukayi dan magana bata hadasu
A cikin mota ta sameshi ya bude mata ta shigo sannan ya kalleta da murmushi yace "wow, u look great", "thank you" tace dashi tana sake jin kanta, tada motan yayi yana cewa "dole nasa miki ido saboda kuraye ne a wajen party dinnan, I need to bring you back home safe and sound kafin Dada yasa a kulleni", dariya ya bata, dan haka tayi dariyarta sannan tace "kai ma ai kasan bazanyi abinda zesa ka shiga matsala ba har Dada ya kulle ka", kada kai yayi sukaci gaba da hira cikin raha har suka kai inda zasu
Tin daga waje akejin kidi bana wasa ba, a waje yayi parking dan kuwa babu daman shiga da mota compound din wurin, tare suka fito ya kulle motan sannan ya zagaya ya riko hannunta to keep her safe dan tin daga fitowansu aka fara kallonta, shi ya mata jagora har cikin gidan sannan ya samu wuri yace ta zauna bari yaje ya nemo uban gayyan wanda ya haa party na ba gaira ba dalili
ada mishi kai tayi alamar taji tana kada kai tareda bin wakan da ke fita daga manyan home theater dinda ke parlourn alamar wakan na shiganta, juyawanshi keda wuya wani matashin saurayi wanda baze wuce sa'an su ba yazo ya zauna kusa da ita yana cewa "hi beautiful", dagowa tayi ta kalleshi, kyakkyawa ne amma duk kyawunshi bekai Jarood ba, "hello", tace mishi tareda cigaba da rawa da kai, murmushi yayi yace "do you care for a dance", kaman jira take tace "sure"

Tana hangoshi ta fara murmushi yayinda ya karaso yana riko hannunta tareda janyota jikinshi, bata damu ba tinda tasan Jarood ne ba wani ba, tuni ta manta da wanda suke rawa tare, shima ganin haka yasan duk maitanshi Jawahir batada lokacin shi saboda haka ya juya ya wucewar sa, ita kuwa rawa take da Jarood hankalinta kwance ba tareda wani fargaba ba
Basu suka bar gidan ba se karfe tara ba sallah bare salati, a gaban gidansu Jawahir yayi parking sannan ya mata peck a kumatu tareda cewa "semun hadu gobe", a gajiye take dan haka kai kawai ta iya kada mishi ta fita daga motar shikuma ya ja ya wuce yana ayyana abubuwa daban daban a ranshi
Tana shiga gida wanka ta sake yi ta nemi wuri ta kwanta ba maganan sallah, kasa bacci tayi gashi har lokacin Dada be dawo ba, Mamah ce ta fado mata a rai, da wurin Mamah take da yanzu an fara mata fadan ina ta fito, tayi sallah, me yasa batajin magana, ya kamata ta gyara halinta, a gama mata fadan kuma ace ga abinci taje ta dauka taci, murmushi tayi wanda ita kanta batasan tayishi ba, tashi tayi ta shiga bathroom dinta tayi alwallah tazo tayi magrib da isha badan komai ba sedan ta rasa abinyi gashi bacci yaki zuwa gashi ba kowa cikin gidan daga ita se me gadi dan me aikinsu seven take wucewa ta dawo seven na safe
Tana idarwa ta wuce kitchen taga tuwon shinkafa cikin cooler da miyan taushe, rufewa tayi ta dauko cup ta hada tea ta dauki cake ta wuce daki, laptop dinta ta dauko ta kunna ta fara kallon 'grownish' har ta gama cin abincinta ta ajiye kayan gefe
Se past 12 Dada ya dawo gida, tanaji aka bude mishi gate dan har lokacin batayi bacci ba, seda taji shigowar shi sannan ta sauke ajiyar zuciya ta kashe laptop din ta kwanta tareda jan bargo da kashe bedside lamp
Dada na parking ya fito a gajiye hannunshi rike da laptop bag yana kokarin shigewa cikin gida me gadinshi yayi saurin karasowa tareda cewa "barka da zuwa Alhaji", dagowa Dada yayi ya kalleshi yana amsa mishi da "yauwa Malam Gado ya aikin?", ya amsa da "alhamdullilah", "Masha Allah", Dada yace yana kokarin shigewa Malam Gado yayi saurin dakatar dashi ta hanyar cewa "idan bazaka damu ba Alhaji dan Allah inaso muyi wata magana duk da dare yayi amma maganar na cina shiyasa nakeso muyita yanzu"
Da mamaki Dada ya dawo ya tsaya yana cewa "da fatan dai ba wata matsala koh?", "ba wata matsala illa na yarinyar wurinka", kallon Malam Gado yayi yace "kana nufin Jawahir?", "kai tsaye yace "eh ita", Dada ya jinjina kai yace "lafiya dai koh?", Malam Gado ya gyara tsayuwa sannan ya kalli Dada yace "karkaga kaman na maka shisshigi dayawa, tsawon zamana a gidan yasa na daukeka kaman dan cikina, Jawahir kuma jika na dauketa, inaso ka sani Jawahir macece, ya kamata ace tana samun kulawa sosai, ni a ganina tinda kai bame wayan zama bane me zai hana ta koma wurin mahaifiyarta saboda a samu asa mata ido ta samu kulawa ta ko wani bangare", jinjina kai Dada yayi sannan yace "kome yasa kace haka?", ba tareda Malam Gado yaji shakkar komai ba yace "kaga yarinyar nan na lura kanta na rawa, ya kamata a samu mai kula da ita gudun dana sani nan gaba, dazu data dawo daga makaranta kara fita tayi ita da wani yaro dake yawan zuwa wurinta kuma basu suka dawo ba se wuraren tara da rabi, sannan koda ta gitta kusa dani bawai sharri ko sa ido ba kayanta warin sigari yakeyi wanda wannan ya nuna koda ace ba ita tasha ba inda sukaje ansha sigari a wurin, ina fada maka ne saboda kasan abinyi a matsayin ka na mahaifinta saboda karkayi gangancin da nan gaba duniya zata zageka"
Sosai jikin Dada yayi sanyi, tabbas shi kanshi yasan beda lokacin kula da Jawahir balle yasa mata ido, cikin sanyin murya yace "nagode sosai Malam Gado daka lular dani akan lamarin yarinyar nan, Inshallah zan san abinyi", "ba komai, ai idan ka gyara an wani kaima se Allah ya gyara naka", cewar Malam Gado yana kokarin barin wurin", kasa kasa Dada yace "haka ne", sannan yama Malam Gado sallama ya shige gida tareda kulle ko ina
Dakin Jawahir ya fara shiga inda ya ganta kwance, tanajin shigowar shi tayi lamo cikin bargo dan bataso yasan idonta biyu, zama yayi bakin gado yana kallonta tareda tunanin hukuncin da ya kamata ya yanke, da farko yayi tunanin maida ita wurin kakarta wato Naja'atu dan baze iya kaita wurin Mamah ba se kuma yayi tunanin Naja'atu ta manyanta yanzu ba lallai ta iya kula da Jawahir ba, shawara daya yazo mishi wanda kuma shi kanshi yayi na'am da wannan shawarar kuma yake gani kaman shine hanya mafi sauki da hankalinshi ze kwanta wato aure
Wata kila idan yayi aure matar ta kular masa da 'arsa tareda bata tarbiyyan da take lacking, da wannan tunanin ya sumbaci kanta duk da ta lullube da bargo sannan ya mike ya fita, a wannan rana Dada cike da tunani kala kala yayi bacci wanda daga karshe ya yanke hukuncin sake aure kawai
WASHEGARI
Yau Mamah da wuri ta tashi saboda tanaso taje ta karbo kayan materials dinda tayi order dinsu daga China a airport, kwana biyu data cire Jawahir da Osama a ranta seta fara kumari tana dawo da jikinta dan yanzu batada matsalan komai a ranta, ta dade da watsar da Jawahir da Osama duk da Jawahir takan fado mata a rai amma rashin ta a kusa da ita shine mafi a'ala dan shine kwanciyar hankalin ta da kwanciyar hankalin Osama harda ita Jawahir din
Shiryawa tayi cikin Black abaya da nude veil fuska ba wani make up daga powder se lipgloss se kwalli amma idan mutum ya ganta kaman wata 'ar shekara ashirin da biyar nan kuwa talatin da biyar take, a gurguje tayi duk wani abu da zatayi ta fito bayan tawa Baba Salamatu sallama
Tuki takeyi hankali kwance ba wani rush rush harta kai airport din, direct inda zata karba kayan ta nufa, duk wani process da zatabi ta karbi kayanta ta yishi ta karbi kayan ba tareda an samu matsala ba, ta kwashi kayanta takai mota
Tana rufe boot ta juyo dan tafiya taci karo da wata matashiyar budurwa wacce zatayi sa'a da Jawahir, murmushi yarinyar ta mata tareda cewa "Good morning", itama murmushin ta mayar mata tana cewa "morning, how are you", "I'm fine", yarinyar ta bata amsa sannan ta kama baki tayi shiru, duk shiru sukayi bame cewa wani abu se daga baya Mamah tace "wani wuri zaki", ada kai yarinyar tayi tace "Abba na nake jira yazo ya daukeni", "oh", Mamah tace ba tareda tasan me zata ce ba, chan kuma setace "would you mind if I drop you home", girgiza kai yarinyar tayi tana murmushi tareda cewa "I won't, amma Abba will be disappointed idan yazo be ganni ba, yace na jira shi", ada kai Mamah tayi alamar gamsuwa tace "ok then, ni zan wuce", "ok, se anjima", yarinyar tace tana matsawa gefe
Mota Mamah ta shiga ta wuce abinta, har ta kai inda zata amma ta kasa manta yarinyar nan dan ta shiga ranta dayawa, se yanzu take dana sanin rashin tambayar sunanta da batayi ba, gashi batasan ina zata sake haduwa da yarinyar ba, murmushi tayi dan yarinyar akwai saukin kai ba kaman Jawahir dinta ba Madam trouble
Department dinta da ake mata dinki a karamin building dinta ta nufa duk suka gaisheta ta amsa musu da fara'ar ta wanda su kansu kwanan nan sunga changes tattare da ita, tailors ne a wurin maza da mata ko wannensu zaune gaban industrial machine sun kai su takwas, kananan ma'aikatan ta ne suka shigo mata da kayan da ta karbo inda ta fara bin ko wannensu tana bashi wanda ze dinka da design din tareda sizes din da takeso, tana gamawa da wurin ta wuce department dinda suke siyar mata da kaya wanda shine upper floor, wurin ya kayatu sosai harda changing room duk akwai, seda ta duba taga yanda komai ke gudana a wurin ta tabbatar komai na tafiya daidai sannan ta karasa office dinta tareda kiran accountant dinta dan su buga lissafi
Koda suka gama lissafi da accountant dinta ta tabbatar komai yayi balance seta sallameta sannan ta dauko laptop dinta dan ta fara aiki amma se aiki ya gagareta saboda yarinyar da ta fado mata a rai
Ita kadai ke yaki da zuciyarta akan taje ta sake dubawa ko zataga yarinyar inda ta wani bangare kuma tana ganin kila ma Abban nata ya je ya dauke ta
Ganin idan ba taje ba bazata samu sauki a ranta ba yasa ta dau car keys dinta ta fice, mota ta shiga tana addu'a a ranta Allah yasa ta ganta, tana parking a harabar airport din ta hangota zaune ga jakanta gefenta ta bata fuska se kalle kalle takeyi da alama ta kosa da jira
Fitowa Mamah tayi ta karasa wurinta ta zauna ita tareda cewa "har yanzu bezo bane?", dagowa tayi ta kalli Mamah ganin itace se tayi murmushi tace "ya kirani wai na jirashi an kirashi wani meeting ne amma nan 30minutes ze zo ya daukeni", da mamaki Mamah tace "amma baki gaji ba?", ajiyar zuciya ta sauke tareda cewa "wallahi na gaji, ga bacci, ga yunwa, ga gajiya, bansan meyasa yaki aiko driver ba yace da kanshi zezo", ta karasa maganan kaman zatayi kuka
Tausayi taba Mamah, Mamah tace "why not in kaiki gidana ki huta, seki kirashi kice yazo ya dauke ki a chan, kinga kafin yazo kin huta kema", shiru tayi kaman me tunani se kuma tace "bazan takura miki ba?", girgiza kai Mamah tayi tace "No, ba wani takura, just call him up", cike da jin dadi ta dauko wayanta ta shiga kiran Abban nata, bugu biyu ya dauka yana cewa "baby na dan Allah kiyi hakuri, I will be with soon, ki
", Bata bari ya karasa ba tace "Abba zanje gidan wata Anty dina kazo ka dauke ni a wurin, will text you the address", bata jira jin me zece ba ta kashe wayan sannan ta tashi taja jakanta tana cewa "let's go"
Suna zuwa gida Mamah ta nuna mata dakin Jawahir tace "shiga ciki, akwai duk wani abu da kike bukata, bari na hada mana breakfast, dama nima banyi breakfast din ba", "ok Anty, nagode sosai", girgiza kai Mamah tayi tana cewa "don't mention", sannan ta kara da "by the way what's your name", murmushi tayi tace "sunana Sabreena", "wow, what a nice name", Mamah ta fada tana murmushi "shiga ciki kiyi abinda zakiyi bari na dora abinci", da fadar haka ta wuce ciki ita kuma Mamah ta wuce kitchen inda ta tarar da Baba Salamatu na gyara vegetables wanda zatayi miya dashi
Sabreena bata ata lokaci a dakin ba tayi wanka ta duba cikin kayanta ta dauko wani tasa sannan ta fito, koda ta fito Mamah ta gama hada musu pancake da tea dan shine abu mafi sauki da zata iya haawa a wannan lokacin, "bismilla Sabreena zo ga abincin", murmushi tayi tana zama kan dining din tace "se naji kaman bayan Abba na kinfi kowa iya fadan sunana", dariya Mamah tayi tace "haba dai, nida sunan ma nake jin shi sabo a bakina, dadi ne dai da sunan ko yaya ka fade shi", a haka sukaci abincin cikin raha har suka kammala
Ringing din wayan Sabreena yasata tashi ta dauko nan taga Abban tane ke kira, mikawa Mamah wayan tayi tana cewa "dan Allah type mishi address din nan", karba Mamah tayi tana typing Sabreena kuma ta shiga kwashe kayan da suka bata, koda ta kai kitchen seta shiga wankewa Baba Salamatu na ta barshi amma tace seta wanke, Mamah dake bakin kofa tana kallon su kwalla ya cika mata ido dan idan Jawahir ce inda taci abinci nan zata barshi ba maganan daukewa balle wankewa
Sabreena na gamawa ta fito parlour tana cewa "kin tura mishi?", "na tura mishi", cewar Mamah dake gyara zaman ta, kallon Sabreena tayi tace "amma bakiji tsoron biyoni ba?", dariya Sabreena tayi tace "tsoron me zanji, ai bakiyi kama da mugaye ba", Mamah tayi murmushi tace "ai mugaye basu da kama", "haka ne", cewar Sabreena, sannan ta kara da cewa "ina ganin ki naga kin kwanta min a rai, shiyasa banji shakkar biyoki ba", ada kai Mamah tayi sannan tace "ko zaki dan kwanta kafin yazo", girgiza kai tayi tace "no, bari na zauna na jirashi nasan yana hanya already", da haka suka zauna zaman hira kaman dama chan sun san juna suna jiran zuwan Abban Sabreena

UWA TA GARI - 10 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Suna zaune sukaji horn alaman ya karaso, cik da zumudi Sabreena ta fita tana jira mahaifinta ya gama parking, yana fitowa ta karasa tareda rungume shi cikeda tsananin jin dadi tana cewa "Abba na, i missed you soo much", murmushi yayi kafin ya bata fuska yace "Sabreena nan garin fah ba Libya bane da zaki tashi kibi mutum ba tareda kin san meshi ba, stop trusting people so easily, this is Nigeria"
Shiru tayi yayin da Mamah dake kallonsu tace "a mata afuwa, it's not her fault, gani nayi ta dade zaune a airport tana jiran ka kuma da alaman akwai gajiya tattare da ita shiyasa nace tazo gidana dan ta samu ta huta kafin ka gama meeting din", se'a lokacin ya kula da Mamah, kallon ta ya tsaya yi yana yaba kyawun halitta irin nata a ranshi
Seda Sabreena ta tabo shi tareda cewa "Abba", sannan ya fito daga duniyar tunanin da ya fada yayi murmushi yana cewa "shikenan ba damuwa, an yafe mata", sannan ya juya ga Sabreena yace "but don't try that again, u got me worried", rike kunnuwanta tayi alaman ban hakuri sannan ya juya wurin Mamah yace "nagode sosai da kika nuna kulawarki akan ta, Allah ya saka miki da mafificin alkhairi, mu yanzu zamu wuce", "ba komai ai yiwa kaine", cewar Mamah dake wasa da gefen mayafinta
Kallon Sabreena yayi tayi saurin cewa "let me get my luggage", sannan tayi ciki, shikuma ya maida hankalin shi kan Mamah yace "amma bansan sunan ba", murmushi tayi tace "sunana Hindu", yace "nice name, nikuma sunana Harun", gyada kai kawai Mamah tayi, Sabreena ta fito janye da akwatin ta sukasa a mota sannan ta juya ta kalli Mamah tace "it was nice meeting you, an zaman nan da nayi dake naji dadi sosai, se nake gani kaman da mommy na nake", murmushi Mamah tayi tana kallon expression din Sabreena da alama she's missing her Mom, dafata tayi tace "it was nice meeting you also, kuma u are always welcome here, duk sanda kikeso zaki iya zuwa, I will be glad to have you here"
Gyada kai Sabreena tayi tana hugging din Mamah sannan tayi breaking hug ta ciro wayarta ta mikawa Mamah tace "I will need your contact number", ba musu Mamah tasa mata sukayi sallama suka shiga mota, Abba yaja Sabreena na dagawa Mamah hannu
Seda taga wucewar su sannan ta koma ciki dan ta dauka abinda zata dauka ta koma office
A cikin mota Sabreena ta kalli mahaifinta tace "Abba the lady is nice koh?", yace "uhm, she's nice", Sabreena ta gyara zama tana cewa "I like her", kallon Sabreena yayi sannan ya maida kallonshi ga titi bece komai ba se tunanin da ya fada
WACECE SABREENA?
Sabreena Harun 'a daya tilo ga Alhaji Harun da matarshi Asiya, Alhaji Harun dan Nigeria ne a jihar Borno, asalin fulanin Borno ne wanda ya taso, yayi karatun secondary dinshi a nan Borno din, a lokacin da ya gama ne ya samu scholarship zuwa Libya inda ya karanci dentistry, be dawo ba seda ya hada masters dinshi sannan ya dawo gida Nigeria ya fara aikinshi a babban asibitin gomnati a matsayin likitan hakori
A lokacin da yake karatu a Libya ya hadu da Asiya mahaifiyar Sabreena itama tana karatu a nan school dinda yake, yayi senior dinta da two years a school din, sakamakon tutorial da yake ma ita da kawayenta soyayya ya shiga tsakani, dan haka koda ya dawo gida Nigeria seya fadawa iyayenshi akaje nema mishi aurenta, basu wahala ba aka bashi dukda kuwa tana karatu haka aka yanke mata karatu sukayi aurensu ya kawo ta Nigeria a nan kano din
Basu dade ba Allah ya bata juna biyu wanda cikin na shiga wata na goma ta haifi diyarta wacce Allah be bata daman ganin abinda ta haifa ba ya karbi ranta, sun sha kukan mutuwar Asiya har sun gode Allah, mahaifiyarshi ita ta karbi rikon Sabreena ana bata madara har ta kai yaye, tana shekara uku, akama Harun transfer zuwa Sokoto, iyayen Asiya sun bukaci a basu Sabreena su rike inda mahaifiyarshi ta bashi shawaran ya kaita inyaso duk hutu ta dingayi a nan Nigeria saboda ta taso cikin dangin mahaifiyarta, koda ace batasan wacece mahaifiyarta ba zatasan dangin ta
Haka ya dauki Sabreena ya kaita Libya inda duk hutu seta zo shima idan ya samu lokaci yana zuwa ya duba ta, ta taso da sanin cewar mahaifiyarta ta rasu wurin haihuwarta kuma mahaifinta yaki ya kara aure saboda tsananin son da yake yiwa mahaifiyarta, soyayya take samu ta kowani bangare hakama kulawa
Harun yasha transfer gari kala kala inda daga karshe ya bude nashi private hospital din a garin Kebbi saboda a duk garuruwan da yayi aiki Kebbi yafi kwanta mishi a rai, be dade da dawowa Kebbi ba yace Sabreena ta dawo tayi University dinta a nan tinda yanzu he's ready to settle down
A halin yanzu Sabreena is 17yrs inda ta gama karatun ta na secondary zata fara jami'a, sosai Sabreena ke tausayin kanta da mahaifinta saboda yaki ya kara aure amma yau da suka hadu da Mamah se taga ta samu wacce zata iya kula mata da mahaifinta da ita kanta, kuma abinda ta gani a idon mahaifinta ta tabbatar idan ta fada mishi kudirin ta baze musa ba
Wannan kenan
Sati biyu kenan da haduwar Sabreena da Mamah inda suka dinke sosai koda yaushe cikin waya suke suna duba lafiyar juna wanda wannan yasa kewar Jawahir ya dan ragu a cikin ran Mamah
Jawahir duniya tai mata dadi dan kuwa sheka ayar ta takeyi sun ranta, babu me takura ta, idan Dada ya fita dawowan shi se yadda Allah yayi dan haka take abinda taga dama, bata nan bata chan, tuni sun shirya da Rumana sun koma kaman ba abinda ya taba faruwa tsakaninsu yayinda shakuwar su da Jarood se habbaka yakeyi dan kuwa Jarood bude mata ido yakeyi da yawace yawace na banza dan har ya fara kaita club
Amma kuma duk wannan iskancin da Jawahir keyi Dada na sane dashi kuma yana kan daukan mataki a cewarshi, abinda Jawahir bata sani ba shine Dada na neman auren wata colleague dinshi na wurin aiki wacce ta nace mai tun ba yau ba, amma yanzu ganin ba sarki se Allah ya amince ze aureta da sharadin zata ajiye aikinta bayan aure ta kular mishi da Jawahir kuma ta amince dari bisa dari, inda har ankai gaisuwa ansa rana nan sati biyu saboda beso a dau lokaci
Ya aikawa Mamah da Yaya Aysha katin aurenshi inda Mamah tace ba inda zata yayinda Yaya Aysha kuma keda niyyar zuwa kodan albarkacin iyayenshi, Naja'atu dataji labarin bataji dadi ba dan taso ace ya dawo da aurenshi da Mamah amma yanzu Osama ya zama babban mutum, yasan what is right and wrong dan haka bazata matsa mishi ba, yaje yayi abinda abinda yaga yafi dacewa dashi
Yau a gajiye Jawahir ta shigo gida saboda rawar da tasha a birthday party din wata course mate din Jarood, tayi mamakin ganin Dada zaune a parlourn yana aiki da system dinshi, kallon time tayi taga 11pm, cikin in'ina tace "Dada yau kayi saurin dawowa", kallonta yayi yana murmushi ba tareda ya nuna mata bacin ranshi ba yace "Yes, yau banda aiki dayawa ne, daga ina kike?", ba tareda tasan abin cewa ba ta fara in'ina Dada ya share maganar da cewa "go and freshen up, kizo kici abinci, i have something to discuss with you", gyada kai tayi ta shige ciki tana tunanin me ze fada mata
Wanka tayi tasa kayan bacci ta fito, a dining ta zauna tayi serving din kanta da jollof rice dinda ke cikin cooler, bata wani ci sosai ba saboda fargaban abinda Dada zece mata
Dawowa tayi ta zauna opposite him tana cewa "Dada na gama", IV din aurenshi ya ajiye gabanta ta dauka tareda budewa tana karantawa, waro manyan idanuwanta tayi tace "Dada aure", yace "Yes Jawahir aure zanyi ko bakyaso", girgiza kai tayi ba tareda tace komai ba yace "Jawahir as you can see I'm always busy, I need someone to take care of you for me, shiyasa zanyi aure", kallonshi tayi tareda shagwabe fuska tace "but I'm old enough to take care of my self", ya girgiza kai yace "no, da sauranki", shiru tayi kaman wata me tunani se kuma ta kalleshi tace "i hope ba irin matan nan masu bully din mutane bace?", murmushi yayi yace "no, she's not one of them, kinsan Farida wacce take aiki a company dina a marketing department", tace "yes, wannan Black beauty din nan", ya gyada tareda cewa "ita zan aura, kuma kinga she's still young tunda she's 25, so zaku fahimci juna sosai", murmushi tayi tace "Allah yasa", tana hararanshi ta gefen ido dan ita harga Allah takura ta za'ayi da wannan aure
Da wannan tunanin ta mishi sallama ta wuce daki tana maimaita zancen auren a ranta
Kuyi hakuri da wannan ba yawa, Inshallah next page zan kokarta nayi me tsayi

UWA TA GARI - 11 - Page 3 - Wattpad
Wasa wasa shirye shiryen biki Dada keyi duk da kuwa ya fuskanci Jawahir baso takeyi ba amma he's doing this for her own good dan haka yayi kaman besan me take ciki ba
Koda ta fadawa friends dinta kwantar mata da hankali sukayi akan karta damu kanta tareda bata shawaran idan matar uban nata ta nemi a zauna lafiya se a zauna lafiya idan kuma ta nuna tsiya takeso toh kar Jawahir ta raga mata
Da wannan gurbatacciyar shawaran ta share maganan auren ta maida hankalinta kan karatu saboda exams din da ke gabatosu
Yau ya kama asabar kuma yaune aka daura auren Osama (Dada) da amaryarshi Farida, ya gyara gidanshi sosai ya canza furnitures da komai saboda zuwan amarya
Da dare aka kawo mishi amaryarshi ya zaunar da ita a parlour sannan ya kira Jawahir dake daki tanajin hayaniyar mutane har gidan yayi shiru, fitowa tayi ta zauna itama ya kalleta da murmushi yace "princess welcome your new mummy home", murmushi tayi ba tareda ta nuna damuwa ko wani abu ba ta saki fuska sosai tace "welcome to the family Anty Farida", itama dagowa tayi da nata murmushin tace "yauwa Jawahir, da fatan na sameki lafiya", "lafiya lau nake as always", cewar Jawahir da duk tabi ta matsu ta koma daki dan haka kurum taji amaryar Dada bata mata ba duk da kuwa sunsha haduwa idan taje company din Dada
Shiru sukayi dukkan su Dada yayi gyaran murya sannan yace "Farida yau Allah ya nufa kin zama matar aure a gidan nan, a matsayinki na matar gidan zan bar miki ragamar kula komai na gidana ciki kuwa har 'ata Jawahir, I'm going to put my trust in you, please don't fail me, ki kula min da gida ki kula min da Jawahir, ku zauna lafiya dan zaman lafiyan ku shine kwanciyar hankali na", a hankali Farida tace "Inshallah zaka sameni me kula da duk wani bukatu na gidan nan, sannan kuma Inshallah baza'a samu matsala tsakanin nida Jawahir ba tinda dukkanmu nan kwanciyar hankalinka mukeso'
Sosai yaji dadin abinda tace ya juya kalli Jawahir dake zaune tana kallonsu, ta kalli wannan ta kalli waccan, murmushi tayi ganin Dada ya dawo kanta, ya gyara zama yace "My princess nasan bakida matsala da Farida, nasan zaku zauna lafiya amma duk da haka zan gargade ki banda rashin kunya, inaso ku hada kanku, karkiga kin kusa kamota a tsayi ki rena ta, ku zauna lafiya da juna, she's your mummy now despite your age wise dan haka a kula sosai kunji Allah ya muku albarka", duk suka amsa da" ameen" sannan yace suyi addu'a kowa ya shige ciki
Yau ya kasance weekend da wuri Sabreena ta tashi saboda tayiwa Mamah alkawarin zuwa gaisheta, wanka tayi ta shirya cikin blue jallabiya da white veil sannan tasa takalmi da jaka ta fito, Abba na zaune yana kallon news @10 na safe, kallonta yayi yace "dama da safe zaki, base anjima ba?", ta girgiza kai tace "no, da safe nace mata zanzo, kuma she promised to cook my favorite alkubus da miyan taushe da ashi, sannan zata mun zobo i just can't wait", dariya Abba yayi ganin yadda take zumudi zataje taci alkubus
Seda ya tsagaita dariyar shi sannan yace "amma dai zakiyi breakfast kafin ki wuce koh?", ta gyada kai tana nufin dining tace "zanyi breakfast, ai bana wasa da abinci", murmushi yayi yana maida hankalinshi kan tv din dan shi kanshi yasan Sabreena is a foodie
Seda taci abincinta ta gama sannan tama Abba sallama zata wuce ya dauko leda ya bata yace ta kaiwa Mamah, murmushi tayi ta karba ta fice, driver din da ze kaita already ita yake jira dan haka basu bata lokaci ba suka dau hanya
A harabar gidan Mamah yayi parking ta fito tareda cewa driver din "Isma'il se yamma zaka dawo daukana, around 6pm haka", ya gyada kai yana cewa "ba damuwa, sena dawo", ta daga mishi hannu tareda shigewa ciki
Da sallama ta shiga parlour din, Baba Salamatu dake kallon Arewa 24 ta amsa mata, seda ta karaso ciki sannan tace "Ina kwana Baba Salamatu", da murmushi ta amsa mata da "lafiya lau, kin zo lafiya", tace "lafiya lau", tana dube dube, Baba Salamatu da ta fahimce ta tace "tana kitchen", mikewa Sabreena tayi ta wuce kitchen
A kitchen ta tarar da Mamah tana tuka tuwon shinkafa ta karasa tana cewa "Good morning aunty na", juyowa Mamah tayi tace "oh Sabreena har kin karaso, sorry kin zo ban gama ba aiki ba, wlh Najib ne da rigimar shi ya kirani wai gashi nan zuwa in mishi tuwon shinkafa da miyan taushe, saukin abin ma miya daya kukeso in ba haka ba ai da na gaji dayawa", dariya Sabreena tayi ganin yadda Mamah ke mita tana tuka tuwon wanda da gani kasan kawai tukawa tayi saboda da alaman gajiya tattare da ita
"Kawo in karasa miki kije ki huta", cewar Sabreena dake tattare hannun rigar ta, kallonta Mamah tayi tace "ai kawai ki barshi na gama, dama beson tuwo yayi laushi dayawa, yafison shi da dan karfi", tare suka karasa aikin suka tattare kitchen din suka fito, a parlour Sabreena ta zauna yayinda Mamah ta wuce daki dan tayi wanka ta shirya
Suna zaune tareda Baba Salamatu suna kallo Najib ya shigo da sallama, suka amsa masa a tare, gaishe da Baba Salamatu yayi ta amsa ya kalli inda Sabreena ke zaune hankalinta na kan TV tana kallo bata dago ta kalleshi ba yace "ke kam rashin kunyar ki se addu'a, baki iya gaisuwa bane?", dagowa Sabreena tayi ta kalleshi, mukut ya hadiye wani yawu daya taru mishi lokaci daya, duk a tunaninshi Jawahir ce zaune, se yanzu ya tuna tama bar gidan gaba-daya
Hararar shi Sabreena tayi kafin tace "Dawa kake?", shareta yayi ya nemi wuri ya zauna yana kallon Baba Salamatu tareda mata alama da ido yana nuna Sabreena dan sanin ko wacece, murmushi Baba Salamatu tayi tace "Allah ne ya aiko ma Mamanka iya daga sama, bari tazo se kaji daga bakinta", shiru yayi yana kallon Sabreena, hada ido sukayi ta aika mishi da harara shikuma ya dauke idonshi a zuciyarshi yana cewa "ita kuma wannan me kama aljanun harara kawai ta iya"
Mamah ce ta fito cikin shirinta na atampha dikin riga da skirt ta kalli Najib tace "har ka karaso kenan?", yace "uhm, na karaso Anty na", ta zauna tana cewa "yasu Yaya Aysha, ina ka baro Adil?", ya tae baki yana cewa "yana gida, yace ze biyo ni na hanashi saboda kar ya samin rani idan zanci tuwo dan yau rowa nakeji", dariya Mamah da Baba Salamatu sukayi dan sun san ba karamin aikin shi bane musamman indai akan tuwo ne, Sabreena ta juyo ta kalleshi tace "yanzu kai bakaji kunyar cewa rowa kakeji ba, da girman ka", sokoko ya tsaya kallonta Mamah dake dariya tace "Sabreena kedai kyale wannan baya girma a rayuwarsa, shi haka yake", maida kallonshi kan Mamah yayi yace "wai Anty na a ina kika samo wannan abar", murmushi tayi tace "wlh ata ce Allah ya bani, a airport muka hadu", girgiza kai yayi yana mikewa yayi hanyar dining yana cewa "nidai yunwa nakeji azo aji dani"
Mikewa Mamah tayi ta nufi hanyar daki tana cewa "Sabreena tai maka kiyi serve dinshi zan shiga toilet kumin uziri", gabadayansu kallonta sukayi Baba Salamatu tayi murmushin su na manya itama ta mike tana cewa "nima bacci nakeji bari naje nadan matse ido", duk da ido suka bita sannan suka kalli juna yayi saurin dauke idonshi dan bayaso yana hada ido da ita dan idanunta tsoro suke bashi, sun cika girma dayawa a cewarshi
Zama yayi kan dining yana jiran ta taso amma yaga batada alaman tasowa yace "Sa
Sa
Safeena bakiji me Anty na tace ba", kallonshi tayi tace "Sabreena not Safeena, kuma I don't want to serve an arrogant person like you, idan ka shirya cin abincin then you ask me to serve you politely", dariya yayi sosai wanda da gani ansan be kai ciki ba ya nuna kanshi yace "ni, ni ne arrogant", tace "yes", ya girgiza kai tareda tashi yayi hanyar dakin Mamah yana cewa "shikenan, bari naje nacewa Mamah na daya kin kira danta arrogant sannan na biyu kuma kinki bashi abinci yaci", ganin da gaske yake shiga dakin zeyi tayi saurin mikewa tana cewa "toh bakaji nace zan zuba maka ba", murmushi yayi sannan ya hadiye murmushin shi ya juyo ya koma kan dining ya zauna tareda crossing kafafuwan shi yana jira ta zuba mai
Turo baki tayi gaba sannan tabi bayanshi, tana zuba mishi tuwon yawunta na tsinkewa gashi tuwon dai dai shi akayi, haka ta zuba mishi tasa mishi miya sannan ta nemi wuri ta zauna kan dinning din tana jira ya mata bismilla dan ta raya a ranta da zaran yace mata bismilla zata wanke hannu itama aci tuwon da ita
Shi kuwa Najib fuska yayi ya fara cin tuwonshi harda santi yana cewa Antynshi ta iya tuwo shiyasa bayaso yaci tuwon kowa se nata, ita kuwa kallon shi takeyi bil hakki duk da yaga alaman ita tuwo take jira amma seya basar kaman besan da zaman ta ba, a haka har ya kusa cinyewa sannan ya dago ya kalleta yaga ta zuba mishi na mujiya, tuni tari ya sarkeshi gashi ba ruwa a kusa dolenta ta tashi ta dauko mishi ruwa yasha
Seda tarin ya lafa sannan ya kalleta yana cewa "ke haka ake bawa mutum abinci ba ruwa a kusa, kuma haka za'a miki aure kije kina kallon loman mijinki har kisa ya kware", tae baki tayi tace "dadin abindai loman mijina na kalla bana wani kato ba", be kulata ya wanke hannu badan ya koshi ba sedan itama ta samu taci, mikewa yayi yana goge hannunshi da tissue yace "idan Anty na ta fito kice mata naje na dawo", bata kulashi harya fice
Seda ta tabbatar ya tafi sannan ta janyo sauran tuwon tana mita wai "ko bismilla ya kasa yiwa mutum tsabar rowa irin nashi, gashi nan hadama yasa ya kasa cinyewa dole dai seda ya barshi", Mamah dake jinta tayi dariya a hankali salon kar taji ta fasa cin tuwon, zama tayi parlour tana cewa "hala Najib din ya fita ne?", da sauri Sabreena ta juyo tana cewa "eh yace zeje ya dawo", daukan remote Mamah tayi tana cewa "alkubus dinki fah na cikin warmer ki dauko ki zuba", seda ta kalli Mamah sannan tace "zanci, amma sena gama cin tuwon nan", kaa kai Mamah tayi tana murmushi dan a iya zamanta da Sabreena ta lura tanada son abinci ga saurin sakewa da mutane, ko bata sanka ba cikin minti alilan zata saba dakai kaman ta shekara da sanin ka
Seda Sabreena ta gama cin tuwon ta sannan ta dauko alkubus ta kara tayi nak ta tashi ta koma parlour ta zauna kusa da Mamah tana yabon abinci ta harda cewa za'a sa mata sauran alkubus din taje dashi gida, sun jima suna hira sannan ta tuna da sakon Abbanta ta dauko ta mikawa Mamah tana cewa "gashi Abba na yace in kawo miki, mantawa nayi dashi tun dazu", karba Mamah tayi ba tareda ta bue ba tace "amma ya kyauta, idan kinje kice mishi na gode", murmushi Sabreena tayi a zuciyarta tace "don't worry Anty, this is just the beginning"
A gidan ta wuni, sosai sukaji dadin zuwanta dan kuwa sunsha hira da labarin Libya, gidan seya musu dadi ya kuma yi lively ba kaman koda yaushe dayake boring ba dan ko Jawahir na gidan wuni take a daki tasa waya da laptop a gaba ta manta da sauran mutanen gidan, sedai idan sune zasu lekata
Se yamma lis driver dinta Isma'il yazo ya dauke ta inda Mamah ta mata alkhairi sosai tareda sake mika godiyar ta ga Abba, seda Mamah ta koma daki sannan ta bue sakon da Sabreena ta kawo mata, designer perfume ne a ciki me kyau na mata, murmushi tayi tana cewa "he's so nice", tareda tashi ta ajiye perf din kan dressing mirror tareda kara gyara kan mirror din
Kwanaki sun ja inda sati daya kenan da yin auren Osama, Jawahir harkar gabanta kawai takeyi a gidan, idan ta fito Allah yasa ta hadu da Farida toh zata tsaya a gaisa, se kuma wurin cin abinci da Dada ya kawo musu al'adar ci tare koda kuwa baya nan, bayan nan ba wani abu dake shiga tsakanin ta da Farida
Farida bata sanin fitan Jawahir amma ta tabbata Jawahir bata dawowa gida da wuri dan kusan sau uku tanajin shigowar ta kuma duka late Jawahir ke shigowa wanda ta dau alwashin gayawa Osama yau idan ya dawo daga aiki
Koda ya dawo taimaka mishi tayi yayi wanka yaci abinci, seda ta tabbata ya gama duka uzirinshi yana shirin kwanciya sannan tace "erhm, idan bazaka damu ba inaso muyi wata magana", kallon ta yayi na dan wani lokaci sannan ya nuna mata gefen shi alamar tazo ta zauna, ganin haka ta karasa kusa dashi kan gadon ta zauna suka jingina da dashboard ya kalleta yace "wace magana zamuyi?", sunkuyar da kai kasa tayi dan batasan ya zai dauki maganar ba, murmushi yayi yace "akan Jawahir ne koh?", dagowa tayi ta kalleshi tana mamakin yanda akayi ya sani, gyara zamanshi yayi ya fuskance ta da kyau yace "a gidan nan duk wanda yace yana da magana dani toh maganar shi baya wuce a kan Jawahir, wanda wannan dalilin yasa na auroki kema kin sani, saboda inaso ki taimaka min mu hada hannu wurin gyara mata tarbiyya", duk da taji ba dadi na cewar saboda Jawahir ya aurota bata nuna mishi ba sema murmushi da tayi tace "Inshallah zanyi kokari wajen ganin na taimaka maka", rungumota yayi jikinshi yana mata godiya yayinda ita kuma ta sake lafewa a jikin nashi tareda kudurtawa kanta duba lamarin Jawahir dan taga da alama ta nan ne kawai zata iya samun soyayyar mijinta kuma zatayi amfani da wannan damar ko dan Osama yasota koda rabin wanda take mishi ne
Washegari da safe ya kasance weekend dan haka dukkan su na gida ciki kuwa harda Osama, Jawahir ta riga kowa tashi amma ta saura daki ba tareda ta fito ba, su Dada kuwa se wuraren tara suka fito tare inda Dada ya zauna parlour tareda kunna TV dan ya kalla news ita kuma Farida ta shige kitchen dan hada musu breakfast
Jawahir na jin motsin su ta fito ta samu Dada a parlour ta karasa inda yake zauna ta zauna tana cewa "Good morning Dada", kallonta yayi da murmushi dauke a fuskar sa yace "morning my princess, kin tashi lafiya?", tace "lafiya lau Dada, nayi miss dinka kullum kafin na tashi ka fita kuma baka dawowa se nayi bacci", matso da ita yayi kusa dashi yana kwantar da kanta kan kafaanshi yace "aiki ne yamin waya my daughter, sabon branch mukeson budewa tareda karo ma'aikata shiyasa kikaga bana zama", zatayi magana Farida dake jinsu tin fitowar Jawahir ta leko daga kitchen dan wani kishi taji na ba gaira ba dalili ganin yadda suke zaune kaman ze maida ita ciki
Seda ta aro sakin fuska, ta saki fuskarta sosai sannan tace "Jawahir dear come help me in the kitchen", turo baki tayi tana kallon kofan kitchen din inda Farida ke tsaye sannan ta kalli Dada dan ta gani ko zeyi magana amma taji shiru, badan taso ba ta tashi ta wuce kitchen din
Albasa Farida tasata yankawa wanda za'a soya kwai dashi amma Jawahir rike wukan kirki ma bata iya ba, da chopping board ta yanka albasan amma kuma duk da haka manya ta yanka shi ba kyan gani kaman ba mace ba, da mamaki Farida ta kalleta tace "Jawahir kwai fa nace miki zan soya dashi ba sauce nace miki zanyi ba da zaki yanka albasan da girma haka, kuma ai ko sauce zanyi bazan yanka albasa haka", ajiye wukan Jawahir tayi sannan ta kalli Farida hannunta daya kan counter tace "bansaba yanka albasa ba, infact this is my first time dan haka hakuri zakayi da abinda kika gani", da fadan haka Jawahir ta bar kitchen din tana gunguni wai tayi abu ba'ayi appreciate ba inda ta bar Farida tsaye tana kallon bayanta wacce batasan sanda ta furta "tirkashi!!", ba
Shin readers kuma gani Farida zata dauka wannan abi'an daga Jawahir kuwa, if Yes then why? If No kuma wani mataki kuke gani zata dauka akan Jawahir?

UWA TA GARI - 12 - Page 3 - Wattpad
Cike da mamakin Jawahir Farida ta karasa aikinta, Jawahir kuwa koda Dada yaga ta fito tana gunguni yasan batayi abin arziki a kitchen din ba, girgiza kai yayi yaci gaba da kallon shi ba tareda yace komai ba, itama zama tayi tana ciro wayarta dake aljihun wandonta ta shiga Instagram tana duba feeds dinta
Koda Farida ta gama jera komai tayi kan dinning sannan ta musu iso zuwa dinning din dan su karya, Jawahir kallon yanda Dadanta ke hira da Farida cike da raha kawai takeyi, se a lokacin ta fara tambayar kanta 'toh meyasa tun tasowar ta bata taba ganin yanama Mamah magana cikin sanyin murya haka ba, se fada koda yaushe?', kawar da tunanin tayi saboda batason abinda ze dinga tuna mata da Mamah
Dada ne ya kalleta yace "my princess ya ba kya cin abincin?", daukon fork tayi ta soma ci tana cewa "ba komai, yanzu zanci", hada ido sukayi da Farida inda ta mata wani sly smile sannan ta maida hankalinta kan Dada sukaci gaba da hiransu, Jawahir ganin bazata jura tana zaune a wuri amma ace hankalin Dada na kan wata daban ba yasa ta mike tareda cewa "I'm full, zan shiga ciki na huta", basu hanata tafiya ba dan Dada yasan Jawahir ba gwanan cin abinci bace, barta dai da ci banza ci wofi amma bazata zauna taci abinci sosai me gina jiki ba
Tana shigewa daki Farida ta kalli Dada sosai ta matsar da plate din abincinta gefe sannan tace "idan bazaka damu ba inaso na sallami masu aikin gidan nan", kallonta yayi da mamaki yace "meyasa?", ta kamo hannunsa tana murzawa a hankali tace "saboda idan ba haka nayi ba Jawahir bazata taba zama cikakkiyar mace ba, sedai ta saura a jerin muna mata dan kuwa I'm sorry to say amma Jawahir lacks a lot of things ta fannin kula da gida, a wannan zamanin ba ko wani namiji bane ze yarda ya zauna da macen da bata iya girki ba balle kula da muhalli, ni a ganina idan na sallame masu aiki se mu raba aikin ni da ita kaga a haka zata fara iya wa da kadan kadan harta saba"
Tunani ya shiga yi kuma yaga tabbas haka din shine daidai dan idan da masu aiki akace tayi wani abun ba lallai ne tayi ba dan zata dinga gani kaman ai da masu aiki me amfaninsu amma idan basa nan kila tayi consider tayi abinda aka satan, amma hakan baze taba yiwuwa ba harsai ya zaunar da ita Jawahir din sunyi magana sannan
Ajiyar zuciya ya sauke sannan ya kalli Farida yace "gaskiya wannan shawarar taki shine daidai, kuma hakan zamuyi amma ki dan bata lokaci su gama exams dinsu tinda sun riga sun fara kuma next week zasu gama, kinga a lokacin tanada dama sosai tinda zasuyi hutu, inyaso masu aikin se'a sallamesu a matsayin an basu hutu kafin ita Jawahir din ta koma school, kinga kafin hutun ta ya kare ta koya wani abin ta fannin gyara gida dama girkin kanshi", murmushin samun nasara tayi tace "madallah, Allah ya mana jagora akan lamarin ta", da "ameen", ya amsa yanajin wani irin dadi a ranshi ganin yadda matar tashi ke kokarin ganin Jawahir ta zama 'a itama kaman yadda sa'anninta suke a ko ina
Sati daya kenan da Farida ta samu Dada ta mishi magana, yau Jawahir na dawowa daga last paper dinta taga alaman canji a gidan dan masu aikin da ke kula da gidan basa nan, gashi dakinta yadda ta tafi ta barshi haka tadawo ta tarar dashi ba abinda aka taba, pillow dinda ke kwance kasa ta dauke ta wurga kan gado sannan ta ajiye bag dinda ke hannunta ta fice tana kwalawa masu aikin kira amma taji shiru
Dada dake kwance daki ya tashi ya fito inda itama Farida dake kitchen ta fito tana cewa "Jawahir lafiya kike kwala kira haka?", ba tareda ta mata wani kallon arziki ba tace "inasu Mariya, haka suka barmin daki ba gyara tsabar kazanta, yaushe muka fara wasa dasu da har zasu bar min daki tun safe ba'a gyara ba", kallonta kawai Farida keyi tana mamakin hali irin na Jawahir, wato ita damuwarta ya kasance duk abinda takeso tazo ta sameshi a haka, batasan wani abu waishi Uziri ba
Dada dake jinsu ya karaso parlour din yana cewa "Jawahir sun tafi gida hutu dan haka ke zaki gyara dakin ki da kanki", da sauri ta kallo mahaifinta tareda cewa "what!!!", ya dage kafada yace "U heard me", da sauri ta karasa gabanshi tace "amma Dada meyas
", yayi saurin dakatar da ita tareda cewa "zo kiji princess dina, kwantar da hankalin ki", yana fada yana janta har suka fice zuwa wurin shan iskan dake gida yayinda ita kuma Farida ta koma kitchen tana tae baki tareda cewa "yarinya duk anbi a lalata ta ba abinda ta iya se tsantsar rashin kunya da fitsara, ai ni kam wallahi bazan dauki wannan ba, ina zaune gidan nan yarinya dole kiyi aiki danni ba boyar ki bace", ita kadai take ta maganganu tana aikinta
A waje kuwa kan kujera Dada ya zauna itama Jawahir ta nemi wuri ta zauna ya kalleta da kyau sannan yace "Jawahir inaso kiyi hakuri da abinda zan fada miki, amma kuma inaso ki sani cewar I'm doing this for your own good", shiru tayi tana kallon shi yaci gaba da cewa "na ba su Mariya hutu ne badan komai ba sedan kema ki samu ki fara wasu ayyukan da kanki kaman gyaran daki, laundry dinki, shara, wanke wanke da dai sauransu, I don't need to be telling you this amma ke kanki kinsan ke macece, wa'annan abubuwan ya kamata ace you are familiar with them, you are eighteen Jawahir nan gaba kadan zaki shiga nineteen, daga nan kuma zakiga maza sun fara zuwa neman aurenki, nasan ko yanzu ma akwai masu tsayar dake tunda yanzu a zamanin nan mazan sunfi ganewa su fara tsayar da mace su fahimci juna tun a waje kafin a kaiga magana da iyaye, Jawahir idan na aurar dake ba tareda kin iya komai ba toh tabbas na cuceki a matsayina na mahaifinki kuma wanda kike hannuna, zakiji kunya kuma nima zanji kunya dan ba makawa za'a iya sallamo ki gida saboda wannan dalilin kawai, dan haka nakeso ki kai zuciya nesa kiyi abinda kike ganin ya dace, I'm here for you, bazan takuraki ba amma inaso kiyi tunani akai, sometimes you can even help your new Mummy a kitchen idan kina free, u need to be familiar with the household chores dan haka na basu Mariya hutu dan ki samu dama", shiru tayi tana kallon Dada dan batama da bakin magana
Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke dan ta sani sarai gaskiya ya fada amma meye dalilin da zesa abinda ba'ayi introduce dinta dashi tin tana yarinya se yanzu data riga ta gama sabawa da rayuwar hutu, rayuwar zaman banza, ba aikin fari balle baki, ita bata ganin zata iya adjust to this new situation amma she will try kodan ta farantawa Dada dinta rai, murmushi tayi ta kalleshi taga shima din ita yake kallo ta kara fadada murmushin ta sannan tace "Dada zanyi kokari wurin ganin nayi abinda ya dace, Inshallah Allah bazan zama silar da zakaji kunya nan gaba ba", kayataccen murmushi yayi ya shafa kanta tareda cewa "Allah ya miki albarka", ta amsa da "ameen", tana kokarin tashi yace "Jawahir zauna akwai maganan da zamuyi kuma", zama ta sake yi tana kallon shi yace "Jawahir magana zamuyi akan sallah, karkiga kaman basan abinda kikeyi ba na sani, kawai dai na sa miki ido ne ina jiran right time dinda ya kamata na miki magana, Jawahir ki taimaka ki daina wasa da sallan ki, ki dingayi akan lokaci dan idan kina wasu ayyukan ladan amma kina wasa da sallah toh duk ayyukan zasu tashi a banza, kar ki ga kaman idan kina wasa da sallah zakici bulus, sam abin ba haka yake ba, nasan na fita hakkin ki na kaiki islamiyya amma bansan dalilin ki na kin zama kiyi karatu ba, idan kika kyautata sallar ki toh tabbas ze zame miki jagora wurin kyautata sauran ayyukan ki dan haka nakeso ki nutsu Jawahir, ki kula da ibadan ki kodan ki samu rabauta"
Kallonshi tayi idonta cike da hawaye amma kuma se taga bazata iya kallon idonshi ba saboda kunya, ada kai tayi kawai tareda cewa "shikenan Dada zan kula sosai, kuma na gode da wannan tunatar wan" da murmushin samun nasara kwance kan fuskarshi yace "Allah ya miki albarka ya baki miji na gari wanda ze kular min dake fiye da yanda nake kula dake", murmushi tayi tareda saurin barin wurin saboda kunya da taji
A ranar da kyar Jawahir ta iya gyara dakinta ta share harda mopping kaman yadda taga su Mariya nayi, koda ta gama bata fita ba ta kwanta kan rug din dakin tana sauke ajiyar zuciya tareda "oh my God!! bayana na ciwo", dariya Farida tayi wacce shigowar ta kenan taji Jawahir na complain, zama tayi kan bedside drower tana cewa "sorry, a hankali zaki saba kinji", Jawahir bata kulata ba sema mikewa da tayi tana shirin cire kayan jikinta saboda tanaso tayi wanka
Ba tareda ta kalli Farida ba tace "kwanan nan Dada na yawan zama gida ko lafiya?", murmushi Farida tayi tace "You should ask him yourself, idan kin gama ki fito muyi lunch ke kadai ake jira", bata kulata ba itama Farida batasa ran zata kulata din ba dan haka ta fice yayin da Jawahir ta daura towel ta shige bathroom
A kwana a tashi har anyi sati biyu, inda Jawahir ta dau nasihar Dadanta take kokari wurin ganin tayi sallah a kan lokaci, sannan kullum idan tashi zata gyara makwancinta da bathroom dinta bayan wannan ba wani abu da takeyi a gidan
Ba yadda Farida batayi da ita ba akan su dinga girki tare amma Jawahir ta nuna ita she's not a fan of cooking dan haka a kyaleta tinda ko anyi girkin ma ba wani abun arziki take ci ba
Koda Farida ta fadawa Dada abinda Jawahir tace shima seya biye mata yace a barta for now, later zata koya, abinda yaba Farida mamaki sosai kenan, ace yarinya kamar Jawahir bata iya komai ba koma a haka ake cewa later zata koya, har se yaushe kenan? Jawahir ganin Dada ya tsaya mata itama seta shantake dan dama ko maganan shiga kitchen din bataso ana mata
A washegarin ranar da Najib ya hadu da Sabreena a gidan Mamah se yaji yarinyar ta kwanta mai, danshi a rayuwa yana son mutum me wasa da raha wanda idan yana wuri ba'a gajiya dashi
Wannan dalilin yasa Najib ya tashi yaje har wurin Mamah ya karbi number din Sabreena, yasha tsiya a wurin Mamah sosai duk da ya nemi ya fahimtar da ita cewar shifa ba son Sabreena yakeyi ba kawai dai yana son ya kulla awance da ita ne amma Mamah bata bashi dama ba dan zolayar shi ta dingayi har ya tashi ya bar mata gidan tana mishi dariya
Ta watsapp ya mata magana wanda da farko bata gane cewar shi bane, se wasa da hankalinta yakeyi har dai ta gaji tace idan be fito ya fada mata ko shi wanene ba zatayi block dinshi
Gudun kar ayi blocking nashi yasa ya fada mata cewar shine ya mata bayanin kanshi sannan fah ta gane, Najib ba karamin takura mata yakeyi ba duk da baya kiranta har bataso ta kunna data dinta ta ganshi online dan zolayarta yakeyi harse ya kular da ita, daga yace mata foodie, se yace mata wacce bata iya serving din abinci ba ko kuma yace taga yana cin tuwo tasa mishi ido tana hadiyan yawu har tasa ya kware tsabar maita irin nata
Sometime ma har bataso ta bue chats dinsu idan yayi mata message amma kuma ba ta iyawa dan ita kanta ta rasa dalilin da yasa idan ya aiko mata da sako seta bude duk da tasan ba abin arziki zata gani ba illa ma ya tsokane ta
Wasa wasa cikin kankanin lokaci shakuwa ya shiga tsakanin Sabreena da Najib wanda idan bata ga sakonshi a wayar ta ba bata samun sukuni dan tunani take shiga na meyasa be mata message ba, inda shima a bangaren shi idan ya mata message batayi reply ba ze shiga tunanin lafiya taki reply dan dadewar da sukeyi suna chat yasa gabadayansu sun zama phone addict se kace wani abun arziki suke fada idan suna chat din
Sabreena ce zaune a dakin ta kan gado tana tunanin Abbanta daya kwana jiya da zazzai, ita ta zauna kanshi tareda samo ruwa a bowl da towel ta goge mishi jiki sannan da kyar ta samu yasha magani bacci ya dauke shi
Kasa barin dakin tayi dan a tunaninta zazzabin ze iya tashi cikin dare, koda Abba ya farka cikin dare ya ganta zaune kan kujera a gefenshi kanta kan gado tana bacci seya tausaya mata dan yasan cewar da ace yanada mata da tilon 'ar shi bazata hana kanta samun baccin arziki ba saboda beda lafiya
Tunanin ta ya tsaya ne kan tayi wa Najib magana dan shi kadai ne ze iya taimaka mata wurin aiwatar da kudirin ta saboda bazata so taci gaba da ganin Abban ta a wannan yanayin ba
Wayanta ta dauko for the first time da zata fara texting din Najib farko dan koda yaushe shine me bue musu shafin hira ba ita ba
Sallama ta mishi wanda cikin kankanin lokaci ya amsa mata sallaman ta yana mamaki dan yasan Sabreena bata mishi sallama sedai shi yayi
Ba tareda tayi wani dogon surutu ba ta type mishi "I want to talk to you about something important" ya dade yana nazarin message dinta kafin ya mata reply da "will call you now", kafin tayi reply watsapp audio call ya shigo wayan ta, tunani ta fara yi na idan ta dauka me zata ce mishi, ta ina za ta fara, ganin call din ya kusa katsewa ta dauka sannan tayi gyaran murya ta kai wayan kunne
A hankali yace "Reena hope everything is alright with you?", rolling idanuwanta tayi a zuciyarta tace "shi wannan baze taba kiran sunan mutum ba wai wani Reena, me kuma Reena", "Reena are you there?", ta sake jin maganar shi tayi sauri ta gyara nutsuwarta sannan tace "yes, dama inaso in maka wata magana ne, zaka iya zuwa gidan mu?", shiru yayi na en dakiku be amsa ba sannan daga baya yace "why not mu hadu a gidan Anty na", da sauri tace "a'a ba zamu iya zuwa gidan ta ba saboda maganan da zamuyi involves her kuma banason taji komai harse mun yanke shawara", da mamaki yace "involves her kuma", tace "Yes", yayi shiru yana tunani kafin yace "shikenan send me your address zanzo gobe by 4pm", cike da murna tace "thank you, will be expecting you", daga haka ta yanke kiran shikuwa murmushi yayi dan from the way she sounds yasan tayi murna da zuwan da yace mata zeyi

UWA TA GARI - 13 - Wattpad
Washegari kaman yadda Najib yayi alawari haka ya shirya ya dau motanshi ya wuce gidansu Sabreena tareda taimakon address din da ta tura mishi, koda ya kai seya kirata a waya ringing biyu ta dauka yace "I'm outside your house", ta window dinta ta leka ta hangoshi sannan tace "just horn, za'a bude maka", kashe wayan yayi ya ajiye sannan yayi horn, ba'a dau lokaci ba gateman din ya bude ya karasa gaban motan Najib yana lekashi yace "kai ne Najib?", cikin nutsuwa yace "eh nine", mutumin yayi murmushi yace "bismilla shiga daga ciki", shiga yayi ya samu wuri yayi parking motarshi yana shirin fitowa yaga Sabreena zuwa sanye da atampha dinki gown wanda ya karbi jikinta sosai
Ita kuwa kunyar shi ma takeji dan tinda suka hadu a gidan Mamah bata kara ganinshi face to face ba se yau, iyakar su chat a waya, ganin ta karaso ya bude ya fito yana cewa "Madam ya akayi ne?", dariya tayi jin abinda yace, wai daga haduwa da ita ya rasa me zece se ya akayi ne, kallon ta yayi ganin tana dariya yace "kodai na fadi ba dai dai bane?", ta girgiza kai tana cewa "a'a mu shiga daga ciki", suna tafiya yace "amma gidan kaman ba mutane dayawa koh?", ta ada kai tace "dagani se Abba na se masu aiki", yaso ya tambayi mahaifiyarta fa amma yayi shiru har suka karasa guest parlour tace "bismilla zauna, ina zuwa", zama yayi ita kuma ta fice daga parlourn
Kitchen ta wuce ta hado mai refreshments ta dawo ta ajiye gabanshi sannan ta nemi wuri ta zauna, ya dau ruwa ya kai baki yana sha seda yasha ya ajiye sannan yace "da fatan dai yau baza'a sani kwarewa ba", kallon shi tayi batasan sanda ta harare shi ba shi kuwa yayi murmushi yana cewa "You have a nice house", tace "you are right, gidan mu nada kyau amma yana lacking home feeling, I don't feel like home idan ina gida saboda ba kowa, daga ni se ni se kuma masu aiki dan Abba na idan ya wuce hospital tin safe se yamma yake dawowa", ada kai yayi yace "so your dad is a doctor?", tace "yes"
Shiru suka danyi kafin ya kalleta yace "so maganan me zamuyi", ajiyar zuciya ta sauke tace "maganan Abba na da Antyn ka", kallonta yayi da mamaki yana tunani meya hada antynshi da Abbanta, ganin ya shiga tunani se tayi murmushi tace "kaga let me give you my story in brief", kallon yayi taci gaba da cewa "Abba na dan Nigeria ne inda Ummi na kuma 'yar kasar Libya ce, I'm the only child, na taso ba tareda na taba ganin mahaifiya ta ba se a hoto saboda mahaifiyata ta rasu ne bayan ta kawo ni duniya, da farko kakata ta bangaren mahaifi ita ta rike ni har na danyi wayo sannan na koma Libya wurin iyayen mahaifiyata inda a nan na san wacece mahaifiya ta dan babu abinda ba'a fada min a kanta ba, seda na gama karatun secondary na dawo nan wanda a halin yanzu ko 2months ban cike da dawowa ba", ajiyar zuciya ya sauke cike da tausayawa yace "Allah ya jikanta", ta amsa da ameen tana goge kwallan da ke kokarin zubowa"
Shiru suka danyi na en dakiku danshi kam yanzu besan me zaice mata ba after hearing her story, gyara zama tayi tace "tin lokacin da mahaifiyata ta koma ga mahallicin ta har yanzu Abba na yaki ya sake aure, wanda a alla a yanzu an kai shekara sha bakwai zuwa sha takwas", kallon ta yayi taci gaba da cewa "dan zamana da Anty na fahimci cewar itama batada miji", kai ya ada yace "haka ne", tace "shima rasuwa yayi?", ya girgiza kai yace "no, rabuwa sukayi and she has a daughter just like you, sedai inaga zama ta girme ki da shekara daya", nan ya dan bata brief history dinsu da Mamah amma be fada mata saanin da suke samu da Jawahir ba kawai dai yace Jawahir prefers to leave with her Dad ne
Shiru tayi kafin daga baya ta kalleshi tace "what do think mu hada Abba na da Anty aure", da sauri ya kalleta tace "don't give me that look and understand what I'm trying to say, kaga idan Abba na ya auri Anty many lifes will be happy, for example Abba na ze samu me kula dashi a matsayin ta na matarshi, Anty zata samu miji whom she can lean on whenever she needs a shoulder, I will be able to experience what a mother's love is, she will be happy, I will be happy and my Abba will also be happy, atleast we will make a small happy family", kallonta yaci gaba da yi yayinda yake tunanin hanya Antynshi zata yarda, shifa beson ya orawa kanshi abinda zesa Antynshi tayi fushi dashi
A hankali Sabreena tace "c'mon say something", ajiyar zuciya ya sauke sannan yace "ok zanyi tunani a kai", da sauri tace "no, ba maganan tunani dan banso a bata lokaci sosai, indan har ka amince I will handle my Abba while you handle your Anty muga result dinda zamu samu zuwa next week Friday", ajiyar zuciya ya sake saukewa danshi Sabreena tasashi a tsaka me wuya ne, dan yana tsananin son Antynshi kwatakwata bayason abinda ze batawa Antynshi rai, shi a ganinshi tinda ita bata dauko maganan auren ba bega dalilin da zesa shi ya dauko ba, abinda be sani ba shine Mamah da Yaya Aysha sun riga sunyi maganar cewar idan har ta samu wanda takeso kuma yake sonta tsakani da Allah toh aurenta zatayi, kallon Sabreena yayi yace "I will see what I can do", marairaice fuska tayi tace "dan Allah ka agaza, do your best hmn", yadda tayi maganan yasashi sakin murmushi sannan ya mike yana cewa "karki damu, kiyi addu'a Allah yasa a samu nasara"
Itama mikewa tayi ta rakashi har bakin mota ya juyo ya kalleta yace "toh Madam foodie ni zan wuce", hararar shi tayi sannan ta fara leka cikin motan tana cewa "kai yanzu haka ake zuwa wurin mutum hannu rabbana atina ko dan tsarabar nan babu", kallonta yayi yana waro ido dan shi gaba-daya ma ya manta yace "sorry foodie, wallahi mantawa nayi amma karki damu zan biya next time idan na tashi dawowa komai 2-2 zan kawo miki", ganin yayi serious tace "look I'm just joking fah", dan dariya yayi ya shige motanshi yana cewa "thanks for the refreshments", daga mishi hannu tayi tana mishi bye bye ya fice daga gidan ita kuma ta koma ciki fuskar ta dauke da murmushin samun nasara
Jawahir ce zaune ita da Jarood a park tana mishi complain akan aikin da takeyi a gida wanda be wuce gyaran nata dakin ba, murmushi yayi yace "don't worry, komai zezo karshe", gyara zama tayi tace "gashi gobe Dada zeyi tafiya, banson zama da wannan matar dan ban yarda da ita ba", kallon ta yayi yace "kaman ya baki yarda da ita ba?", tace "i donno, kawai dai batamin bane", dariya yayi yace "kawai kedai kiyi abinda ke gabanki, kar kiyi abinda zata samu abin fada a gaban Dada", ada kai tayi tace "sure"
Haka sukaci gaba da hira ganin yamma ya gabato yace ze sauke ta gida, koda ta shiga gida batabi ta kan kowa ba ta shige dakin ta
Washegari da safe Dada ya tashi da shirin shi, seda sukaci abinci sannan duk suka mishi rakiya a bakin mota ya tsaya ya musu nasiha kan su zauna lafiya sannan ya juya ya kalli Jawahir yace "toh princess a kula da kyau, a dinga taya new Mummy aiki kinji, kuma banda yawace yawace", murmushi tayi tace "Inshallah Dada"
A gabansu ya shige mota driver dinshi ya jashi zuwa airport, suna shigewa ciki Jawahir na kokarin shiga daki Farida tace "Jawahir wanke wanke na jiranki a kitchen, zan gyara bedroom din babanki dan haka kiyi wanke wanke kafin na fito, idan na gama zaki rakani market", da "toh", Jawahir ta amsa ta wuce kitchen din, wani irin dariya Farida tayi tace "Yes", sannan tayi hanyar dakin Dada cike da tsananin jin dadi
