UWA TA GARI - 14 - Page 4 - Wattpad
Koda Jawahir ta shiga kitchen mamaki ne ya kamata ganin yadda Farida ta mata magana, ita ta amince zatayi wanke wanken ne dan kawai kar Farida ta samu abin fada, nan ta wanke kwanikan kaman yadda taga Mariya nayi, tana gamawa ta koma daki tayi wanka ta canza kaya ta zauna zaman jiran Farida dan muddin bataso ta batawa Dadanta rai dole tabi Farida sahu da kafa amma kuma bataso ta bawa Farida fuskar da zata rena ta dan ta kula Farida bata iya samun wuri ba
Itama Farida tana gama gyara daki tayi wanka ta shirya cikin atampha dinkin skirt and blouse ta yafa babban mayafi ta fito ta leka dakin Jawahir ta kirata sannan suka fice
Babu me tankawa wani a cikin su duk sunyi shiru Farida nata faman tuki abinta, a gaban mall din da zatayi siyayya yayi parking suka fito suka shiga ciki, wuri Jawahir ta samu ta zauna yayin da Farida ta shiga zagaya wurin tana daukan abinda tasan suna bukata a gida harta gama ta biya aka pack mata shi a leda, kiran Jawahir tayi wai tazo ta kwashi kayan, leda uku ne ajiye a wurin, Jawahir na karasowa ta dauki leda daya ta fice abinta ta bar Farida tsaye tana mata kallon mamaki, kwashe sauran kayan Farida tayi ta kai mota suka wuce gida
A waje tayi parking tace "Jawahir shiga da kayan ciki, ni zan fita se zuwa yamma zan dawo, idan kina jin yunwa you can help yourself with something in the kitchen", fita Jawahir tayi ta kwashi kayan tace "se kin dawo", sannan tayi ciki ba tareda ta jira amsar Farida ba
Farida tafi minti biyar a wajen bata tada mota ba tana tunani, ajiyar zuciya ta sauke sannan ta tada motan ta fice, bata tsaya ko ina ba se wani haddaden estate inda tayi horn a gaban gida na biyar aka bude mata gate ta shige, parking tayi ta fito ta shiga cikin gidan bakinta dauke da sallama
Manyan en mata ne su uku zaune a parlourn wanda a alla duk zasuyi shekara daya da Faridan kowa na harkan gaban, zama tayi sannan tace "Nafi how far", wacce aka kira da Nafi tana canza tashan TV tace "amarya a gidan Osama se yau ake ganinki", dariya kawai tayi wacce ke zaune kusa da Nafisa tana shan fruits wanda aka yayyanka mata a bowl tace "kedai manta da ita, ba tayi aure taji dadin aure ta manta damu ba", matsowa kusa da ita Farida tayi tana dafa kafaanta tace "Salma har da ke", gira kawai Salma ta gada mata ta girgiza kai sannan ta juya kan dayan wacce ke zaune a kujera daban gaba-daya hankalinta na kan laptop dinda ke ajiye a hannun kujeran Farida na murmushi tace "ai nasan sweetheart dina bazata taba fushi dani ba", ba tare da ta juyo ba tace "Rida nafi kowa fushi dake", pity face Farida tayi tace "haba har da ke Zulaika", Zulaika ta juyo ta kalleta tace "uhmm, har dani", Farida ta taso taje wurin Zulaika tana cewa "toh yi hakuri my habibti, my sweet chocolaty, my one and only true love kinji", Nafisa da Salma dariya suka yi yayin da Zulaika ta kalleta tace "kalaman soyayyan da kike fadawa Osama kika zo nan kina min bitansu, toh naki na hakura", dariya suka sake yi Salma tace "yau dai munga wasu a rana", Nafi tace "kedai 'yar uwa ai ba'a magana"
Dauke laptop din Farida tayi ta ajiye kan center table sannan tazo ta zauna tana kamo hannun Zulaika tace "haba my bestie karki bari su mana dariya mana", kallonsu Nafisa Zulaika tayi sannan tace "manta dasu, ai sun san bazan iya fushi dake ba", gwalo Farida ta musu su kuwa suka ce "oho, mun dai ganku a rana"
Farida, Zulaika, Nafisa da Salma duk kawaye ne tun suna yara, unguwar su daya dukkansu kuma cikin ikon Allah school dinsu ma ya zamana aya wanda kullum idan school bus ze sauke su su hudun ake saukewa tare kasancewar basu da nisa da juna, wannan dalilin yasa suka kulla awance tsakaninsu, Nafisa ce babbar su dan duk ta basu kusan wata goma, idan Farida da Zulaika month dinsu daya wanda wannan dalilin yasa sukafi shakuwa har suke kiran kansu da bestfriends, Salma itace karamar su kuma itace gentle a cikin dan duk ta fisu nutsuwa da kuma kaifin tunani, dukkansu same year aka haifesu months dinne ya banbanta, tare suka taso har iyayensu sunsan da kawancensu, har suka kai matakin Jami'a inda dukkan su suka zabi school aya wato BUK dake garin kano kuma duk sun samu admission dayake sunada kokari sosai, koda suka gama school gabadayansu sun samu aiki kasancewar iyayensu suna da connections a cikin garin Kebbi, fara aikinsu da wata biyar suka hada kudi suka siya wannan gidan da suke ciki a yanzu, four bedroom bungalow ne inda ko wannensu ya dau daki daya, koda suka fadawa iyayensu basu nuna kin amincewa ba suka bar su suka tare a sabon gidan su dan basa son takurawa yaransu duk da kasancewar su mata
Wannan kenan
Farida ta dade a gidan suna hira, se bayan da sukaci lunch sannan duk suka koma dakin Farida sanda take budurwa suka bude sabon shafin hira, a nan Farida ta koro musu irin halin Jawahir da yadda suke zama da Jawahir inda ta kara da cewa "ni wallahi yarinyar nan tana shiga min hanci dayawa, kunga yadda take makalewa jikin Osama kaman zata koma ciki shikuma baze hanata ba, gashi batajin maganata ni yau ma nayi mamaki da tayi wanke wanken da na sata, ga shegen son sa kananun kaya", Nafisa ce tayi saurin magana tace "amma lallai Farida kin badani, ace yarinya karama kaman Jawahir ta gagare ki, ai kawai hanya zaki nema kiyi wrapping dinta around your finger yanda se abinda kikace shi zatayi"
Shiru Farida tayi tana kallon Zulaika da Salma dan jin me zasuce, Salma ce ta budi baki tace "a gaskiya wannan ba shawara bace, ki dai bita sannu a hankali, da sannu zata saki jiki dake", Zulaika tayi saurin fadin "wannan yarinyar da ganin ta 'yar rainin hankali ce, dan haka dole mu koya mata hankali, ni da nice a wannan gidan da tuni na maida ita boyi boyi na se abinda nace, akan me zan zauna da zankadediyar budurwa a gida kuma ace ni zan girka taci, sannan kuma na mata wanke wanke Allah ya tsare ya kiyaye, gaskiya bestie kinyi bacci dayawa, kin bata chance sosai", girgiza kai Salma tayi yayinda Farida ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tace "toh ni yanzu me kukeso nayi, banson nayi abinda ze zamemin matsala tsakani na da Osama", tsaki Zulaika tayi yayinda Nafisa tace "wannan abu me sauki ne, kawai kizo muje wurin wannan baban nan daya miki istikhara akan Osama, bazamu fito mu fada mishi gashi gashi ba, kawai ce mishi zakiyi Osama ya daina kulaki saboda Jawahir kuma ita bata ganin girman ki kinaso ya taimaka miki, shikenan an wuce wurin", shiru tayi yayinda Salma ta tashi tana cewa "wannan abun bada ni ba", sannan ta fice Nafi da Zulaika suka bita da harara sannan Zulaika ta maido hankalinta kan Farida tace "Rida ba se kinyi wani dogon tunani ba, tinda bawai wurin boka zamu ba", a hankali Farida tace "me banbancin inda zamu da wurin boka", murmushi Nafi tayi tace "da banbanci, ai ba laifi bane idan mace nason ta mallaki mijin ta, ko wace mace da kika gani tanaso ace ita take mulkin gidanta, dan haka idan kin shirya muma a shirye muke, yanzu ma semu raka ki", kallon Zulaika tayi inda ta ada mata kai alaman suje sannan Farida tace "shikenan, muyi sallah semu wuce", da murnar su suka mike suna cewa "ko ke fa, amma da kin zauna kina kunsawa kanki bakin ciki"
Da wannan bahaguwar shawarar sukayi sallah suka shirya suka fice a motar Nafi dan ita tafisu sannan kan unguwar da baban yake
Koda Jawahir ta shiga da kayan kan dinning taje ta ajiye su sannan ta wuce dakin ta, ko zama batayi ba ta cire jallabiyan dake jikinta ta dauko wani blue pencil jeans da yellow top tasa, sosai kayan suka matse ta, veil ta dauko black ta daura a kanta, sannan ta dauko bag da takalmi duk baki tasa ta fashe jikinta da turare ta fice se kamshi takeyi
Malam Gado dake zaune bakin gate ya kunna radio yana kokarin seta ta ya kalleta yace "Jawahir ina zuwa haka", kaman batasan Allah yayi ruwanshi a wurin ba ta bude gate ta fice abinta, girgiza kai yayi yace "Allah ya shirya", sannan yaci gaba da abinda yakeyi
Ita kuwa a daidaita ta tsayar inda ta bashi address din gidansu Rumana tace ya kaita, a kofar gidan ya sauketa ta biyashi sannan ta shiga kwankwasa gate din, me gadin sune ya bude mata ta shige ciki da yake ya riga yasan ta, koda taga ba kowa parlour bata tsaya ba ta hau sama inda tasan dakin Rumana yake, seda ta kwankwasa sannan ta shiga ciki inda taga Rumana kwance tana kallo a laptop dinta, zama tayi kan gadon tana cewa "ke wai baki ganni bane", dagowa Rumana tayi tace "na ganki mana, kawai dai banso na dauke kaina daga wannan movie din ne", tsaki Jawahir taja itama ta nemi wuri ta kwanta tana kallon movie din tace "kinsan dai zamuje shopping ne koh", kallon ta Rumana tayi tace "ai ni kam sedai na rakaki dan babu enough kudi a hannu na", shiru Jawahir tayi kafin daga baya ta dauko wayanta tana kiran Jarood ta kalli Rumana tace "dan Allah ki shirya bari na kira Jarood yazo ya kaimu, nasan maybe ma ya biya", tashi Rumana tayi tace "ai indai ze biya bani da matsala dan dama akwai wani gown da nakeso na siya dan inaga ni shi kadai ma zan siya"
Daukan wayan da Jarood yayi ne yasa Jawahir taba kulata ba ta maida hankalinta kan wayan da takeyi tace "Jarood kana ina ne?", "Ina gida", ya bata amsa tace "pls shopping zaka kaimu nida Rumana", shiru yayi na en dakiku yana tunani sannan yace "amma dai bazaku dade ba koh, dan inada wurin zuwa anjima", da sauri tace "bazamu dade ba", yace "kina gida ne", tace "a'a ina gidansu Rumana", yace "ok, gani nan zuwa"
Be dau lokaci sosai ba ya karaso inda duk suka fito suka sameshi a mota, suna shiga yaja motar yana tambayar su a inda zasu yi shopping suka fada mishi, hirace ta barke a cikin motan suna cewa Zahra tayi miss ta koma gida hutu, haka sukaci gaba da hira har suka karasa inda zasu dukkansu suka fito ya rufe motan sannan ya bisu ciki
Siyayya Jawahir tayi shi harna fitan hankali wanda duka kuma ba wani kayan arziki bane ta siya ba, sun zo biyan kudi Jarood yace su barshi inda ya ciro credit card dinshi ya mikawa matar da ke tsaye a counter din akayi debit din kudi, Jawahir da Rumana kallon juna sukayi sannan Jawahir tayi miskilin murmushi tana dage gira irin "i told you so" dinnan, tana mika mishi card dinshi suka kwashi kayan su suka fice
Mamah dake tsaye gefe tin dazu tana kallonsu ta dafe kanta dake sara mata tana cewa "it can't be, for goodness sake Jawahir batada tunani ne zatayi irin wannan shigar duk suran jikinta na waje koh mayafin arziki babu", nan da nan zuciyarta ta bata shawaran tabi bayan Jawahir din ta mata magana
Da sauri itama ta fice inda ta tarar suna kokarin shiga mota tayi saurin cewa "Jawahir! Jawahir dear", juyowa Jawahir tayi saboda muryan Mamah da taji, bata fuska tayi ganin Mamah na karasowa wurinta tayi sauri tace "Jarood let's go, I don't want this woman to meet me here", Rumana ce tace "haba mana Jawahir, just listen to her for once mana", kafin Jawahir tayi wata maganar Mamah ta karaso inda suke tace "Jawahir how are you?", tana turo baki gaba tace "as you can see I'm doing good without you", ganin Jawahir na neman bada ita a bainar jama'a tace ", dan Allah kizo muje coffee shop din chan muyi magana, I need us to discuss pls", bata fuska Jawahir tayi tace "I don't have anything to discuss with you", Mamah batayi kasa a gwiwa ba tace "pls my baby, listen to Mama", Jawahir zata kara yao wata maganar Jarood yace "go with her Jawahir, zamu jiraki a mota", ba dan taso ba sedan bata iya yiwa Jarood musu tayi gaba Mamah tayi saurin kallon Jarood tace "tnx son", sannan ta juya tabi bayan Jawahir
Table suka samu suka zauna waiter yazo ya tambaye su wani irin coffee suke so Jawahir tace "cappuccino", itama Mamah tace "same" Jawahir tayi saurin tsayar da waiter din ganin ze juya tace "pls I think I will just have water if that's ok with you", murmushi yayi yace "sure", sannan ya juya ya wuce
Riko hannun Jawahir dake kan table Mamah tayi Jawahir ta janye hannunta Mamah tace "my baby laifin me na miki hmm, why do you hate your mummy", Mamah ta tambaya muryarta na karyewa, shiru Jawahir tayi dan ita kanta bata da amsar wannan tambayar, ajiyar zuciya Mamah ta sauke tace "nasan you don't like me and I'm ok with it as far as you are happy cos your happiness is all that matters to me", kallonta Jawahir tayi sannan tace "as if", yawu Mamah ta hadiye sannan tayi murmushin karfin hali tace "my daughter really looks beautiful amma dressing dinta ne kawai ya bata mata kyawunta", Jawahir zatayi magana waiter din yazo ya ajiye musu abunda suka bukata ya bar wurin
Seda Jawahir ta kwankwade ruwan ta sannan tace "and what is wrong with my dressing?", kai tsaye Mamah tace "they are too tight", wani bazawarin dariya Jawahir tayi sannan ta kalli Mamah tace "and so", Mamah tace "it doesn't suit you, a matsayinki na 'yar musulma kuma wacce tasan what is wrong or right kema kinsan wannan shirin be kamace ki ba, ki dinga suturta jikinki Jawahir, wani kamilin namiji ne ze ganki a irin wannan shiga yaji sha'awar aurenki? babu, se watsassun maza wanda burinsu ne su lalata yara mata, dan Allah ki zamo me kamun kai Jawahir karki bari mutane su dinga miki kallon wacce batada mutunci bayan ni nasan da mutuncin ki, ki dinga kula Jawahir wannan rayuwar da kika daukar wa kanki it won't pay you, zakizo kina ciza yatsa ne nan gaba kina dana sani"
Idanun Jawahir jajawur hawaye ya cika mata ido amma ko kadan taki yarda su zubu ta kalli Mamah muryar ta na rawa tace "kin gama?", mamaki jin abinda Jawahir tace Mamah tayi Jawahir taci gaba da cewa "well thanks for the lectures, amma inaso ki sani you don't have the right to tell me what to do or what to wear", da sauri Mamah tace "Jawahir I have every right to tell you what to do because I'm your mother and you are my daughter", cikin daga murya Jawahir tace " you are not my mother and I am in no way your daughter!", gabadaya mutanen wurin kallo ya koma kansu Jawahir taci gaba da cewa "Yes kece kika haife ni and I'm very disappointed that I can't change that fact but you were never my mother, bakya sona saboda bakya son abinda nakeso and just few months ago you disowned me if I can remember", cikin sanyin murya Mamah tace "I've never disowned you Jawahir bazan taba ita kaurace miki ba", Mamah ta karashe tana goge hawayen dake zubo mata da gefen mayafinta gwanin tausayi, Jawahir ta kalli gefe tace "I see, in that case explain to me abinda yasa kikace kin barwa Dada ni, u've never even checked on me for once since then, why now?", shiru Mamah tayi dan batasan me zatace ba, Jawahir ta mike daga kan kujerarta ta kalli mutanen dake kallonsu tace "kun ganta, she can't even answer my question", juyawa tayi ta kalli Mamah tace "kinsan wani abu, dake da babu duk daya kuke a gurina useless mother kawai", Mamah ji tayi kaman an caka mata wuka a kirji, kukan da takeso tayi ma ya gagara saboda bakin ciki, sosai tayi dana sanin yiwa Jawahir magana, da tasani ta kyaleta taci gaba da harkar gabanta aci gaba da zaman lafiya ba tareda rayuka sun baci ba
Najib dake tsaye wurin tun dazu tsakamakon kiranshi da wani abokin shi yayi ya fada mishi abinda ke faruwa a coffee shop din ya karaso idanunshi na zubar da hawaye, Jawahir dake shirin barin wurin taji saukar kyakkyawan mari a fuskarta wanda yasata dagowa dan ganin koh waye a wurin, ganin Najib ne ta bude baki zata magana ya kara sakar mata da wani, dafe kumatunta tayi tana kuka tace "yaya Najib base ka nunawa duniya cewar kaima ka tsaneni ba, ai dama duk wani jinin wannan matar ba so na suke ba", ya daga hannu ze kara mata Mamah tayi saurin rike hannunshi tana cewa "Najib karka tabata, kyaleta, Jawahir wuce gida, Allah ya kiyaye hanya", ba tareda Jawahir ta kuma kallonsu ba ta fice daga wurin tana kuka wanda Mamah kejinshi har cikin ranta, zama Mamah ta dafe kai da kirji saboda tsananin bugawa da kirjinta keyi
Dagota Najib yayi ya ciro 1k ya ajiye kan table din kudin coffee din da suka siya sannan yajata suka bar wurin ana binsu da kallon tausayi mutane na mamakin me Mamah tayi wa Jawahir har take mata irin wannan tsanar
Tinda Najib ya fara tuki ba wanda yayi magana cikinsu kowa da abinda yake tunani a ranshi, ganin ya dau hanyar gidansu tace "Najib take me home", ba tareda daya kalleta na yace "a'a Anty na You need someone beside you", cikin tsawa tace "nace ka kaini gidana koh kaima rashin kunyar zakamin ka nunamin bani na haife ka ba", sosai ta bashi tausayi dan yasan cewar duk zafin abinda Jawahir ta mata ne yasa take react hakanan, juya akalar motarshi yayi zuwa hanyar gidanta yana share hawayen daya zubo mishi na tausayin Mamah inda nan take yaji wata muguwar tsanar Jawahir ta darsu a ranshi har yanaji kaman idan aka bashi wuka akace ya caka mata baze kara ko minti aya ba ze aikata lahira
Yana parking Mamah ta fice da sauri ta shige cikin gida ya biyota yana kiran ta amma tuni ta shige daki ta kulle kanta, nan kasa ta zauna tana kuka me tsuma zuciyar me sauraro, gaba-daya ta rasa meke mata dadi, ta rasa wani laifi tayi Jawahir ke hukunta ta haka, shin bin umarnin iyaye da tayi ta auri Osama laifi ne?, koko laifi ne ka haifi yaro ka tsawata mishi?, wani irin kiyayya Jawahir ke mata haka?, babu irin tunanin da batayi ba
A yau Mamah tayi kukan maraici na rashin uwa da uba da zasu share mata hawaye wanda koda akace mata iyayenta sun rasu batayi kuka irin shi ba, tayi kukan bakin ciki da kuma dana sanin beyewa Osama da tayi tun farko wurin tarbiyar tar da Jawahir, babu abinda ke mata yawo a kwakwalwa se kalaman da Jawahir ta jefe ta dasu wato "useless mother", meya kai 'yar cikinka tace ma useless, ai babu bakin cikin da yakai wannan, nan Mamah ta kwanta kan rug din dakin tanaci gaba da kuka inda take dafe kirji saboda tsananin zafin da yake mata
Ga Farida na shirin yin maganin Jawahir, shin kuna ganin zata samu mafita wurin da zataje, ya zasu kaya da Jawahir?
Wannan rashin kunyar da Jawahir tayi wa Mamah kuna ganin Mamah zata dau mataki akai, ko ko zata kyaleta taci bulus kenan?

UWA TA GARI - 15 - Page 3 - Wattpad
A mota ba irin maganar da Jarood da Rumana basuwa Jawahir ba amma ta sharesu se share hawayenta takeyi da hannu, babu irin tambayar da basu mata ba, ganin ba amsa musu zatayi ba suka kyaleta kowa yaci gaba da harkar gabanshi, a kofar gidansu Rumana yayi parking Rumana ta fito tareda yi mishi sallama sannan ta kalli Jawahir tace "a rayuwa komai dan sannu ne, kibi komai a hankali Jawahir, ki daina cusawa zuciyarki tsana ta ba gaira ba dalili", tana gama fadin haka tayi shigewarta gida dan haushi Jawahir din ta bata, Jarood be tanka musu ba dan inda sabo ya saba ganin fadan Jawahir da Rumana, dan haka yaja motar yayi gaba
Maimakon ya kai Jawahir gida se yayi hanyar gidansu da ita, horn yayi aka bude mai ya shiga yayi parking sannan ya fito ya zagaya ya bude mata itama ta fito, bata damu da tambayar shi inda ya kowa ta ba ko meyasa ya kowa ta nan din ba, rike hannunta yayi ya fara tafiya tana binshi tamkar raumi da akala, koda ya shige cikin gida parlourn tsit ba kowa, be tsaya nan ba ya jata har bedroom dinshi ya bari ta zauna kan gado sannan ya bude fridge din da ke cikin dakin ya dauko mata ruwa ya mika mata
Ba musu ta amsa ta kai baki, seda ta kusa shanye wa sannan ta ajiye tana maida numfashi, zama yayi kan kujerar dake facing din gadon ya zubawa Jawahir ido yana jira yaji me zatace amma ta mishi shiru, ganin shirun yayi yawa yace "Jawahir yimin magana mana, fada min what happened, meyasaki kuka haka?", share wasu hawayen tayi sannan tace "Jarood I'm a bad girl, I hate my life, my life has no meaning, bansan meyasa nakeyiwa Mamah irin wannan kiyayyar ba, tinda nake yarinya batada burin da ya wuce ta faranta min rai amma ni ta bangarena ba haka bane, kullum cikin bakanta mata rai nakeyi kaman wacce akawa baki, most of the time sena mata ba daidai ba nake dana sani", kara share kwallan ta tayi sannan ta kalleshi tace "what is wrong with me Jarood?"
Ajiyar zuciya Jarood ya sauke yana girgiza kai danshi besan me zaice mata ba, gaba-daya tayi complicating rayuwarta da kanta, dagowa yayi ya kalleta sannan yace "Jawahir you might not like what I'm going to say now amma inaso ki sani gaskiyar magana zan fada miki", kallonshi tayi yace gaba da cewa "ba kowa ne ya maida rayuwarki haka ba illa mahaifinki, shine ya cusawa zuciyarki tsanar majaifiyarki ba tareda kin sani ba, if not kiyi tunani ki gani, shi kadai ne me goya miki baya koda kinyi ba daidai ba, shine wanda koda wasa be taba tsawata miki ba unlike Mamah da idan kikayi laifi nan take zata nuna miki rashin dacewar abinda kikayi inda ke kuma gaskiya ce bakyaso shi yasa kike ganin bakinta koda yaushe"
Shiru tayi tana nazarin kalaman Jarood amma ko kadan ta kasa bawa Dada fault, ita a ganinta komai yake faruwa laifin Mamah ce tinda itace bata tashi tsaye ba a lokacin da ya dace ace ta tashi ta tsayawa kanta da family dinta dan haka her Dada is not to be blamed
Kallon Jarood tayi tana dafe kai sannan tace "I want to forget all this, inaso na manta da komai koda na lokaci alilan ne amma I don't know how", murmushi Jarood yayi sannan ya mike ya nufi drawer din gefen gadonshi ya dauko mata wani tablet cikin sachet dinshi ya mika mata yana cewa "duk sanda kikaga kinaso ki manta da damuwar ki just take one of this, zaki manta da komai, it helps a lot", kallon maganin da ke hannunta tayi sannan tayi murmushin tace "thanks for caring, u are like a brother I never have", zama yayi kusa da ita yana riko hannunta yace "anything for you Jawahir, anything", wani murmushin ta sake tana kwanciya kan kafadarshi shi kuma yana bubbuga mata baya to calm her down, bame magana cikinsu kowa ya lula nashi duniyar tunanin
Farida da kawayenta sunyi nasarar samun malamanin da sukaje wurinshi wanda suke kira da Baba, idan ka ganshi baza kace yana aikin malanta ba dan zaure nema dashi yana karantar da alibai, a nan zauren suka zauna kan tabarma kasancewar aliban sun tashi daga karatu, gaida shi sukayi ya amsa musu fuskarshi dauke da annuri yace "kaman Farida nake gani", ta sunkuyar da kai tana cewa "eh Baba nice", yace "Masha Allah da fatan dai komai lafiya", Farida zatayi magana Nafi tayi saurin cewa "Baba lafiya ba lafiya ba", ya juyo gareta yace "toh meke faruwa?", Nafisa ta gyara zama da kyau sannan tace "Baba kamar dai yadda ka sani kwanakin baya munzo wurinka akan munaso a mana istikhara akan auren Farida da Osama kuma kace mana da alkhairi sosai a ciki, yanzu kuma gashi aure tun ba'aje ko ina ba an fara samun matsala saboda shi Osaman yanada wata yarinya wacce tsohuwar matarshi ta haifa mai, yarinyar nan batada kunya ko na rabin cokali gashi shikuma ya dau son duniya ya daurawa yarinyar har yana zagin aminiyar mu akan ta", daga Farida har Zulaika kallon Nafi sukayi ganin yadda ta shararo karya, Baba ya gyada kai yace "yanzu dai a takaice kunaso ita yarinyar ta shiga taitaiyin ta kenan ko me??", Nafi ce taci gaba da cewa "Baba so muke wannan yarinyar ta dinga bawa kawarmu respect, kuma duk abinda aka sata tayi zatayi ba tareda wani musu ba, sannan shi kuma Osama wannan son da yake yiwa 'yar tashi ya koma kan Farida" murmushi Baba yace yace "wannan duka ba wani matsala bace, ita yarinyar me sunanta", a hankali Farida tace "Jawahir", yace "shikenan ina zuwa, sannan ya mike ya shige gida
Yana shiga ciki Farida ta kalli Nafisa tace "Nafi ina kika samo wannan labarin da kika fadawa Baba", hararar ta Nafi tayi sannan tace "ke yanzu ban taimaka miki ba, soyayyar da Osama ke yiwa Jawahir ze dawo kanki", Zulaika tace "hakane Bestie, kawai a bar maganan tunda aikin gama ya riga ya gama", duk shiru sukayi suna jiran fitowar Baba, be dade sosai ba ya fito hannunshi rike da kullin magani guda biyu ya zauna sannan yace "wannan turaren wuta ne ki tabbata kin turara gidan lokacin da ita Jawahir din ke gida sannan kuma wannan ki dafawa Osama shayi dashi, sauran aikin koma ki barshi a hannu na", karba tayi sannan tace "amma Baba shi Osaman baya gari kuma se yayi wata biyu sannan ze dawo", murmushi yayi sannan yace "wannan duk ba matsala bace, yau da daddare zan miki aiki Inshallah, idan dai addu'an mu ta karbu keda kanki zakiga canji ko kafin ya dawo, amma idan ya dawo ki tabbata yasha shayin da wannan maganin", da "toh" ta amsa mishi sannan ta bue jaka ta ajiye mishi kudi masu dan yawa suka mishi godiya sannan suka mishi sallama suka wuce
A mota se tayata murna sukeyi wai yanzu ne zataji dadin aure inda ita kuwa tunani kawai takeyi dan bataso tayi abinda nan gaba zatayi dana sani, ganin kaman tana wasuwasi yasa Nafisa taci gaba da zugata har Farida ta fara ganin gwara kawai tayi abinda Baba yace duk abinda ze faru ya faru, koda suka koma gida ita bata shiga ba, a nan waje ta musu sallama sannan ta dauki tata motar ya wuce gida
Shida da en mintuna ta kai gida, jin gidan kaman ba kowa ta fara leke leke ko zataga Jawahir amma ba Jawahir ba labarin ta, ko ba'a fada mata ba tasan fita tayi dan haka ta wuce dakinta inda tayi wanka ta canza kaya sannan ta fito ta shige kitchen dan ta girka abinda zasuci
Farida ta kai karfe goma tana jiran dawowar Jawahir wacce ba ita ta shigo ba se sha dayan dare, a gajiye ta shigo gida, tana ganin Farida tace "sannu", sannan tayi hanyar dakin ta, da sauri Farida tace "dakata Jawahir daga ina kike?", juyowa Jawahir tayi ta kalleta tace "ina ruwanki da inda na fito, naga da zaki fita dazu ban tsaya tambayarki inda zaki ba toh ke yanzu me na tambaya ta inda na fito", wani kululun bakin ciki ne ya tokare Farida a makoshi, Jawahir bata koma kulata ba tayi wucewarta daki tana mitan ana shiga rayuwarta dayawa, Farida ma dakin ta ta wuce tana cewa "zanyi maganinki yarinya, se inga bakin rashin kunyar banza kawai"
Jawahir wanka tayi tasa kayan baccin ta sannan tazo ta kwanta dan so take tayi bacci saboda ta gaji amma ta kasa, banda tunanin Mamah ba abinda ta keyi, juyi kawai takeyi a kan gado tana jan tsaki, ganin baccin ba zuwa zeyi ba ta tashi zaune ta dauko laptop dinta ta kunna, movies dinta ta shiga inda tayi selecting 'Honey 3 dare to dance' ta fara kallo wai ko in tana cikin kallo bacci ya dauketa amma ina, har aka gama ba bacci ba alamun shi kuma ba abinda ta gane a Film din dan gaba-daya ma hankalinta baya kai, kashe laptop din tayi ta ajiye gefe
Tunawa tayi da maganin da Jarood ya bata ta mike ta bude jakarta ta ciro shi, zama tayi tana kallon maganin tana tunani, girgiza kai tayi ta ajiyeshi gefe tana cewa "no, I don't want to be addicted to this", nan take zuciyarta tace mata "ai it's just for today kawai", girgiza kai tayi tana contemplating tasha ko kar tasha, ta kai 10munites kafin tayi making up mind dinta ta balla daya tasa baki sannan ta fita ta nufi kitchen inda ta dau ruwa ta kora maganin sannan ta dawo daki ta kwanta
Ba'ayi minti biyu ba ta fara jinta tana yawo a sararin samaniya inda idanuwanta suka mata nauyi suna kokarin rufewa tana kokarin bude su dan kuwa maganin ya mata karfi, batayi minti biyar ba wani nannauyar bacci ya dauke ta irin wanda ko motsi mutum baya iya yi
Mamah tayi kuka har ta gode Allah, ganin kukan baze amfane ta da komai ba sema ciwon kai dayake kokarin sa mata yasa ta tashi ta cire kayan jikinta sannan ta shige bathroom dinta, wanka tayi tayi alwallah ta fito, dogon riga tasa sannan ya shimfida sallaya tasa hijab ta zauna tareda dauko Al Qur'ani ta fara karanta dan ta samu nutsuwa a zuciyarta
Ko nan da chan Najib ya kasa motsawa yana nan zaune a parlour yana jiran fitowar ta har akayi magrib sannan ya tashi ya wuce masallaci, ana idar da sallah ya sake dawowa ya zauna har lokacin bata fito ba, Baba Salamatu dake zaune tin dazu itama tana jiran fitowar Mamah tace "Najib kaje ka huta kaga gobe seka dawo, kafin nan itama ta warware", shiru yayi mata dan baya ganin ze iya tafiya ya bar Mamah a wannan halin
A haka aka sake kiran isha ya sake fita yayi sallah ya dawo, zaman shi da en mintuna Mamah ta fito kaman babu abinda ya faru da ita, murmushi tayi ganin Najib zaune tace "son baka tafi gida ba?", dagowa yayi ya kalleta da kyau ya tabbata ta warware sannan yace "yanzu nakeda niyar tafiya", Baba Salamatu dake addu'a a inda tayi sallah ta shafa sannan tace "wannan yaron beda niyyar tafiya, ba yanda banyi dashi ba akan ya tafi gobe ya dawo amma ya kiya", zama Mamah tayi kusa dashi tace "Najib ina matukar alfahari dakai kasancewar ka dana duk da bani na tsugunna na haife ka ba amma nasan koni ce na haife ka iya abinda zakamin kenan", riko hannuwanta yayi yace "Anty na kinsan duk duniya bayan mahaifiya ta kece next person da nake matukar so da darajawa, dan Allah Anty na ki dena shiga rayuwar Jawahir tunda ta nuna bataso ko dan gudun bacin ran ki, idan kinaso kiji dumin yaranki a jikinki ki kirani ko ki kira Reena zamuzo"
Murmushi tayi tana shafa kanshi tace "Allah ya maka albarka, kuma Inshallah zanyi yadda kace", shima murmushin yayi sannan yace "dama akwai abinda nakeso na fada miki wanda naketa kwankwanto a kai, amma ganin abinda ya faru yau naga bazan iya barinki haka ba", kallon shi tayi tace "Najib fadi inji", kanshi kasa yace "promise me zakiyi duk abinda nace", tace "indai befi karfi na ba", yace "Inshallah baze ma fi karfin ki ba", "ina jin ka", tace dashi ya gyara zama sannan yace "Anty na dan Allah kiyi aure, idan kikayi aure zaki rage damuwa sosai", murmushi tayi tace "Najib kenan, ni kaina inaso nayi auren amma mazajen da ke zuwa wurina ne duk babu wanda ya kwanta min a rai har yanzu", shiru yayi na en dakiku sannan yace "idan na zaba miki miji zaki aure shi?", ba tareda dogon tunani ba tace "indai ya kwanta min", yayi murmushi sannan yace "shi kenan Anty na, Allah ya bamu alheri", ta amsa da "ameen" sannan ya tashi ya musu sallama ya fice, Baba Salamatu dake zaune tana jinsu tace "Najib akwai hankali da kaifin tunani", murmushi kawai Mamah tayi tana tunanin wani irin miji Najib ze samo mata
Washegari Farida ta tashi, kota kan Jawahir bata bi ba tayi aikinta tayi breakfast taci abinta sannan ta koma daki ta kwanta danta huta, har sha biyun rana Jawahir bata tashi ba, kiran sallar azahar ne ya tashi Farida ta tashi tayi sallah, jin har yanzu da alama Jawahir bata fito ba ta nufi hanyar dakin Jawahir, kwankwasa kofar tayi amma shiru, da sallama ta shiga dakin taga Jawahir kwance tayi rashe rashe kan gado tana bacci without any care in the world, mamaki ne ya kama Farida dan tasan Jawahir bata kaiwa wannan lokacin bata tashi ba, karasawa cikin dakin tayi ta fara bubbuga bayan Jawahir tana cewa "ke Jawahir, Jawahir, tashi mana, ke bakiga rana tayi bane", juyi Jawahir tayi taci gaba da baccinta Farida ta tsaya tana kallon ikon Allah dan ta tabbata wannan baccin da Jawahir keyi bana lafiya bane, kara gwada tashin ta tayi amma duk a banza, dan haka ta sadaukar ta fice abinta tana mamakin yaushe kuma Jawahir ta dauko wannan sabon halin nata
Jawahir ba ita ta tashi se la'asar, sakayau ta jita bata da sauran damuwa sema jinta da tayi kaman she's born again dan duk abinda ya faru tsakaninta da Mamah tuni tayi watsi dashi gefe, mika tayi sannan ta mike ta nufi hanyar bathroom ba sallah bare salati, sosai ta bata lokaci tana wanka, seda ta gama gyara jikinta sannan tayi alwallah ta fito, kaya tasa ta shimfida sallaya ta tada sallahn asuba, tana idarwa ta ora da azahar sannan tayi la'asar ta mike ta nannade sallayarta ta fice dan ta nemawa kanta abinda zata ci saboda ji take kaman an yashe mata kayan ciki tsabar yunwa
A kitchen taci karo da Farida dake gyara kayan miya, fridge ta bude tana cewa "ina wuni Anty", ba tareda da Farida ta juyo ba tace "se yanzu kika tashi Jawahir, kin duba lokaci kuwa?", rufe fridge din Jawahir tayi bayan ta dauki abinda take bukata sannan tace "uhmm", kawai ta fita abinta, da kallo Farida ta bita tana girgiza kai a zuciyarta tace "zanyi maganinki ne", Jawahir zama tayi kan gadonta ta dauko slice bread dinta ta shafa mishi nutella sannan ta dauki wayarta ta dannawa Jarood kira, ringing biyu ya daga tareda cewa "Jawahir ya akayi?", fuskarta dauke da wani irin annuri na jin dadi tace "Jarood thank you soo much, kai kaga yadda nayi bacci kamar wacce batada damuwa a duniyar nan kuma na tashi na jini yanda nakeso, yanzu haka jin kaina nake kaman wata babyn da batasan me damuwa a rayuwa ba", ta bangaren Jarood wani makarin murmushi yayi yace "Allah Jawahir", tace "Allah kuwa", yace "ai idan dai zakiyi trusting dina I will introduce you to a life you never expect, rayuwar da zaki zama boss din kanki without care babu wanda ya isa ya takaki kaman dai irin rayuwar da kikeso", tace "shine tuntuni baka sani a hanya ba", yayi murmushi yace "bazaki gane bane, You are still a baby amma tinda yanzu you are ready ba matsala, hope zaki samu fitowa yau", shiru ta danyi tana tunani sannan tace "yau inaso in huta, amma Inshallah gobe zamu hadu", ada kai yayi kaman tana kallonshi yace "shikenan, see ya", sannan ya kashe wayan ita kuma taci gaba da cin abinta tana tunani wani irin rayuwa ne wannan da Jarood ze nuna mata

UWA TA GARI - 16 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Farida ce zaune a parlour tana tunani tinda yau Jawahir na gida ta ina zata fara, dan so take tayi duk abinda zatayi ta gama ba tareda Jawahir tayi suspect wani abu ba, tashi tayi ta leka dakin Jawahir inda ta hango ta zaune kan gado tana waya da Jarood, ganin haka yasata barin wurin ta koma dakinta, inda ta ajiye maganin da ta boye taje ta dauko sannan ta dawo parlour
Burner ta kunna tasa turaren da Baba ya bata sannan ta koma kitchen da saurinta taci gaba da aikinta tana murmushi dan ta tabbata warin turaren seyaje har dakin Jawahir dan ita kanta da take kitchen yana damunta saboda beda wani kamshi me dadi
Jawahir data gama waya tana tunani taji wani irin kamshi mara dadi na ziyartar ta, nan da nan ta toshe hanci tareda mikewa ta fice, zuwa tayi ta cire burner din daga jikin wuta kanta na mugun sara mata sannan ta karasa kitchen rike da kai da hannu bibbiyu, a bakin kofa ta tsaya tace "wannan wani irin turare ne kikasawa mutane haka se kace turaren en bori?", Farida ta tsorata da jin muryar Jawahir amma seta hade fuska ta juyo tana kallon yanayin Jawahir din tace "turaren tsari ne nasa saboda na lura shedanu sunyi yawa a gidan nan, ko kinada matsala da wannan ne", hararar ta Jawahir tayi tace "ai kuwa dai da shedanu a gidan nan tinda ga daya nan tsaye a gabana", sosai Farida taji zafin maganar da Jawahir ta mata, taso ta maida mata da magana amma seta shareta tareda juyawa taci gaba da aikinta dan tafiso tabi komai a sannu
Jawahir ganin Farida bata kulata ba seta ja tsaki sannan ta fice, wurin show glass dinda aka ajiye kayan turare taje ta dauki air freshener ta fara bin lungu da sako na gidan tana fesawa, seda ta karar da gwangwani daya sannan hankalinta ya kwanta ta ajiye gwangwanin ta koma daki abinta
Ranar rasa sukuni tayi dan kanta ne ya matsa mata da ciwo, duk tabi ta gagara yin komai tsabar ciwon kai, ganin abin ba sauki ta dauki paracetamol biyu tasha ta nemi wuri ta kwanta duk da taga yamma tayi
Washegari
Jawahir taji sauki, dan haka tana tashi ta wuce bathroom tayi wanka sannan tayi alwallah ta fito, shiryawa tayi sannan tayi sallah, tana idarwa ta tashi ta fice dan nemawa kanta abinda zataci, a kitchen taci karo da Farida wacce ke juye ruwan zafi a flask, haka kawai taji tanaso ta taimaka mata dan haka tace "ina kwana Anty", kallon Jawahir Farida tayi sannan tayi murmushi dan taga alama aikinta ya fara ci dan Jawahir bata taa gaishe ta da murmushi kwance a fuskarta ba, most of the time ma idan zata gaishe ta bata ko kallon inda take, itama amsa wa tayi da "lafiya lau Jawahir, kin tashi lafiya?", tace "lafiya", sannan ta karasa cikin kitchen din tana cewa "akwai abinda zan tayaki dashi?", mamaki ne ya kama Farida ta kalli Jawahir da kyau dan tabbatarwa kanta ita tayi maganar sannan ta girgiza kai tace "for now no, amma anjima by 12pm ki fito mu hada lunch tare", da "toh" Jawahir ta amsa mata sannan ta dauki plate ta zuba chips din da taga Farida ta soya ta hada tea ta fice ba tareda ta kuma cewa komai ba
Mamaki gaba-daya ya hana Farida yin kwakwaran motsi, wai yau itace Jawahir kewa magana haka cikin saukin kai da ladabi, lallai da taimakon Baba Jawahir zata dawo a tafin hannunta amma zatayi kokari tabi komai sannu a hankali ba tareda ta nuna maitarta na son ganin Jawahir ta shiga hankalinta a fili ba
Da wannan tunanin ta karasa aikinta sannan itama ta dauki abincinta taje kan dinning ta zauna tana tunanin Osama dan tinda ya tafi ya kira yace ya sauka lafiya be kuma kira ba
Sabreena ce zaune a dakin tana chatting da Najib, banda murmushi ba abinda takeyi saboda ya fada mata yayiwa Mamah magana kuma tace idan har ya zabo mata miji kuma ya kwanta mata zata aureshi wanda su kuma sun tabbata idan mahaifin Sabreena yaje ya nemi auren Mamah zata yarda, dan haka ta mishi alkawarin itama yau zata wa Abba magana kuma tasan he won't say no dan ta tabbata yanason Mamah kawai dai besan yadda zeyi ya tunkare ta bane
Se yamma Abba ya dawo daga wurin aiki a gajiye, Sabreena dake zaune parlour tana kallo ta taso da saurinta jin sallamar shi, "Abba sannu da dawowa", ya zauna yana janyo hannunta ta zauna kusa dashi yace "yauwa Sabreena ya gida, ya zaman kadaici?", ta marairaice fuska tace "wallahi Abba zaman kadaici kam akwai shi", murmushi yayi sannan yace "don't worry kin kusa komawa school dan dazu aka kirani akace min admission dinki ya fito and guess what?", cike da zumudi tace "na samu admission", yayi murmushi yana shafa kanta yace "Yes my daughter, kin samu admission, zaki karanci insurance", da murnar ta tace "ai Abba kome suka bani I'm ok with it Allah yasa in shiga a sa'a", ya amsa da "ameen" sannan ya mike yana cewa "bari na dan watsa ruwa in zo", tace "toh Abba, when you are done I want to discuss something with you", yace "ok dear", sannan yayi hanyar dakin shi ya barta zaune
Be dau lokaci sosai ba ya dawo parlour, ta kawo mishi abinci da ruwa, tare suka zauna sukaci, seda suka gama ta tattare ko ina sannan ta dawo ta zauna ya kalleta da murmushi yace "ya dai, me labari", dariya ya bata tace "kai Abba irin wannan kashe murya haka se kace wanda yake zance", shima dariyar yayi yace "toh ya na iya, tinda babu wacce zanje zance wurinta kinga ai se muyi a gida ko ba haka ba", ta girgiza kai tana dariya tareda kara jin son mahaifinta a ranta dan Allah yayi shi mutum me mugun saukin kai
Gyara zama tayi ta fuskance shi sosai sannan tace "Abba", ganin yadda tayi serious shima seya koma serious mood ya kalleta yace "what is it Sabreena, tell me", seda tayi kasa da kai sannan tace "Abba i want you to get married", da saurinshi ya girgiza kai tareda cewa "no", ta marairaice tace "dan Allah Abba kayi tunani, kaga na samu admission yanzu, there won't be anyone to take care of you, kuma nima inaso nasan mother's love, I want to have someone I can share my worries with, someone that can advice me when the need arise", riko hannunta yayi yace "I'm I not enough, Sabreena I've always been there for you, idan kina bukatar shawara ina baki, ina kula dake daidai gwargwado, me nake lacking? tell me saboda insan yadda zan magance matsalan", girgiza kai tayi tace "no Abba, kana kokari sosai and I'm grateful for that amma a matsayina na 'ya mace akwai abubuwan da bazan iya fada maka ba saboda kunya, akwai abubuwan da kona fada maka babu abinda zaka iya yi, Please Abba let's make our family complete, I need a mummy and you need a wife, so why not just get married again", kallonta yayi ganin kwalla na neman ya cika mata ido yace "don't cry sweetheart, ni kaina inason kara auren nan amma ina tsoron in auro wacce zatazo tayi destroying happiness din da muke sharing, I'm happy seeing you happy, so why do you want me to bring in someone that will destroy this happiness that we share?", goge hawayen ta tayi tace "Abba wallahi wacce nakeso ka aura is not a home destroyer, infact we will all be one big happy family, Abba baka ganta ba, she's gentle and beautiful please Abba think about it", with amusement yake kallonta yace "harkin zabamin mata kenan", ta ada kai yace "won't you allow me to choose my choice tinda kin fiso kiga na kara aure", tace "Abba i know she's your choice, I saw the way you looked at her sanda ka ganta", da mamaki ya nuna kanshi yace "ni", tace "yes", yace "wow, wacece toh, dan naga da alama na santa", tayi murmushi dan tasan ta kusa cin nasara tace "Anty ce", da mamaki yace "Anty kuma", tace "eh, my new Anty, wacce ta dauke ni daga airport har ka ban gift in kai mata last two wee
", bata karasa yace "oh oh Hindu", tace "eh ita", yayi 'yar dariya yana kallon Sabreena yace "you this girl what will I do without you", dariya tayi tana rufe fuskarta da tafin hannunta tace "so, do you need her contact number", ya kalli Sabreena with admiration dan komai tayi tana tuno mishi da matarshi yace "no", da sauri ta dago tana bata rai tace "Abbaaaaa", yayi dariya sannan yace "inaso in karbi number dinta directly ne, so you should tell her she's having a visitor tomorrow by 4pm", tsalle Sabreena tayi tareda rungume Abbanta tana cewa "Thank you, thank you, thank you sooo much Abba na, I promise you won't regret this", shima murmushi yayi bece komai ba Sabreena ta mike tareda daukan wayanta ta shige dakin dan ta kira Najib ta fada mishi yadda sukayi da Abban ta
Zama tayi kan gadonta sannan ta fara kiran Najib, lokacin da ta kirashi yana alwallah dan haka be daga ba seda ya gama sannan ya kirata, ringing daya ta dauka tareda cewa "Ya Najib guess what?", murmushi yayi dan ko bata fada mishi yasan tayi nasara dan haka yace "Abban ki ya amince", tace "yes" tareda bashi labarin yanda sukayi dashi, shima yaji dadi sosai yace "shikenan zan kira Anty na yanzu in fada mata bakonta zezo gobe", tace "i just can't wait", basu wani yi dogon hira ba sukayi sallama, seda yaje masallaci ya dawo sannan ya shiga kiran Mamah a waya, dauka tayi tareda cewa "Najib ya akayi, kodai yunwa kakeji", dariya yayi yace "shikenan Anty nikuma bazan iya kiran ki ba se idan ina jin yunwa", tace "toh na sani, ai naga kai baka wasa da abinci ne", dariya yayi yace "toh ba dalilin kiran kenan ba, na kira ne na fada miki gobe bakon ki zezo ku gana", seda taji faduwar gaba tace "Najib wai dama da gaske kake?", yace "eh mana Anty na, bafa wasa nakeyi ba, and mun riga mun yi magana dashi, gobe zezo by 4pm", ajiyar zuciya tayi sannan tace "shikenan Najib Allah ya kaimu goben", yace "ameen", sannan ta kara da cewa "amma fa banyi promise dinka komai ba so don't keep your hopes high, idan be mun ba bazan matsawa kaina ba", murmushi yayi sannan yace "nasan ze miki ne, and pls Anty na ki bashi chance ne, ku fara sanin juna kafin ki yanke hukunci, date him for like a month haka, kinga you will be able to make a wise decision, stop judging people by first impression", dariya tayi tace "zan gwada, I will try, but always know that first impression matters", shima dariyan ya mata sannan ya mata sallama ya ajiye wayar tareda kwanciya kan gado yana cewa "Allah yasa ki amince Anty na, kodan ki samu farin ciki a rayuwarki"
Ta bangaren Jawahir kuwa a ranan samun kanta tayi dayin duk wani abunda Farida ta sata ba tareda musu ba, tare sukayi girki duk da Jawahir ba girkin ta iya ba sedai ta dauko wannan ta dauko wancan, yayinda suna gamawa Farida tace tayi wanke wanke ta gyara kitchen din
Jawahir tayi abinda aka sata daidai gwargwado yanda zata iya sannan ta koma daki ta sake wanka ta shirya ta fito, for the first time ta dauki kafanta taje har dakin Farida wacce ke kwance tana chatting da kawayenta, juyowa tayi dan ba karamin mamaki tayi ba ganin Jawahir, murmushi Jawahir tayi tace "Anty zan dan fita unguwa in dawo", bata hanata ba tace "shikenan amma karkiyi dare", tace "toh" sannan ta fice ba tareda tunanin komai ba
Fitowan ta yayi daidai da zuwan Jarood dan dama sunyi waya zezo ya dauke ta, shiga motar tayi shi kuma yaja ta kalleshi tace "se ina yanzu", yayi murmushi yace "you will see", kallon agogo tayi tace "bansan inyi dare ne that's why I'm asking", kallonta yayi da mamaki sannan ya maida hankalinshi kan titi yace "you don't sound like the Jawahir I know, yaushe kika canza da har bakyaso kiyi dare a waje, unbelievable", itama kallonshi tayi tace "yea it's strange, nima haka kawai naji ni yau da son aikata duk wani abu da Anty Farida ta sani, kuma tace kar nayi dare, ina tsoron tsallake maganar ta", kiiii Jarood ya taka wani wawan birki ya juyo yana kallon Jawahir dake kallonshi a tsorace saboda ganin yadda ya taka brake, horn din da ake musu a baya yasashi komawa gefen titi yayi parking sannan ya kalli Jawahir yace "when did this start?", tace "what", a tsawace yace "tin yaushe kika fara jin son aikata duk abinda matar mahaifinki ta saki ba tareda musu ko wani abu ba", tace "it started today", chan kasan makoshi yace "this woman will destroy my plans, I need to do something fast", Jawahir tace "me kace", ya juyo da fake smile a fuskarshi yace "Jawahir don't let that woman use you, daga yau idan ta saki abu kice bazakiyi ba, if not zata maida ke baiwa a gidan mahaifinki, and again inda zamu yau dole ne muyi dare, kila har kwana ma zamuyi dan haka karkisa ran komawa gida any time soon", shiru tayi dan batasan me zatace ba, gaskiya Jarood ke fada ko kuwa ba haka bane?, zata iya kin bin maganar Farida kuwa? haka tayi ta tunani ita kadai tana tambayar kanta questions din da basu da amsa yayinda Jarood ya maida hankalinshi kan titi yaci gaba da driving yana tunani wani step ya kamata ya auka yanzu, ya riga ya bari ta saba da zuwa party, ya bata pills ta karba har tayi amfani dashi but she's not addicted yet, he can't introduce her to another thing so soon idan ba haka ba zata iya sillewa daga hannunshi, so yake Jawahir ta dinga bin duk wata hanya daze dorata akai saboda duk sanda ya nemi aikata kudirin shi a kanta ta bada hadin kai ba tareda ta musa mishi ba

Tana karasowa inda yake tsaye yana jiranta ya kamo hannunta suka karasa cikin gidan, tin daga compound din ta fara shakkar shiga dan en mata ne iri iri da mazaje a wurin, kowa da abinda ya keyi na Allah ya wadar, a haka suka karasa parlourn gidan inda taga mutane zaune daga masu shan shigari, se masu shan shisha, giya, wiwi, kayan maye dai babu irin wanda babu a wurin, ga wani irin kidi dake tashi daga speakers din da ke parlourn

", be bari ta karasa ba ya sake cewa "i said get the hell out of my car this minute and don't let me repeat myself", ganin ranshi a matukar bace yake yasata fita jiki a sanyaye dan tunda take bata taa ganin bacin ran Jarood irin wannan ba, tin bata gama rufe mishi motar ba yaja abinshi yayi gaba tabishi da kallo har sai da ya bacewa ganinta, nan take taji bata kyauta mishi ba dan da tasan ranshi ze aci da batace mishi zata tafi ba, ganin tsayuwar nata ba abinda ze kara mata taja er tsirarun kafafuwanta ta shige gida

Kuka ta fashe dashi tana kiran sunayen Allah tareda duk wani addu'a da yazo bakinta, tabbas wannan mafarkin ba komai bane fac wani ishara da Allah ke son ya nuna mata, batayi kasa a gwiwa ba ta tashi ta dauro alwallah tazo ta tada salla tana rokawa Jawahir gafara da kuma kariya daga wurin ubangiji mai kowa mai komai

Yau Farida da tsananin farin ciki ta tashi dan kuwa daren jiya raba dare tayi suna waya da Osama, ta gama shirin ta na bacci zata kwanta taji ringing din wayarta, koda ta duba taga Osama ne se abun ya bata mamaki dan batayi tunani ma ze kira ba, daukan wayar tayi a tunaninta gaisawa kawai zasuyi ya tambayi lafiyarsu sannan ya mata sallama amma ga mamakin ta seya bige da hira wanda bata taa sanin cewar yana hira har haka ba, wannan dalilin yasa takeji kaman duk duniya ba wanda ya kaita farin ciki a yau dan kuwa a yanzu batada wata matsala a tattare da ita
Bata damu kanta da takurawa Jawahir ba tinda tasan ba wani aiki bane a gidan, da kanta ta shiga kitchen tayi breakfast taci ta ajiyewa Jawahir nata sannan taje tayi wanka ta shirya ta fice kota kan Jawahir bata bi ba saboda ta je ta bawa su Zulaika labari
Jawahir tun tashinta ta kasa yin komai saboda jikinta duk a mace yake, ta kira Jarood yafi a kirga amma yaki ya daga waya, tashin ta kuma taci gaba da kiranshi taji wayar a kashe, take taji komai ya fita ranta dan haka tayi kwanciyarta a daki duk da dai ba barci takeji ba, sedai bata ganin koh nan da chan zata iya zuwa saboda Jarood na fushi da ita
Kafin 4pm Mamah ta gama abinda zatayi ta shirya cikin bakar jallabiya tana jiran isowar bakonta, 4:30pm Harun (Abba) ya iso, Mamah najin horn dinshi tayi sauri taje ta yafa babban gyale sannan ta fito dan tarban shi, sanin cewar baze shigo ba harse an bashi izini yasata fita compound din gidan inda ta hangoshi zaune cikin mota

Yasha sosai sannan ya ajiye sauran yana cewa "kaman kuwa kin san na kwaso kishi", murmushi kawai tayi kanta a kasa tace "sannu da zuwa, ya hanya?", yace "hanya alhmdllh, na sameki lafiya?", tace "lafiya lau", daga nan kuma se wurin ya dauki shiru bame magana
Ya dauki tsawon lokaci sannan ya gyara zama yace "Hindu nasan dai mu yanzu ba yara bane da zamu tsaya batawa kanmu lokaci, mun wuce wannan stage din, ko ban fito na fada ba kinsan abinda ya kawo ni amma kuma gwara dai kiji daga bakina, inna gamsar dake falillahil hamd, idan kuma baki gamsu da abinda zan fada miki ba seki bari na sani", shiru tayi tana jinshi yaci gaba da cewa "wato Hindu shakera na sha takwas da aure wanda Allah besa munyi wata zama me tsayi da matar tawa ba sakamakon rasuwa da tayi wurin haihuwar Sabreena wacce ta zamo kamar 'ya a gurinki yanzu, tin daga wannan lokaci ban sake wani auren ba duk da inason yi din amma kuma ina tsoron auro wacce zata hanawa Sabreena kwanciyar hankali, sedai kuma tin ranar da nazo nan gidan daukar Sabreena na ganki duk wannan tunani ya gushe a kwakwalwata, a lokacin ne na tabbatar wa kaina tabbas na samu abokiyar rayuwa wacce zata kula dani ta kuma kular min da 'yata amma se na rasa ta hanyar da zan tunkare ki saboda gani nake kamar bazaki amince ba, a lokacin da na hadu dake nasa an min bincike a kanki inda na gano cewar aurenki mutuwa yayi kuma kina da 'ya daya wacce ke gurin mahaifinta a halin yanzu, labarin cewar bakya bawa manemanki fuska shi ya karasa karya min gwiwa naga bazan iya tunkarar ki da wannan zancen nason aurenki ba amma Allah cikin ikon sa seya turomin Sabreena inda ta sani gaba ita a lalle so take na kara aure, a lokacin da take min maganar kece mace ta farko da ta fado min a rai, kuma ga mamaki na itama Sabreena ke takeso na auro na kawo gida a matsayin mata, Sabreena ta taso ba tareda tasan me ake cewa mahaifiya ba dan kuwa bata taba zama da mahaifiyarta ba, nasan ke kadai ce wacce zata iya kawar wa Sabreena zafin rashin uwa da take fama dashi, zan baki lokaci kiyi tunani, inaso na aureki ne bawai saboda Sabreena kadai ba, sedan wannan bawa dake gaban ya kamu da sonki na tsakani da Allah", Mamah bata san sanda murmushi ya subce mata ba jin wai ya kamu da sonta

A ciki kowa harkan gabashin yakeyi kaman dai yadda tazo ta tarar dasu ranar farko, bata yarda ta bar kusa da Jarood ba, duk inda yasa kafa itama nan take sawa, yau wani wuri daban ya samu yaja kujera yace ta zauna sannan shima ya zauna, kallonshi tayi tace "bazaka shiga abokan ka ba?", yace "no, I'm here to keep you company, if you need anything let me know", kaa kai tayi tace "just get me a soft drink", murmushi yayi ya mike tayi saurin riko hannunshi ya juyo tace "don't poison my drink", murmushi kawai yayi ya fice ya barta zaune a wurin tana kallon yadda wadan nan bayin Allah ke watse wa da rayuwarsu without any care in the world, tana zaune ya dawo ya ajiye mata Chi exotic da cup shikuma ya bude kwalbar champagne dinda ke hannunshi ya soma sha, bata ce dashi komai ba ta tsiyaya drink dinta a cup ta soma sha, suna hira sama sama, ganin yana neman shanye champagne din tace "pls Jarood ya isa hakanan, don't get yourself drunk", kallonta yayi da murmushi yace "bakisan dadin da ke cikin abin nan bane, try it and see", da sauri ta girgiza kai tace "no, thank you", dage kafada yayi yaci gaba da shan kayanshi

Koda ta shiga gida zaune ta tarar da Farida a parlour tana jiran shigowar ta, sanin cewar tayi laifi na kin fada mata zatayi dare se duk jikinta yayi sanyi dan kuwa bataso tayi abinda ze batawa Farida rai, a hankali tace "Anty sannu da gida", kallon ta Farida tayi da harara tace "kema sannunki da dawowa gantalalliya", shiru Jawahir tayi tareda bata rai dan bataga dalilin da zesa ta kirata da gantalalliya ba, tinda itama Farida ai tana nata gantalin bawai batayi ba, ci gaba da tafiya tayi zata shige dakinta Farida tace "dawo ki fada min daga ina kike", seda Jawahir ta sauke ajiyar zuciya na takura sannan ta dawo tace "fita nayi da Jarood, kuma yanzu a gajiye nake dan haka duk maganan da zakiyi ki bari seda safe", tana fadar haka ta wuce ta bar Farida zaune tana mamakin hanya Jawahir ce wannan, dan ita a iya saninta kwana biyu kwata kwata Jawahir bata musa mata balle wata irin magana na rashin kunya ya shiga tsakani, a hankali tace "lallai aiki na nema ya koma baya", tashi ta ta wuce dakin ta tareda kudirin gobe zata koma wurin Baba dan muddin aikin nan ya lalace tasan Jawahir ba raga mata zatayi ba dan dama ba kunya ne da ita ba
WASHEGARI
Jawahir ba ita ta tashi ba se sha biyun rana, tayi mamakin yadda akayi Farida batazo ta tashe ba, seda tayi wanka ta gyara dakin ta kaman yadda ta saba sannan ta fita, koda ta shiga kitchen Farida ta riga tayi duka ayyukan ta sedai ba alaman ta ajiyewa Jawahir abinci, ba tareda wani dogon tunani ko damuwa ba Jawahir ta haawa kanta tea da bread ta dauka ta koma dakinta, tana cin abinci tana tunanin haduwar da zasuyi da Najib yau, "ko wani magana zamuyi?", ta tambayi kanta, ta dai san cewar da wuya Najib yace yana sonta dan haka batasa wannan a rai ba, kila dai wata magana daban ze mata, tana gama cin abinci ta maida cup din kitchen sannan ta leka dakin Farida danta gaisheta taga bata nan, tae baki tayi tace "ace kullum mutum se ya fita amma a haka ake cemin gantalalliya", tsaki taja sannan ta koma parlour ta kunna tv tayi zaman kallo tana jira ayi sallah sannan tayi shirin haduwa da Najib
Seda tayi sallahn azahar sannan ta dauko black jallabiya tasa, batayi makeup ba dan batada wannan time din a halin yanzu dan haka ta dan gyara fuskarta ta dauki pink veil ta yafa sannan ta dauki purse tasa kudi a ciki ta dauki wayanta ta fice, seda takai kofar fita sannan ta tuna batasa turare ba, da sauri ta dawo ta dauki turare tana sawa tace "aiko ban maka kwaliyya ba nasa turare ka dan ji kamshi", seda ta gama ta tabbatar komai yayi balance sannan ta fice
Restaurant din da yace su hadu taje, seda ta zauna sannan ta duba lokaci, ganin biyu saura minti biyar yasa ta gyara zama dan tasan duk yadda akayi yana hanyar zuwa, tafi arfin minti goma zaune tana jiranshi, duk waiter din da yazo wurinta seta daga mishi hannu alaman bata bukatar service dinsu for now, harta cire ran zezo se gashi ya shigo da dan saurinshi ya fara dube duben ta inda ze hango ta, koda ta ganshi bata nuna ta ganshi ba sema dauke kai da tayi harse da ya hango ta da kanshi ya karaso, zama yayi yace "sorry, hold up ne ya tsayar dani a hanya", daga mishi kai kawai tayi ita ala dole fushi takeyi, ganin reaction dinta seta bashi dariya amma gudun yayi dariya ta raina shi seya murmusa kawai sannan yace "baki yi order din komai ba?", ta kara daga kai, ya girgiza kai sannan ya juya yama waiter din alama da hannu, yana zuwa Najib yace "I will like to have jollof rice with grilled chicken and salad with a soft drink", kaa kai waiter din yayi sannan ya juya ga Jawahir ta kalleshi da murmushi a fuskarta tace "just get me soft drink, a chilled one precisely", nan ma kai ya sake kaa wa sannan ya bar wurin
Yana barin wurin Najib yace "meyasa bazakici abinci ba?", a hankali tace "a koshe nake", kallonta yayi yana mamakin yadda akayi ta zama haka so silent, unlike Jawahir din da ya sani me tsiwa, ganin yayi shiru tace "kace zamuyi magana", ya gyara zama yace "Yes, akan Anty na ne", nan da nan annurin fuskarta ya canza ba tareda ya kula ba yaci gaba da cewa "she's going through a lot because of you", shiru tayi a daidai lokacin da waiter ya dawo ya ajiye musu abinda suke bukata yace "enjoy your meal", sannan ya bar musu wurin, kallonta Najib yayi yace "Jawahir ba dogon zance nazo muyi ba, nasan you don't like your mom, basai kin fada ba amma inaso ki sani uwa uwa ce komai lalacewar ta balle kuma taki ba lalacewa tayi ba, Jawahir kin samu uwa me hankali da sanin ya kamata wanda a zamanin nan daidai kun mutane irinki ke samun mahaifiya irinsu, she loves you Jawahir amma ke sam bata gabanki, banzo dan na tilasta ki akan kiso mom dinki ba amma inaso ki bata chance, let her show you how much of a mother she can be to you, kuma idan kika bata chance dinnan babu rashin kunya dan as far kika ce zakiyi rashin kunya this relationship will not work, ki zauna kiyi tunani Jawahir, bawai nace dole kiyi abinda nace bane", shiru tayi tana processing abinda yace, yanzu dama wannan kiran duk saboda Mamah ne
Ajiyar zuciya tayi ta kalleshi tace "You are my brother right?", yace "yes off course", tace "can I share something with you?", yace "why not, dan Allah feel free", murmushi tayi dan kuwa dadin zamanta a wurin takeji, ko ba komai yau ta zauna gata ga Najib, tana kallonshi bata dauke ido ba tace "I'm going to share something with you, wanda ban taba fada kowa ba not even my Dada", shiru yayi yana jiran yaji me zatace, taci gaba da cewa "I love my Mom, amma ban taba fadawa kowa ba dan kona fada ba wanda ze yarda dani saboda yadda nake behaving, Mamah is the best thing that has ever happened to me, ita ce wacce ta fara koya min yadda ake sallah, addu'o'i, wankan tsarki da kuma yadda ake karatun Alkur'ani duk da ban sauke ba a islamiyya dan ba zama nakeyi a islamiyyan ba saboda banason karatun, a wurina wannan duk takura ne, kaga kuwa duk wacce ta koya maka duka wannan ta gama maka komai a rayuwa, ko sau daya Dada be taba zaunar dani ya tambaye ni ya nake wankan tsarki ba duk da yasan cewar ni baligar mace ce, maybe a tunaninshi zan koya a Islamiyya amma ni ba abinda na kowa a Islamiyya dan ba ganewa nake ba saboda bana maida hankali, banason Mamah, kuma bansan dalili ba amma deep down nasan inason ta, bansan meyasa nake kinta ba, bansan meyasa banajin maganar ta ba, kuma bansan meyasa nake mata rashin kunya ba duk da kuwa nasan cewar ba daidai bane, a kullum idan na tashi seta fado min a rai, burina shine in sata a ido koda sau daya ne a rana amma bazan iya ba saboda ko yaya na ganta wata irin kiyayyar ta ce ke darsuwa a raina wanda shikesa ni nake mata rashin kunya a karshe kuma inzo ina dana sani, na karanto maka wannan bayanin ne ba dan komai ba sedan na fahimtar da kai cewar babu ta yadda za'ayi naba Mamah chance dan bazan iya ba, I can't endure it even though I want to"
Hawayen da ya gani a idanunta yasashi tausaya mata, lallai Dada ya cuceta dan da ace be fifita Jawahir akan Mamah sanda take karama ba da haka duk bai faru ba, amma Jawahir ganin kome tayi Dada baya bari a tsawata mata yasa take ganin kaman duk abinda tayi daidai ne wanda wannan yasa take jin kiyayyar Mamah saboda itace me tsawata war, cikin sanyin jiki yace "i understand what you mean, kuma na gane inda kika dosa amma inaso ki sani wannan kiyayya da kikewa mahaiyarki babu idan ze kaiki se halaka, shedan ne ke nema ya shiga tsakaninku kuma yaci nasara ko kuma ince yana kan cin nasara, Jawahir I want you to fight this, ki yaki shedan daga zuciyarki, ta yadda zakiji saukin samun daman kasancewa da mahaifiyarki", ciki kuka tace "how?", yasa hannu ya share mata hawayen ta sannan yace "it's easy, just go back to Islamiyya", shiru tayi na en dakiku sannan tace "I don't think I can", yace "yes you can, just believe in yourself, I will enroll you in one idan ki naso", a hankali tace "zanyi tunani, idan na yanke hukunci zan bari ka sani, hope I can contact you", yace "yes, please any time", murmushi tayi ta kada kai yace "let's eat, the food is getting cold", tace "go ahead, ga drink dina nan", murmushi yayi ya fara cin abincin shi ita kuma ta kura mishi ido tana kallon yanda yake ci cikin nutsuwa, komai nashi abin birgewa ne, a zuciyarta tace "dama haka yake da saukin kai", dagowa yayi suka hada ido ta sakar murmushi ba tareda ta dauke idonta ba yaci gaba da cin abincin shi, duk dagowa se sun hada ido su sakarwa juna murmushi a haka har ya gama suka tashi ya biya kudi a counter sannan suka fice, mota ya shiga yace "muje in sauke ki", duk da ba nisa amma bata musa ba ta shiga dan bata gaji da ganin shi ba, a kofar gida ya sauke ta, ta kalleshi tace "I will call soon to let you know my decision", yace "no problem", sannan ta mishi sallama ta shige gida shi kuma yaja motarshi yana me jin dadin samun nasara da yayi

Kaman yadda Abba yayi alkawarin zuwa ganin magabatan Mamah haka ya cika alkawari, seda akayi sallan la'asar sannan shida wani abokinshi suka shirya suka tafi ganin mahaifin Yusuf, a harabar gidan suka tsaya me gadin ya shiga ciki da ya nema musu izinin shiga, be jima ba ya fito tare da musu iso har zuwa parlour
Da sallama suka shiga, inda suka sameshi zaune kan kujera hannunshi dauke da jarida yana karantawa, tsoho ne sosai amma kudi da hutu ya boye tsufanshi sedai kana kallon fuskarsa zakasan shekaru sun ja
Har kasa suka tsugunna suna gaishe shi ya amsa fuskarsa dauke da murmushi yace "madallah sannunku da zuwa", shiru Abba yayi kanshi kasa abokinshi ne ke amsa duk wani gaisuwa da sukeyi Alhaji Abubakar yace "Masha Allah ku tashi daga kasa ga wuri ku zauna", ya fada yana nuna musu kujera, tashi sukayi suka zauna kan kujera ya gyara zama yace "Aysha ta sanar dani zuwanku, amma duk da haka zanzo in kara jin bayani daga wurin ku", wadda suka zo tare da Abba me suna Ibrahim ya budi baki yace "dama Alhaji ba komai bane ya kawo mu nan ba, abokina ne yaga 'yar wurinka Hindu yace yanaso, sun daidaita tsakaninsu tace yazo ya ganka a matsayinka na madaurin aurenta", kaa kai yayi yace "Masha Allah na gamsu da wannan bayanin dan ita kanta Hindu munyi magana da ita sannan nasa Yusuf ya bari anmin bincike a kanka kuma alhmdllh bamuji wani aibi tattare da kai ba, bana shakkar baka auren Hindu dan koh a fuska na kalleka nasan kai nutsatsen mutum ne, Hindu da kake gani marainiya ce, a garin nan bata da uwa bata da uba seni dana zame mata uba, ta fito gidan mutunci da karamci dan haka nakeso ka rike ta amana, banda zalunci ganin batada gata, Hindu tana da gatan ta dan duk wani abu daze tashi nine nan zan tsaya mata, haka idan aka zalunce ta zan tsaya tsayin daka ganin na kwatar mata hakkin ta"
A hankali Abba ya budi baki yace "Inshallah zan rike Hindu hannu bibbiyu, zan zame mata uwa in zame mata uba, in Allah ya yarda bazaka kamani da laifin zalunci koh makamancin shi ba", kaa kai Alhaji Abubakar yayi yace"Allah ya baka ikon rike amana", duk suka amsa da "ameen", sannan yaci gaba da cewa "munyi magana da Hindu tace idan munyi magana da kai ka yanke muku rana amma bataso aja lokaci", cikin nutsuwa abokin Abba yace "Alhaji idan muka eba sati biyu yayi", Alhaji Abubakar yace "Allah ya kaimu lokacin rai da lafiya", duk suka amsa da "ameen" sannan Ibrahim ya mikawa Alhaji Abubakar kudi yace "ga sadakin ta, Naira dubu dari ne", karba Alhaji Abubakar yayi yace "Allah yasa musu albarka", nan ma suka sake amsa masa da "ameen", sannan suka mai sallama bayan an tsayar da ranar aure nan da sati biyu
A hanya Abba ya sauke Ibrahim ya karasa gida sannan shi ya karasa wurin Mamah, tarba me kyau ya samu daga wurin ta, seda suka dan taba hira sannan yake fada mata an tsaida rana nan da two weeks kuma ya bada sadakin ta dubu dari, murmushi tayi tace "Allah ya kaimu, amma sadakin baka ganin yayi yawa?", shima murmushin yayi yace "beyi yawa ba sema kadan da yayi, dan inaso auren yayi albarka yasa na bada darin ban bada fin hakan ba", a hankali tace "toh Allah ya musu albarka", ya amsa da "ameen", jin ana kiran sallan magrib yasa shi mikewa yace "bari na tafi magrib yayi zan tsaya masallaci nayi salla sannan na karasa gida, I can't wait to tell Sabreena this good news, nasan se tafi kowa farin ciki", murmushi Mamah tayi tace "my regards to her, kuma kace mata fushi nakeyi da ita kwana biyu ta daina lekowa nan", dan dariya yayi yace "don't worry zan kawo ta gobe ta wuni a nan", "da kuwa naji dadi", cewar Mamah yayin da suka karaso daidai inda parking, leda ya dauko a motar ya mika mata tareda cewa " har na manta na miki tsarabar", karba tayi tace "baka gajiya?", yace "saboda me zan gaji, ai bazan taba gajiya da miki hidima ba", murmusawa tayi tace "nagode, Allah ya kara budi", yace "ameen", tareda shiga mota suka yi sallama yaja motarshi ita kuma ta koma cikin gida
A parlour taga Baba Salamatu zaune ta karasa ta zauna tareda cewa "Baba kinga harsun gama magana da Alhaji an tsaida rana nan da sati biyu sannan ya bada sadaki dubu dari", Baba Salamatu cike da farin ciki tace "Masha Allah, Allah ya kaimu lafiya yasa ayi a sa'a, ya bada zaman lafiya tareda kawo kazantar daki", rufe fuska Mamah tayi tace "kai Baba, ai kinje da nisa", Baba Salamatu ta murmusa tace "barni naje kinji, gwara naga kin fara ajiye yara en dagwai dagwai dasu", cike da jin kunyar Baba ta tashi ta shige dakinta tana cewa "bari nayi sallah", zama tayi kan gado ta bude ledan da Abba ya kawo mata, turare ne masu kanshi guda biyu da chocolate har pack biyu, ita dariya ma ya bata chocolate sekace wata yarinya, tattarawa tayi ta ajiye gefe sannan ta mike ta shige bathroom dan dauro alwallah
BAYAN KWANA BIYU
Wasa wasa Jawahir ta shiga tunani kan shawarar da Najib ya bata kuma harga Allah ta amince zata koma islamiyya kodan rayuwarta tayi kyau amma kuma batada confidence din kiranshi ta fada mishi, bata fasa fita da Jarood ba duk da kuwa tasan cewar kasancewar ta dashi ba abinda yake tsinana mata se saon Allah, sannan ita da Farida yanzu sun koma zaman doya da manja a gidan, idan Farida ta tashi zatayi girkin ta tayi ayyukan ta ba tareda ta nemi Jawahir ba itama Jawahir gaisuwa kawai ke hadata da Farida kuma taji dadi da Farida ta daina shiga harkarta ta daina sata aiki dan dama baso takeyi ba duk da kuwa har yanzu tanajin shakkar Farida a ranta, har zuwa yanzu basuyi waya da Dada ba shi be kira ba itama bata kira ba duk da taji Farida na waya tana cewa yace cikin satin ze dawo, ita dai ta zubawa sarautar Allah ido
Yau ganin zaman kadaicin ya isheta seta tsinci kanta ta daukan waya ta kira Najib, ringing biyu ya dauka tareda mata sallama ta amsa sannan tace "Ya Najib zan iya ganin ka?", ba tareda dogon tunani ba yace " nayi busy for now, amma kinason wani abu ne?", tace "a'a dama inason na maka maganan islamiyya dinne, na yarda zan koma", cike da farin ciki yace "like for real", tace "yes, amma wanda ake zuwa weekend kawai nakeso saboda by next week zamu koma school", yace "ok no problem, gobe zanzo se muje mu duba muga wanda zeyi", tace "ok, se kazo", sallama sukayi suka kashe wayan ta dauko laptop dinta ta kunna dan ta debe wa kanta kewa
WASHEGARI
Kaman yadda Najib yayi alkawarin zuwa kaita duba islamiyyan da takeso haka ya cika alkawari yaje, sha biyu na rana a kofar gidan ta mishi ya kirata a waya tareda shaida mata yana kofar gidan, bata dau lokaci ba ta fito sanye da high waist skirt da top ta yafa karamin mayafi akai, girgiza kai yayi yace "no, jeki canza kaya, ko kisa hijab akan kayan ko after dress amma baza muje musu haka da karamin mayafi ba", bata fuska tayi tace "me wannan shigar tayi, nifa hijabina daya ne kuma dashi nake sallah bana fita dashi", kallonta yayi yace "karki bari mu samu matsala idan nace kiyi kiyi, idan nace ki bari ki bari banson musu, yanzu koma ki canza kaya", kallonshi kawai takeyi ba tareda ta motsa daga inda take ba dan ita bata saba da tayi abu ace mata ba daidai bane, abinda ke kawo mata matsala da Mamah kenan, kallonta yayi yace "ko bakiji bane", ba tareda tace komai ba ta juya ta koma ciki, bata dade ba se gata ta dawo sanye da blue hijab ta shiga motar ta zauna ba tareda ta mishi magana ba, murmushi kawai yayi a zuciyarshi yace "lallai akwai aiki a gaba", tada motar yayi suka dau hanya, suna cikin tafiya bame ma wani magana wayarshi tayi ringing, Sabreena ce ta kira, dan haka ya dauka sannan yasa earpiece suka fara hira, tin Jawahir na jure jin hirar duk da batajin me Sabreena ke fada har ta kasa jurewa ta soma hawaye, ita kanta batasan dalilin hawayen ta ba amma ta tabbata yanada sanadi da wayar da yakeyi dan a ganinta idan hiran yakeso meyasa bazeyi da ita ba tinda itace a kusa dashi se wata daban chan, wato ma yanada budurwa kenan
Kashe wayan yayi, yayi parking gaban wata Islamiyya sannan ya juyo dan yace mata sun iso ya ganta da hawaye, mamaki ta bashi ya kalleta da kyau yace "Jawahir lafiya, me aka miki, danna ce kisa hijab ko ki canza kaya shine kike kuka", bata kulashi ba ta fito daga motar ta tsaya, shima fitowa yayi yazo ya tsaya gabanta yace "look Jawahir bawai nace ki canza kaya dan wanda kikasa beyi bane, a'a nace ki canza me saboda islamiyya zamu kuma they don't tolerate such dressing, idan suka ganki a haka ba lallai su daukeki ba", kallonshi tayi cike da takaici tace "nifa ba abinda ya sani kuka kenan ba", yace "toh me ya saki kuka?", ta share hawayenta tace "ba kai bane, ina zaune amma ka kasa yin hira dani se wata chan daban", shiru yayi yana kallonta dan besan me zaice ba, me yake nufi da saboda yana hira da wata take kuka, badai kishin shi takeyi ba, "tirkashi", ya fada a zuciyarshi yana kallonta, kallonshi tayi tace "kuma bakace komai ba", yadda tayi maganar seta bashi dariya tareda tausayi dan kuwa tsantsar sonshi ya hango a idanunta bayanshi a nashi bangaren ba haka bane, sharewa yayi yace "toh yi hakuri, hakan baze sake faruwa ba, yanzu dai mu shiga ciki lokaci na tafiya", goge fuskarta tayi tabi bayanshi har suka shiga kowa da abinda yake sakawa a ranshi

UWA TA GARI - 21 - Page 2 - Wattpad
A bakin kofar Islamiyyar suka hadu da wani saurayi Najib ya karasa wurinshi yace "bawon Allah, dan Allah office din shugaban makarantar zaka nuna mana", kwatance yayi musu suka karasa Najib na gaba Jawahir na baya gabanta se dukan uku uku yakeyi, haka kawai takejin faduwar gaba dan batasan ya zatayi ba idan sukace bazasu kare ta ba dan harga Allah Islamiyyan ya kwanta mata
Da sallama suka shiga office din shugaban makarantar wanda ya amsa musu daga ciki sannan ya basu izinin zama, zama sukayi suka gaisa da Najib itama Jawahir ta gaisheshi sannan Najib yace "dan Allah kanwata ce nakeso na sata Islamiyya idan akwai class din da zezo daidai da ita a inda ta tsaya a karatu", gyara zama shugaban makarantar yayi sannan ya kalli Jawahir yace "izuninki nawa?", shiru tayi tana kallon kasa tana wasa da bakin hijabin ta yayi murmushi dan ba yau ya saba dealing da irinsu ya cigaba da cewa "baki sani ba?", ta daga kai alaman "eh", yace "hadisi fah, kinyi nisa kuma wannan kikeyi", a hankali tace "sanda nake zuwa Islamiyya arba'una hadis ake mana amma bansan inda aka tsaya ba", bece komai ba ya tashi yaje kan shelf dinshi ya dauko arba'una hadis ya dawo ya bude yace "karanta", da kyar ta iya karanta guda biyar da fassara, Najib duk kunya ta isheshi ji yake kaman kasa ta bude ya binne kanshi a ciki dan kunya, "fiqihu fah?", Nan ma ta girgiza kai, litattafai ya tambaye ta duk bata iya ba, daga karshe shida kanshi ya sauke numfashi na gajiya sannan ya kalli Najib yace "a gaskiya anyi sake akan karatun ta", shiru Najib yayi dan besan me zaice ba ya cigaba da cewa "ajujuwan mu duk sun wuce ta, babu wanda zamu iya sata sedai munada aji wanda muke yi asabar da lahadi daga karfe 2 na rana zuwa 6, ajin mata da maza ne harda matan aure amma matan auren ajinsu daban sedai karatu daya ake musu kuma yawancinsu naga duk sa'anninta ne zata iya zama cikinsu tayi karatu tinda suma basuyi nisa ba dan bamu dade da bude wannan ajin ba, ko wata uku ba'ayi ba, bari na kira malamin ajin inji yadda zamuyi", ajiyar zuciya Najib ya sauke yace "ba matsala"
Yaro shugaban makarantar ya samo yace a kira mishi malam Abbas, basu dade ba Malam Abbas din ya shigo da sallama duk suka amsa mai ya karaso ya tsaya gefen shugaban makarantar yace "kayi kirana ya Sayyid", Ya Sayyid yace "eh, dama daliba ka samu, ban sani ba ko zata samu gurbi a ajinka dan kwata kwata batayi nisa a karatun ba, murmushi yayi yace "ba damuwa, zamu san abinyi", godiya Najib ya mishi na amincewa da ita sannan suka tautauna kan litattafan da zata siya, da kuma hijab dinda zata dinka dan ajin hijab kawai suke sawa har kasa, nan take Najib ya biya kudin litattafan aka bata sannan ya karba kyallen hijab din ya musu sallama suka fice tareda alkawarin sabon sati zata fara zuwa Inshallah
A mota ba wanda yayiwa wani magana, ita duk kunya ta isheta Najib yasan bata iya komai ba a fannin Islamiyya duk da tasan ita ba dakikiya bace kawai dai rashin maida hankali ne, shi kuwa tunani kawai yake me Mamah da Dada keyi har da basu maida hankali kan karatun Jawahir ba dan kuwa a wannan karon ba Dada kadai bane me laifi ba harda Mamah tinda it's part of her responsibility
A bakin kasuwa yayi parking tareda fitowa yace mata ta fito, ganin yadda yake mata magana ba tareda da sake fuska ba tayi sauri ta kamo hannunshi dan ta tsayar dashi, tsayawa yayi ya juyo yana kallonta tace "Ya Najib nasan I'm a disappointment to you saboda na baka kunya a gaban malaman nan amma i promise I will change, wallahi this time around zan maida hankali kan karatu kodan kayi alfahari dani", ajiyar zuciya yayi sannan yace "karkiyi karatu dan nayi alfahari dake, kiyi karatu dan duniya tayi alfahari, ni bakimun laifi ba dan nasan cewar ba laifinki bane harda na iyayenki, sedai a wannan karon idan baki maida hankali ba toh ze zama laifinki dan kin samu second chance kikayi watsi da damar ki", a hankali tace "Inshallah bazanyi watsi da damata ba, this time around zan zauna nayi karatu", sosai yayi farin ciki dan yaga determination tattare da ita, yasan cewa wannan lokacin zatayi karatun tinda tace zatayi, "Allah yasa wa karatun albarka", ta amsa da "ameen", sannan tace "toh ka sake fuska mana, kamin murmushi tinda nace zanyi karatun", besan sanda yayi murmushin ba, ya girgiza kai sannan yace mata "muje mu siya hijabin"
A gaban wani shago da suke siyar da yadin hijabi suka tsaya ya mika musu kyallen yace "wannan nakeso, wanda ze isheta a dinka har kasa", nan suka yanko mishi ya biya kudi sannan suka nuna mishi shagon da za'a dinka mishi, har guda biyu ya dinka mata sannan ya maida ita gida, yaso ya fada mata maganan auren Mamah amma bayaso taji daga bakinshi gwara dai taji daga bakin Mamah da kanta, dan haka yace "Jawahir dan Allah wata alfarma zaki mun", tace "Allah yasa befi karfina ba", murmushi yayi yace "so nake ki samu rana kije ki gaida Aunty na", shiru tayi kaman bazata amsa ba sannan daga baya tace "shikenan, zanje anjima", murmushi yayi yace "Thank you", ta daga mishi hannu ba tareda tace komai ba, shima hannu ya daga mata sannan yaja motarshi ya bar wurin, seda ta daina ganin motarshi sannan ta shige gida
Da yamma ta shirya cikin straight gown dinkin material ta yafa veil sannan ta leka dakin Farida, kwance ta ganta tana chatting tace "zanje na duba Mamah, maybe na dawo bayan isha ko kuma gobe", kallonta Farida tayi tace "wacece kuma Mamah da har zakije ki kwana wurinta?", ba tareda ta damu da tone din da Farida ta mata amfani dashi wurin magana ba tace "mahaifiyata ce, wurin mahaifiyata zani", shiru Farida tayi na en sakwanni sannan tace "if I can remember mahaifinki ya cemin kun riga kun yanke zumunci tsakanin ku, yanzu kuma wani gulma ne ze kaiki", cikin bacin rai Jawahir tace "wannan ba damuwar ki bane, kuma baki isa ki hanani ganin mahaifiyata ba, sannan bana zo neman izinin tafiya bane, na dai fada miki ne kawai danna fita hakkin ki, sena dawo", tana fadar haka ta juya ta fice abinta Farida tace "karma ki dawo, wawiyar yarinya kawai, kina dab da dawowa tafin hannuna karki ga na miki shiru kwana biyu ban gama shirin da nakeyi bane", Jawahir ko juyowa batayi ba tayi tafiyar ta Farida kuwa tayi kwafa tareda daukan waya taci gaba da chatting dinta
A daidaita ta samu ta fada mishi inda zata, har gaban gidan Mamah ya kaita ta biyashi sannan ta shiga gidan, a hankali take tafiya dan batasan wanne zataje ta tarar ba, ta tabbata idan batayi kokari ta kai zuciya nisa ba se an samu matsala a wannan ziyarar nata dan kuwa ita da Mamah basa zama inuwa daya ba tareda sun samu sabani ba
Da sallama ta shiga Baba Salamatu dake zaune parlour tana kallo ta amsa mata tareda cewa "a'a Jawahir yau kuma kece a gidan", zama tayi tace "eh nice, wurin Mamah nazo", Baba Salamatu tace "bata dawo daga wurin aiki ba tukun dan tace zata biya kasuwa tayi siyayya kafin ta dawo", tashi Jawahir tayi tace "idan ta dawo ina daki", kallonta Baba Salamatu tayi harta shige dakinta sannan ta girgiza kai, ita dai Jawahir bazata canza ba, ta shigo ba gaisuwa kuma tana mata magana da gadara kaman da sa'arta take magana
Kwanciya tayi kan gadonta wanda yake nan a gyare kaman dama ansan da zuwanta, wayanta ta dauko tayiwa Najib text kamar haka "I'm at Mamah's place, and I'm sleeping over", murmushi yayi daya ga text dinta ya tura mata da "I'm glad", shiru tayi tana kallon dakin da kayan cikinshi, yana nan yanda yake ba abinda aka taba mata
Tana cikin kalle kallenta taji shigowar motar Mamah alamar ta dawo, bata fito ba taci gaba da kwanciyar ta, tanaji Baba Salamatu na mata sannu da dawowa tareda fada mata tana ciki, sallama Mamah tayi Jawahir ta amsa sannan Mamah ta shiga dakin, a bakin gado ta zauna Jawahir ta mike zaune Mamah tace "Jawahir yau kece a gidan?", tace "uhm", Mamah tace "Dadanki yasan kinzo?", Jawahir ta girgiza kai tace "be sani ba, dan baya gari kuma bamuyi waya ba", shiru Mamah tayi tana kallon yadda Jawahir ta rame har ta dan dishe ma, Mamah ta gyara zama da kyau tana fuskantar Jawahir tace "is something wrong, you look pale, bakida lafiya ne?", kallon Mamah Jawahir tayi inda ta hango damuwa arara a idanunta, girgiza kai tayi tace "I'm fine Mamah, just stress ne", Mamah ta riko hannun Jawahir tace "wani irin stress, bakya samun bacci ne?", Jawahir tace "ina samun bacci, don't worry about me I will be fine", shiru Mamah tayi dan batasan me zatace ba dan kaffa kaffa takeyi karta batawa Jawahir rai ta fice daga gidan, ganin shirun yayi yawa Jawahir tace "Baba Salamatu tace min zaki biya kasuwa, what did you buy, akwai kayan dadi a ciki", girgiza kai Mamah tayi tana mamakin yadda Jawahir ta canza lokaci daya haka, a hankali tace "Jawahir aure zanyi, kayan da zanyi amfani dashi naje siya", kallonta Jawahir keyi kaman bata yarda da abinda Mamah tace ba, seda ta gama processing maganan sannan tace "Mamah aure kuma?", Mamah tace "eh", shiru Jawahir tayi batace komai ba Mamah tace "ko bakyaso nayi ne", Jawahir ta girgiza kai tace "na isa in hanaki, tinda ban iya na hana Dada ba kema bazan hanaki ba Allah ya baku zaman lafiya but don't expect me to be at the wedding dan ko na Dada ma I didn't participate", kaa kai Mamah tayi tace "I won't force you amma i would like you to give the man I'm going to marry a chance, saboda kusan juna, I know you will like him", shiru tayi batace komai ba Mamah tace "Are you hungry, should I prepare something for you to eat", da sauri Jawahir tace "yes please, I'm starving", tashi Mamah tayi tace "ina zuwa", sannan ta fice tana mamakin yadda akayi Jawahir ta canza, bazata tambayeta dalilin canzawar ta ba dan a ganinta gwara a tafi a hakan kawai tinda ita kanta Jawahir din bata nuna komai ba
Kwanan Jawahir biyu a gidan Mamah ta koma gida saboda ta fara shirin komawa school wanda zasu resume nan da sati daya, alhmdllh basu samu matsala da Mamah ba duk da ba wani hira sukeyi ba dan kuwa babu alaman shakuwa tattare dasu sedai Mamah na iya bakin kokarin ta dan taga taja Jawahir a jiki, da Jawahir ta koma gida tunanin halin da zata shiga ta somayi dan ta tabbata idan Mamah tayi aure mantawa da ita zatayi tunda a yanzu ma da batada aure ta manta da ita inaga tayi aure, gashi nan bawai tana jin dadin zama da Farida bane, tunani ta shigayi kala kala wanda daga karshe ta yankewa kanta fita daga harkan kowanne daga cikinsu, daga Mamah har Dada da Farida zata park dinsu ta ajiye gefe tayi abinda ze fisheta duniya da lahira wato maida hankali kan Islamiyyan ta kenan, dan kuwa wannan karon ta dau alwashin maida hankali saboda Najib yaji dadi
