UWA TA GARI - 22 - Page 2 - Wattpad
NOT EDITED
Wasa wasa an shiga satin biki, Mamah komawa tayi gidan Yaya Aysha da ita da Baba Salamatu har ranar daurin aure inda aka daura auren Hindu da Harun (Abba), ba wani taron azo a gani aka yi ba dan walima da suka shirya se kuma en uwanta da kogi da suka zo shaida biki wanda basufi su goma ba
A ranar Mamah ta tare a gidanta inda Sabreena tace wurin Yaya Aysha zatayi sati daya harse Mamah ta gama cin amarci sannan ta dawo, dariya ta ba mutane amma haka Abba ya barta taje tinda mahaifiyarshi bata samu zuwa bikin ba saboda ciwon kafa daya matsa mata kwana biyu
A ranar bikin a ranar Jawahir ta fara zuwa Islamiyya dan haka bataje ba kuma dama batayi alkawarin zata ba, sedai tayiwa Mamah text message na Allah ya sanya alkhairi, a Islamiyya sosai ta maida hankalinta a karatun da ake mata, batawa kowa magana ba dan batama son tayi kawaye saboda abinda ya kawota tayi shi takeso tayi ba tareda wani distraction ba, tayi mamakin ganin Najib a kofar Islamiyyan sanda ta fito tafiya gida, murmushi ya mata yace "just want to be sure you came", itama murmushin tayi ta karasa gabanshi tace "I told i would be serious, don't worry, kullum zan dinga zuwa Saturday, Sunday", kaa kai yayi yace "let me escort you home", tafiya suka farayi tace "bakazo da mota ba", yace "Yes yana wurin gyara, ya samu matsala", tace "oh", shiru sukayi dukkansu sannan daga baya tace "ya Adil, bana ganinshi", kallonta yayi yace "ai bakya ziyara shi yasa bakya ganinshi", a hankali tace "kunyar big mommy nakeji shiyasa bana zuwa, nasan tana fushi dani", be boye mata ba yace "fushi lamba daya ma kenan kiji da kyau, inda zaki iya kije ki wanke kanki", shiru tayi tana tunanin ta yaya zataje gidan yaya Aysha da sunan tazo ziyara
Har kofar gida ya rakata, seda yaga shiganta sannan ya juya ya tari napep zuwa inda zashi, dinga compound takejin hayaniyar mutane a parlour bata damu ba dan tasan bazasu wuce kawayen Farida ba, da sallama ta shiga inda Salma ce kawai ta amsa mata fuska a sake, Nafisa da Zulaika kuwa kare mata kallo sukayi suka dauke kai, Farida kuwa dariya tayi tace "Jawahir yau kuma ustaziya aka zama irin wannan hijabi har kasa haka", bata kulata ba ta wuce dakinta dan Farida batasan Jawahir ta fara zuwa Islamiyya ba
Tana shigewa daki suka kyakyale da dariya Salma dake kallonsu tace "amma Farida bakya kyautawa wallahi, Ni yarinyar nan banga aibun ta ba, kuma fa ki sani amana mahaifinta ya bar miki ita, da zaki kwantar da kanki a wurinta da kuwa kun zauna lafiya, hararta Farida tayi sannan tace "ai ke dama haka kike, koda yaushe bakya son gaskiya", da mamaki Salma ta kalleta tace "nice banason gaskiya ko ke?", ganin abin nasu na nema ya zama rigima Zulaika tayi saurin cewa "ya isa, abeg mu daina tada jijiyoyin wuyanmu saboda wata chan da bama gabanta, ko bakuga yadda ta sharemu tayi shigewarta daki ba, shine mu zamu tsaya kace nace saboda ita, Nafisa, Salma ku tashi ku tafi, mijinta ya kusa dawowa, kema tashi kije ki gyara jikinki kar yazo ya ganki a hargitse", tashi Farida tayi ta wuce ko magana bata sake yi ba su kuma suka fice daga gidan
Jawahir dake daki take jinsu ta koma ta zauna tareda cewa "lallai ma Dada, wato nice baze kira ba tinda yayi amarya, har ze dawo bansani tinda bana gabanshi yanzu, haushin Dada taji ya dirar mata lokaci daya tace "after all we've gone through together shine ze juya min baya saboda yayi amarya?" shiru tayi tana tunanin rayuwarta da Dada kafin Farida ta shigo ciki, lallai Farida ta raba ta da farin cikinta, batasan kuka takeyi ba seda taji hawaye a fuskarta, kiran sallar magrib taji ta tashi ta shiga bathroom ta wanke fuskarta sannan tayi alwallah ta fito tayi sallah, tana idarwa ta dauko Qur'ani tana bitar karatun da aka mata a Islamiyya, tafi minti talatin a wurin kafin taji shigowar Dada da sallaman shi sannan taji ihun Farida na farin cikin ganin mijinta, da ace ada ne da yanzu itama ta fita tarban mahaifinta amma a yau se taji batason ganinshi ma kwatakwata, dan haka ta tashi ta daura isha ta sallame sannan ta tashi ta shige bathroom tayi wanka ta fito ta shirya tayi kwanciyarta kota kansu bata bi ba
A bangaren Dada kuwa yayi murnar ganin iyalinshi, se nan nan takeyi dashi yayinda duk rabin hankalinshi ke kan Jawahir, jira yakeyi yaga ta ina zata fito dan ya shaidawa Farida cewar ta fada mata yau ze dawo amma gashi yaji shiru kaman bata gidan sannan yanaso ya tambayi Farida inda Jawahir take wani abu na hanashi wanda ya rasa dalili, daga karshe hakura yayi ya zauna kan dinning kaman yadda Farida ta bukata, seda ta gama cika mishi ciki sannan ta jashi zuwa daki ba tareda taje ta sanar da Jawahir dawowar mahaifinta ba
Jawahir kasa bacci tayi, duk inda ta juya tunanin Dada ne a ranta, wayarta ta dauko dan ta debewa kanta kewa tinda bacci yaki zuwa amma taga subscription dinta ya kare gashi batada kudi a account dan kwana biyun nan Jarood ne ke turo mata da kati gashi yau be turo ba, wurgi da wayar tayi ta koma ta kwanta, nan ma dai bacci ya gagara zuwa, ganin haka seta tashi ta nufi drawer dinda ta ajiye maganin da Jarood ya bata ta dauko, tinda tasha so daya bata kuma bi takanshi ba amma yau saboda takaicin Dada da matarshi, da kuma auren Mamah yasa ta ciro daya tasa a baki, batayi la'akari da cewar yau din rana ce me girma a wurinta ba kasancewar ta koma Islamiyya, bata dubi albarkacin wannan ba ta kora kwayan da ruwa ta koma kan gado ta nemi wuri ta kwanta, ko kwakwaran minti biyar ba'ayi ba bacci yayi awon gaba da ita
Washegari ba ita ta tashi ba se karfe goma, sakayau take jinta ba wani tunanin Dada balle matarshi sedai ciwon kai aya matsa mata, tashi tayi ta shiga bathroom tayi wanka sannan ta dauro alwallah ta fito, seda tasa kaya sannan tayi sallah ta fice dan nemawa kanta abinda zataci saboda yunwa dan rabonta da abinci tin jiya da safe, se kayan ruwa data dinga durawa cikinta
A parlour taga Dada zaune shika dai yana aiki a laptop, tsaya tayi ta kare mishi kallo taga yadda yayi kyau yayi haske har wani dan jiki ya kara alamar hutu ya zauna a jikin shi, tabe baki tayi tace "I can see you are back", dagowa yayi ya kalleta, ganin itace ya saki murmushi yace "my princess, tin jiya naketa zuba ido ina son ganin ki se yanzu Allah yayi, na leko dazu naga kina bacci", rolling idanuwanta tayi ta nemi wuri ta zauna sannan tace "i thought you've forgotten about me", ya waro ido tareda girgiza kai yace "na isa, kullum idan nayi waya da new mummy dinki se nace ta kai miki waya mu gaisa saboda nayi misplacing naki number se tace min bakya nan ko kina bacci, amma ina bata sakon gaisuwa ince ta gaishe min dake, I even told her to tell you I was coming back", kallon Dada tayi da kyau tace "well, she never told me", girgiza kai yayi yace "I can see ai, but forget about that and tell how you are doing, kinyi rashin lafiya ne naga kin rame kuma kin dishe", ajiyar zuciya tayi tace "I'm not fine, yau almost one month kenan banda kudi se Jarood ne ke bani, sannan I'm sorry to say amma matarka na takurawa rayuwata daya, batason zaman lafiya dani, ko abinci bata girkawa dani a ganin plus jiya Mamah tayi aure", da sauri ya kalli Jawahir jin Mamah tayi aure, zuciyar bugawa ta farayi ba kakkautawa kaman wanda aka aiko wa sakon mutuwar mahaifiyarshi yace "aure kuma?", ta daga kafada tace "Yes aure, i thought she's free to do so tinda kaima kayi, ai ba haramun bane, the look on your face seems like I told she's committing fornication", gyara murya yayi sannan ya gyara zamanshi tareda dauko wayarshi yace "give me your account number", nan take ta karanto mishi ya mata transfer din 200k sannan yace "about your new mummy I will talk some sense into her, karki damu, hope all is settled now", ta girgiza kai tace "no", dan ita a ganinta gwara ta fadi duka matsalolinta yanzu tinda yanzu ne takeda dama kafin nan gaba ta rasa damarta, kaa kai yayi yace "tell me, what is wrong", tace "nothing is wrong kawai dai I need a car saboda ina gajiya da shiga napep kullum, gobe zamu koma school, kuma na shiga Islamiyya na Saturday and Sunday so, I need a means of transportation", da murmushi ya kalleta yace "kinga shiga Islamiyya?", tace "Yes Dada", yace "wow, I'm impressed", murmushi tayi ganin yadda Dada yaji dadin komawarta Islamiyya sannan yace "ki dauka key din BMW din nan ya zama naki, amma akwai documents dinda na ajiye ciki ki ciremin", da murna ta rungume shi tana cewa "tnx Dada", yace "don't mention, anything to make you happy my dear", komawa tayi ta zauna yacigaba da cewa "nawa ne kudin registration na wannan year din, nasan zaki siya sabon reading and writing materials koh?", tace "eh Dada Amma honestly speaking bansan komai a kai ba tukun saboda bana cikin class group amma idan naje gobe I will make enquiry", yace "ok Allah ya, kiyi karatu sosai kinji, I want to be proud of you one day", da murmushi tace "Inshallah Dada", cikinta ne yayi kara alamar yunwa ta dago ta kalli Dada, ganin expression din fuskarshi se duk suka sa dariya ta mike tana cewa "let me get myself something to eat before I starve to death"

UWA TA GARI - 23 - Wattpad
NOT EDITED 
Jawahir seda ta gama cin abinci sannan ta koma daki, riga da wando ne jikinta ta dauki hijabin Islamiyyan ta ta daura akai sannan ta fito, dakin Dada ta nufa inda taga Farida kwance da alama yanzu ta tashi daga bacci, ba tareda ta kalleta ba ta nufi inda yake ajiye makullin mota ta dauki wanda yace ta dauka, da mamaki Farida tace "ke kuma lafiyanki kuwa, da izinin wa kika dauka?", Jawahir ta kalleta sannan tace "da izinin Dada, sannan bani yayi halak malak ba aro ba", da fadan haka ta fice ta bar Farida da sakakken baki, tashi tayi daga kwancen da take ta zauna tace "ni wannan yarinyar wai har yanzu maganin Baba be fara aiki a kanta bane, wani lokacin kaman yana aiki wani lokacin kuma taga ba haka ba, da sauri ta mike ta shige bathroom bata ata lokaci ba tayi abinda zatayi ta fito, a dakinta taje ta shirya sannan ta fito parlour, ba Dada haka ma Jawahir bata gidan, dan haka ta koma daki ta dauki wayarta ta kira Dada, ringing biyu ya daga tareda mata sallama ta amsa sannan tace "kayi nisa ne?", yace "ina gurin umma ya akayi?", ta bata fuska sannan tace "dama fita nakeso nayi amma bazan dade ba?", ba tareda tunanin komai ba yace "se kin dawo"
Kashe wayar tayi ta dauki key din motar ta da mayafi se jakka ta fice, koda tabar gidan bata tsaya ko ina na se gidan Baba, yana nan zaune a gaban gidanshi yanama manyan talibanshi karatu ta karaso, har kasa ta tsugunna ta gaisheshi ya amsa mata da murmushi sannan ya kalli talibanshi yace "kudan bamu wuri", duk mikewa sukayi suka bar wurin ta gyara zama kan tabarmar da kyau sannan tace "Baba yarinyar nan fah har yanzu bata shakka ta", murmushi yayi irin nasu na manya yace "Farida wannan yarinyar da kike gani bazataji shakkar ki ba, saboda a kullum addu'ar mahaifiyarta na bibiyarta, kinsan ance addu'ar iyaye baya faduwa kasa banza musamman ma na mahaifiya, duk da ita yarinyar bawai ta bama addini wani muhimmanci bane amma mahaifiyarta tsaye take a kanta da addu'a ba dare ba rana, har tsayuwar dare takeyi akanta, kinga kuwa ba yanda za'ayi kenan, kawai idan kinason kwanciyar hankali ki fita harkar ta", shiru tayi tana processing abunda Baba yace sannan ta dago tace "shikenan Baba amma shi mijin nawa ya za'ayi dashi kenan", murmushi ya sake yi yace "me kikeso dashi", ba kunya tace "Baba ni kawai so nake ace ni kadaice a gabanshi kuma duk abinda na fada mishi ya dinga yarda dashi", kallonta yayi yace "aiko a yanzu ma kece a ranshi", tace "Baba ba kaman yadda nakeso ba", shiru yayi yana tunani kafin yace "shikenan zan miki aiki amma kuma banda rashin kunya tsakanin ku, zan jawo miki hankalinshi gareki, sedai kuma karkiga kin samu abinda kikeso kiyi rashin kunya, ke zaki wahala nan gaba ba wani ba", kaa kai tayi tace "Inshallah Baba", sannan yace "shikenan, jeki zakiga aiki, keda kanki zaki dawo ki bani labari", kallonshi tayi tace "ba magani ko rubutu ko wani abu", ya girgiza kai yace "babu, kije kiyi amfani da wanda na taba baki, idan kuma kinyi amfani dashi ba matsala", hannu tasa a jaka ta ciro kudi zata ajiye mishi yace "jeki da abinki, idan kika aiki kuma yayi miki seki dawo ki kawo min", godiya ta mishi sannan ta mike ta mishi sallama ta wuce, shikuma ya kira daliban shi sukaci gaba da karatu
Jawahir yawo ta dingayi a gari da motar ta, murna fal a cikinta tayi mota, duk da dai ba sabuwa bace amma bazaka ganta kace ta tsufa ba, se dab azahar ta tsaya a bakin tayi withdraw kudi sannan ta wuce Islamiyya, koda aka ganta da mota se aka bude mata gate tayi parking a ciki da yake akwai parking space a compound din, gaisawa tayi da gate man din sannan ta wuce masallacin dake ciki, ba wani babba bane, sedai an kawatashi da kyau wanda dalibai ke sallah a ciki idan ta kamasu, alwallah tayi tayi sallar azahar sannan ta wuce aji, ba kuwa dan ba'a fara zuwa ba, malaminsu ne zaune a kan desk dinshi yana duba litattafai ta gaishe shi ya amsa sannan ta nemi wuri ta zauna, kallonta yayi yace "da fatan kina gane karatun da akeyi?", tace "eh ina ganewa malam", yace "ok, duk abinda baki gane ba feel free to ask", ta kaa mishi kai sannan ta ciro litattafan ta tana duba wanda sukayi jiya, bata dade da zama ba wata wacce a shekaru zasuyi sa'a da Jawahir ta shigo da sallaman ta, amsa mata malamin yayi tareda cewa "Khadijah yau kece da wuri haka", zama tayi tace "wallahi banson zaman baya ne shi yasa nazo da wuri", kaa kai yayi yace "ai hakan yafi", sannan ya tashi yace musu yana zuwa ya fice, juyawa tayi bayanta inda taga Jawahir gaba-daya hankalinta na kan Qur'anin ta tace "sannunki", Jawahir ta dago tace "yauwa sannu", yarinyar tace "kece sabuwar daliban da aka kawo jiya koh?", Jawahir ta kaa kai ba tareda tace komai ba yarinyar tace "sunana Khadijah, I'm 19 years next month zan shiga 20, kuma inada aure", murmushi Jawahir tayi a zuciyarta tace "ni na tambaye ta age dinta ne", sannan tace "Sunana Jawahir", Khadijah tace "how old are you", Jawahir tace "19", Khadijah tace "wow, ashe shekarar mu daya", Jawahir ta kaa kai tace "inada tambaya", Khadijah tace "Allah yasa na sani", Jawahir tace "how comes kina yarinya kikayi aure kuma har yanzu kina zuwa Islamiyya a wannan ajin, dan a tunanina wannan ajin na wa'anda basuyi karatu bane", murmushi Khadijah tayi tace "mamana da babana sun rabu, so wurin matar babana na tashi shi yasa ban samu karatu sosai ba saboda bata barina naje Islamiyya sedai na mata aikin gida, aure kuma dan unguwar mu ne ya ganni yace yanaso, ni kuma na amince har akayi auren shine ya kawoni wannan Islamiyyan, yanzu wata na uku da aure, wata na daya da fara zuwa Islamiyyan nan dan dani aka budeta saboda malaminmu da mijina abokai ne", Jawahir ta kaa kai alamar ta gamsu tace "na gane", Khadijah tace "kefa", Jawahir ta girgiza kai tace "nawa is a long story, amma to cut the long story short ni da kaina na hana kaina zuwa Islamiyya, se yanzu wani yayana ya samin ra'ayin dawowa", ganin an fara cika a ajin Khadijah ta tashi daga wurinta ta dawo kusa da Jawahir ta zauna sannan ta mikawa Jawahir hannu tace "friends", murmushi Jawahir tayi ta mika mata hannu itama tareda cewa "friends", a haka malaimsu ya dawo yace "zamu fara karatu, wa'anda sukayi latti kuma sunma kansu dan bazamu jirasu ba", duk nutsuwa sukayi inda ya bari suka biya mishi wanda ya musu jiya kafin ya kara musu
Sabreena da Najib ne zaune a garden din gidansu Najib suna shan iska, ajiyar zuciya Sabreena tayi tace "at last I can now breath, Mamah has now become my new mummy", kallonta Najib yayi yace "I'm happy for her, she has gone through alot gaskiya", shiru sukayi dukkansu sun lula duniyar tunani Najib ya katse musu tunani da cewa "Reena I want to ask you a favor", kallonshi tayi tace "I'm all ears", yace "take of my aunt kinji, make her happy, treat her like a mother, she deserves it", kallonshi tayi da kyau tace "I will, but why do you ask such favor", girgiza kai yayi yace "I already told you she has gone through alot, I'm not in the best position to tell you about her past, but I trust my aunt when the right time comes she will tell you", kaa kai tayi alamar gamsuwa tace "Allah ya bani ikon kula da ita", yace "ameen", hira suka shigayi na rayuwarsu da school dinda Sabreena zata fara zuwa gobe, koh kadan be fada mata da Jawahir ba balle ya fada mata nan school din Jawahir ke zuwa, ganin yamma tayi sosai ya duba agogonshi inda yaga shida saura minti takwas, da sauri ya tashi yana cewa Sabreena "Reena nayi mantuwa, bari naje na dawo", itama mikewa tayi tana cewa "ina zaka?", amma ina har ya kai bakin motarshi tsabar sauri, tana kallo aka bude mai gate ya fice sannan itama ta shige cikin gida tana gunguni wai kwana biyu nan baya zama suyi hira kaman da
A gaban Islamiyyan su Jawahir ya tsaya tareda fitowa daga mota yana jiranta, yana nan tsaye har aka kusa gama wucewa ba ita ba alamun ta, Jawahir seda ta tsaya sukayi sallama da Khadijah bayan sunyi exchange din number sannan ta shiga motar ta aka bude mata gate, tana hango Najib ta nemi wuri gefen titi tayi parking sannan ta fito ta karasa wurinshi tana cewa "Ya Najib", kallonta yayi yace "ke nazo dauka, se gashi kuma kinyi mota", murmushi tayi tace "da safen nan Dada ya bani", yace "ya dawo ne", tace "eh, jiya da daddare ya dawo", hannu yasa a aljihu yace "yanzu ya za'ayi kenan, bari na wuce tinda kinada abin hawa", kallon motar ta tayi ta juyo ta kalleshi saboda bataso su rabu yanzu tace "I'm hungry, ka kaini inci abinci", kallonta yayi da murmushi dan yasan karya takeyi yace "shiga motarki zan biyoki a baya, tinda bazamu barshi a nan ba", shiga motar ta tayi suka kama hanya tana gaba yana binta a baya har suka kai gida, ta shiga tayi parking sannan ta fito ta shiga motarshi tace "muje", ya kalleta sannan ya maida kallonshi kan titi yace "me zakici?", gaba-daya attention dinta na kanshi tace "akwai shawarma joint idan kayi gaba kadan, muje mu siya", a wurin siyar da shawarma din suka tsaya ya siya musu kowa daddaya, se taga ya kara siyan daya daban, batace komai ba, seda suka shiga mota sannan tace "Adil zaka kaiwa wannan", yace "no, a friend", ta kalleshi tace "a he/ she" da murmushi yace "she", take ta bata fuska bata sake magana ba, shikuwa ko kulata beyi ba har suka kawo gida yayi parking sannan ya juyo ya kalleta yace "idan kika bata bakya kyau, sannan inaso ki sani, she's just a friend nothing else plus you are my cousin, so, definitely kin fita matsayi a wurina, banaso kina daga hankalinki idan kikaji ina waya da mace ko ina hiran wata, remember ni namiji ne sooner or later aure zanyi", kallonshi tayi tace "wa zaka aura?", yaja hancinta tareda yin dariya saboda ta bashi dariyar, kwata kwata bata iya boye kishin ta, "nima bansan wanda zan aura ba tukun, amma kullum ina addu'a Allah ya bani ta gari", shiru tayi batace komai yace "shiga gida, anyi sallah, se next week zanzo na daukeki idan an tasheku daga Islamiyya", bata mishi magana ba ta bude motar tayi ficewarta tana maida kwallan da ke kokarin zubowa ba dan komai ba sedan Najib yace yana addu'an Allah ya bashi ta gari, wato batama cikin lissafinshi kenan tinda ita kanta tasan idan ana maganan mata na gari nata ciki, kallonta Najib keyi harta bacewa ganinshi sannan ya lumshe ido yana shafa sumar kanshi, furzar da iskar bakinshi yayi yana cewa "may Allah make this easy for me", dan kuwa besan ya zeyi da Jawahir ba, gashi banda soyayyar ba abinda yake gani a idanunta idan suna tare, uwa uba kuma bata iya boye kishin ta, ganin tunanin ba inda ze kaishi ya tada motarshi ya bar unguwar

UWA TA GARI - 24 - Page 2 - Wattpad

Kwata kwata Farida taki yarda ta hakura da lamarin Jawahir dan ko kadan bata son ganinta a kusa da ita, bata sha'awar mu'amala da ita dan haka bazata zauna ta nade hannu tana kallon Jawahir na abinda taga dama a wannan gidan ba, wannan dalilin yasa da yamma ganin Dada be dawo ba ta dauki waya ta haa conference call tsakaninta da Zulaika da Nafisa amma batasa Salma a ciki, duk wani abu da Baba ya fada mata shi ta maimaita musu sannan ta kara da cewar "nifa gaskiya bazan iya hakura ba dan wallahi yarinyar nan tana shiga gonata dayawa, wai kuji har kyautar mota ya mata dan kawai ta bukaci hakan wannan irin so yake mata, gaskiya so nake na kawar da ita daga ganinshi", Zulaika ce ta fara cewa "toh ke yanzu me kikeso muyi?", tace "ku nemamin mafita, Nafisa ina wannan malamin nan naki na Katsina?", Nafisa tace "yana nan", Farida tace "wurinshi zamuje", shiru Nafisa tayi na dan wani lokaci kafin tace "ogan naki ze barki ne?", Farida tace "dolenshi ma", Nafisa dake ganin karfin halin Farida tace "shikenan, duk sanda kika shirya ki bari na sani", da "toh" ta amsa musu sannan ta katse wayar tana cewa " 'yar iska, ba zaman dare ba, koh rubutu uwarki ke baki kikesha senasa kwana bakin titi yafi miki kwana gidan nan dan wallahi se kin gane bakida wayau tinda kince ke bakida kunya, fitsararra kawai"
Washegari Monday tinda sassafe Jawahir ta tashi tayi wanka ta shirya ta fice daga gidan abinta dan a halin yanzu da Farida ke gidan bata cika son zama ba saboda gudun bacin rai, direct school dinsu ta nufa inda ta wuce hostel dinda Zahra tace mata take, kiranta tayi a waya dan ta fada mata room number dinta, ba wani sha wahalar ganewa ba saboda kasa take ba sama ba, su biyu ne a dakin Zahra na bunk din sama, kallon Jawahir Zahra tayi tace "yana ganki da sassafe bayan yau bana tunanin za'ayi wani lectures, kalla time ko 9 fah batayi ba", zama Jawahir tayi bayan ta gaida roommate din Zahra wacce ke shirin sannan tace "just felt like coming to school ne shi yasa,wannan karan you resumed early, kuma har kin samu roommate", Zahra tace "toh ba abinda nakeyi a gida, there's nothing fun to do, komai kayi idon mom da dade na kai shi yasa kawai na dawo, roommate kuma da kika gani tama rigani zuwa, dan nazo na tarar da ita", Jawahir ta ada kai sannan tace "nawa ne school fees dinmu wannan karon", fada mata Zahra tayi tareda duk wani details da take bukata har time table dinsu ta nuna mata wanda aka tura a class group yayinda ita kuma tayiwa Dada message ta watsapp harda kara riban da zata samu
Kwanciya tayi a bunk din Zahra tace "bacci nakeji", Zahra tace "yi baccinki, nima aiki zanyi dan ban gama settling ba, me zakici idan na gama" Jawahir na gyara kwanciya tace "duk abinda kika dafa", da haka Zahra ta barta tayi bacci ta cigaba da aikin gyara kayanta
Koda Jawahir ta tashi Dada ya riga ya turo mata kudin dan yaga message din harda kari ya mata, tana gama cin abinci suka fita da Zahra zuwa cafe dan ta biya, an cika a cafe din dan haka suka nemi wuri daga gefe suka zauna suna hira duk da Jawahir ba wani maida hankali tayi kan hiran ba
Iya gajiya Sabreena ta gaji dan bata saba da wannan wahalar ba ga rana, yawo takeyi cikin school din ta rasa ma ta ina zata fara, seda ta fara zuwa admin block ta karbi admission letter dinta sannan ta fara registration, ganin process din ba sauki bane ta nemi wuri ta zauna bayan ta siya coke me sanyi da kore kishi, tayi dana sanin cewa Najib yayi zamanshi duk da ya nace seya rakota tace ya barshi, seda ta gama hutawa a lokacin har an kira sallah sannan ta tashi dan taje tayi sallah, da tambaya ta gane masallacin inda tayi alwallah a waje sannan ta shiga ciki, tana cikin sallah taji an zauna kusa da ita, sallame sallarta keda wuya Jawahir dake zaune gefe tace "kin idar?", juyowa Sabreena tayi tace "na idar", Jawahir tace "ara min hijabinki inyi sallah", kallon kayan jikin Jawahir Sabreena tayi, wando da top a jikinta se karamin veil data daura a kanta, cire hijabin dake jikinta tayi ta mikawa Jawahir wacce ta amsa tareda "Thank you" sannan ta mike ta tada nata sallan, koda ta idar bata wani tsaya dogon addu'a ba ta cire hijabin ta mikawa Sabreena tareda sake cewa "Thank you", sannan ta mike zata tafi Sabreena tayi saurin cewa "dan Allah ko zaki iya nuna department din Insurance", Jawahir "hanyar zanbi, muje", tafiya sukeyi Sabreena nata kallon Jawahir ganin kamannin ta da Mamah sosai, indai kasan Mamah kaga Jawahir kasan one way or the other sun hada wani abun da kamannin ya aci harta tafiyansu da magana
Juyowa Jawahir tayi tace "kinata kallona", Sabreena tayi murmushi tace "kinmin kamada new mommy dina", Jawahir tace "new mommy?", Sabreena ta ada kai sannan tace "yea, i mean my Abba's new wife", Jawahir bata kawo komai a rai ba tace "kinsan ance Allah bibbiyu yake halitta", Sabreena ta girgiza kai tace "naku kamannin ya aci sosai, harta tafiyarki da magana duk irin nata", murmushi kawai Jawahir tayi tace "what's your name?", ta amsa mata da "Sabreena", Jawahir tace "nice name, I'm Jawahir, are you new here?", Sabreena tace "yes", Jawahir tace "welcome to this amazing University", hira suka dingayi sama sama Jawahir na nuna mata wurare har suka karaso gaban department din Jawahir tace "mun iso", Sabreena ta kalli Jawahir tace "nagode sosai, without your help da bansan ya zanyi ba", 'yar dariya Jawahir tayi tace "don't mention, ai duk wani fresh student dole seda tambaya zesan wuri, Goodluck", "Thank you", Sabreena ta sake cewa sannan ta shige cikin department din yayinda Jawahir ta kara komawa kafe inda Zahra ke jiranta dan har yanzu layi be kai kansu ba
Najib ne zaune a parlour yana cin abinci yayinda Adil ke buga game na PS4, Yaya Aysha kuma na zaune gefe tana hira da Najib wanda gefa gefa Adil kesa musu baki, kallon Adil tayi tace "Adil ya kamata ka fara shirin tafiya dan kasan nan da sati uku za'a koma school, dole kaje kayi registration dinta Allah yasa ka samu admission", hankalinshi kan tv yace "Ummi karki damu, Sudan ai ba kaman Nigeria bane, yau idan naje sena gama komai na a yau, Nigeria ne zakiga mutum ya jera sati daya zuwa biyu yana registration", Najib ya kaa kai bayan ya cika baki da abinci yace "hakane kam" Adil ya kalli Najib yace "don't talk with food in your mouth, that's disgusting", Yaya Aysha dake jinsu tace "fada mishi, tinda shi haryau ya kasa girma", ya kalli Yaya Aysha yace "wallahi Ummi a gabanki kawai nake wannan duka", ta harareshi tareda cewa "saboda ka raina ni ba", yace "a'a saboda ke kadaice wacce idan ina gabanki nake jina kaman yaro", Adil ya kyalkyale da dariya yace "lokacin da wasu suke so su girma wani ke maida kanshi yaro", Najib yace "naji"
Da sallama Yusuf ya shigo duk suka nutsu sannan suka gaishe shi ya amsa bayan ya zauna kusa da Yaya Aysha inda ta tashi dan kawo mai ruwa, seda yasha ya kore kishi sannan ya kalli Najib yace "seka shirya by next week zaka wuce Abuja, na samar ma aiki a FIRS kuma alhamdulillah an samu saboda suna daukan sababbin ma'aikata, Monday zasu ma interview duk da Alhaji Bala yace kar na damu akwai vacancy kuma Inshallah ka samu ma", dadi Najib yaji sosai harda rungume shi dan be taba tunanin mahaifinshi na nema mishi aiki ba se yau, and he really appreciate it saboda it came as a surprise", bayan duk sun gama tayashi murna Yaya Aysha tace "amma banso yayi nisa dani ba, a Canada yayi karatu sedai ya dawo hutu, yanzu kuma ace a Abuja zeyi aiki ga Adil na shirin tafiya Sudan", Yusuf ya kalleta sannan ya saki murmushi yace "ki kokarta ki haifo mace, kinga koda yaushe seta kasance tare dake, ko ya kukace yarana", Najib yace "gaskiya ne Abba, hakan ya dace ayi kawai 100%", da sauri Adil yace "ban yarda ba, ace a 18yrs anmin kanwa, banso, nine dai auta ko kunaso", dariya sukayi Yaya Aysha tace "ai Adil kasha kuruminka, ni a wannan age din ina naga ta haihuwa, koda Allah ya bani Allah ya raya minku ya muku albarka", duk suka amsa da "ameen", sannan sukaci gaba da hira
A gajiye Sabreena ta dawo gida, ba kowa a parlour dan haka ta wuce dakin da aka bata ta dinga kwana kafin ta koma gida, wanka tayi ta canza kaya sannan ta fice zuwa kitchen inda taga Yaya Aysha kokarin hada abincin dare, gaisheta tayi ta amsa da murmushi tareda cewa " en makaranta, har kin dawo, ince dai anci karfin registration din", Sabreena ta jingina da counter tace "inafa, ko ina naje layi, ga rana, ai registration dinnan seya kai sati, gashi koda na samu naje class ma ba'ayi lectures ba", Yaya Aysha tace "kila se zuwa next week lectures zeyi karfi, duba cikin oven na ajiye miki abincinki", zuwa tayi ta bude ta ciro sannan ta dauki a fridge ta fice zuwa parlour, zamanta keda wuya sega Najib yace "a'a university student", ta harare shi tareda cewa "shine baka fada min haka registration din keda wuya ba", ya daga hannu sama yace "kefa kikace karna rakaki, kuma wuyanshi yasa nace zan rakaki saboda komai ya miki sauki", batace komai ta fara cin abincinta yace "I'm going to Abuja by next week", da sauri ta kalleshi yace "Abba ya samar min aiki", cike da jin dadi tace "wow, congrats, I'm happy for you", yace "Thank you", hira suka farayi inda take bashi labarin ta hadu da me kama da Mamah sunan yarinyar Jawahir, murmushi yayi yace "she's my cousin", ta kalleshi tana processing abinda yace sannan ta zaro ido waje tace "u mean she's my new mommy's daughter", ya kada kai tace "and that makes us sisters", ya kara kaa kai, out of words tace "wow, how comes I didn't know about her, infact batamazo wedding din ba", ya daga kafada yace "I told it's somehow complicated but maybe should ask your new mummy", ya fada yana murmushi tace "I still can't believe it, now I have a sister", tashi yayi ya nufi hanyar kitchen yana cewa "You better believe it"
Girgiza kai tayi taci gaba da cin abincinta dan kuwa wannan labari da taji yanzu ya girmama

UWA TA GARI - 25 - Wattpad
NOT EDITED
Sati daya kenan da suka koma school, a kullum se Sabreena tayi yawo cikin makaranta neman Jawahir amma bata ganin ta kuma batasan course din da takeyi ba balle taje department dinsu, da taimakon wata course mate Halima ta samu ta gama registration dinta, kuma kasancewar yau Friday take shirin komawa gida, sati dayan da tana Mamah ya cika
A bangaren Mamah amarci sukeci hankali kwance, cikin sati daya tayi kyau abinta dan kuwa a yanzu batada wani matsala sena Jawahir dan tana yawan kiran layinta amma baya shiga, abinda batasani ba shine Jawahir a call divert tasa numban Mamah dan bataso wani abu ya haata da new family din Mamah
Mamah zagewa tayi a cikin dan yiwa Sabreena favourite alkubus dinta sanin cewar yau zata dawo, Abba tin da akayi auren ya dau hutun sati daya daga wurin aiki ita kuma Mamah hutun wata daya ta dauka, Baba Salamatu bayan biki da kwana uku ta koma kauyen su zaman yaranta da jikokin ta, ba yanda Mamah batayi da ita zauna ba tace tafiya zatayi tinda yanzu Mamah tayi aure, alkhairi me yawa Mamah ta mata da Yaya Aysha danko Najib ba'a barshi a baya ba
Najib shirye shiryen tafiya Abuja yakeyi yana tunanin taya ze fadawa Jawahir ze koma Abuja da zama, haka kurum yake jin faduwar gaba duk sanda ya tuna ze tafi yabar Jawahir, gashi throughout satin nan tunaninta ya kasa barinshi kasancewar basu hadu ba kuma basuyi waya ba, be dauki hakan komai ba dan a ganinshi he only cares for her ne as a brother and nothing, one thing she's sure about shine ya fara developing feelings ma Sabreena, dan kuwa idan yana tare da ita wani nutsuwa da nishadi yakeji yana saukar mishi musamman ma idan ya fara takura mata tana bataso

cewa "she's nice, just like her mom", seda sukayi rabin hanya sannan Jawahir ta tsaya ta juyo ta kalli Sabreena tace "do you mind if we just take snacks and drinks, restaurant din da nake cin abinci basu bude ba", ta fada tana nuna wani restaurant da yake nan a kulle, kallon wurin Sabreena tayi tace "I don't mind, let's have some snacks kawai", da haka suka karasa wani shago inda Jawahir tace a bata meat pie da coke sannan ta juya ta tambayi Sabreena wacce ke kokarin ciro kudi daga jaka abinda takeso, dagowa tayi tace "egg roll da lacasera", seda Jawahir ta gama siya ta biya kudi sannan ta Kaman yadda Farida tayi kudirin zuwa Katsina seda taje, koda ta fadawa Dada zata bikin kawarta Katsina be hanata ba harda bata gudunmawa takai, ita da Nafisa da Zulaika suka dau hanyar Katsina, sun samu ganin malamin da sukaje nema sedai ba biyan bukata dan shima cewa yayi ta hakura saboda Jawahir bazata bata saukar da kai ba kaman yadda Farida keso, Farida taji haushin wannan maganar dan haka ta bukaci a illata rayuwar ta indai wannan baze gagara ba, murmushi malamin yayi yace baze gagara ba dan already rayuwarta ma na kan hanyar bata so ta kwantar da hankalinta, wani garin magani ya bata yace ta zubawa Jawahir a abinsha indai har tasha toh an gama magana, duk da batasamu biyan bukata yadda takeso ba wannan dinma ya faranta mata rai, haka suka dawo gida inda Farida ke neman aikata kudirin ta na Allah wadar (Allah ka kiyashemu mugun hali)
Washegari da misalin karfe daya Jawahir ta shirya cikin riga da wando sannan ta dauko hijabin Islamiyyanta ta daura akai ta fice, bata dauki mota ba dan tasan cewar Najib zezo daukanta, koda ta taje Islamiyya Khadijah ta riga tazo nan suka zauna suna muraji'an karatun da aka musu last week har malaminsu ya shigo, bayan sun gama tilawa aka kara musu yace su dauko hadisin su yau hadisi zasuyi, Jawahir ta nutsu kasancewar tanason hadisi sosai, malamin ya fara da cewa "        (    )    :        : ( )     : (  )     : (  )      : (    ) 
Wato an karbo daga Bahaza dan Hakeem daga babanshi daga kuma kakanshi (ma'awiya bin hayda) Allah ya kara musu yarda yace : Ya Rasulullah wanene yafi cancanta ayima biyayya? se yace (mahaifiyarka), na sake tambayarshi na biyu wanene yafi cancanta ayima biyayya? se yace (mahaifiyarka), na uku na tambayeshi waye kuma yafi cancanta ayima biyayya? yace (mahaifiyarka), se na sake tambayarshi na hudu se yace (mahaifinka sannan wanda yafi kusada kai wanda yafi kusada kai)
Wato seda yace ayima mahaifiya biyayya sau uku sannan yace mahaifi se kuma wanda yafi kusa da kai wanda yafi kusa da kai
Wannan hadisi yana nuna mana cewar komai zakayi mahaifiya itace farko, kuyi mata biyayya, kubi maganar ta, saboda mahaifiya ba abin wasa bace, bari na baku wani tarihi, cewar malam "Wani bawan Allah ne ya rasu akaje jana'izar shi kasa taki karbar shi, se akaje wurin Annabi Muhammad SAW akace "ya manzon Allah, ga wani bawa nan ya rasu amma kasa taki karbar shi", se manzon Allah Sallallahu alaihi Wasallama yace, "aje a samu iyalanshi aji ko yana aikata wani abu", se akaje aka samu iyalanshi amma sukace babu wani abu da yake aikatawa, se manzon Allah ya tambaya "shin mahaifiyar shi nada rai?", akace "eh Ya manzon Allah", yace "toh aje a tambayi mahaifiyarshi ko wani laifi ya taba mata", da aka tambayi mahaifiyarshi se tace ita babu abinda ya mata, se manzon Allah yace "a'a ta dai yi tunani babu abinda yake mata da har ranta kedan sosuwa", se tace "babu abinda yake min, amma tabbas akwai abinda yakeyi wanda yakesa raina sosuwa duk da ni bawai na daukeshi laifi bane amma idan yayi nakan ji ba dadi a raina, se raina ya sosu", se aka tambaye ta wani abu kenan, se tace "wato danta ya kasance idan ze siya abu, allal misali ze siya atampha toh se ya siyo guda biyu, ita daya matarshi daya amma fa na matarshi yanafin nata tsada, toh wannan abin yana sosa mata rai duk da bata taba furta mishi ba", se manzon Allah yace "toh idan ba kin yafe mishi wannan laifin ba kasa bazata taba karbar shi ba", shiru duka ajin sukayi suna jimamin wannan tarihi malam yacigaba da cewa " ga wani tarihi kuma na wani bawan Allah da mahaifiyarshi", " Wani bawan Allah ne yaje wurin manzon Allah Sallallahu alaihi Wasallama goye da mahaifiyarshi a baya, se yace "ya manzon Allah, ga mahaifiyata, ta tsufa nike mata wanka, in bata abinci, in bata ruwa sannan in goyata inje duk inda zani da ita, shin ya manzon Allah na biyata? ki taimakawa rayuwata Mamah, banson na mutu ina me saa miki, wallahi zan canza Mamah, infact nama canza daga yau, I know I've said so many hurtful things to you, I know I'm not a good girl, nasan da ace bakida tawakkali da yanzu kin kamu da hawan jini duk saboda ni, please Mamah I need you to sincerely forgive me for my wrong doings, Mamah remember I'm your only daughter, you wouldn't want me to go astray would you?, girgiza kai Mamah tayi Jawahir cikin kuka tayi murmushi sannan tace "then please forgive me", kowa a parloun seda jikinshi yayi sanyi jin maganganun Jawahir, kuka sosai Mamah keyi tace "Jawahir I've forgiven you, na yafe miki, ni dama bakimun komai ba, dan haka ki kwantar da hankalinki kinji baby na", murmushi Jawahir tayi badan ta gamsu da abinda Mamah tace ba, dan haka ta saura yanda take tana cewa "no Mamah, baki yafemin ba tinda banji a jikina ba", Najib da tun shigowarsu ko uhm bece ba balle uhm uhm ya mike yazo kusa da Jawahir yasa hannu ya mikar da ita da kyar yana cewa "tinda tace ta yafe miki ta yafe miki ne, ki daina kukan hakanan zakisawa kanki ciwo", girgiza mishi kai tayi tana rike dashi tace "no Yaya Najib ka bari in nemi gafarar mahaifiyata koh na samu rahamar ubangiji, dan Allah kar ka hanani Yaya Najib", rikota yayi da kyau yace "Jawahir look at me", dago jajayen idanuwanta tayi ta kalleshi yace "kinaso ki sani kuka ne?", ta girgiza kai yace "I don't want to see you cry, it hurts me so much dan Allah Jawahir ya isa haka Aunty na tace ta yafe miki", kallon Mamah dake kallonsu tayi tace "da gaske kin yafe mun", Mamah ta kaa kai Jawahir ta maida hankalinta kan Najib tace "pls take me home", babu wanda ya hanata tafiya dan haka Najib yaja hannunta suka fita

UWA TA GARI - 27 - Wattpad
A gaban gidansu yayi parking sannan ya juyo ya kalleta, ta daina kuka yanzu, sai jan hanci da takeyi tareda ajiyar zuciya wanda zesa kowa ya kalleta yasan cewar taci kuka, ruwa ya dauko a gefenshi ya mika mata, ba musu ta amsa takai baki, seda ta kusa shanyewa sannan ta cire daga bakinta tareda sauke numfashi sannan ta kalleshi da murmushin da iyakar shi lee tace "thanks for today", shima murmushin yayi yace "u are welcome", shiru sukayi gabadayansu kowa da abinda yake tunani, jin shirin yayi yawa tace "Ya Najib zan shiga ciki, zakazo gobe koh?", kallonta yayi ya girgiza kai alamar "a'a", da sauri tace "meyasa?", kaman wanda beson yin magana yace "I'm traveling to Abuja tomorrow, bazan samu zuwa ba", shiru tayi batace komai ba ya cigaba da cewa " Abba ne ya sama min aiki a Abuja a FIRS, I'm having an interview on Monday so I'm leaving tomorrow", kallonshi tayi tace "yaushe zaka dawo", ya daga kafada tareda girgiza kai yace "I'm not sure, I can start working immediately, it depends", a hankali tace "Allah ya baka sa'a yasa ka samu abinda zakaje nema", yaji dadin addu'ar ta dan haka yace "ameen", fuskarsa dauke da murmushi, daga haka duk sukayi shiru
Sunfi minti biyar ba wanda yayi magana cikinsu har seda yaga an fara kiran sallar magrib sannan yace "an fara kiran sallah I need to go", kallonshi tayi idanunta cike da hawaye tace "I'm going to miss you", cike da zolaya yace "i know", hararar shi tayi wanda ita kanta batasan tayi ba, murmushi kawai ya mata sannan yace "I will surely miss you too, but don't worry whenever I'm less busy zan dinga kiranki muna gaisawa" ta kaa mishi tareda cewa "promise?", yace "i promise", sannan yaci gaba da cewa "pls ki dinga zuwa Islamiyya banda shiririta, ki dinga zuwa wurin Mamah kuna gaisawa tinda bakyason zuwa wurin Ummi sannan ido you need anything don't hesitate to call me", sunkuyar da kanta tayi tace "bawai banason zuwa bane, bana samun lokaci ne, amma Inshallah zanje", yace "shikenan, you don't have to explain yourself, bari naje karna rasa jam'i", "toh", tace sannan ta fita daga motar ta zagaya ta side dinshi tana daga mishi hannu, shima hannu ya daga mata sannan ya wuce, seda ta daina ganin motarshi sannan ta shige gida tana goge guntun kwallar ta dake neman zubowa
A parlor ta hadu da Fareeda, sannu da gida ta mata duk da tasan ba amsa wa zatayi ba amma ga mamakin ta setaga ta amsa mata fuska a sake, mamaki ne ya kama Jawahir a zuciyarta tace "hala dai wannan ma yau taji wani hadisin dake magana kan kyautatawa mutane ne kaman yadda nima naji hadisi akan uwa?", harta shige daki tana tunanin canzawar Fareeda, cire kayan jikinta tayi sannan tayi wanka tareda dauro alwallah tazo tasa kaya marasa nauyi sannan tayi sallar magrib, bata tashi kan sallayarta ba har seda taji anyi isha sannan, tashi tayi tayi sallan Isha sannan ta linke sallayarta ta fice daga dakin dan nemawa kanta abinda zataci
A dinning table ta hadu da Fareeda tana cin abinci, har lokacin Dada be dawo ba dan dama tasan baya dawowa da wuri, da sauri ta juya zata koma daki saboda gudun surutun Fareeda taji Fareeda ta kirata, ba yanda ta iya haka ta juyo ta karaso wurin Fareeda tace "ga abinci nan kici", da mamaki Jawahir tace "yau kuma dani akayi abincin", Fareeda tace "kiyi hakuri, nasan bana kyauta miki amma gashi nan kici, daga yau zan dinga dora abinci dake a gidan nan, kinji", badan Jawahir taso ba ta dauki plate ta zuba jollof rice da fried plantain din da Fareeda tayi sannan ta bue fridge ta dauki coke, zata wuce Fareeda tayi saurin tashi tareda karasawa gaban fridge din ta dauko chi exotic tace "sha wannan, yafi sanyi, coke dinnan yanzu nasa, shiyasa ba sanyi", Jawahir bata musa ba ta ajiye coke din hannunta sannan ta karbi exotic din ta shige daki dan dama Allah Allah take ta bar wurin, tsalle Fareeda tayi harda tapi tareda cewa "Yes, Allah yasa tasha koda kadan ne", komawa tayi ta zauna kan dinning tana cewa "nama san zata sha danna lura tanason shan zaki", da wannan tunani taci gaba da cin abincinta hankali kwance dan kuwa tasan cewar burinta ya kusa cika
Bangaren Jawahir kuwa tana shiga daki taga wayanta na ringing, ajiye abincin hannunta tayi a side drawer sannan ta dau wayan dan duk a tunaninta Najib ne ya kirata, sedai wanda take tsammani bashi bane, sunan Jarood ta gani baro baro kan screen din wayanta seda taji buguwar zuciya kafin ta nutsu, ita kanta tasan bata kyauta mishi ba dan rabonta dashi anyi sati biyu kenan, tin sanda ta fara hulda da Najib ta manta da shafin Jarood, kara kira yayi ta gyara nutsuwarta kaman yana gabanta sannan ta daga tareda mishi sallama, amsa wa yayi yana cewa "haba Jawahir me duniya da har zaki shareni har na kusan sati biyu, ko kirana bakya yi, a school ma baki nemeni ba, kuma jiya na ganki a school da wata yarinya", a hankali tace "I'm sorry nayi busy ne kwana biyun nan shiyasa baka jina", kasancewar tayi kuka sosai a gidan mamah yasa muryanta be fita sosai yace "ya naji muryarki haka?", a hankali ta sake cewa "banjin dadi ne, yau da zazzai na tashi", cike da tausayi yace "ayyah, sorry dear, Allah ya baki lafiya, yanzu yaushe zamu hadu kenan, I am missing you", shiru ta danyi na wasu dakiku kafin tace "tommorow, by 7pm, amma bazan dade a waje ba kasan Dada ya dawo yana gari", cike da jin dadi yace "ok, Allah ya kaimu, se goben, wish you quick recovery", da haka ya kashe wayan ita kuma ta girgiza kai tana cewa "Jarood kenan", sannan ta dauki abincinta ta fara ci, ba tareda wani tunani ba ta dinga korawa da exotic din da Fareeda ta bata duk da taga alamar a bude take harta gama sannan ta tattare komai ta mayar kitchen ta dawo ta kwanta tana tunanin abinda ya faru yau, ga Mamah da take kokarin ganin ta yafe mata, ga Fareeda data ullo da wani sabon salo, ga Najib da a yanzu ta tabbata tana tsananin sonshi dan har bataso su rabu sannan kuma ga Jarood wanda take jin dadin kasancewa dashi badan komai ba sedan idan tana taredashi mantawa takeyi da damuwarta gabadaya, tana cikin wannan tunanin bacci ya dauke ta a nan inda take kwance

UWA TA GARI - 28 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Washegari da kasala Jawahir ta tashi daga bacci tareda ciwon kai me tsanani, tafi awa biyu kwance kan gado ba tareda ta motsa ba, ganin lokaci ya kure dan har takwas tayi yasa ta kokarta ta mike tareda daukan wayarta tayiwa Najib text kaman haka "Wherever you go and whatever you do
May sunny days and happy times follow you
Wish you all the best in life
Miss you", sannan ta tura mishi ta mike ta shiga bathroom, wanka tayi tayi brush sannan ta dauro alwallah ta fito, wayanta dake blinking kan gado ta dauka inda taga Najib ne ya mata reply da "thanks dear, on my way, miss you too", murmushi kawai tayi ta ajiye wayar sannan ta shirya ta shimfida sallaya ta fara sallah, tsintar kanta tayi da kasala wanda yasata yin raka'a ta biyu a zaune ba tareda ma tasan tayi ba, koda ta idar seta koma ta kwanta tanajin gajiya tattare da ita saboda sallar da tayi

tana fito da halshe waje saboda zafin da takeji ta kalli Jarood wanda ke mata dariya ta ata fuska sannan tace "shine baka fada min ba dadi ba", seda ya tsayar da dariyarshi sannan yace "akwai dadi, dan baki saba bane, amma kara sha kiji zakiji dadinshi", ta girgiza kai alamar bazata sha ba yace "c'mon, try once more kinga ni lokaci daya ma zan iya shanyewa kuma bazanji komai", tace "ai ka saba ne", yace "ai kema da haka zaki saba", daukan nashi yayi lokaci daya ya kai baki be sauke cup din ba seda ya shanye sannan ya kalleta yace "kin gani", itama dauka tayi zatayi irin nashi amma tana kaiwa baki ta sauke cup din tana cewa "bazan iya ba, it's bitter", yace "no, it's bitter sweet, yanzu dan baki saba bane shiyasa kike gani kaman it's bitter amma idan kika saba zakiga cewa ba komai a are not, tinda har kake karfafa min gwiwa insha wannan abun, amma don't worry I'm in for it", tana fadan haka ta dauki cup din gabanta ta kai baki, bata sauke ba seda takai karshe sannan ta tae baki UWA TA GARI - 29 - Wattpad

kuma na zauna, ita kuma bata lekoni ba", dariya kawai yayi ya tashi yana cewa "bari na watsa ruwa tinda naga alaman abincin yau be sauka ba tukun", seda ta haa mishi ruwan wanka ta ciro mishi jallabiya ta ajiye kan gado sannan ta fice zuwa kitchen inda taga har Sabreena ta kusa gama girkin
Washegari tin safe Dada ya tashi ya fito parlour ya zauna yana jiran tashin Jawahir dan kuwa kwata kwata ya kasa bacci a daren, tunanin irin tarbiyyar da yabawa Jawahir kawai yakeyi, shidai yasan yana kokari daidai gwargwado amma ya rasa me matsalar ta (ni kuwa nace Dada baka kokari, tinda baka sanin fitar ta balle shigowarta), Fareeda kuwa baccinta tasha harda minshari dan kuwa ita yau take juma'a a wurinta, koda ta tashi daga bacci taga ba Dada se tayi tunanin ya wuce aiki ne tinda yau Monday, fitowa tayi bayan tayi wanka, a parlour ta hadu dashi tace "dama kana gida, nayi tunanin ka fita", ba tareda ya kalleta ba hankalinshi kan magazine dinda ke hannunshi yace "ina jira Jawahir ta tashi daga bacci ne, I want to talk to her", cike da siyasa tace " shikenan bari na dora maka breakfast kafin ka fito daga wanka, maybe ta tashi by then", ajiye magazine din hannunshi yayi sannan ya mike tace "me kakeso for breakfast", yace "scrambled egg da coffee", har daki ta rakashi sannan ta dawo ta fara soya mishi kwai
Har yayi wanka ya shirya Jawahir bata tashi ba, ko kafin ya zauna kan dinning seda ya leka dakin ta yanda ya barta a daren jiya haka ya iske ta kwance, zama yayi sukayi breakfast tareda Fareeda duk da bashi da appetite amma haka ya tuttura kar Fareeda taga kaman bayason ci ne sannan ya dawo parlour yaci gaba da zaman jiran Jawahir dan alkawari ya daukarwa kanshi baze fita ba harse ya samu yin magana da ita
Jawahir se sha biyu na rana ta tashi tareda wani azababben ciwon kai, tafi minti biyar zaune kan gado tana rike da kanta sannan ta tashi dan yin wanka, ganin kayan jikinta yasata tunanin meyasa ta kwana da gown, nan take komai ya fara dawo mata ta koma ta zauna kan gado tareda hannu akai tace "na shiga uku ni Jawahir meya kaini? Allah yasa Dada be ganni a haka ba", daukan wayarta tayi dan duba lokaci taga har sha biyu ta gota ga uban missed calls daga Najib da Jarood da kuma Zahra da Rumana ga guda biyu na Sabreena, se yanzu ta tuna yau Monday, Najib zeje interview batayi wishing dinshi luck ba, suna da class 9 to 11 shima batayi attending ba maybe ma shiyasa su Zahra suka kira, girgiza kai tayi tana nadaman abinda ta aikata amma kuma it's too late, dana saninta ba abinda ze canza, haka ta tashi jiki ba kwari ta cire kayan jikinta sannan ta daura towel ta shige bathroom, wanka tayi ta dauro alwallah sannan ta fito, seda ta gama shiryawa sannan ta tuna jiya ma batayi magrib da isha ba ana binta bashi, haka ta dukufa salloli duk da ba wani maida hankali tayi kan salar ba saboda duk tunaninta ya rarrabu ta rasa meke mata dadi a duniya, sedai ta danganta abubuwan dake faruwa da ita da hakkin Mamah dake binta, dan bazata lakaba ma shedan abinda be ji ba be gani ba balle ace sharrin shaidan ne, wannan batada haufi hakkin Mamah ne ke binta ta wannan hanyar, ta dade tana addu'a kan Allah ya yafe mata ya kuma yaye mata wannan sabuwar rayuwar da take neman fadawa ciki harda hawayenta
Dada sake lekowa yayi yaga ko har yanzun bata tashi ba nan ya ganta kan sallaya, komawa parlour yayi ya zauna yana jiran fitowar ta
Taji shigowar Dada, dan haka data idar ta fita dan taje ta sameshi duk da gabanta na faduwa dan batasan me zataje ta tarar ba, a parlour ta ganshi zaune yana kallo amma kwata kwata hankalinshi bayakan tv, zama tayi jiki a sanyaye tace "ina wuni Dada", se a lokacin yasan ta fito ya kalleta sannan ya amsa mata da "lafiya lau, kin tashi lafiya?", kanta kasa tace "lafiya lau", daga nan duk sukayi shiru, kallonta Dada ya sakeyi yace "je kici abinci sekizo", kai ta girgiza alamar bazataci ba, be takura mata ba yace "shikenan toh tinda haka kika zaba", shiru tayi yaci gaba da cewa "Jawahir saboda ke yau banje aiki ba na zauna jiran tashin ki", dagowa tayi ta kalleshi ganin ita yake kallo tayi saurin maida kanta kasa ya cigaba da cewa "so nake ki fada min laifin me na miki kike nema ki bata rayuwarki, tarbiyya ce ban baki ba ko kuwa bana wadata ki ne a gida?, dan bangane ba, saboda ni a iya sanina na baki ilimi, tarbiyya da kuma gata, toh me kikeso Jawahir?", shiru tayi dan batada amsan da zata fada mai, ya sake cewa "ke nake saurare, me kikeso ki fada min indai har befi karfina ba zan miki shi saboda kibar rayuwar da kikasa kanki a ciki, dan abin naki kara gurbacewa yakeyi a kullum tinda yanzu har ya kaiga ki dauki giya kinasha kina 'ya mace kuma 'yar musulma haba Jawahir wannan ba yi bane", nan ma dai shiru tamai tana hawaye ya sake cewa "bazakiyi magana ba, koh so kike raina ya aci?, dan kinga ana lallaa ki", da sauri ta kalli Dada dan tunda take be taba amfani da wannan tone din ya mata magana, be taba daga mata murya ba amma yau gashi yana daga murya, a zuciyarta tayiwa Jarood Allah ya isa dan gani take da be kaita wannan wurin ba da bazata sha ba, a hankali cikin sanyin murya tana hawaye tace "Dada banda wani hujja da zan iya kare kaina akan abinda na aikata jiya sedai ina mai baka hakura kuma Inshallah na maka alkawarin bazan kara ba, na jiyan ma tsautsayi ne, Dada Jawahir din da ka sani a da da yanzu ba daya bane, wallahi na shiryu dan har Islamiyya na fara zuwa sedai bansan abinda yasa na aikata abin da nayi jiya ba", ta karashe tana kuka, kallonta ya tsaya yi dan tabbas baze manta ba ta taba fada mishi ta shiga Islamiyya amma kuma sedai ya za'ayi ta aikata abu kuma tace batasan dalilin da yasa ta aikatawa ba, wannan ai rainin wayo kawai takeso ta mishi, cike da bacin rai yace "wani shiryuwa kikayi, wannan shi ake kira tuban muzuru, bani da lokacin ki yanzu amma inaso ki sani nayi grounding dinki for two weeks, ko nan da gate banaso na ganki balle naji labarin kin fita, car keys, laptop da phone dinki duk zaki bani su yanzun nan sannan kuma Islamiyya kin daina zuwa zan nemo miki malami ya dinga zuwa gida yana miki karatu plus a halin yanzu banda tabbacin zan sake bari ki koma school sedai your behavior for this two weeks will determine whether you are going back to school or not, yanzu dauko min car keys, laptop da phone din", tashi tayi ta shige daki tana kuka duk ta tattaro abinda yace ta kawo ya mika mishi dan batasan me zatayi ba, wannan shine first time da Dada ya behave hakanan, shiyasa bata sani ba hakuri zata bashi ko kuma taurin kai zata mishi tace bazata bayar ba dan bata taa ganin bacin ranshi haka ba, shiyasa kawai ta dauko ta bashi dan batason a sake samun wani matsalan, dakinshi ya shiga ya ajiye sannan ya dau briefcase dinshi ya fice daga gidan rai bace, Fareeda dake leke daga dakin ta ta koma kan gado tana me jin haushin hukuncin da Dada ya yanke dan ita a ganinta taya za'ayi Jawahir tayi shaye shayen idan tana kulle a gida, wannan dalilin yasa ta kudurtawa ranta bawa Dada hakuri ya bari Jawahir taci gaba da zuwa school saboda kar lectures ya wuceta
Jawahir kam dakinta ta koma tasa makulli ta fada kan gado tana kuka tareda nadamar abinda ta aikata, babu wanda take blame irin Jarood dan a ganinta shi ya jata

UWA TA GARI - 30 - Wattpad
Sati daya kenan da Dada ya hana Jawahir zuwa ko ina, tayi baki ta rame dan koh abincin kirki bataci, bata fita daga dakinta, daga sallah se barci, gashi a halin yanzu babu abinda take sha'awa irin taga ta kara shan abinda tasha sedai ba yanda za'ayi ta samu, wannan dalilin yasa ta maida hankalinta kan kwayoyin da Jarood ya bata kwanakin baya ba tareda ta damu da duba expiring date ba dan yanzu tama kusa gama shanyesu, be wuce pills uku zuwa hudu ya rage mata ba wanda wannan yasa hankalinta mugun tashi dan idan ya kare batasan a ina zata samu wani ba tinda yar yanzu Dada ko kallon inda take ma bayayi balle ya saurare ta
Fareeda ba irin maganan da batama Dada ba amma ya nuna mata shifa be tashi maida wa Jawahir kayanta ba sannan har yanzu be amince ta fita ba dan kuwa jira yake Jawahir ta biyo shi ta bashi hakuri sedai ita ko ganin Dadan ma bata yi dan gani take kaman yanzu be damu da ita ba saboda ta soma shaye shaye shi yasa bata damu da binshi ba, Fareeda ganin idan ta zauna komai ze kwabe mata seta dauki niyyar zuwa wurin Naja'atu mahaifiyar Dada ta fada mata ko zatayi mishi magana dan bata shirya barnar kudin ta a banza ba domin kuwa ba karamin kudi ta ajiyewa malamin ba
Najib da Mamah sunfi kowa damuwa kan rashin samun Jawahir a waya, ba kaman Najib dayakeso ya fada mata cewar ya samu aiki harma ya fara an bashi office, sedai duk sanda ze kira wayarta not reachable yakeji, wannan dalilin yasa ya dawo gida weekend dan kawai ya samu ganawa da Jawahir, sosai yasha fada wurin Abba da Ummi kan tun ba'a kai ko ina ba ya fara wasa da aikinshi, in ba haka ba mena dawowa weekend sati daya da fara aiki, shidai hakuri kawai ya basu ba tareda ya fada musu dalilin shi na dawowa ba domin burinshi be wuce ya gana da Jawahir ba yaji koh lafiya
Bangaren Mamah ma hankalinta ba karamin tashi yayi ba da Najib ya fada mata ya kira Jawahir baya shiga kuma kullum yana cikin kira dan a rana siya kira bila adadin amma duk a banza dan ba shiga yakeyi ba, wannan dalilin yasa ta kira kawayen Jawahir Zahra da Rumana tace ko sunga Jawahir a school amma sukace kwana biyu kenan bata zuwa kuma sun kira wayarta baya shiga, itama bangaren Sabreena hakan ne, sosai Mamah ta shiga tashin hankali dan ta tabbata ba lafiya tinda har ba'a samun Jawahir a waya, gashi kuma bata zuwa school, Jawahir duk da ba gwanar chatting bace koda yaushe zaka samu wayarta a kunne, Abban Sabreena ne yayi kokarin kwantar mata da hankali sannan ya bata shawaran taje ta duba Jawahir, cewar ba lallai Dada yaso hakan ba zancen banza ne, be kamata akan 'yarta ta zauna ta nade hannu ba kaman wacce batada say akan Jawahir, da wannan ta samu kwarin gwiwa ta kira Najib danya rakata gidan Dada ganin Jawahir sedai batasan cewar shima kanshi abinda yakeso din kenan ba
Jarood ma dai a cikin tashin hankali yake dan tuni ya riga ya gama hada puzzle din da ya hana Jawahir zuwa school kuma phone dinta be shiga, ko ba'a fada mai ba yasan cewar Dada yaganta ko kuma yaji labari, tinda shine wanda yake tareda Jawahir the last time ta fito, shine ya fita da ita harta sha giya ta bugu duk da ba intention dinshi bane, ita ta nuna abinda takeso kenan, shikuma be takurawa kanshi wurin hanata ba dan a tunaninshi ta wannan hanyar ne kawai ze iya cimma burinshi kan Jawahir dan kuwa har yanzu yana nan da kudirin shi ba wai ya cire shi a rai bane
Yau Saturday, kuma yaune Mamah da Najib sukayi zasuje wurin Jawahir saboda washegari Najib ze koma bakin aikinshi, har gida Najib yaje ya dauki Mamah suka wuce gidan Dada, ganin kaman hankalinta ba'a kwance yake ba yata kokarin kwantar mata da hankali sedai ina Mamah hankalinta na kan Jawahir, wani hali take ciki? me zataje ta tarar? Is her Jawahir ok? tambayoyi ne kala kala ke popping a kanta wanda batada amsansu
A gaban gidan yayi parking sannan ya fito ya kwankwasa gate din sannan yaja baya ya tsaya zuciyarshi na bugawa, ba'a dau lokaci ba Gado yazo ya bude gate din, da yake ba sanin Najib yayi ba seya tsaya yana jira Najib yayi introducing kanshi tareda fada mishi wanda yazo nema, mika mishi hannu Najib yayi sukayi musabaha tareda gaidashi sannan yace "wurin Jawahir muka zo, tare muke da mahaifiyarta tana cikin mota", ya karasa yana nunama Gado motar, kallon motar Gado yayi sannan ya kalli Najib yace "bawan Allah kayi hakuri, wallahi mahaifinta seda yamin kashedi kan kar in bari kowa ya ganta, kar in bari ta fita haka kuma kar in bari a shiga wurinta da sunan anzo gaidata", da mamaki Najib yace "subhanallah, meyafaru aka yanke mata wannan tsastsauran hukunci haka?", dayake Gado nada labarin abinda ya faru se ya gyara tsayuwa ya kwashe komai ya fadawa Najib, ba karamin mamaki Najib yayi ba jin wai Jawahir ta fara shaye shaye, girgiza kanshi yayi yace "inaa, ban yarda ba", kallonshi Gado yayi yace "bawan Allah koni shaida ne dan a ranar data dawo nina bude mata gate ta shigo gidan nan tana layi sedai a gaskiya ina gani hajiyar gidance ta fadawa Alhaji dan bayanan ma sanda ita Jawahir din ta dawo", shiru Najib yayi dan besan me zaice ba, idanunshi sunyi jazir saboda bacin rai, be taba sanin lalacewar Jawahir ya kai nan ba, he was starting to trust her and now this, shaye shaye, su da suke maza ma basuyi se ita da take mace, Mamah data dade da fitowa daga motar kuma duk a kunnenta Gado ya bada labarin ta kalli Gado cikin dauriya tace "kaini wurin Jawahir ko ka kira min ita, dan yau bazan bar nan wurin ba harse naga 'yata, dan koh ba'a fada min ba nasan tana cikin kunci", shiru Gado yayi na en dakiku yana tunani sannan ya kalli Mamah yace "shikenan, bari nayiwa hajiyar gidan magana", bata kulashi ba ya wuce, ita kuwa takaici ne ke cinta ace duk mutuncin dake tsakanin iyayensu yau itace zata shiga gidan Osama ace se an tambayi hajiyar gidan, ai koh da aure ko ba aure akwai mutunci
Suna nan tsaye ya dawo yace "tace wai kuyi hakuri amma bazaku samu damar ganin Jawahir ba harse Alhaji ya bada izini", Najib da ranshi ya gama baci ya kalli Gado yace "koma kaje ka fada mata cewar mahaifiyar Jawahir ce tazo, kuma tanason ganawa da 'yarta", cikin sanyin jiki Gado yace "bawan Allah kayi hakuri, wallahi kona koma bazata saurareni ba dan hajiyar nan ba imani ne da ita ba, akwai abubuwa da dama dake faruwa a gidan dani ina gani amma na zabi nayi shiru saboda bazan iya tunkarar Alhaji da irin wannan zancen ba, sedai yau tinda Allah ya kawo ki Hajiya zan fada miki kodan ki samu ki nemarwa Jawahir mafita", cike da mamaki Mamah da Najib ke kallon Gado, cikin i'i'na Mamah tace "me kake nufi", fita yayi daga gidan yaja gate sannan ya gyara tsayuwa yace "kwanakin baya naje ina bawa flowers din da suka zagaye gidan ruwa, a dai dai wurin window din hajiyar gidan nan naji kaman tana waya tana cewa aikin malamin nan na Katsina yayi aiki duk da ban tabbatar ba naga alama, kunga idan bazan amfana da ita ba toh kowa ma baze amfana ba, ko ba'a fada min nasan Jawahir take nufi, dan dama ba wani shiri sukeyi da Jawahir in ba, kwanakin bayama har aiki takesa ita Jawahir din, su shara da wanke wanke da wanki, sedai kwana biyu kuma Jawahir din ta daina, wannan maganar ta dameni arai shi yasa na kasa mantawa sedai bani da wani mataki da zan iya dauka, kuma nasan ko na fadawa Alhaji ba lallai ya yarda ba", Najib shiru yayi dan beda ta cewa saboda shi be yarda da aikin malamai ba, a wurinshi superstition ne kawai, dan haka ya juya wurin Mamah dake hawaye dan kukan ma yaki fita yace "Aunty na, muje kawai, daga baya zamusan abinyi", girgiza mishi kai tayi tace "idan kaga nabar wurin nan toh da Jawahir ne dan yau Jawahir bazata kwana gidan nan ba, idan anyi duniya dan manzo sena tafi da 'yata, bazan barta matar uba na muzguna mata ba, idan ada nayi wauta da shakarci wannan karon bazanyi ba, zan jira anan har sai sun fito min da ita", ta karashe maganar ta tana sakin kuka me cin rai, janyo ta Najib yayi jikinshi yana bubbuga bayanta alamun lallashi sannan cikin sanyin murya yace "Aunty na toh muje mu dawo, nasan idan muka dawo zuwa dare lokacin Dada ya dawo", girgiza kai tayi ta nemi wuri a kasa wurin ta zauna, saukin abin ma area din ba mutane dayawa, Najib rasa yanda zeyi da ita yayi, ganin da gaske take ba tafiya zatayi ba seya dagata yace "indan bazaki tafi ba toh ki shiga mota ki zauna, har Allah ya kawo shi", haka kuwa sukayi, duk suka zauna a mota suna jiran dawowar Dada yayinda Gado ya koma cikin gida cike da jimami ganin halin da Mamah ke ciki

UWA TA GARI - 31 - Wattpad
Bayan zamansu da minti talatin sega motar Dada ta doso unguwar kasancewar ranar weekend ne kuma ba wani nisa yayi ba, tin daga nisa ya hango motar su Najib gaban gidanshi sedai ko kadan beyi tunanin su bane, Najib na ganin motar Dada yayi reverse din nashi motar saboda yaba Dada damar shiga da tashi gida, horn Dada yayi wanda yasa Gado tasowa da sauri yazo ya bude mishi gate, shiga yayi yayi parking a inda ya saba parking sannan ya kashe motar ya fito dan zuwa dubawa koh bainshi ne a waje, sedai ga mamakin shi Mamah ya gani tsaye a gabanshi tana mishi kallon da yasa shi shan jinin jikinshi
A hankali yace "Hindu kece?", harara ta watsa mai dan a ganinta silly question ya tambayeta, idan ba itace bace toh wacece da har yake tambaya, koh zaice be gane ta bane? ba tareda ta amsa shi ba tace "Jawahir nazo dauka", da mamaki ya kalleta yace "Jawahir kuma?", tace "eh", yayi shiru yana tunani sannan yace "ita tace kizo ki dauke ta ko dai yin kanki ne?", murmushin takaici tayi sannan tace "yin kaina ne, koh zaka hanani daukar 'yata ne?", yayi murmushi wanda baka isa kace ga irin murmushin da yayi ba sannan ya kalli Mamah yace "I'm sorry to say amma babu inda zaki da Jawahir, zaki iya ganinta ku zanta amma fa bazata biki ba dan Jawahir bazata je tayi agolanci a gidan wani ba, duk rintsi tana gidan mahaifinta inda aka fi sanin darajar ta", cike da kuluwa Mamah tace "inda akafi sanin darajar ta kuma duk da haka ake wulakanta ta, inda akafi sanin darajar ta amma kuma ba'a damu da ita ba, wani hali take, wani hali zata shiga duk ba'a damu da wannan ba, me taci, me tasha duk baka sani ba kuma a haka kake ikirarin anfi sanin darajar ta a nan, toh bari in fada maka wani abu ka sani, Hindun da ka sani ada ba itace tsaye a gaban ka yanzu ba, dan haka idan zaka tashi daga mafarkin da kakeyi na cewar zaka iya takani ka taka Jawahir kuma ka zauna lafiya gwara ka tashi daga wannan baccin dan kuwa wannan Hindun da kake gani a gaban ka yanzu ta wuce duk yadda kake tsammani ta wuce tunanin ka, akan Jawahir babu abinda bazata iya ba", mamaki ne ya kama Dada, kallon Mamah yakeyi yana bude baki yana rufe wa alamar yanaso yayi magana sedai babu abinda ke fitowa, haka Hindu ta canza? ya tambayi kanshi dan ya tabbata Hindun da ya sani a baya ko yatsa kasa mata a baki bazatayi motsi ba gudun kar ta cije wannan yatsar amma a yanayin da ya ganta yanzu ya tabbata bazayi shakkar cije yatsa ba idan mutum ya kuskura yasa matashi a baki
Najib kam yana tsaye yana kallon draman dake unfolding dan dama yasan da kyar idan Dada ze yarda su tafi da Jawahir, Fareeda dake kitchen tana girki taji kaman haniya a compound ta ajiye kitchen towel din da ke hannunta tareda kashe gas cooker dinta sannan ta fito dan ganin ko waye, sedai ta kasa karasawa ganin Dada tsaye da Mamah wacce koh ba'a fada mata ba tasan mahaifiyar Jawahir ce dan kuwa ga kamanni nan, nan take taji ranta ya aci sedai bata nuna ba ta aro murmushin dole ta orawa fuskarta sannan ta karasa gaban Dada babu kunya ta rungume shi tareda cewa "honey ashe ka dawo, baki kayi ne?", murmushi yayi sannan ya juya ya kalli Mamah yace "Hindu meet my lovely wife Fareeda, Fareeda meet my ex wife Jawahir's mother Hindu", cike da izgilanci Fareeda ta mikawa Mamah hannu sannan tace "oh, it's nice to finally meet you, I always wanted to meet the woman who gave birth to such a beautiful young lady", hararar ta Mamah tayi dan tuni Fareeda ta fice mata a rai tun bata hadu da ita ba jin abubuwan da tayiwa Jawahir balle yanzu data ganta gaba-daya se taji bata mata ba, dan haka ta maida attention dinta kan Dada tace "ni fa banzo nan dan ku batamin lokaci ba, daughter dina nazo dauka, kuma yau bazan bar gidan nan ba seda ita", shiru Dada yayi dan shidai harga Allah beda niyyar bata Jawahir, he can clearly remember sanda tace mishi ta yafe mishi Jawahir har abada yayi yanda yaga dama da ita a hospital sanda Jawahir ta fado daga kan dutse lokacin da taje hiking taji ciwo, sedai yasan cewar a ranar acin rai ne yasata wannan maganar shi yasa bazeyi using dinshi against her ba amma kuma duk da haka baze bata Jawahir ba
Ajiyar zuciya ya sauke sannan yace "kar ki bari mu tsaya muna ja in ja akan abinda bekai ya kawo ba, Jawahir ce dai bazan bayar ba kiyi hakuri", ganin ze wuce tayi saurin shan gabanshi tace "wallahi baka isa ba, I have every right to be with my daughter and I want my daughter now, like right now", ta fada idanunta na cikowa da hawaye dan gani take idan bata tafi da Jawahir yau ba setayi karamin hauka, Najib ganin yadda ake neman wulakanta antynshi yasa shi zuwa inda take tareda rikota yace "Aunty na muje gida, wannan mutumin baze yarda ki tafi da Jawahir ba, kiyi hakuri wata rana zamu dawo", girgiza mishi kai tayi tace "Najib kasan Allah?", ya kaa mata kai alaman eh tace "toh wallahi tallahi ka dai ji rantsuwar dan musulmi koh, bazan bar gidan nan ba seda Jawahir", shiru gabadayansu sukayi dan duk sun rasa me zasuce mata, Fareeda a zuciyarta addu'a kawai takeyi Allah yasa kar Dada ya yarda dan tafiso a bar mata Jawahir taci gaba da ata mata rayuwa, Dada kuwa jikinshi ne yayi sanyi jin rantsuwar da Mamah tayi, kallon Mamah yakeyi yaga duk tayi wujiga wujiga tayi wani iri ga idanunta duk sun kumbura alamar ta dade tana kuka, seda ya sauke ajiyar zuciya dan yasan hukuncin da ze yanke yanzu ba lallai ne yayi favor dinshi ba, sedai this is the only way daze iya solving wannan problem din ba tareda yayi sonkai ba, kallon Mamah yayi yace "shikenan, zan kira Jawahir ta zabi wurin wanda takeso ta zauna, sedai inaso ki sani bazan takura mata ba, idan ta nuna wurina takeso taci gaba da zama so be it, dole ki hakura, idan kuma tace wurin ki zata zauna shikenan, duk abinda ze biyo baya ba ruwana na zame hannuna a ciki dan i won't be responsible", without thinking twice Mamah tace "naji na yarda", Dada yace "shikenan, bismilla mu shiga ciki", nan Dada da Fareeda wacce duk ranta ke ajagule sukayi gaba inda Mamah da Najib ke biye dasu a baya har cikin parlour inda duk suka nemi wuri suka zauna sannan Dada ya kalli Fareeda yace "kiran min Jawahir"
Tashi Fareeda tayi tana turo baki gaba tayi hanyar dakin Jawahir, ba tareda sallama koh knocking ba ta bude dakin Jawahir inda ta ganta kwance rigingine kan gado tana kallon ceiling, tayi zurfi sosai cikin tunani da gaba-daya she's oblivious to what is happening around her, cike da jin haushi Fareeda ta karasa gaban gadon sannan tasa hannu ta zubawa Jawahir kyakyawan duka a cinya kasancewar guntun riga ne a jikinta, da sauri Jawahir ta tashi zaune tana susa cinyarta da har yayi ja tareda kallon wacce ta dake ta, ganin Fareeda tsaye gaba-daya se haushin ta da takeji tuntuni na fadawa Dada tayi shaye shaye ya taso mata da batasan sanda tace "bakida hankali ne zaki dakeni a cinya, koh bakisan da zafi ba", baki bude Fareeda ke kallon Jawahir sannan ta nuna kanta da yatsa tace "ni kike cewa banda hankali", hararta Jawahir tayi sannan ta koma ta zauna tana janyo pillow dan kara kwanciya Fareeda da takaici ya isheta tace "ai se ki tashi mahaifinki na kiranki, yana parlor", da fadan wannan ta fice rai bace ta bar Jawahir zaune wacce ke tunanin yau kuma da wacce Dada yazo, kodai ya hakura ne yanzu ze bata wayanta da kuma motarta da laptop dinta sannan yace she's free to go back to school on Monday, girgiza kai tayi dan kawar da wannan tunanin ta tashi ta canza kayan jikinta zuwa doguwar riga na atampha sannan ta daura dan kwalinshi ta fita, zaune taga Dada, Mamah, Najib da Fareeda, jin motsin ta yasa duk suka juyo suka zuba mata idanu, Mamah da Najib mamakin ramar da Jawahir tayi sukeyi, Dada kanshi seda abin ya bashi mamaki dan tun ranar da ya mata fada be sake bi ta kanta ba , ita kuwa tsayawa tayi tana binsu da kallo daya bayan daya gabanta na dukun uku uku dan gani takeyi kaman Dada ne ya kira Mamah da Najib dan ya fada musu abinda ta aikita

UWA TA GARI - 32 - Wattpad
Dada seda ya hadiye wani kullutu daya tsaya mai a wuya dan yasan with the way he treated Jawahir da wuya ta yarda ta zauna wurinshi, kallon ta yayi yace "nemi wuri ki zauna", zama tayi kan carpet gefen kujera kanta kasa da kuwa a tsorace take barin ma da taga Najib zaune a wurin gashi kuma ya kura mata idanu se kallonta yake
Dada ne yayi gyaran murya sannan yace "Jawahir ga mahaifiyar ki nan, tace ke tazo dauka ki koma wurinta da zama, ban bata go ahead ba amma nace ke zaki yanke inda kikeso ki zauna dan bazan takura miki ba, sedai kuma inaso ki sani idan kika bar nan she will be the one to take out all of your responsibilities but you are free to visit whenever you feel like because I will never ditch you", shiru Jawahir tayi tana kallonsu daya bayan daya, Fareeda ta fara kallo inda taga tsanarta kwance a idanun Fareeda, Najib ta kalla taga yana kallonta with pleading eye's, ko ba'a fada ba tasan zeso ta koma wurin Mamah da zama, kallon Mamah tayi inda taga hawaye kwance a idanunta, itama Mamah kallon Jawahir din takeyi, addu'a kawai takeyi Allah yasa Jawahir ta amince, koh kallon Dada Jawahir batayi ba dan kuwa ya fice mata arai dan gani take kaman be damu da ita
Tunani tayi idan ta koma wurin Mamah zata samu opportunity din da zata nemi gafarar Mamah sannu a hankali sannan she will be able to make up for all those bad days they share, sannan kuma za tafi shakuwa da Najib idan tana wurin, zata samu kuma taci gaba da zuwa school da Islamiyya din ta ba tareda wani ya hanata ba, plus komawarta wurin Mamah ze bata dama tayi bounding da family dinta, su Yaya Aysha kenan, sake kallon Mamah tayi a hankali Mamah ta mata mouthing "please", mayar da kanta tayi kasa tana goge kwallar da ya zubo mata sannan ta kalli Dada tace "zan bi Mamah", ajiyar zuciya Mamah ta sauke wanda batasan tana rike dashi ba, Najib kuwa seda murmushi ya subuce mishi, Fareeda kam da harara tabi Jawahir dan ba karamin bakin ciki take ciki ba a halin nan, cikin sanyin murya Dada yace "are you sure?", hoping she will say no, kaa mishi kai tayi tace "Yes" dan ko ba komai zata samu damar gyara kurakuranta sannan zata rabu da wannan munafukar Fareedar, kallon Mamah Dada yayi da murmushin da bekai ciki ba yace "you win, seta hada kayanta ku tafi, and please take good care of her", "I will", cewar Mamah dake kokarin mikewa ta karasa wurin Jawahir tace "muje na tayaki hada kayanki mu wuce", Jawahir bata musa mata ba ta mike itama suka shige dakin Jawahir, Fareeda ma tashi tayi kaman iska ta bar wurin zuwa nata dakin inda Dada shima ya shige nashi dakin dan yaji da abinda ke damunshi, nan suka bar Najib zaune a parlour inda shima ya dauki wayarshi ya fara danne danne
Suna shiga daki Jawahir ta nemi bakin gado ta zauna saboda jirin da takeji sakamakon rashin cin abinci da batayi kwana biyu, kallonta Mamah tayi tace "are you ok?", ta amsa mata da "yes", murmushi kwance a fuskar ta sannan tace "thanks for coming to get me", murmushi Mamah tayi dan kuwa wani irin farin ciki ta tsinci kanta a ciki, zama tayi gefen Jawahir sannan ta janyota jikinta ta rungume ta tareda cewa "you don't have to thank me, it's something I should have done long ago, but nevertheless I'm still here and I promise this time around you won't regret staying with me inshallah", kara rungume Mamah Jawahir tayi tana hawayen farin ciki tareda jin wata irin nutsuwa na saukar mata, janyeta Mamah tayi daga jikinta ta goge mata hawayen sannan tace "enough tears has been shed for a day, ya isa hakan nan, bari mu hada kayan kar mu bar Najib zaune", kaa kai Jawahir tayi sannan ta tashi ta dauko trolley dinta guda biyu babba da karami sannan suka fara haa duk wani necessary abu da suka san zata bukata dan Mamah tace base ta kwashi kaya dayawa ba
Suna gamawa Jawahir ta canza kayan jikinta sannan suka janyo trolley din suka fito, Najib na ganinsu ya mike ya karbi na hannun Mamah ya kai mota Jawahir na biye dashi a baya, a booth suka sa kayan, ta juyo zata koma ciki dan yiwa Dada sallama Najib ya riko hannunta, kallonshi tayi seta sauke kanta kasa saboda ganin yadda ya kura mata idanu, a hankali ya matso gaban ta kafin ya kai bakinshi daidai saitin kunnenta yace "I miss you baby girl", kasa motsawa tayi daga inda take dan jin yadda ya mata magana kaman yana mata raa a kunne wanda yasa buguwar zuciyarta ta karu dan har ji take kaman kila Najib ma na jin bugun zuciyarta saboda how close they are, kallonta yayi jin tayi shiru yace "didn't you miss me?", ta bude baki zatayi magana sukaji gyara murya a bayansu, sake mata hannu yayi ya juyo inda sukaga Mamah tsaye tana kallonsu da gira daya a dage alamar neman karin bayani, murmushi kawai Najib yayi tareda susa keya inda Jawahir kuma ta wayance da cewar "Mamah bari nawa Dada sallama in dawo", bata jira cewar Mamah ba ta shige gida, a kofar parlour taci karo da Dada yana kokarin fitowa ya kalleta yace "I was coming to you, na zata kin wuce ne", ta girgiza kai ya mika mata kayan dake hannunshi, phone dinta ne da laptop, da murna ta karba tace "thanks Dada", yace "please Jawahir be a very good girl kinji, dan Allah ki kiyaye abinda ya faru ranar nan banson na kara jin ance kiyi abinda ba daidai ba", cikin sanyin jiki tace "Inshallah Dada I will be of my best behavior", rungume ta yayi yace "I will miss you princess, always come visit kinji", ta kaa mishi kai alamar taji yace "je kiyiwa second mommy dinki sallama", ba dan taso ba ta wuce dakin Fareeda inda ta ganta kwance tana chatting amma ba alamar rahama a fuskar ta, a bakin kofa ta tsaya tace "Aunty Fareeda zan wuce", ba tareda Fareeda ta kalleta ba tace "Umma ta gaida A'isha", girgiza kai kawai Jawahir tayi ta fice daga dakin, har bakin gate Dada ya rakata, seda yaga shigarta mota sannan ya koma cikin gida yana me jin kewar tilon 'yarshi, wannan karon Jawahir ce ta zauna a gaba Mamah na zaune a baya tana chatting da Abban Sabreena inda take fada mishi tareda Jawahir zasu dawo, sosai ya mata murna sannan ya musu addu'ar kaiwa gida lafiya
Har gida Najib ya kaisu, a compound din gidan sukayi parking inda sukaga Sabreena tsaye already tana jiransu dan Abba ya fada mata da Jawahir za'azo dan shi kanshi yana gida, da sauri Sabreena taje ta rungume Jawahir da bata gama fitowa daga mota ba tace "welcome home sister", da mamaki Jawahir ke kallon Sabreena dan ranar da suka zo da Najib ta ganta amma saboda hankalinta baya jikinta se kwata kwata bata gane ita bace, murmushi Jawahir tayi tace "it's nice to see you again Sabreena, it's been a long time", kaa kai Sabreena tayi tace "yeah, we have alot to catch up on", da Najib daya gaji da tsayuwa dan tuni Mamah ta shige ciki ya kallesu yace "tun da an manta dani azo a kwashe kaya ni zan wuce", kallonshi Sabreena tayi ta turo mai baki gaba tareda cewa "mood spoiler", murmushi kawai yayi dan dama ya saba da rigimar Sabreena, booth ya bude ya sauke musu bags din Jawahir, Sabreena taja babban sannan ta kalli Jawahir tace "muje", karamin bag din Jawahir ta dauka zata bita Najib ya tsayar da ita, tsayawa tayi ba tareda da kalleshi ba yace "rest for now, I will come back later, because we have a lot of things to talk about, I need explanations", da sauri ta kalleshi tace "explanations about what?", be bata amsa ba yace "se nazo later", da fadar haka ya shige motarshi ya barta tsaye wurin dan har yanzu be manta da zancen shaye shayen da akace tayi ba
Cike da tunani kala kala taja trolley dinta ta shige ciki, se kallon gidan takeyi dan tsarin shi ya mata sosai, a parlour ta hadu da Sabreena da Mamah da Abba inda suke arguing kan inda Jawahir zata zauna, gaishe da Abba Jawahir tayi ya amsa mata da murmushi sannan ya kara da cewa "welcome home my daughter", murmushi tayi ta sunkuyar da kanta, Sabreena ta kalleta tace "yauwa sister please ki cewa Mamah ta bari muyi sharing din room daya, I know you won't mind", murmushi Jawahir ta mata, duk da tanason privacy amma she can't say no to Sabreena saboda ganin yadda ta marairaice mata, kallon Mamah tayi tace "zamu zauna daki daya, don't worry", shrugging shoulder's Mamah tayi tace "shikenan, bari naje nayi wanka, Sabreena please get her something to eat nasan tanajin yunwa", da "toh", Sabreena ta amsa mata sannan taja hannun Jawahir suka shiga dakinta tace "sister yi wanka bari na kawo miki abinci", zama Jawahir tayi kan gado tana yaye mafayinta tace "please something light nakeso", Sabreena tace "ok", sannan ta fice, seda Jawahir tayi wanka tasa kaya marasa nauyi tayi sallar la'asar sannan taci abincin da Sabreena ta ajiye mata, tana gamawa ta nemi wuri ta kwanta dan duk a gajiye take ga ciwo da kanta kenan, gashi she's still yarning for that stupid drink, da kyar ta samu bacci ya dauke ta dan tuni Sabreena ta fice dan taya Mamah aiki a kitchen
