UWA TA GARI - 33 - Page 2 - Wattpad
NOT EDITED
Zaune suke kan dinning Mamah da Abba se Sabreena da Jawahir suna cin dinner bayan duk sun idar da sallolin su, jefa jefa suna hira duk da Jawahir bata gama sakin jiki dasu ba amma suna kokarin janyota cikin hirar su, koda suka gama Sabreena da Jawahir ne suka tattare kwanikan sannan suka koma parlor suka zauna suna kallo
Kaman yadda Najib yayi mata alkawarin dawowa bayan isha se gashi yazo, da sallama ya shigo parlour duk ya gansu zazzaune, suka amsa mishi sallaman shi sannan ya nemi wuri ya zauna suka gaisa da Abba da Mamah sannan Jawahir da Sabreena ma suka gaishe shi ya amsa, Abba ne yace "gobe zaka koma bakin aikin ka koh?", yace "Inshallah Abba", Abba yace "toh Allah ya bada sa'a, amma wannan karon idan kaji a maida hankali dan Allah, ka zauna ka gina kanka a wurin kafin ma kayi tunanin dawowa gida", murmushi yayi yace "Inshallah Abba zan kiyaye, nagode", Mamah ce tace "bari na zubo maka abinci", yace "a'a yi zamanki, Sabreena ta zubomin", ai kuwa komawa tayi ta zauna Sabreena kuma ta tashi ta shige kitchen shikuma yabi bayanta ya zauna kan dinning, ko kaan Jawahir bata damu ba dan hankalinta ma yana kan wani maganan da yace mata zasuyi
A dinning kuwa hira sukeyi sosai shida Sabreena yana cin abinci, seda yayi kusan rabi sannan yace "Sabreena can I ask you a favor?", tace "sure, why not", seda yakai abinci bakin shi ya haiye sannan yace "please take care of Jawahir, sannan wasu halayen nata ki dinga kauda kai kaman rashin maganar ta, bata cika magana ba idan batason yi", murmushi Jawahir tayi tace "idan dai dan wannan ne karka damu, ai an riga an zama daya, I will treat her like my sister so you don't have to worry", yaji dadin maganan ta dan haka yace "Thank you very much Reena", murmushi tayi ba tareda ta amsa shi ba, nan sukaci gaba da hirar su har ya gama ta dauki plate din ta mayar kitchen, shikuma ya koma parlour ya zauna
Kallon Mamah yace "Aunty na inason yin magana da Jawahir idan ba damuwa", kallonshi tayi da mamaki tace "dan zakayi magana da 'yar uwarka kuma seka tambaye ni, jimin wani iyayi, sai kace da chan kana tambaya na", dariya duk ta basu ya sunkuyar da kai kasa Mamah ta kalli Jawahir tace "daughter tashi dauko mayafinki kije waje kiji me zaice", cikin sanyin jiki Jawahir ta tashi ta shige daki, mayafin Sabreena dake kan gado ta janyo ta yafa ta fito, koda ta fito baya parlour ya riga yayi waje, Sabreena kallon Jawahir tayi ganin itama tayi hanyar kofa, gaba-daya se taji ba dadi daga baya kuma se tayi la'akari da Jawahir in kanwarshi ce dan haka seta saki ranta taci gaba da kallonta
A zaune ta ganshi kan white plastic chair yana danna waya, karasawa tayi ta zauna kan empty chair din da ke gefenshi tace "Yaya Najib", dagowa yayi ya kalleta yace "sis, how are you feeling now", "I'm feeling good, just a like headache that's all", kaa kai yayi yace "Jawahir you disappointed me, kin sani?", a hankali ya girgiza kai alamar a'a ya sauke ajiyar zuciya sannan yace "why did you do it?", fuskarta cike da alamun tambaya tace "do what?", yafi minti biyu be bata amsa ba sannan ya kalleta yace "why did you get drunk, hell, what where you even thinking in the first place", ya karashe maganar muryarshi na nuna alamun bacin rai, tuni hawaye sun wanke mata fuska yace "ba kuka nace kimin ba, baki zaki bude ki fadamin meye dalilin ki na zuwa shan giya, me kika rasa me kikeso?", cikin kuka tace "wallahi yaya Najib believe me ni kaina bansan me yasa na sha ba, Jarood ne yace zamu fita and I didn't object, shine ya kaimu club yace a bashi his usual ni kuma a kawomin soft drink, bansan abinda yasa ba a wannan lokacin se naji nima inaso nasha abinda zesha din dan naji dadin da ke ciki, shine nima na karba", kallonta kawai yakeyi dan besan me zaice mata ba, it's her will, ita ta zabi ta sha bawai wani ne ya tilasta mata ba
Jin yayi shiru tace "Yaya Najib please forgive me wallahi I don't know what came over me", hannunta ya riko wanda ta hade wuri biyu alaman neman gafara yace "it's ok Jawahir, but promise me you won't drink that shit again", da sauri ta girgiza kai tareda zame hannunta tace "I'm sorry I can't promise you", da mamaki yace "why?", dan shi yanzu lamarin ta ya fara bashi tsoro, ba tareda ta kalli idanunshi ba tace "saboda its the thing I'm craving most right now, like ji nake kaman idan ban sha zanyi hauka, Yaya Najib I need your help, please let Mamah know that I need help, nasan cewar shan giya haramun ne, infact ada ko warinshi banaso Amma right now babu abinda nakeso kaman shi, yaya Najib ya zanyi da rayuwata?",ta karashe tana kuka me cin rai, tausayi ta bashi jin abinda ta fada, dan haka ya janyo tareda dora kanta kan kafadarshi yana bubbuga bayanta alaman lallashi, cikin sanyin murya yace "shiiii, stop crying, Inshallah everything will be ok, we will find a solution to this kinji", kaa mishi kai tayi tana jan hanci, handkerchief din dake hannunshi ya mika mata dan ta share hawayenta da kuma hancinta, karba tayi ta goge fuskarta sannan yace "I'm going back to Abuja tomorrow, but inshallah I will communicating with you and my aunty, sannan zanyiwa Aunty na magana because you need help Jawahir and inshallah we will help you, go back to school on Monday and if possible go to Islamiyya tomorrow kinji", a hankali tace "Inshallah, thank you very much Yaya Najib", murmushi yayi sannan yace "zan bari a kai Sabreena Islamiyya dinku so that you won't feel lonely", murmushi tayi tace "that's so thoughtful of you, thanks again", hancinta yaja yana cewa "stop thanking me, what are families for", murmushi tayi yace "there, keep smiling like that and stop crying, komai me wucewa ne kinji", ta kaa mishi kai, sannan yace "mu shiga ciki kar suka mun dade", tashi sukayi tana gaba yana biye da ita a baya
A parlour suka samesu zaune Sabreena har tayi wanka ta canza kaya, Najib yace "Sabreena gobe ki shirya tareda Jawahir zaku Islamiyya zan kira malaminsu yau in sanar dashi zuwanki", dadi Sabreena taji tace "Thank you Yaya", murmushi kawai ya mata sannan yace "ku shiga ciki zamuyi magana da Aunty na", mikewa Sabreena tayi tace "uhm, su yaya Najib masu Aunty, da bamu da Aunty da mun shiga uku", dariya duk sukayi banda Jawahir da murmushi kawai tayi duk da kuwa maganan Sabreena ya bata dariya amma batayi dan matsalar da take tattare dashi ma kawai ya isheta
Seda ya tabbatar sun shige daki sannan ya kalli Mamah, zeyi magana Abba yace "nima dai bari na baku wuri", da sauri Najib yace "a'a Abba yi zaman ka, dan muna bukatar shawara", alama Mamah tayi mishi daya zauna dan already ba abinda be sani ba saboda Mamah ta zanta mishi komai data dawo, zama yayi Najib ya kalli Mamah yace "Aunty na i think Jawahir needs help islamically like a kaita wurin malamin da aka san ze taimaka da addu'o'i saboda nima yanzu na gane cewar matsalar ta ba ordinary bane tinda she's not an addict, bawai she's addicted to drinking bane amma gashi yanzu lokaci daya yana nema ya zame mata matsala bayan so daya kawai tasha", kaa kai Mamah tayi tace "nima nayi wannan tunanin dan haka munyi magana da Abban Sabreena yace akwai wani abokin babanshi a kano, malami ne sosai, wurinshi mukeso mu kai Jawahir koh za'a samu dacewa amma se next weekend", hamdala Najib yayi sannan yace "mashallah Allah yasa a dace, sedai bazan samu binku ba saboda wannan karon bazan dawo ba", Abba yace "karka damu, kayi zamanka, kuma nasan duk abinda ake ciki Aunty zata sanar da kai, ka kwantar da hankalinka komai zeyi dede", se yanzu yaji hankalinshi ya kwanta yace "shikenan Allah ya bada sa'a, ni bari na wuce", kiransu Sabreena Mamah tayi suka fito suka mishi rakiya har bakin mota ya fice yana daga musu hannu, suna komawa ciki Mamah da Abba suka musu saida safe inda suma suka shige daki, seda Jawahir tayi wanka sannan ta dauko laptop dinta ta kunna musu money heist season 2 suka fara kallo
Washegari tareda Jawahir sukayi aikin gidan, Sabreena tayi shara da goge goge inda Jawahir kuma tayi wanke wanke, sannan suka zo suka tsaya suna taya Mamah hada breakfast, ba wanda yakai Mamah farin ciki dan sosai taga canji tattare da Jawahir, ada Jawahir batasan ta taya Mamah aiki ba amma yau gashi wai itace harda tsayawa tana kallon yadda Mamah ke girki, tareda suka gama sukayi setting dinning sannan Mamah tace duk suje suyi wanka, seda sukayi wanka suka shirya sannan suka zo sukayi breakfast, daga nan kuma suka koma daki sukaci gaba da kallonsu daga inda suka tsaya
Kaman yadda Najib yace haka kuwa tare sukaje Islamiyya, da yake ya riga yayiwa malaminsu bayanin Sabreena shi yasa ba'a samu wani matsala ba, sosai Khadijah taji dadin ganin Jawahir, koda ta tambayeta dalilin ta na rashin zuwa kwana biyu se cewa tayi batada lafiya ne, nan Khadijah tace "kwarai, gashi jikinki ya nuna kam, wannan kanwarki ce?", ta tambaya tana nuna Sabreena tace "eh, kanwata ce, sunanta Sabreena, Sabreena meet my friend Khadija she's married", da murmushi Sabreena tace "it's nice meeting you", zama sukayi sukaci gaba da hira kafin malam ya shigo, koda ya shigo ya jiki yayiwa Jawahir dan shima abinda Najib yace mishi kenan, karatu sukayi sosai a ranar kuma sosai Sabreena taji dadin Islamiyyan dan koh ba komai zata karu
Washegari ma tare sukaje school suka kuma dawo tare, Najib kuwa kullum yana kiransu yaji lafiyar su musamman ma Jawahir dayake tsoron kar taje tasha wani abun wacce ita kanta kokari kawai takeyi amma kuwa ji take kaman zata mutu, cikin en kwanakin nan tuni suka shaku da Sabreena kuma ba laifi yanzu tana dan sakewa Mamah tana zama ayi hira da ita harda dariya, Zahra da Rumana ma sunsan cewar Jawahir ta koma wurin Mamah kuma ita da Sabreena sisters ne dan haka suka dauki Sabreena kaman kawarsu itama
Jarood ba irin kiran da bayama Jawahir amma bata dauka, daga karshe ma a Black list tasa sunan shi sannan koh kadan bata yarda su hadu a school dan duk wani possible spot da tasan yana zama ko bin wurin bata bi
Yau friday, kuma yaune suke shirin dan gobe zasu Kano, kwana aya kawai zasuyi dan haka suka fada a Islamiyya cewar zasuyi tafiya se wani weekend din zasuzo

UWA TA GARI - 34 - Wattpad
Washegari da wuri suka gama ayyukan su dan yanzu sun raba aiki ne, yau idan Sabreena tayi shara da goge goge, Jawahir zatayi wanke wanke, washegari kuma se su canza Jawahir tayi shara da goge goge Sabreena kuma tayi wanke wanke, wannan tsarin Mamah ce ta ajiye musu shi kuma duk sukayi na'am da hakan
Seda sukayi breakfast sukayi wanka suka shirya sannan, Abba yayi driving dinsu zuwa airport inda sukayi boarding plane dinsu dan dama sunyi booking, a gidan mahaifiyar Abba kakar Sabreena suka sauka, sosai taji dadin ganinsu inda ta dinga wasa da Sabreena irin wasan kaka da jika dinnan sannan ta koma kan Jawahir itama ta mata wasa kafin ta koma ga Mamah da Abba, sosai Mamah ta duka kasa suka gaisa se sama mata albarka takeyi da yake bata taa ganinta ba dan koh lokacin bikin batasamu zuwa ba, shima Abba gaishe ta yayi ta amsa tanata sa musu albarka wanda yasasu jin dadi, me aikinta ta kira ta kawo musu kayan motsa baki yayinda hira ta barke tsakaninsu dan ko maganan hutawa ma basayi
Seda sukayi sallar azahar sannan suka ci abinci, nan Abba ke fadama mahaifiyar shi dalilin zuwansu kan nemawa Jawahir maganin matsalar da ke neman matsa mata dan da kyar ma ta iya kai sati dayan nan saboda wani lokacin har kuka take musu gashi koh a makaranta batasamu kuma ba'a siyarwa balle ta siya, sannan tareda Sabreena suke zuwa suke dawowa, bataso tayi abinda Sabreena zata fadawa Mamah har Mamah taji haushin ta shiyasa tayi kokari wurin ganin batasha din ba duk da ba sauki bane a wurinta, shiyasa koda Mamah ta mata maganan zuwa Kano bata musa ba tace ta amince aje din
Cike da tausaya wa ta kalli Mamah dake kwalla tace "yarinya ta karki damu, duk abinda da kikaga Allah ya jarabceki dashi ba komai bane mukaddari ne, kuma Allah baya takurawa bawa da abinda yafi karfin shi, ki goge kwallar ki dan Inshallahu komai yazo karshe, Malam Abdul aziz aminin baban Harun ne, Inshallah bayan sallar la'asar se kuje dan anfi samunshi a wannan lokacin, ku mishi bayani komai na tabbata baze rasa taimakon da ze baku ba kinji", gyada kai Mamah tayi tareda cewa "na gode sosai Hajiya Allah ya saka da alkhairi", murmushi kawai tayi tace "me na godiya kuma, ai yanzu Jawahir itama ta zama jikata, abinda zan tsaya na yiwa Sabreena itama shi zan mata babu wani banbanci tsakaninsu dan haka ma ki daina min godiya, zan kira shi malam Abdul aziz din saboda yasan da zuwanku", ta karashe tana daukar er nokia dinta danta kirashi
Duk wannan tauttaunawar da ake yi su Jawahir basa wurin dan suna daki a kwance wai su sun gaji bayan jirgi sukabi ba mota ba
Kamar yadda Hajiya tace haka kuwa akayi, seda duk suka sauke sallar la'asar sannan suka fice a motar da ake kai Hajiya duk inda takeson zuwa dan kuwa danta be rageta da komai ba, duk wani bukatu nata yana kokarin ganin ya sauke shi, a gida suka bar Sabreena da Hajiya inda Abba da Mamah da Jawahir kuma suka tafi, dama chan yasan da zuwansu, dan haka ba'a bata musu lokaci ba aka bari suka ganshi, babban dattijo ne dan kuwa ya tsufa sosai amma kuma yana gane mutane, wannan birkicewan da ake yi idan an tsufa duk beyishi ba, suna zama yayi murmushi dan tuni ya riga ya gama jin abinda ke tattare dasu, shikuma baiwar da Allah ya mishi kenan tun yana yaro, idan yaga mutum yana sanin damuwar dake tareda shi, a haka yake taimaka bayin Allah ba tareda ya karbi ko sisin su ba duk da shima bawai kudin ne dashi ba se dai akwai wadatar zuci, koh sadaka aka bashi kazo neman taimako beki ya dauki koh nawa bane ya baka dan kaje ka biya naka bukatun ka, shiyasa kwata kwata kudi be zama a hannunshi duk da manya manyan mutane na yawan aiko mishi da sadakan kudi, kayan abinci harma da sutura
Zama su Mamah sukayi sannan suka gaisheshi ya amsa musu da murmushi a fuskarshi sannan ya kalli Abba yace "a'a Harun ashe da rabon zamu gana, yaushe rabona dakai, ko ka shigo borno ma baka lekowa sedai ina ganin aike akai akai kuma ina godiya", murmushi Abba yayi kanshi kasa yace "Amin afuwa malam wallahi yanayin aiki ne amma Inshallah za'a gyara", kaa kai malam yayi sannan ya maida hankalinshi kan Mamah da Jawahir yace "sannunku da zuwa, koh a kawo ruwa ne?", da sauri Mamah tace "a'a malam wallahi alhamdulillah", kaa kai yayi sannan ya kalli Jawahir dake makale jikin Mamah yace "jikata sannu", dagowa tayi ta kalleshi sedai ta kasa amsa mishi dan kuwa ya mata kwarjini dayawa, murmushi yayi sannan ya kalli Mamah yace "Inshallah kukan ki ya kare, dan tun shigowarku naga abinda ke tafe daku musamman ma ke", ya nuna Mamah "kinsawa ranki damuwa dayawa amma Inshallah komai yazo karshe", kaa kqi Mamah tayi tana goge kwallar ta tace "Nagode Mallam", kallon Jawahir yayi yace "jikata sakacinki da ibada shiya janyo miki halin da kike ciki yanzu, danma mahaifiyarki tana tsaye a kanki da addu'a ba dare ba rana da abin yafi haka muni", hawaye Jawahir keyi dan tasan ba karya yayi ba
Gyara zama yayi sannan yace "matar mahaifinki ta taba baki lemu kika karba kika sha ba lallai ki tuna ba wannan lemun shine silar komai dan ba haka kawai yake ba, zan bari ayi miki rubuta se kisha, idan kika sha duk wani goba da aka sa miki a lemun nan zaki amayar dashi dan muddin baki amayar dashi ba bazaki taba daina shan kayan maye ba, bayan wannan akwai wasu rubutun da suma zan miki na tsari ki dinga sha, akwai wanda ake sha bayan sallar asuba da kuma wanda zakisha kafin ki kwanta, idan an kawo duk zan miki bayani", kaa kai Jawahir tayi duk suka hada baki wurin mishi godiya sannan yaci gaba da cewa "sannan akwai wani abokin ki da kuke tare dashi, ki kiyaye shi dan Yaron nan baya nufanki da alkhairi", seda taji faduwar gaba jin ya ambaci Jarood duk da be fadi suna ba tasan dashi yake, kuma dama tasan Jarood baya sonta da alkhairi dan abokin kwarai baze maka abinda Jarood ke mata ba sedai tana mamakin yadda akayi ya canza mata lokaci daya dan a da ba haka yake ba, yana kula da ita ne kaman kanwarshi dan har gidansu yake kaita, tasan kanwarshi kuma tasan mahaifiyarshi kuma suma duk sun santa amma yanzu dole ta watsar da Jarood dan ta tabbata idan tana taredashi bazata taba yin abinda tayi niyya na alkhairi ba
Nan Malam ya kira daya daga cikin dalilan shi ya basu abinda zasu rubuta a allo su wanke sannan yace "kuyi shi da yawa ga jarka chan se a dura a ciki, amma fah kuyi sauri kar a barsu zaune", nan yaron ya amsa mishi sannan ya dauki jarka biyu 5litre da goran faro ya fice, sosai su Mamah suka mishi godiya Abba ya mishi alkhairi me tarin yawa sannan fita suka zauna waje dan su jira rubutun yayinda wasu kuma suka shiga dan ganawa da Malam
Cikin awa aya aka kawo musu rubutun malam ya kara yi musu bayani sannan suka sake mishi godiya suka wuce
Suna zuwa gida suka korowa Hajiya yanda akayi ai kuwa tace basuga ta zama ba, nan tace Jawahir tasha wanda akace idan tasha zatayi amai, bata musu ba dan itama abin ya isheta, karba tayi hannun Mamah wacce ke miko mata, harta kai baki Mamah tace "kiyi bismilla", murmushi tayi dan ita tama manta sannan tayi bismilla ta kafa kai, seda tasha kusan rabi sannan ta ajiye sauran, duk kallonta sukeyi dan suga reaction dinta sedai ba wani reaction da suka gani, murmushi ta musu tace "I'm fine, it's
", ai kuwa bata gama magana ba zuciyarta ya fara tashi, tashi tayi zata toilet amma ta kasa dan gaba-daya ji tayi kafafuwanta sun kasa daukar ta, Hajiya ce ta kalleta cike da tausayawa tace "karki damu, zauna bari a kawo roba kiyi a ciki", da sauri Sabreena taje ta samo roba aikuwa tana sawa daidai bakin Jawahir Jawahir na amayar da abinda ke cikinta, seda ta amayar da abincin da taci tas sannan ta fara aman wani bakin abu me shegen yauki kaman majina, ta amayar dashi sosai kafin aman ya tsaya, ruwa aka bata ta kuskure bakinta sannan ta gyara zamanta kan kujera tana maida numfashi yayinda Sabreena kuma ta wuce toilet tayi flushing din aman sannan ta yarda robar a shara ta wanke hannunta tasa hand sanitizer sannan ta dawo, gaba-daya sun tauyawa Jawahir ganin yadda ta galabaita ba kaman Mamah da har kwalla seda tayi ganin only daughter dinta a wannan halin, tabbas duk inda yara suke muddin ba uwarsu a wurin toh fa basu da gata dan ba kowa bane ze kullar maka da amanar ka tsakani da Allah ba, goge kwallar ta tayi sannan ta kalli Sabreena da duk sukewa Jawahir sannu ganin yadda take ajiyar zuciya tace "Sabreena dan Allah taimakawa sister dinki tayi wanka kuyi sallah", da "toh" Sabreena ta amsa sannan ta taimakawa Jawahir suka shige daki shikuma Abba yace musu zashi masallaci dan already an kira sallah, kallon Mamah dake kokarin tashi Hajiya tayi tace "Hindu", Mamah tace "na'am", tareda komawa ta zauna Hajiya tace "ki rage damuwa kinji, banaso ina ganin ki cikin damuwa, yanzu tinda Allah yasa komai yazo da sauki seki fidda komai a ranki ki tsaida hankalinki wuri aya ki rike yaranki da mijinki kinji", kaa kai Mamah tayi tana godiya ga Allah daya bata sirika me saukin kai irin wannan, tashi tayi sannan ta taimakawa Hajiya itama ta mike suka shiga ciki saboda gabatar da farilla

Sosai Jawahir taji dadin rubutun da tasha dan kuwa jin kanta takeyi kaman wacce aka sauke dutsen dala daga kanta, a ranar tayi baccin da ta dade batayi irinshi ba, bangaren Mamah tana idar da sallolin ta ta dauki waya ta kira Najib ta shaida mishi nasarar da aka samu wanda ya nuna farin cikinshi sosai har Mamah tana mamakin abinda yasa yanzu Najib ya damu da Jawahir bayan tasan cewar a da ko kallon inda Jawahir take baya yi, tana ajiye wayar ta tashi ta wuce kitchen ta hadowa Jawahir abinci ta kai mata sedai koda taje Jawahir ta riga da tayi bacci saboda tayi weak sosai batajin zata iya yin wani abu, shiyasa tana idar da sallar isha ta nemi wuri ta kwanta ba tareda ta nemi abinci ba, haka Mamah ta hakura tayi addu'a ta tofa mata sannan suka fito tareda Sabreena wacce ke chatting da Najib tana fada mishi Jawahir dinma tayi bacci, Abba na dawowa duk sukaci abinci sannan suka zauna zaman hira, basu suka tashi ba se wuraren karfe goma, lokacin da duk suka nema makwanci lokacin Mamah ta dukufa kan sallayarta tana kai kukanta ga ubangijinta wurin nemawa Jawahir yafiya tareda shiriya, sosai ta dade tana addu'a har seda kafafuwanta suka soma mata zugi saboda tsayuwa sannan ta sallame ta nemi wuri ta kwanta tanajin wani sanyi a ranta dan a yanzu kam komai yazo mata da sauki, abinda ya rage mata shine ta gyara tarbiyyar 'yarta
Washegari Jawahir da karfinta ta tashi da asuba, tareda Sabreena sukayi sallah sannan suka dau Alqur'ani suka fara biya inda aka kara musu a Islamiyya, seda sukaga ya zauna musu sosai sannan suka ajiye, kaman yadda sukeyi a gida yauma tareda Mamah suka hada breakfast suka kuma gyara gidan duk da Hajiya nada me mata aiki, seda sukaci suka sha sukayi nak sannan Hajiya tace da driver dinta ya nunawa su Jawahir gari kafin su tashi tafiya, ai kuwa sunsha yawo cikin garin Borno, se wuraren la'asar suka dawo gida sukayi sallah sannan suka shirin tafiya, cikin awa daya sukayi duk abinda zasuyi suka gama Hajiya ta cika su da tarin kyaututtuka sannan driver dinta ya dauke su zuwa airport, before Isha sun kai gida, koda sukaje gida basu nemi abinci ba saboda gajiya se Abba daya ce a haa mishi tea sannan duk suka shige ciki dan su huta
Washegari Monday dan haka da shirin zuwa school suka tashi, sukayi aikinsu sukaci abinci sannan sukayi wanka, tuni Abba ya fice zuwa wurin aikinshi, wuraren goma kuma Mamah ma ta fice zuwa office dinta dan already ta koma bakin aikinta kuma alhamdulillah sosai yanzu business dinta ke moving, su Jawahir basu suka bar gida ba se wuraren sha biyu a cikin motar Jawahir dan tuni Dada ya aiko mata da abinta kuma sosai tayi farin ciki dan ko ba komai ze rage mata cacan kudin napep
Tareda Sabreena suka wuce school, a gaban department dinsu ta ajiye ta sannan ita kuma ta karasa nasu department, tana parking ta nufo hanyar shiga department dinta Jarood ya tare ta, sosai gabanta ya buga ganinshi tsaye ya zuba mata mayun idanunshi kuma bashi da niyyar daukewa, gefenshi tabi zata wuce ya kara tare ta tareda cewa "Jawahir we need to talk", ba tareda ta kalleshi ba tace "we have nothing to talk about", da sauri yace "Yes we do, dan ban gane me kike nufi dani ba, sanin kanki ne bani na baki liquor kika sha ba, ki kika nuna kinaso ni kuma ba baki abinda kikeso then why are you treating me like it's all my fault, bayan kisan ba laifi na bane", seda ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tace "nasan cewar ba laifinka bane, kawai dai I need some space me shiyasa kaga na kaurace maka", cike da rashin yarda yace "kuma I'm the only person you need some space from", bata kalleshi ba haka kuma bata bashi amsa ba dan kuwa batada amsar da zata bashi, sosai yaji ranshi ya aci yayinda bakin ciki ya cika zuciyarshi tareda wani irin tsanar Najib dan kuwa yanada masaniyar cewar sun sasanta kansu da Najib wanda tunda hakan ya faru Jawahir ta fara canza mishi, duk da yanda yakejin bacin rai hakan be hanashi sausauta murya wurin yi mata magana ba, cikin sanyin murya yace "shikenan, tinda haka kika bukata i will let you go, I will give you all the space you need, you have my number, you know my home, you know where to find me, so whenever you feel like you've gotten enough space you need I will willingly take you back as a friend and sister", murmushi me ciwo tayi tana goge guntun hawayen da yayi nasarar digowa daga idanunta dan kuwa sosai takejin Jarood a cikin jikinta kaman dan uwanta sedai halayenshi bazasu sa ta zauna dashi a matsayin kawa koh kanwa ba dan haka ma bata da ranar sake waiwayarshi, dagowa tayi ta kalleshi tace "Allah ya sada mu da alkhairi", da fadan haka ta raa ta gefenshi ta wuce yayinda yabi bayanta da kallo harta bace ma ganinshi, iska me zafi ya furzar daga bakinshi sannan a fili yace "yanzu duk burin da naci a kan yarinyar ke nema ya rushe haka, ina wallahi bazan yarda", sannan a zuciyarshi yace "I will act cool now, but when the right time comes zatasan koni waye", da wannan tunanin shima ya juya ya wuce
Wasa wasa tun daga wannan lokacin Jarood ya fita harkar Jawahir kaman yadda ta bukata dan ko a hanya ya ganta baya nuna ya santa, wa'anda suka sansu tare sunyi mamakin wannan canji da aka samu, karatu yayi nisa a yayinda fannin Islamiyya ma ba'a barta a baya ba dan kuwa tana kokari ba laifi, amintarsu da Khadijah yayi nisa sosai yayinda ita da Sabreena suka zama kaman wasu best friends komai tare sukeyi, ko a school tare suke lunch, ta bangaren Najib kuwa aiki yayi nisa kuma ba laifi yana kwasan albashin shi ba tareda wani matsala ba, sosai yake waya da Jawahir da Sabreena dan kuwa har yanzu ya kasa tantace me yakeji dangane dasu biyun duka, ta bangaren Sabreena yasan yana jinta har cikin ranshi wanda a kullum yakeson jin muryarta sannan kuma ya tsokaneta sannan ne hankalinshi ze kwanta while ta bangaren Jawahir kuwa ba'a magana dan da yake kwana yake tashi saboda a kullum text message dinta yake fara cin karo da na fatan alkhairi a gurin aiki, sannan da daddare seta tabbata ta tura mishi text take kwanciya, shikuma Najib mutum ne da yakeso a damu dashi kuma abinda Jawahir keyi kenan wanda wannan yasa ko a wurin aiki tunaninta ne a ranshi
Wurin Jawahir kam son Najib takeyi kaman tayi yaya, sedai kunya na 'ya mace ya hanata fitowa ta fada kowa dan kuwa koh Sabreena bata fadawa ba balle Mamah, saukin ta ma shi Najib din yana bata lokacin shi dan koda yaushe ya samu lokaci yakan kirata suyita hiransu, ta bangaren Sabreena kuma itama din hakan ne dan kuwa batajin zataso wani mahaluki kwatankwacin yadda takeson Najib dan kuwa ya dade da sace zuciyarta ba tareda ya sani ba, kuma itama ta kasa fadawa kowa dan a ganinta hakan ba daidai bane ta budi baki tace tanason Najib
Wannan kenan

UWA TA GARI - 36 - Page 2 - Wattpad
YEAR LATER (BAYAN SHEKARA DAYA)
Abubuwa da dama sun faru cikin wannan lokutan, Jawahir sosai ta nutsu ta maida hankalinta kan karatun ta wanda Mamah ke alfahari da ita ta wannan fannin dan kuwa sosai take ganin canji tattare da ita, gaba-daya school din last two weeks duk suka karkare exams dinsu na wannan semester din, yanzu Jawahir na shirin zuwa 300level while Sabreena kuma 200level yayinda Jarood sune graduants na wannan shekarar kuma da first class ya fita dan kuwa duk iskancinshi baya wasa da karatun shi dan a kullum mahaifinshi seya jaddada mishi muhimmancin karatun
Jawahir
Cikin shekara dayan an samu canji sosai tattare da ita ta fannin addini, makarantar ta da kuma mu'amalarta da mutane dan kuwa every Friday tana zuwa ziyara wurin Yaya Aysha koh kakarta Naja'atu mahaifiyar Dada koh kuma wurin Dada amma bata taa zuwa gida gaida Dada ba sedai ta bishi office shima kuma be takura ta kan lallai seta zo gidan ba
Every month se Dada ya tura mata kudi a account for her upkeep, data nunawa Mamah kudin da Dada ke turo mata se tace ta rike kayanta duk sanda takeda bukata she's free to use it tinda kudinta ne sedai Jawahir kwatakwata bata taa kudin ba dan kuwa Abba ma yana iya kokarinshi dan be rageta da komai ba, yanda yake kula da Sabreena haka yake kula da Jawahir idan ka gansu baza kace ba ciki daya suka fito ba
Tsakaninta da Najib kuwa se abinda yayi gaba dan a halin yanzu ma bata iya boye son da take mishi, duk karshen wata yakan zo gida yayi kwana biyu ya koma, Sabreena ko kadan bata nuna shakuwar dake tsakanin Najib da Jawahir ya dame ta ba sedai kuma na ciki na ciki dan ba karamin kishi takeji ba idan taganshi da Jawahir sedai ya ta iya
Sabreena
Babu abinda ya canza tattare da it, she's still the happy, jovial and free Sabreena that you all know, sosai itama take kokari bangaren karatun ta, matsalar ta guda daya ne yanda take bala'in son Najib amma shi ta lura ya tarkata hankalinshi ya bama Jawahir duk da itama yana kwatankwata yi mata abubuwan da yake ma Jawahir amma ta kasa gane inda ya dosa gashi kuma ita bazata iya fitowa tace mishi gashi gashi ba, shiyasa ta zubawa sarautar Allah ido tareda addu'ar idan har Najib alkhairi ne a gare ta toh Allah yasa ya zama mijinta, idan kuma ba alkhairi bane Allah ya bata wanda ze zame mata alkhairi, duk sonda takewa Najib besa ta canza yanayin mu'amalarta da Jawahir ba sema wata irin shakuwa ma dake kara shiga tsakaninsu
Najib
Matashin saurayi me kyau da aji ga kudi nan sun zauna mishi dan kuwa duk wata 2
5m yake karba albashi saboda ba karamin matsayi aka bashi ba, matan Abuja kuwa rubibinshi sukeyi amma shi matan Kebbi ne suka sace zuciyarshi wanda yake hanashi kwanciyar hankali, gaba-daya ya rasa ya zai yi da Jawahir da Sabreena danshi harga Allah yakejin sonsu gaba-daya a duk iliharin jikinshi wanda be taba sanin cewar it's possible ace namiji nason mata biyu lokaci daya ba, sosai suke walahar da zuciya da gangan jikinshi, ya kasa fitowa yacewa Jawahir yana sonta saboda yadda yake ganin soyayyar shi a idanun Sabreena kuma beso yayi abinda zesa ta shiga wani halin, haka zalika ya kasa fitowa yacewa Sabreena yana sonta saboda Jawahir, dan Jawahir kam batama iya boye kishinsa da takeyi, muddin suka fita tare taga ana kalle mata shi tofa seta aikawa mutum da harar da zesa ka auke ido koda kuwa Sabreena na wurin dan ita har yanzu wautar ta yasa ta kasa gane cewar Sabreena ma na son Najib
Mamah ta dade da fahimtar abinda ke faruwa tsakanin su ukun nan sedai ko kadan batasa musu baki ba dan a cewar ta Najib namiji ne dan haka he needs to fight his own battle
Back to story
Jawahir ce zaune a kan gadonsu tana kallon account balance dinta dan yanzun nan Dada ya turo mata da kudi, kudinta sunkai wurin dubu dari biyar harda en canji, Sabreena ce ta shigo ta zauna gefenta tana cewa "sister me kike kallo haka?", dagowa Jawahir tayi tace "Dada ya kara turomin kudi, kalli yanzu inada 560,000k a account kuma bansan me zanyi dashi ba", da sauri Sabreena tace "ki bayar a dinga juya miki mana", "wa nasan zan bawa?", cewar Jawahir dan kuwa batasan wanda zata ba kudi ya juya mata ba, Najib ba business yakeyi ba balle tace zata bashi, Sabreena ce tace "kiyi shawara da Mamah i no she will help", murmushi Jawahir tayi tace "tnx sis, kin kawo shawara"
Tashi sukayi suka wuce parlour inda Mamah ke kallon kulfi a starlife, tana ganinsu ta saki murmushi dan ba karamin dadi takeji ba idan ta gansu barin ma yanda suka hada kansu kaman wa'anda suka fito ciki daya, zama sukayi suka sata a tsakiya yayinda Jawahir gaba-daya hankalinta ya ta'allaka kan cikin dake gaban Mamah, she still can't believe that in the next two to three months itama zata samu baby sibling, mace ce namiji ne basu sani ba tukun da Mamah taki yarda tayi scan amma kome Mamah ta haifa she will still love the baby with all she has got, Sabreena ce ta zungure mata kai tana cewa "kallon ya isa hakan nan, karki hadiye mana baby tun bezo duniya ba, dariya sukayi gabadayansu Mamah ta shafa cikinta sannan ta kallesu tace "ya akayi, da magana ne?", Jawahir ce tace "eh Mamah, dama kudin da Dada ke turomin naga sunyi yawa kuma bansan abinda zanyi dashi ba, shine Sabreena ta bani shawaran in bayar a dinga juya min ni kuma bansan wa zan bamawa ba", shiru Mamah tayi tana tunani kafin tace "ke yanzu me kikeso a miki da kudin", kai tsaye tace "Zan ba sister 150k a ciki, kema ki cire abinda zaki cire se sauran ki bari amin business dashi", girgiza kai Mamah tayi tace "nikam na gode amma ba abinda zan cire dan kuwa Abbanku be rage ni da komai ba gashi kuma inada nawa business a hannu wanda ke tafiya daidai alhamdulillah, sedai zan baki shawaran kiba kanwarki 200k ke kuma se kiyi amfani da 300k sauran ki barshi a account dinki", ba tareda dogon tunani ba Jawahir tace "shikenan hakan za'ayi", godiya sosai Sabreena tayi Jawahir tace ta daina mata godiya
Nan Mamah tace "dama ina neman wanda ze zuba hannun jari a fashion house dina if you want you guys can join me", cike da jin dadi sukace "Mamah me ze zai hana", murmushi tayi tace "shikenan, zan duba nawa kuka zuba sannan isan percentage dinku da kuma abinda zaku dinga karba duk wata", duk sun gamsu, nan da nan Jawahir ta mata transfer din 500k a business account dinta, Sabreena ce ta kalli Mamah tace "amma Mamah za mu dinga miki modelling kinji", murmushi Mamah tayi tace"why not, ai yanzu ma harda shawaranku zan dinga running fashion house dina dan akwai sabbabin designs da nakeso na dinka amma bansan wani material zanyi amfani dashi ba, so kunga tinda ku yanzu kuna fita kuna shiga makaranta kusan irin materials din da aka fiso, se kubani shawaran wanda zan siya", cike da jin dadi Jawahir tace "Inshallah Mamah duk sanda kikeda bukatar mu zaki samu shawara daga garemu", albarka duk tasa musu sannan tace suje su hada dinner dan ita kam kallo zatayi
Najib ne zaune a office dinshi yasa system gaba yana kallon email dinda aka turo mishi wanda oganshi yace ya karanta sedai kuma gaba-daya hankalinshi baya wurin dan kuwa ya lula duniyar tunani, knocking akayi a kofar office dinshi amma beji ba, seda aka sake knocking sannan ya dawo daga duniyar tunanin da ya fada ya dago yace "come in", wani kyakkyawan saurayi ne ya shigo wanda da an ganshi anga bafullatani, ajiyar zuciya Najib ya sauke ganin wanda ya shigo, mika mishi hannu saurayin yayi sukayi musabaha sannan ya nemi wuri ya zauna yace "Najibullahi lafiya na ganka haka, kwana biyu ina lura da kai kana yawan fadawa tunani ko a gida ma yau seda kayi hakan da muke breakfast", ajiyar zuciya Najib ya kuma saukewa sannan yace "Salim bazaka gane bane dan ni kaina na kasa gane wannan al'amarin dake yawan jefani cikin tunani", gyara zama Salim yayi yace "do you mind sharing your problem, koda bazan gane ba i might have a solution", shafa sumar kanshi Najib yayi sannan yace "Salim I'm in love", cike da excitement Salim yace "wow bro that's good news", girgiza kai Najib yayi sannan yace "with two girls", da sauri Salim ya kalleshi yace "kanason kace min mata biyu kakeso lokaci daya", ya kaa kai alamar "eh", Salim yayi dariya yace "mazaje, ai haka akwai", kallonshi Najib yayi yace "the worst part is they are sisters", kallon hala baka da hankali Salim ya fara mishi kafin yace "hanya lafiyarka kalau Najib, ya za'ayi kaso sisters kuma a lokaci daya, wannan ai hankali baze dauka ba, dama ace ba sisters bane wannan is possible yana faruwa", hannu Najib yasa cikin sumar kanshi sannan ya dawo da hannunshi kan fuskarshi yace "they are not biological sisters, step sisters ne, infact ba babansu daya ba haka zalika ba mamansu daya ba", Salim be gane me Najib ke nufi ba dan haka yace "bro explain better", matsowa gaba Najib yayi da kujerar shi sannan ya dora hannayenshi kan table dinda ke gabanshi ya fara ba Salim labarin Jawahir da Sabreena, shiru Salim yayi yana jinshi harya kai karshe sannan yace "amma Najib kasan cewar kai kake wahalar da kanka, i mean zaka iya auren dukkansu dan kowaccensu da aure a tsakaninku, kuma dan ka auri daya daga cikinsu wannan be haramta maka sake auren dayar ba", girgiza kai Najib yayi yace "Salim I can't, Jawahir tana sona dan ita kwatakwata ma bata iya boyewa, haka ma Sabreena itama tana sona duk da ita tanada kawaici, I don't want to hurt there feelings kuma banso na zama sillar samun sabani tsakaninsu danna tabbata idan Sabreena ta gani ta kawar da kai Jawahir bazata gani ta kawar da kai ba saboda ita bata iya boye kishinta", cike da gamsuwa Salim yace "na gane, why not kayi istikhara tsakaninsu ka nemi zabin Allah tinda kace bazaka iya hada su biyun ba", girgiza kai Najib yayi yace "inaga I will just go for Jawahir dan gaskiya nafi sonta", murmushi Salim yayi ya buga kafadar Najib yace "it's ok, ko masu mata biyu ma haka yake a wurinsu, sunason daya fiye da yadda suke son dayan wannan ba wani abu bane, kayi istikharan, kai da kanka zakaga wacce tafi dacewa dakai", a hankalin yace "toh idan su biyun duka ne fa?", Salim yace "seka aure su duka, amma zan baka shawara, ka fara yiwa ita Sabreenan magana tinda naga alamar she's more matured sannan karka boye mata komai idan har ta fahimce ka ita dayar komai zai zo da sauki duk da kace tanada kishi she won't want to loose you", kaa kai Najib yayi yace "thanks bro, Inshallah zanyi yadda kace", tashi Salim yayi yace "dama nazo nace maka muje muyi lunch ne ganin baka fito ba, gashi lunch break harya kare, sedai anjima, see you later", daga mishi hannu kawai Najib yayi ya koma bakin aikinshi yana tunanin shawarar da Salim ya bashi
Salim Muhammad dan garin Katsina ne, tare aka musu interview da Najib lokaci daya kuma cikin sa'a duk suka samu, gwamnati ce ta hadasu apartment daya tinda duk basu da aure, two bedroom flat suke kowa da dakinshi, cikin kankanin lokaci suka saba, tare suke zuwa aiki su koma gida tare, ranar friday kuma kowannen su ya kama hanyar garin su
Wannan kenan

UWA TA GARI - 37 - Wattpad
Kaman yadda Salim ya bashi shawara haka kuwa yayi, seda ya tashi kwanciya sannan yayi alwallah yayi nafila raka'a biyu yayi addu'ar istikhara (wanda zan rubuto muku a karshe) sannan ya nemi wuri ya kwanta cike da tunanin en matanshi da suka hanashi samun sukunin zuciyar sa, a ranar bacci barawo ne ya sace shi dan kuwa ya dade beyi bacci ba se juyi yakeyi akan gado
Lambu ne wanda ya kawatu da kayan itatuwa da furanni ga tsuntsaye na shawagi a sama gwannin sha'awa, zaune yake yana kallon tsuntsayen yanajin wani nishadi na saukar mishi, kyakyawan murmushi ne kwance a fuskarsa wanda da ka gani kasancewar bana komai bane na kwanciyar hankali ne, "Assalamu alaikum noorul kalbi", dago da fararen idanunwanshi yayi yana kallon kyakkyawar fuskar dake mishi sallama, fadada murmushin sa yayi sannan yace "Amin wa'alaiki salam Ya Habibty", zama tayi gefenshi tareda ajiye kayan fruits din da already an gyara an yayyanka sannan ta dago ta kalleshi tace "bismilla, eat up, it's all for you", girgiza kai yayi yace "no, feed me", bata musa ba, cikin sanyinta ta fara bashi yana amsa yayinda ya kure ta da idanunshi, tana cikin bashi tace "noorul kalbi baka gajiya da kallona ne?", ajiyar zuciya ya sauke sannan yace "bazan taba gajiya da kallon kyakyawan fuskarki ba Habibty", a hankali tace "koda na tsufa", yace "har mutuwa ta raba bazan gaji da kallon ki ba", nan take kwalla ya cika mata ido tace "noorul kalbi ka daina kiran mutuwa", dariya ta bashi saboda yanayin da tayi maganar cike da shagwaba dan haka ya dan dara sannan yace "ai mutuwa dole ce", zata bashi amsa taji hayaniyar yara, dagowa tayi takai dubanta wurin, take annurin fuskarta ya karu ganin yara nata gujegujen su ga wata nata binsu tana kokarin kamosu, maida kallonshi yayi inda take kallo, shima murmushin yayi ya mike tsaye tareda kamo ta yace "come, let's go and play with them", bata musa ta bishi a baya, sedai basu kai ga karasawa ba ta cire hannunta daga nashi ta saura tsaye a wurin, juyowa yayi yace "muje mana noorul kalbi, ki daina baya baya dasu", cikin sarkakiyar murya tace "I can't", daga haka ta fara bacewa ganinshi, iya tashin hankali ya shiga tashin hankali amma kuma ya kasa tabka komai har ta bacewa ganinshi gabadaya, zubewa yayi a kasa ya fara kuka kaman karamin yaro yayinda wacce ke wasa da yara tazo inda yake itama ta tsugunna gabanshi sannan ta rugumeshi cikin tsigar lallashi, cikin muryar kuka yace "Qurratul aeyn Habibty left me, kinsan bamuyi haka da ita ba, she promised to stay", itama idanunta cike da kwalla tace "I know, but what can we do, Allahn da yafimu sonta ya karbi a barsa, kuma sooner or later dama she's meant to leave, let's face reality, our children need us, yanzu ba lokacin kuka bane", dagowa yayi yana kallonta tareda share hawayenshi yace "you are right let's forget everything for the happiness of our children", murmushi ta sakar mishi sannan ta kara janyoshi jikinta tareda kissing din sumar dake kanshi
Tapping dinshi yaji anayi a kafa, da sauri ya bude ido tareda mikewa zaune yana addu'ar tashi daga bacci sannan ya kalli Salim dake tsaye kanshi yace "why did you wake me up?", da mamaki Salim yace "bakaji kiran sallah ba, ka tashi karmu makara, by the way why are you sweating bayan ga fan da AC a kunne", rike kanshi yayi wanda ke sara mishi sannan yace "long story, bari nayi alwallah mu wuce masallaci", fita Salim yayi ya bashi wuri shikuma ya tashi yaje yayi alwallah ya fito ya zira jallabiya sannan ya fice suka wuce masallaci
A hanyarsu ta dawowa ne Salim yace "hala kayi istikharan ne?", kaa mishi kai yayi sannan yace "nayi, and it's complicated dan na kasa tantance me mafarkin da nayi ke nufi", "wa Allah ya nuna maka a mafarki?", Salim ya tambaya, kai tsaye yace "su duka biyun", shiru Salim yayi ya bude kofa suka shiga gida Najib ya rufe sannan Salim yace "that means duka su biyun Allah ya zabamaka kenan", kaa kai yayi sannan ya juyo ya kalli Salim dake zaune yana kokarin daukar remote yace "but Jawahir left" cike da rashin fahimta Salim yace "what do you mean by she left?", zama Najib yayi yana yamutsa gashin kanshi yace "I don't know, muna zaune da ita having a discussion when we sight Sabreena playing with children da suka kai uku, nan na riko hannunta nace tazo muje wurinsu Sabreena, she followed me but on our way going she stopped and disappear kaman iska", shiru Salim yayi dan kuwa al'amarin akwai rikitarwa, duk iya kure tunaninshi ya kasa fassara wannan mafarki, kallon Najib yayi sannan yace "why not ka nemi karin bayani wurin malamai", girgiza kai yayi yace "no, banson jin abinda ze daga mun hankali, Inshallah this weekend idan naje gida i will talk to my Dad, nasan ze bani shawara me kyau", kaa kai Salim yayi yace "Hakane, Allah ya tabbatar da alkhairi", Najib ya amsa da "ameen" sannan ya mike dan shiga daki ya kalli Salim yace "go and start getting ready karmuyi latti balle kai me sanyin jiki kaman mace", murmushi kawai Salim yayi dan ba yau aka fara ce mishi yanada sanyi ba
Addu'ar istikhara:                            (  )
Fassara: Ya Allah ina neman zabinka domin iliminka, kuma ina neman ka bani iko domin ikon ka, kuma ina rokonka daga falalar ka mai girma, domin kaine mai iko, ni kuwa bani da iko, kuma kaine masani, ni kuwa ban sani ba, kuma kaine masanin abubuwan fake
Ya Allah! Idan ka san cewar wannan al'amari ( seka ambaci bukatar ka) alheri ne a gareni a cikin addinina, da rayuwata, da kuma karshen al'amari na a wata rayuwar, da magaggaucin al'amari na da majinkircinsa, ka addara mini shi, kuma ka saukake mini shi, sannan ka albarkance ni a cikin sa
Kuma idan ka san wannan al'amari sharri ne gareni a cikin addinina, da rayuwata, da karshen al'amari na, a wata rayuwar, da magaggaucin al'amari na da majinkircinsa ka kawar dashi daga gareni, kuma ka kawar dani daga gareshi, kuma ka addara mini alheri a duk inda yake, kuma ka sanya ni in yarda dashi

UWA TA GARI - 38 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Zaune Jawahir take tana chatting da Najib a waya Sabreena ta shigo dakin, kallo daya tayiwa Jawahir ta dauke kai dan tasan da wanda ake chatting din, Najib ne kaai wanda Jawahir ke bata lokacinta ta zauna tana chatting dashi, bathroom Sabreena ta wuce tana kokarin hadiye kishin daya taso mata, alwallah tayi ta fito ta kalli Jawahir da se murmushi takeyi a zuciyarta tace "kome yake fada mata dake sata murmushi haka oho", shimfida sallaya tayi sannan tace "sister anfa kira sallah", Jawahir ta dago ta kalli Sabreena tareda mika mata waya tace "ungu nan yaya Najib ze miki magana", bata musa ba ta karba wayar tareda zama kan gado yayinda ita kuma Jawahir ta wuce bathroom
Sallama ta mishi dan yasan itace sannan tace "Jawahir wai zakamin magana", shiru yayi yana kallon text din dan shi dai yasan bece a ba Sabreena waya ba, ganin shirun yayi yawa ta kuma type mishi "are you there", nan da nan ya mata reply da "Yes, dama na tambayi sister dinki abinda zan kawo muku idan zan dawo tace ita bata sani ba, shine nace bari na tambaye ki", shiru tayi tana kara karanta text din, wato ma Jawahir aka tambaya tinda batasan abinda zatace a kawo ba shine yace a bata wayar gata second option, takaici ne ya kamata sedai ta hadiye abinta sannan ta rubuta mishi "ka siyo duk abinda kaga ya dace, ni sallah zanyi yanzu", daga haka ta ajiye wayar ta tada sallarta dan har yanzu Jawahir bata fito ba, yana karanta abinda ta turomai yasan ranta ya aci kuma he won't blame her, Jawahir ce da laifi ita da ta bata wayar ba tareda yace ta bata ba tinda idan yanason magana Sabreena ai yana da number dinta
Shima ajiye wayar yayi kan desk dinshi yana tunanin abinda ya dace yayi
Jawahir na fitowa itama ta shimfida nata sallayar ta tafara sallar ta, bayan ta idar tayi addu'o'inta ta dawo ta zauna gefen Sabreena dake game a nata wayar fuskar ta ba annuri ko kadan dan kuwa ta fara gajiya da ganin yanda Najib yafi fifita Jawahir a kanta, a hankali Jawahir tace "sister meya ce miki?", ba tareda Sabreena ta kalleta ba tace "tambaya na yayi abinda ze siyo mana idan ya tashi dawowa", ganin yadda Sabreena tayi maganar cike da dacin rai yasa Jawahir cewa "kina jin haushi na koh?", da sauri Sabreena ta kalleta tace "sister saboda me zanji haushin ki?", "saboda ina son wanda kike so", cewar Jawahir tana kallon expression din Sabreena, gabadaya Sabreena rasa abin fada tayi dan batamasan me zata cewa Jawahir ba tinda ba karya tayi ba sedai ita kam batajin haushin ta, zata iya cewa tana jin kishi amma badai haushi ba, riko hannunta Jawahir tayi tace "don't worry it's ok to fall in love with him, after all bake kika sawa kanki soyayyar shi a zuciyar ki ba so I won't judge you, nima bani na sawa kaina ba sedai na girma da soyayyar Yaya Najib a raina, most of the time idan zezo nan gidan ina lura da yanda kike jin dadi, haka kuma idan yazo ina ganin yadda kike kallonshi", cikin sanyin murya Sabreena tace "how did you
", da sauri Jawahir ta katse ta da cewar "I'm not a fool to not notice, amma karki damu, duk da nasan inada mugun kishi bana kishin kasancewar ki da Najib wanda a kullum nakewa Allah godiya daya ciremin kishinki a raina dan in har ina kishin kasancewar ki da Najib bansan ina zansa raina ba", hawaye ne ya cika ma Sabreena ido tace "but he only loves you", Jawahir tayi murmushin karfin hali tace "waye yace miki haka, ke bakya ganin irin kallon da yake min shi yake miki?", girgiza kai Sabreena tayi dan ita kam bata taa lura ba Jawahir ta matse hannun Sabreena dake cikin nata sannan tace "sister inaso mu hada kai wurin ba yaya Najib farin ciki, nasan cewar sooner or later dole yace yanason daya daga cikinmu, what I want with you is duk wacce ya zaba dole dayar ta hakura tasawa zuciyarta dangana, idan har ke ya zaba toh kuwa ni zan hakura dashi", da sauri Sabreena ta girgiza kai tace "no, nikam bazanyi wannan sonkan ba, indai har zaki hakura toh nima na hakura yaje can ya nemi wata, ko kuma ya haamu mu biyun duka", dariya Jawahir tayi tana tashi daga zaunen da take tace "Sabreena do you think zanyi zaman kishi dake ne, that won't happen, koda zan zauna da kishiya ba zan zauna dake a matsayin kishiya ta ba", Sabreena na kallon tace "why", kai tsaye Jawahir tace "saboda inada kishi, ni kuma banason nayi kishi dake shiyasa kigaka ko yanzu ma ban damu ba", shiru Sabreena tayi dan ita dai al'amarin ya daure mata kai
Mamah dake tsaye bakin kofa jinsu ta shigo ciki sannan tace "Jawahir banason in sake jin kince bazaki iya zaman kishi da kanwar ki ba, ba gwanda ma kin zauna da ita akan kije ki zauna da wacce baki sani ba baki san halayyar ta ba, idan har Najib yace ku biyun duka ze hada toh kuwa ku duka din ze hada, idan kuma ya nuna daya cikinku yake so, shikenan se dayar ta hakura kaman yadda Jawahir tace saboda samun kwanciyar hankali ko waccenku, shima Najib din wannan weekend din idan ya dawo zan nemi shi dan na gaji da wannan wasan jeka ka dawo din da yake, idan da har yana don daya cikinku ne toh ya fito ya fada ya daina min wasa da zuciyar yarana", murmushi sukayi jin abinda tace a karshe sannan Sabreena tace "Inshallah Mamah yanda kikace haka za'ayi", kallon Jawahir Mamah tayi dan jin ta bakin ta, ajiyar zuciya ta sauke dan yanzu bata iya yiwa Mamah musu sannan tace "fine Allah ya zaba mana abinda yafi alkhairi", murmushi Mamah tayi sannan ta hadasu ta rungume tareda cewa "that's my babies, Allah ya muku albarka", a tareda suka kalleta sannan sukace "Mamah mufa ba babies bane, ga baby nan a cikin ki", dariya tayi tace "ja'iran yara dama nazo tambayanku abinda zamu dora dan na rasa me zan dafa", nan suka fara bata shawaran abinda zasuyi da daddare, wannan tace wannan wancan tace wannan hardai daga karshe suka tsaida abinci daya sannan duk fice gaba-daya dan taya Mamah aiki
A gajiye Dada ya shigo gida, da sallama ya shiga parlour sedai alamar ba kowa a ciki, dakin shi ya wuce ya cire kayanshi ya watsa ruwa sannan ya fito sanye da Jallabiya yayi hanyar dakin Fareeda dan ya duba ta saboda kwana biyu batajin dadi, cak ya tsaya da bude kofar jin abinda take cewa wanda da alama waya takeyi, "ke ni tin last week naje nayi test kuma an tabbatar min da ciki ne dani a ranar ban dawo gida ba seda na tabbata an zubar min dashi danni ban shirya zaman renon yara ba", shiru tayi na dan lokaci alaman tana sauraren abinda ake cewa ta daya bangaren sannan ta saki dariya tace "trust me mana, ai tunda waccan tsinaniyar ta bar gidan ya dawo a tafin hannuna se abinda nace, yanzu haka ba yanda beyi ba kan inje asibiti na nuna mishi nifa bazanje ba, seda na tabbata ya wuce aiki sannan na fice nayi test din, kinga gashi anyi komai an gama ba tare ma daya sani ba", shiru ta kuma na dan wani lokaci sannan tace "eh na biyu kenan dana zubar, na uku ma idan yazo zubdashi zanyi dan banga zan iya ba", zufa ne kawai yake karyo wa Dada ta ko ina na jikinshi, ga hannunshi dake rike da kofar har yanzu na wani mugun rawa saboda bacin rai, tasan bata shiyar tara zuri'a dashi bane ta aure shi, dan rashin imani irin nata ta zubar mishi da gudan jinin har biyu bama daya ba, iya tashin hankali ya shiga tashin hankali, be taba tsammanin ta wannan bangaren Allah ze sakawa Mamah ba dan koh ba'a fada mai ba yasan be kyautawa Mamah ba kuma yasan bataji dadin zama dashi ba, yau Fareeda da ace tasan yadda yakeson yara da batayi gangancin zubar mishi da ciki ba
Rai bace ya bude kofar dakin ya shige ciki, gadan gadan yayi kanta, ai Fareeda na ganin yanayin shi ta saki ihu dan na tabbata har makota sunji dan kuwa ba karamin tsorata tayi ba, bata tsammanin ze dawo da wuri haka ba har yaji maganganun da yayi, bata gama tunani ba taji saukar mari a fuskarta wanda yasata kefewa kan gado, hannu yasa ya dagota sannan ya kara mata wani, seda ya mata lafiyayyu guda uku sannan yace "amma kin cuceni kin cuci rayuwata kuma bazan taba yafe miki ba wawiya jahila, in banda jahilci irin naki Allah ya miki kyauta irin kyautar da ba kowa yake bawa ba amma ki wulakantar da kyautar, kuma kinyi so daya be miki ba seda kika sake har kina ikirarin idan na uku ma yazo shima zubar da shi zakiyi, ciki da ubanshi ba cikin shege ba, cikin halal kika wulakanta haka, dan kin cika tantiriyar er iska shine zaki zubar min da ciki, kisan yadda nake burin sake ganin gudan jinina kuwa, kisan yadda nakeson yara kuwa, dama haka kike?", Ita dai Fareeda kanta kife kan gado banda kuka ba abinda takeyi dan bata taa tunanin asirinta ze tuno haka ba, duk da marin da tasha da kuma maganganun da ya fada mata wannan besa taji tana dana sanin abinda ta aikata ba", dagota yayi sannan ya burkitota daga kan gadon ta fado kasa yace "wallahi awa aya na baki ki tattara kayanki ki barmin gida na sake ki saki daya", kallonshi tayi da mamaki sannan ta saki dariya ta mike tsaye tareda rike kugu tace "wallahi baka isa kamin wannan wulakantaccen sakin ba, zan tafi amma inaso ka sani zan dawo", da fadar haka ta shige bathroom dan wanke fuska ta barshi tsaye wurin
Hawaye ne ya gangaro mishi yasa hannu ya goge sannan ya fice daga dakin ta, dakinshi ya shige ya dauki car key dinshi ya fito, koda Gado ya ga yanayinshi yasan ba lafiya dan haka ya bude mishi gate ba tareda ya nemi dalilin fushin uban gidan nashi ba

UWA TA GARI - 39 - Wattpad
Dada direct gidan mahaifiyarshi ya nufa Naja'atu, tana zaune a parlour tana karanta littafin addu'o'inta ya shigo da sallama, dagowa tayi ta kalleshi ta cikin medicated glass dinta sannan ta amsa mishi sallamarshi, yanayinshi kawai da ta gani tasan cewar ba lafiya ba, zama yayi ya gaisheta ta amsa tareda tambayanshi iyali ya mata shiru, bata kuma tambayar shi ba itama taja bakinta tayi shiru dan dama tsakaninta dashi ba wani hiran arziki, zezo su gaisa ya karaci zamanshi ya tashi ya wuce, ranar da kuma yake da sha'awar cin abinci a gidan yace mata a zuba mai abinci, sedai yau gani tayi bazata iya shareshi ba dan a yanayin da ya shigo mata ma tasan yana da damuwa, ajiye littafin hannunta tayi ta cire glass dinta sannan tace "Osama lafiya na ganka haka?", goge kwallar shi yayi sannan yace "Ummi Fareeda ta cuceni", tae baki tayi jin ya ambaci Fareeda dan kuwa shekara daya da en watanni kenan da auren shi amma har yau batasan kammanin wannan Fareedar ba dan kuwa bata taa zuwa gidan ba, "me ta maka?", ta tambayeshi tana harararshi dan a ganinta shine ya kamata ya kawo matarshi tazo ta gaisheta a matsayinta na uwarshi amma beyi hakan ba, "Ummi can you imagine wai yarinyar nan ta zubar min ciki kuma ba so daya ba har so biyu, Ummi yanzu ace a yanda nake burin sake ganin gudan jinina shine zata zubar, kuma har na sallameta daga gidana ba alamun nadama tattare da ita balle ta bada hakuri", Ummi kam al'amarin ya girmama a wurinta dan bata taa tunanin the so called Fareeda zatayi haka ba, kallon danta tayi tace "ko wani dan adam da nashi littafin kaddarar, kai kuma naka kaddarar kenan dan haka se kayi hakuri itama ka nutsar da ita dan kila yarinta ne ke damunta kar kayi gaggawar daukar hukunci ", da sauri yace "wani irin yarinta Ummi, wacce takai kusan shekara ashirin da shida ce yarinya, haba mana Ummi karki daure ma karya gindi mana", a fusace ta dago tace "toh ubana me kakeso nayi koh nace, ita wannan Fareedar taka na santa ne, ban taa ganinta ba balle nasan yanayinta, kai kaga zaka iya ka aurota ba tareda shawarar kowa ba, yanzu da kuka samu matsala ta nuna maka true colors dinta shine zaka zo mun da kukan ka me kakeso na maka, kaga Osama bani da lokacin dagawa kaina hankali yanzu, shekaru na sunja, bani da wani buri yanzu daya wuce in samu gamawa da duniya lafiya dan haka karkazo nan kana daga mun murya akan wacce ko kammanin ta ban sani ba", da mamaki yace "Ummi kinaso kice mun Fareeda bata taa zuwa gidan nan ba?", "karya zan mata?", Ummi ta tambayeshi tana kallonshi, jingina da kujera yayi yana dafe kanshi tareda jinjina lamarin Fareeda, ba so daya ba, ba so biyu ba tasha tace mishi zata taje ta gaida Ummi, ashe ba nan take zuwa ba, toh idan ba nan take zuwa na me yasa take mishi karya
Mikewa yayi yace "bari naje Ummi, I will deal with my problems my own way", bata kulashi ba taci gaba da karatun ta a zuciyar ta tana cewa "in Banda wawancin Allah ya baka maka nutsasiya, wacce tasan ya kamata ka tashi ka bijera rahamarsa akan wani bazan dalilinka wanda bekai ya kawo ba, ai yanzu gashi ka fara ganin ishara dan kuwa Allah ba azzalumin sarki bane, baya barin hakkin wani kan wani dole ya kwatarwa Hindu hakkin ta koh a nan gidan duniya koh a lahira", da haka taja tsaki taci gaba da karatun ta cike da takaicin Osama
Fareeda kayanta wanda tasan zata bukata su ta zuba a akwati sannan taja kayanta ta bar mishi gidan, direct gidan da suke sharing dasu Zulaika ta wuce, sosai sukayi mamakin ganinta da jaka, Salma dake zauna da remote a hannu tace "Fareeda lafiya dai koh?", seda ta zauna sannan tace "ina fa lafiya, wayan da nakeyi da Zulaika dazu ashe Osama labe yamin duk yanajin abinda nake fada", da sauri Zulaika tace "mun shiga uku, yanzu me yace?", cike da jin haushin Dada tace "manta da dan bazan wai seda ya gama marina sannan yamin saki daya, kalli yadda duk ya kumbura mun fuska", cike da jimami Salma tace "kice ai da bakya jin magana, se kizo su Nafisa su dinga baki shawarar da bai dace ba, ni da nake dora ki kan hanya nice wacce batasan me takeyi ba, toh ai gashi nan sun kaiki sun baro, gashi sun kashe miki aure", hararar da Nafisa ta aika mata dashi ne yasa taja bakinta tayi shiru inda Fareeda kuma tace "ai wallahi be isa ya sallameni yanzu ba, duk inda zan shiga dan ganin ya maida ni gidanshi se na shiga", Zulaika tace "wannan haka yake, amma for now ki ba kanki time, ki fita harkar shi, kidan huta kema na wani lokacin kafin ki koma", girgiza kai Fareeda tayi tace "a'a so nake kafin in gama idda ya dawo dani gidanshi, dan haka zama be ganni ba, Nafisa dake zaune gefenta tace "hakane 'yar uwa, zama be ganki ba, kuma Inshallah zaki koma dakinki very soon, dan duk inda zamu muga Osama ya dawo ya haukace miki se munje", Salma ce ta mike tace "ku dai bi duniya a hankali", basu kulata ba dan inda sabo sun saba da wannan halin nata, ita a kullum cikin musu nasiha take, wannan kuma baze hanasu zama anjima susha hirar su ba
Fareeda da Zulaika da Nafisa kuwa zama sukayi a parlour sukaci gaba da bata gurbatacciyar shawara wanda ita kuma take dauka
Jawahir ce kwance kan gado ta kasa bacci, banda juyi ba abinda takeyi, gefenta kuwa Sabreena ce ke sharar baccinta hankali kwance, tunanin maganar Mamah takeyi, ita dai tasan batada tabbacin Najib na sonta dan gani take kaman son Yaya da kanwa yake mata yayinda yake son Sabreena amma baya nunawa Sabreena hakan sosai saboda kar ya bata ma ita Jawahir din rai, a kullum wannan shine nata hasashen, sannan idan kuma har yace hadasu zeyi toh bata tunanin zata iya, bata tunanin zata iya kishi da Sabreena akan Najib badan komai ba sedan Sabreena mace ce data riga ta gama sannin sirrinta, she knows about her past, kuma wannan ne kaai dalilin da zesa bazata yarda ba dan bataso taga ranar da Sabreena zata budi baki ta mata gori akan shi, tasan sabanin da suka samu da Mamah, tasan labarin giyan da tasha wanda da ita ma aka je Borno neman magani, tasan labarin ta da Jarood, toh akan me zata hada kanta kishi da wacce ta santa ta ko wani fanni, ai wannan ba mai yiwuwa bane, haka ta dinga tunani tunani har seda bacci barawo ya dauke ta
Washegari friday, kuma ranar ne suke sa ran dawowar Najib, ya fada musu karfe uku ze baro Abuja dan ranar friday 2pm suke tashi daga aiki, daga Jawahir har Sabreena hada kai sukayi suka dage suka mishi girki, duk da be fada musu inda ze fara sauka ba, Mamah de se kallon yaranta takeyi tana addu'an Allah yasa Najib yace dukkansu yakeso dan kuwa idan ya zabi daya toh batasan da wani baki zata lallashi dayar ba, sedai duk da haka koda ze zabi daya tafiso ya zabi Sabreena dan batason abinda za'aga kaman anyi son kai aciki, idan har ya zabi Sabreena toh hankalinta zefi kwanciya duk da kuwa zataso ya auri Jawahir ma dan a hannunshi ne kawai zata samu kwanciyar hankali na cewar 'yar ta na hannun mutum na gari, sedai kuma bata cire tsammani ba tin da ance kana naka ne Allah kuma na nashi dan haka batasan wani tanadi Allah yama yaran nata ba
Wa kuke gani Najib ze zaba? Idan yace su duka ze hada kuna gani Jawahir zata yarda? Idan kuma yace daya cikinsu yakeso ya Mamah zatayi ?

UWA TA GARI - 40 - Wattpad
Najib na barin wurin aiki mall ya wuce dan siyawa su Jawahir abinda ya musu alkawari duk da besan me zai siya ba, koda yaje mall din se ya yanke shawarar siya musu turare da kayan chocolates, bayan ya siya musu kowa da nashi daban daban sannan ya dauki hanyar Kebbi dukda yasan cewar zesha tafiya amma yafiso ya tafi da motar gida, album din Deen squad yasa yanaji yana tukinshi cikin kwanciyar hankali saboda zeje ganin taurarin shi
Se wurin 10:40pm ya kai Kebbi dan kuwa ba karamin gudu ya dingayi ba, duk da kasancewar dare yayi wannan be hanashi wucewa gidansu Jawahir straight ba, yana horn gateman dinsu ya bude mishi gate ya shiga da motarshi yayi parking sannan ya fito ya nufi hanyar daze sadashi da parlour gidan
Suna zaune sun gaji da jiranshi sukaji knocking, koh ba'a fada musu ba sunsan shine, gabadayansu an rasa wacce zata tashi taje ta bude kofar, seda ya sake knock sannan Mamah ta kallesu tace "an rasa wacce zata bude kofar ne?", cikin sunne kai Sabreena ta tashi kasancewar itace karama taje ta bude mishi, murmushi ya sakar mata ta mayar mishi da matarni sannan tace "bismilla shigo ciki", shiga yayi da sallamar shi su Mamah suka amsa sannan cikin wasa tace "zamu cika taran mazan jira", dariya yayi yana zama yace "a min afuwa aunty na wallahi hanya ne bakyau", tace "toh ya hanya", yace "alhamdulillah", seda suka gaisa sosai ta tambayeshi ya aiki yace fine sannan ta tashi ta basu wuri tareda cewa "Najib see me before you go", da "ok", ya amsa mata sannan ta shige daki
Tana shigewa ya juyo ya kalli Jawahir da Sabreena dake zaune, ajiyar zuciya yayi wanda besan ma sanda yayishi ba, Jawahir kallonshi takeyi bil hakki da gaskiyarta dan kuwa bataso ta kwari kanta, tayi kewar shi dan haka take mishi kallo me cike da tsantsar kauna ba tareda taji kunya koh shakkar Sabreena dake zaune ba, Sabreena kuwa gaba-daya ta maida hankalinta kan tv duk da ba kallon takeyi dan hankalinta na kan Najib sedai idan ka ganta zaka zata tv take kallo
Jawahir ce ta katse musu shirun da cewa "Ya Najib kazo lafiya?", kallonta yayi cike da tsantsar so da bege yace "lafiya lau sis na sameku lafiya?", tace "lafiya lau", kallon Sabreena yayi yace "Reena har yanzu ba'a daina fushin dani bane?", murmushi tayi me kayatarwa sannan ta juyo ta kalleshi tace "ni na isa inyi fushi dakai, ai komin fushin da zanyi dakai cikin kankanin lokaci zan sauko", murmushi ya sakeyi har hakoranshi na nunawa yace "i thought you are still angry with me ai, but tinda kince bakya fushi dani shikenan, na sameku lafiya?", tace "lafiya lau", duka wannan hiran da Najib keyi da Sabreena Jawahir ji take kaman ana soka mata mashi a kirji, a haka kuma ake cewa idan yace su biyun duka yakeso dole su yarda, ita ina zata iya da wannan kayan takaicin

promise you that no matter what bazan taba fifita daya akan daya ba, duk zan baki equal rights dinku, sedai inaso ki tayani addu'a Allah ya bani daman kwatanta adalci", kaa mishi kai tayi tana goge hawayenta ta bude mota zata fita ya riko hijabin ta, juyowa tayi ta kalleshi yace "baki ban amsa ta ba, I said I love you banji reply ba", murmushi tayi tana rufe fuskarta da tafin hannunta tace "ai kaima kasan amsar already", yace "nikam bansani ba se naji daga bakinki tukun", cike da jin kunyarsa tace "I love you too", badan yana kallon fuskarta ba yana ganin yadda bakinta ke motsawa ba da baze san abinda tace ba, murmushi yayi yace "ana kiran Sallah, idan anyi Isha zan shigo ciki", da "ok", ta amsa mishi sannan ta fice ta shige gida ranta fari kalli at least Najib bece baya sonta ba, koba komai zata samu damar yin rayuwar aure da Najib
A parlour taga Mamah da Jawahir ta musu sannu gida sannan ta fadi sakon Mamah na gaisuwa ta shige daki saboda ajiye hijabinta, kowa ya kalli Sabreena yasan tana cikin farin ciki koma be wuce kila ta hadu da Najib bane dan bata fada musu tare suke ba

UWA TA GARI - 43 - Wattpad
Bayan sallar isha Najib ya shiga cikin gidan, gabadayansu basa parlorn dan sun shiga yin sallah se tv dake kunna yana aiki shi kadai, zama yayi a parlorn ya jingina kanshi da kujera tareda lumshe idanu yana tunanin ta ina ze bullowa Jawahir tinda ya samu ya gama da Sabreena, dama fargabanshi Jawahir dan yasan cewar Sabreena bazata bashi matsala ba shiyasa ya fara tunkarar ta sedai beda wannan assurance din akan Jawahir, har ya fara tunanin ya kyaleta daga baya ya mata magana amma kuma yaga gwara yayi once and for all ya huta dan so yake yayi duk abinda ya dace saboda a wannan zuwan nashi beso ya koma ba tareda ya samu amincewar soyayyar Jawahir da Sabreena ba, tinda Allah yasa na Sabreena yazo mishi da sauki yanzu zeyi kokari ya fuskanci Jawahir duk da baya tunanin nata zezo mai da sauki
Yana nan zaune Mamah ta fito tace "a'a Najib kaine zaune anan, tun yaushe ka shigo", yace "ban dade da shigowa ba Aunty na, ya kike, ya gida, ya fama da jiki kuma?", ta zauna tana murmushi tace "duk wannan tambaya lokaci daya haka, toh ina lafiya, kuma komai ma lafiya lau", yayi dariya yana sosa keya yace "Aunty na ta kaina kenan, ban taa tunanin zan ganki da katon ciki da girma na haka ba", tayi dariya tace "kaji ka da shiririta, ai ko Ummin ka bata wuce haihuwa ba, ba abin mamaki bane ka ganta da ciki itama", ya girgiza kai yace "kai haba, naga Ummi da ciki yanzu ai na daina kwana gidan, se ziyara, nida nake shirin aure ace ina haihuwa Ummi na haihuwa ai abin kuma se yayi muni", tasa dariya tana jefa mishi pillow tace "ja'irin yaro kawai, ai ba kanka farau ba, kai baka taba ganin inda yara na haihuwa iyaye ma na haihuwa ba, ai ba abun kunya bane", yace "nikam bazan iya ba dan a ganina da kunya", bata kai ga magana ba su Jawahir suka fito suna hirar komawa school
Sabreena ce ta kalli Najib tace "Ya Najib baka tafi ba?", yace "ban tafi ba Reena, magana nakeso nayi da Jawahir", duk da faduwar gaba da taji seda ta saki murmushi tace "oh, ok, bari mu baku wuri", yayi saurin cewa "kuyi zamanku, waje zamuyi da Jawahir koh sis?", ya tambaya yana kallon Jawahir da kallonshi kawai takeyi amma bazaka taba gane wani expression ne a fuskarta ba, tace "uhm", tashi yayi yace "Aunty na daga nan zan wuce se gobe zanzo muyi sallama, Reena se munyi waya", suka mishi saida safe shikuma ya fice Jawahir tabi bayan shi, daki Sabreena ta koma dan batamason ta zauna a parlor balle Mamah ta karanci halin da take ciki, ita kuwa Mamah murmushi kawai tayi a ranta tace "Najib dai na nema ya raba min kan yara, nidai har kullum addu'ata be wuce kar su yarda wani namiji ya shiga tsakaninsu da har kawunansu zasu rabu ba", ba karamin dadi takeji ba ganin yadda suke komai tare, amma yau kam duk sai taji ba dadi saboda yadda Jawahir ta kasa sakewa, addu'a ta musu na Allah ya sausauta musu lamarin su kafin ta tashi ta shige kitchen dan bawa cikinta hakkinsa saboda wutsil wutsil dinda abin cikin keyi
A harabar gida kuwa Jawahir da Najib ne zaune akan white plastic chairs ta sunkuyar da kanta kasa tana wasa da yatsun hannunta dan haka kurum taji yau bazata iya hada ido dashi ba gashi tana tsoron jin me zaice mata, shi kuwa tsura mata idanu yayi yana kallon yanayin ta dan shima haka nan ya tsinci kanshi da fargaban abinda ze fada mata, gashi bayason abinda ze ata mata rai

kafin na fada inajin fargaban hakan", itama cikin mugun faduwar gaba tace "Ya Najib karka damu, ka fadi duk wani abu da kakeso ka fada ni kuma na maka alkawarin zan saurareka da kunnen basira, kuma zanyi kokarin fahimtar ka", ajiyar zuciya ya sauke yace "Jawahir ki tabbata bazaki tada hankalin ki ba?", tace "Ya Najib ban maka alkawarin wannan ba, na dai ce zan saurareka da kunne basira, zan tada hankali bazan tada hankali ba wannan se naji dame kazo sannan, dan ban so na maka alkawarin da bazan iya cikawa ba", shiru yayi yana sauraren ta har takai aya sannan yace "shikenan, dama maganan da zanyi akan ni dake ne", ta dago ta kalleshi tana mamakin dalilin da yasa yau Najib ya kasa fitowa ya fada mata abinda ke ranshi bayan tasan cewar shi he's a straight forward guy, ganin kallon da take mishi yasashi cigaba da cewa "I love you Jawahir", ajiyar zuciya ta sauke jin abinda yace "I've always loved you Jawahir, tin baki kai haka ba nakeson ki sedai ban nuna miki ba saboda wasu halayya da kika dorawa kanki a lokacin wanda a yanzu alhamdulillah kin gyara su", bata iya cewa komai ba yaci gaba da cewa "Jawahir dan Allah inaso ki soni koda rabin son da nake miki ne", dagowa tayi fuskarta cike da annuri mara misaltuwa tace "Ya Najib ba se ka rokeni kan naso ka ba saboda dama chan ni mai sonka ce", murmushi yayi yace "Allah koh", ta rufe fuskarta tana cewa "Allah kuwa Ya Najib", yayi ajiyar zuciya yace "bakisan yadda naji sanyi a raina ba jin wannan kalaman daga bakinki, yanzu fada min kina sona", ta kuma rufe fuskarta da tafin hannunta yace "fada min mana, yau kuma kunyata akeji", tace "Ina sonka mana Ya Najib, aiko ban fada maka ba ya kamata ace ka karance ni a duk sanda muke tare", yayi dariya tareda cewa "ayya Jawahir ai ba karatun karantar halayen mutane nayi ba balle na karance ki", kaa kai tayi shiru ya biyo baya, ita duk farin ciki ya cika ta yau yayanta Najib data dade tanaso yace yana sonta, shima kuma a nashi bangaren yana tunanin yadda ze fada mata cewar bafa ita kadai bace a zuciyarshi ba akwai Sabreena
Ganin suna batawa kansu lokaci ya gyara zama tareda fuskantar ta sosai ta kamo hannuwanta yana wasa da en tsirarun yatsunta wanda yasasu jin wani irin yanayi da basu taba ji ba barin ma shi da laushin hannunta yasashi lumshe idanu sannan ya bude yace "Jawahir", ta kara dagowa tace "na'am", yace "Jawahir akwai abinda nakeso na fada miki kuma", nan take taji gabanta ya fadi tace "ina jinka", yace "Jawahir during all those times da bama tare someone came into my life and made it special", faduwan gabanta ne ya karu yaci gaba da cewa "Jawahir i don't know how it happened but the beautiful moments I shared with her made me fall for her", nan take ta dago a razane tana kallonshi, ganin yadda ta razana yasa yayi saurin cewa "but that doesn't mean I don't love you, I
I mean I love you too but I also love her and there is nothing I can do about it, I want the both of you in my life, bazan iya rayuwa babu ku ba", idanunta cike da hawaye murya na rawa tace "who is she?", a zuciyarta tana addu'ar Allah yasa ba Sabreena bace duk da ta riga tasan ita dince, a hankali kaman wani mara gaskiya yace "Sabreena", hawayen da suka taru a idanunta ne sukayi nasarar zubowa ta zare hannunta daga cikin nashi tareda kokarin tashi yayi saurin maida ita ta zauna yace "wait Jawahir I can explain", ta girgiza kai tareda cewa "you don't need to explain because I understand everything, everything is crystal clear to me now, wato tinda banda hali me kyau, banda hali na gari shine ka zabi kaso wacce takeda duk wani good qualities da akeso a wurin mace, yanzu kuma da kaga na gyara hali na shine ka dawo amma kuma ka zabi ka haamu da wacce ta gama sanin sirrina ta gama sanin wacece ni, da kasan kana sona a lokacin me yasa baka nemi ka gyara min rayuwata daidai da yadda kakeso ba, meyasa baka fito kace Jawahir ina sonki amma halin ki ne banaso ba ka gani koh zan gyara koh bazan gyara ba, Ya Najib kasan tun yaushe nake dauke da sonka a zuciyata, tun banyi wayo ba Ya Najib, tun bansan me soyayya ba, saboda kai nake kin kula samari saboda inada hope na cewar wata rana kaima zaka soni, shine yanzu bayan ka nuna min kana sona se kuma ka zabi kayi breaking heart dina duk a lokaci daya da zance wata, watan ma ba kowa ba fac Sabreena, ina ka taba gani koh ka taba jin inda namiji ya cewa mace yana sonta sannan kuma at the same time yace mata bayan ita akwai wacce yake so kuma wacce yakeso dinma ba wata bare ba, se wanda suka san juna suka san sirrikan junansu, we are sister Ya Najib how could you! gaskiya Ya Najib baka kyautawa zuciyata ba, baka kyauta min ba, amma ba komai nasan cewar wannan kaddara tace, kuma na karbeta hannu bibbiyu, bazan taba yarda na hada miji da Sabreena ba, it's either me or her, babu zancen hada mu, muddin kuwa kace bazaka zaban daya ba toh ni zan hakura na bar mata amma ina mai tabbatar maka da cewar soyayyar ka itace zata zama ajilina", tana kai karshe ta tashi ta barshi zaune a wurin dan bazata iya zama ta saurari wani abu daga bakinshi ba, zaune kawai yake a wurin kaman an dasashi dan kasa tashi ma yayi, ya lura cewar ba kishi ne yasa Jawahir kuka ba, maganan shi na cewar akwai wasu halayenta da bayaso ne ya mata zafi, kuma tabbas ya yarda da ace a lokacin yana nuna mata kuskuran ta dazata gyara dan ya lura tana jin maganar shi, sannan kuma ya lura da ace wata yace yanaso ba Sabreena ba bazata dau abin da zafi haka ba zata mishi uziri amma kasancewar Sabreena ce shiyasa taji zafi a ranta, kanshi dake sara mishi ya dafq yana tunanin halin da Jawahir ta sashi a ciki da halin da ita take ciki yanzu dan baya tunanin ze iya zaban daya ya bar daya sannan kuma baya tunanin ze iya rayuwa ba tareda da Jawahir ba dan a wurinshi duk rayuwar da babu Jawahir a ciki toh tabbas babu Najib ma a ciki, Jawahir ta riga da ta zama wani gii na rayuwarshi da baya tunanin his life will ever be complete without her, duk sanda ze hango future dinshi da Jawahir yake hango wa
Jawahir kuwa ta kofar kitchen tabi ta shiga, seda ta tsaya ta wanke fuskarta a kitchen sannan ta shige ciki, babu kowa a parlor wannan dalilin yasa ta shige dakin da babu kowa a ciki, dakin da akayi niyyar sauketa da, tasa makulli ta kulle dan kar a dameta ta kwanta kan gado tana tunanin abubuwan da ya wakana tsakaninta da Najib, hawaye kawai takeyi ba kakkautawa dan ta riga ta makeup mind dinta bazata taba auren Najib ba muddin ze auri Sabreena dan bazata iya kishi da wacce ta gama sanin ko ita wacece ba, da wannan tunani tunanin ne ta dau wayarta tayiwa Mamah text kamar haka "super mom don't look for me, ina extra room na kwanta, I want to be alone so don't stress yourself looking for me, love you", tana gama turawa ta kashe wayarta gaba-daya ta gyara kwanciyar ta tana karanta hasbunallahu wa ni'imal wakil har ta zamu zuciyarta ya sausauta radadin da yake mata, a haka bacci ya dauke ta
Mamah na ganin text din Jawahir ta girgiza kai tareda cewa "Allah ya sanyaya miki zuciya Jawahir", batayi kokarin kiranta ba dan tanaso ta bata space for the main time

kayan jikinta tasa jeans three quarter da top sannan ta dauko tsintsiya da paker da mopper ta fara gyaran dakin, Dada kam se kallonta yakeyi yana mamakin yaushe Jawahir ta zama haka danshi a iya saninshi Jawahir daga bacci se bacci dan ko abinci be dameta ba
A makare Najib ya tashi daga bacci da salati dauke a bakinshi, ganin har takwas tayi ya shiga bathroom a gurguge yayi alwallah yazo yayi sallar asuba sannan ya koma bathroom din yayi wanka ya fito ya kimtsa ya haa abubuwan da ze bukata sannan ya fito, Abba da Ummi na zauna ya fito ya gaishe su suka amsa cike da sakin fuska sannan Ummi tace "dazu na leko naga kana bacci, ga breakfast dinka chan dan banaso kana barin kanka da yunwa", yace "toh", sannan ya mike yaje dinning ya zauna yana cin abinci badan abincin na mishi dadi ba, sedan babu yadda zeyi ne, yana gama ci yace musu zeje ya gaishe da Hajja kakar Jawahir kenan wato Naja'atu dan tinda iyayensu Yaya Aysha suka rasu yaran suka maida Naja'atu kakarsu tinda a garin Kebbi basu da wacce ta fita, nan suka mika sakon gaisuwarsu sannan ya musu sallama ya wuce
Seda ya tsaya ya siya kayan provision dayasan zata bukata sannan ya kama hanyar gidan, tana zaune a palor kamar kullum tana en karance karancenta abinku da en boko bata rabuwa da karance karance ya shiga da sallama ta amsa mishi tana mishi tace "ga ango, ga ango na maraba maraba, maraba da mutan Abuja", yayi murmushi ya zauna gefen ta yana cewa "Hajja sunnu da gida, na sameku lafiya?", tace "lafiya lau", sannan ta kwalla wa 'yar aikinta kira tareda ce mata ta kawowa ango ta abin motsa baki, nan ya mikawa 'yar aikin kayan da ya shigo dashi sannan ya gyara zama yace "matas akwai magana fah", tace "da matsala kenan", yace "babba ma", nan ta gyara zama tace "ina jinka", be boye mata komai ba ya koro mata yanda sukayi da Abbanshi da kuma yanda sukayi da Sabreena da Jawahir sannan ya kara da cewa "Hajja dan Allah ki kira Jawahir ki mata magana ko zata saduda", Hajja tace "kai dan Allah rabani da zancen Jawahir, yarinyar da daga ita har Dadanta ba jin maganata suke ba, ka dai je shi baban nata ka mishi magana kila ta saurare ka", yace "a'a matas kar muyi haka dake, wallahi Jawahir dinda kika sani ada ba ita bace ta yanzu ba, ta canza kuma na tabbata zataji maganar ki", Hajja tayi shiruuu sannan tace "shikenan naji, zan gwada sa'ata amma fa ban maka alkawari ba, idan ta amince fine, idan kuma bata amince ba seka hakura ka auri Sabreena kawai", yace "shikenan Hajja nagode, bari na gudu dan sauri nakeyi yau zan koma Abuja", Hajja tace "tsaya ina zuwa", ta mike da kyar saboda tsufa sannan ta shige kitchen bata jima ba ta dawo ta transparent plastic container har guda hudu ta mika mishi tace "gashi nan, musamman saboda kai na bari aka yi ta", sosai yaji dadi ya mata godiya yana duba abinda ke ciki, daya nikakken yaji ne, daya kuma dambun nama, daya kuma chinchin sena karshen kuma ridi ta bari aka mishi dayawa dan tasan yanda yake sonsu, a zama daya ma seya cinye, godiya ya sake yi sannan ya bar gidan
Gida ya fara zuwa ya dauki duk wani abinda ze dauka sannan yama iyayenshi sallama bayan yasa an cika musu store da kayan abinci sannan kuma ya ajiye musu 200k wai na cefane, shi Abba ma dariya abin ya bashi yace "kai zoka dau kudinka, kayan abinci ma daka siyo Allah yasa albarka", Najib ya girgiza kai yace "a'a Abba, nima lokaci yayi daya kama in fara dawainiya daku, tun tasowar mu baka taba tauye mana hakki ka hanamu abinda muke bukata ba, tinda yanzu Allah yasa nima na fara samu toh Abba ka barni in muku kodan ladan da zan samu", Abba yayi murmushi yace "shikenan Allah ya maka albarka, amma fa karka dinga takura kanka tinda bawai gazawa nayi ba", Najib yace "Inshallah Abba bazan takura kaina ba, sena dawo, ku tayani da addu'a", Yaya Aysha tace "ai kullum cikin yinta muke, Allah ya tsare ya kikaye hanya, ya kare ka", ya amsa da "ameen", sannan ya musu sallama ya wuce
Seda ya biya gidan Mamah ya musu sallama Sabreena ta rakoshi har bakin mota yace "banga 'yar uwarki ba", tace "eh taje tayiwa babanta sati daya kafin a koma school", be nuna mata komai ba yace "ok", sannan ya bata kudi na sallama taki karba, ba yanda beyi da ita ba kan ta karba taki, daga karshe ya maida kudinshi sannan ya mata sallama ya wuce, direct gidan Dada ya nufa yacewa Malam Gado ya kira mishi Jawahir, kiri kiri tace ace mai bata nan ta fita, badan malam Gado yaso na yaje ya fadawa Najib, waya Najib ya dauka ya shiga kiranta amma taki dauka, daga karshe ma kashe wayar tayi se ji yayi ance kishi switch off, sosai abinda tayi ya bakanta mishi rai, haka yaja mota ya kama hanyar Abuja ranshi duk a jagule yayinda a bangaren Jawahir kuwa karfin hali kawai takeyi, a ganinta nisanta kanta da Najib ne mafita a gareta yanda bazata kwallafa rai a kanshi ba sedai the more take ignoring dinshi the more wutar sonshi ke ruruwa a kokon ranta
