UWA TA GARI - 45 - Wattpad
Allah ne ya kai Najib Abuja lafiya dan bacin rai ma yasa tukun kawai yakeyi da wani mugun speed, koda ya isa gida Samir shima ya dawo, ganin yanayin Najib din ne ya sashi tambayar ko lafiya, koro mishi yadda sukayi da Jawahir na kin fitowa da tayi yayi Salim yace "ai na fada maka give her some up, she needs to think", Najib ya girgiza kai tareda kwanciya kan kujera ya dauki wayarshi yaci gaba da kiranta bata dauka har kiran Sabreena ya shigo mai ya kashe sannan ya kirata suka gaisa inda take tambayar shi ko ya kai gida lafiya yace mata "lafiya lau", seda suka sha hirar su sannan ya mata sallama ya kashe wayar yaci gaba da kiran Jawahir amma duk a banza
A WEEK LATER
Cikin sati dayan nan duk Najib ya zama wani iri saboda kin daukar wayarshi da Jawahir batayi gashi aiki yayi mishi yawa ba daman komawa gida wannan karon, Salim ne kaai ze tafi amma shi Najib akwai meeting dinda za'ayi a Lagos kuma dashi za'aje, rashin kin daukar wayarshi da Jawahir batayi besa yaji ta fice mishi a rai ba sema kara shiga ranshi da takeyi dan kaman kullum kara mishi wutar sonta a keyi, ya kai ya kawo koh da Sabreena yake waya se ya dinga ji kaman some part of him is missing saboda kwana biyu da yayi beji muryar Jawahir ba, duk ya rame ma saboda ita
Ita kuwa ta bangaren ta hutun ta take yi a wurin Dada, kullum ya fita ze dawo mata da kayan ice cream dasu yogurt inda ita kuma zata mishi girki kuma ba laifi yana dadi, Dada a ranshi yakan ji dadi dan yaga canji tattare da ita sosai wanda wannan yasa ko daya beyi regretting komawarta wurin Mamah da tayi ba
Hajja ta kirata kan zancen Najib inda ta nuna ita fa kar a takura mata, tinda tace batayi toh batayi dinne koda kuwa sonshi ze illata ta dan ba karamin azubtawa takeyi da soyayyar Najib ba amma kafiya da taurin kai sun yanata saukowa su fuskanci juna yadda ya dace
Duka wannan bidirin da akeyi Dada beda labari kuma Jawahir bata fada mishi dan a cewar ta me amfanin fadan
Yau take Sunday, kuma yaune take shirin komawa gida wurin Mamah, fita da ita Dada yayi ya mata siyayya sosai sannan ya maida ita gida ta hada kan kayanta, seda tayi la'asar sannan ta fito, Dada na compound zaune da newspaper a hannunshi taje tasa kayanta a mota sannan ta dawo tace "Dada ni zan wuce", ya dago yace "ki gaida gida princess, indan kun sake samun hutu ki zo kimin holiday kinji", tace "don't worry Dada zan dinga zuwa akai akai", dan a halin yanzu ma tausayi yake bata saboda bame kula dashi, ya kaa kai yace "I will send you your school fees and feeding money", tace "ok" sannan tayi hugging dinshi tareda cewa "bye, ka rage tunani kaji my Dada I love you", yayi murmushi yace "Inshallah princess, love you too and take care uhm", tace "toh", sannan ta wuce, mamaki yakeyi wai shi yau Jawahir ke cewa ya rage tunani, ita da ada lamarin mutane be shafe ta ba koda kuwa shine da yake ubanta, lallai yayi sakaci sosai wurin bata tarbiyya amma dayake Allah ya hadata da UWA TA GARI se gashi cikin kankanin lokaci ta gyara halayenta, yana kallonta ta shige mota yace "Allah ya kare min ke yayi miki albarka", seda ta mishi horn ya dago ta daga mishi hannu alamun bye bye sannan ta bar gidan Malam Gado ya rufe gate dinshi tareda komawa wurin zamanshi yana jin radio
Da sallama ta shiga gida, ba kowa a parlor dan haka ta wuce daki straight ta ajiye kayanta sannan ta fito ta wuce kitchen, a chan ta gansu, Mamah na zaune kan stool tana shan kunun kanwa inda Sabreena kuma ke soya nama kan gas, da sauri Sabreena tace "sister kin gama hutun", ta karasa ciki itama ta zauna tana cewa "na gama, gashi na dawo", Mamah tace "sannu da dawowa, ya kika baro gidan", Jawahir tace "lafiya lau", Mamah tace "amma fa kinyi jiki cikin sati dayan nan me sirrin?", tayi dariya inda Sabreena tace "laaa Mamah ban gaya miki ba, ai kullum take shan yogurt da ice cream harda shawarma, kuma kullum seta dauka a hoto ta turomin tareda emoji din gwalo harda cemin kwalele na", Mamah tace "yayi, kice ke dadi ma ya kaiki kenan", tayi dariya tareda cewa "kai Mamah wani dadi, bari na rage kayan jikina nazo na tayaku aiki dan naga aikin da yawa", Mamah tace "Abbanku ne ke hanya, yace bayan isha ze iso gida", Jawahir tace "Allah ya kawo shi lafiya, ya babies dinmu, suna kicking", Mamah tace "taba kiji", hannu takai ta taba ai kuwa taji kicking sedai ta kasa tantancewa baby daya ne ko biyu, haka ta tashi cike da farin cikin sun kusa samun kanne ta bar kitchen din
Farida ce zaune gaban malaminta tana koro mishi yadda takeso ta koma gidan Osama dan zaman haka baze yi ba, kuma tanaso idan ta koma duk rintsi kar ma yayi tunanin sakin ta balle har ya saketa din, malam ya nisa sannan yace "an gama indai wannan kikeso amma aikin ki na bukatar kudi dayawa", hannu na rawa ta bude jaka ta ciro wrapper din dubu daddaya har guda uku ta nuna mishi tana cewa "malam kagansu, akwai kudi indai kudi ne ni kawai aiki nakeso kamin, idan kamin koh nawa ne zan baka", yayi wani makarin murmushi ganin makudan kudi yace "an gama hajiya, yanzu dai ki ajiye dubu dari da hamsin wanda za'a fara aiki dashi, ke da kanki zakiga canji dan har inda kike zezo ya sameki ya maida ke gida", tayi murmushi tareda dire dubu ari biyu tace "malam ga dari biyu nan se'a yi aikin yanda ya dace", yace "kije zakiga aiki da cikawa", ta mike tana mishi godiya sannan ta fice dan komawa gida dan kosu Zulaika basusan inda taje ba gashi har yanzu ta kasa fadawa iyayenta aurenta ya mutu
Tana wucewa malam ya kwashi kudi ya zuba a aljihun babban rigar shi tareda cewa "ai kuwa zakiga aiki da cikawa, ai yau romo zamuci nida iyalina, bari naje kande ta dora mana shinkafar gwamnati da jar miya tareda romon kaza tinda an dade ba'a sadu ba", da wannan ya kulle dan dakin dake zaure inda yake aikin malantan shi na karya sannan ya shige cikin gida yana kwalawa matarshi kira
Bayan isha kaman yadda Abba ya shaida musu haka ya dawo cike da murnar ganin iyalinshi, sosai ya samu tarba me kyau daga wurin matar shi wacce ke tattalin mijinta kaman kwai, seda yayi wanka sannan ya fito sukaci abinci se kallon Mamah yakeyi saboda ganin yadda take komawa yarinya kullum a idanunshi, tayi kyau sosai ga cikin jikinta ya karbeta se dai duk ta kumbura gashi cikin yayi kato dayawa wanda wannan yasashi cewa "hanya bazaki hakura haka kiyi scan dinnan ba, girman cikin nan na bani tsoro", tayi murmushi tace "karka damu, Allah dai ya raba lafiya, nafison na haihu ba tareda nasan abinda ke cikin ba, amma ko a haka ma instinct dina na cemin namiji ne", yayi murmushi yace "idan ba haka bane kuma fah?", tace "hakan ne ma, because my instinct never fails" yayi dariya yace "ok, we shall see, kuna dai jinta koh, se lokaci yazo taga saanin hakan", sukayi dariya suna kallon Mamah din take magana confidently
Meeting dinda su Najib sukaje yi a Lagos a daddafe yayishi ya dawo, haka wannan satin ma a daddafe yayi aiki dan Allah Allah yake weekend yayi dan ji yaje kaman idan beje yasa Jawahir a idonshi ba hankalinshi baze taba kwanciya ba, duk yadda Salim yaso kwantar mishi da hankali abu ya gagara dan ko baccin arziki ma bayayi, yayi kiran, yayi text din amma duk an banza wani lokacin har kashe wayan takeyi sedai yaji switched off, be taba sanin haka Jawahir keda kafiya ba se yanzu, Salim na zauna gabanshi yana kallon yadda Najib yayi nisa cikin tunani yace "why not ka hakura da Sabreena tunda naga alamun babu yadda za'ayi ka hakura da Jawahir", dagowa Najib yayi yace "I don't know what to do, a halin yanzu komai ma zan iya yi if it means me getting my Jawahir back", cike da mamaki Salim yace "harda hakura da Sabreena?", Najib ya kada kai a hankali alamun "eh", Salim ya girgiza kai cike da tausayin Sabreena yace "guy miyasa ka yaudari kanka kan cewar kanason Sabreena bayan ba sonta kakeyi ba?", Najib yayi ajiyar zuciya tareda cewa "I thought I love her, amma ganin yanda nake neman rasa Jawahir yanzu se naga koh na auri su biyun babu ta yadda zan yi adalci tsakaninsu dan a gaskiya bana jin Sabreena yadda nakejin Jawahir a yanzu", Salim ya kaa kai cike da haushin Najib yace "in that case free her, don't lead her on indai kasan ba aurenta zakayi ba, kuma wannan weekend din tare zamuje inga wannan Jawahir in dake neman zautar da kai", Najib yace "fine, you are free to come with me, na tabbata kaima you won't blame me for loving her", harararshi Salim yayi jin abinda yace sannan ya fice daga office yanajin zafin abinda Najib ke shirin yiwa Sabreena duk da kuwa be santa ba amma ya tausaya mata dan yasan dole se anyi breaking heart dinta a nan

da taki yi, da kuma yadda yakejin a yanzu yanaso ya hakura da Sabreena dan baya ganin se iya rasa Jawahir a kan hakan, kuma koh ya hadasu bazeyi adalci ba dan se yanzu ya fahimci tsakaninshi da Sabreena shakuwa ce ba soyayya ba inda shikuma yayi mistake ya dauki shakuwar da sukayi a matsayin soyayya wanda Jawahir yake ma wannan", har ya gama bayaninshi yayi shiru Mamah batace komai ba yace "Aunty na kinyi shiru", ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tace "me kakeso nace Najib, ka dai san yadda yaran nan suke a wurina, idan nace zan goyi bayanka bamuyiwa Sabreena adalci ba ko kadan dan kuwa bana tunanin Jawahir na maka soyayyar da Sabreena ke maka, lokaci daya baze yu muzo muce tayi hakuri ba saboda yanzu ka fahimci cewar Jawahir kakeso ba ita ba, ai maganan ma bayi making sense ba, kayi hakuri Najib amma wannan karon kazo da abinda bani da karfin taimaka maka akai", shafa kanshi yayi sannan ya kalli Mamah yace "ni zanyi fahimtar da Sabreena, kwarin gwiwa nakeso ki bani Aunty na", cike da tausayi Sabreena tace "shikenan, Allah ya taimake ka amma ka bari gobe ka dawo dan bazan yarda ka hana 'yata bacci ba dan na tabbata zata shiga damuwa idan ka fada mata", idanunshi jazir jijiyoyin kanshi duk sun fito tsabar tashin hankali yace "Allah ya kaimu goben, seda safe aunty na", tace "Allah ya tashe mu lafiya" , ya tashi ya fice ya hadu da Salim zaune a compound yace mai "muje, gobe zan dawo danna fahimtar da Sabreena shawarar da na yanke sannan in daidaita tsakanina da Jawahir", cike da tausayin Sabreena Salim yace "Allah ya kaimu goben"
Bacci nakeji

Dagowa Najib yayi ya kalli Jawahir yasa hannu yana goge mata hawayen ta cikin disasshiyar murya yace "stop wasting your tears, it's all over, I'm all yours now", girgiza mishi kai tayi tace "why did you do it?", without thinking twice yace "because I don't want to loose you, I want to be with you till my last breath", sanyi taji a ranta jin abinda yace sannan tace "and I promise I will be by your side too, I love you Ya Najib", yayi murmushi har hakwaranshi na nunawa, he's been longing to hear those words from her, riko hannunta yayi yana murzawa yace "and I love you more", murmushi tayi itama sannan tace "I have to go in, inaso naje na bawa Sabreena hakuri on your behalf, even though I'm not sure she will listen to me", ya gyada mata kai sannan yace "tell her to please forgive me", tace "I will", sannan ta juya ta shiga ciki, seda yaga shigarta sannan ya bude kofar motar ya zauna a seat din me zaman banza sannan ya kalli Salim yace "take me home", Salim be musa ba ya tada motar tareda cewa "ka dinga bani directions tinda ba sanin gari nayi ba", Najib ya gyada mishi kai alamar toh
A parlor Jawahir ta hadu da Mamah ta zuba uban tagumi ta zauna kusa da ita tace "Mamah Sabreena", Mamah tace "I know, zan mata magana amma taki bude kofar wai she wants to be alone, Abbanku ma daya gaji ya shige daki wai a kyaleta inta gaji da kanta zata bude", a hankali Jawahir tace "maybe I should talk to her", Mamah tace "bari anjima, give her some space, right she doesn't want to see anybody, ina Najib din?", Jawahir tace "ya wuce", Mamah ta gyada kai sannan tace "toh Allah ya shige mana gaba", Jawahir ta amsa da "ameen", suka zauna shiru kowa da abinda yake rayawa a ranshi
A bangaren Sabreena kuka takeyi sosai yayinda zuciyarta ke mata radadi, tana yawan ji da kuma karanta labarai kan breakups da yanda yake azabtar da zuciyar dan Adam amma bata taa sanin haka zafin rabuwa da masoyi yake ba, se take gani kaman masu rubuta wa ma ko kwatan abinda ake ji basa rubuta wa balle har susan wannan feelings din, idan ba dai ya faru a kanka ba bazaka taba sanin ciwo da radadin shi
Ko kadan batayi blaming Jawahir akan abinda ya faru ba, Najib kadai take blame se kuma soyayya wacce bata mata adalci ba, amma kuma ya ta iya haka nata addarar yazo kaman yadda Najib ya fada mata kuma dole tayi imani da addara ta kuma karbeshi hannu bibbiyu

Komai ya koma musu normal kaman ba abinda ya faru tsakaninsu sedai har yanzu Sabreena bata bawa Najib fuska ba danko kiranta yayi bata dauka, tun washegarin ranar ya koma bakin aikinshi tareda Salim, a halin yanzu komai na tafiya mishi smoothly sedai rashin maganan da Sabreena batayi dashi ne yake damunshi, a kullum da safe se Salim ya turawa Sabreena good morning text message da daddare kuma ya tura mata na goodnight har tazo ta saba da sakon shi a kullum seta jira ya turo ta karanta take bacci, ya riga ya fadawa Najib shi son Sabreena yake dan tun randa ya ganta yaji ta kwanta mai kuma Najib ya bashi goyon baya dari bisa dari amma be fito ya fada mata yafiso ta sakewa dashi sosai sannan dan yasan har yanzu tanason Najib dubada yadda ko magana bataso yana hadasu

my fault back then ina facing abubuwa kala kala gashi mutum da muka je neman magani wurinshi yace in rabu da kai that's why, but don't worry as far as you want our friendship back I can be your friend again", yayi murmushi yace "why not, ai dama ke kikace in baki break kuma na fada miki I'm always available if you need me", tace "okay", sannan ta mika mishi hannu tace "friends", yace "friends", tareda shaking hannunta, nan suka fara hirar yaushe rabo ta bashi labarin abubuwan da suka faru da ita, komawarta wurin Mamah da duk wani abu daya gudana a rayuwarta baya nan, shima nan ya bata na banza duk sun watse sun barshi gashi yanzu responsiblity din gidansu ya dawo kanshi, se supermarket din mahaifiyarshi da suka tsira dashi wanda shike taimakon su
Sosai Jawahir ta tausaya mishi inda tace "nawa ake bukata na aikin da za'a mishi?", yayi murmushi cike da takaici yace "10million Naira", dan ada 10milliion ba komai bane a wurinsu gashi en ta'adda sun assara dan hatta kadarorinsu sun kwashe abu sekace aiko su akayi, nan tace "don't worry I will see what I can do", ya kalleta da mamaki yace "what do mean", tayi murmushi tace "nothing", kallonta kawai yakeyi a zuciyarshi yana cewa "Allah me iko, yau da ace Allah ya bani ikon aikata kudirina akan yarinyar da ba wannan zaman zamuyi ba a yanzu, amma gashi yanzu ga dukkan alamu she's trying to help me", maida kanshi gefe yayi dan karta gane yanayin da yake ciki da na dana sani, nan sukayi sallama ya wuce inda zashi tabi bayan shi da kallo tana mamakin yanda rayuwa ze iya canzawa mutum farat daya, ace duk kudinka cikin lokaci kankani Allah ze iya maidaka talaka haka duk talaucinka kuma cikin kankanin shima zaka iya zama attajiri, wayanta ta dauka ta kira Dada inda ringing biyu ya daga, seda suka gaisa take tambayarshi inda yake yace mata yana office, nan tace mai tana zuwa yace setazo
Daga wurin bata koma class ba ta wuce inda tayi parking ta dauki motarta se company din Dada, kasancewar an santa yasa secretary dinshi barinta ta shiga ba tareda ta bata mata lokaci ba, yana ganin ya saki tareda murmushi yace "princess har kin karaso?", tace "na karaso Dada, ya aiki", yace "aiki alhmdllh, ya akayi? u sound worried sanda mukayi waya", ya gyara zama tace "Dada kasan friend dina dinnan Jarood?", nan da nan ya bata fuska dan bason Jarood din yakeyi ba yace "wani abu ne ya sameshi?", tace "yes Dada", sannan ta bashi labarin da Jarood ya bata ya gyara zama yace "yanzu me kikeso nayi", tace "Dada I want you to help them, nasan idan mahaifinshi ya samu lafiya ya fara tafiya komai zezo mishi da sauki dan he will retrieve what he lost", juyawa Dada yakeyi a kujerar shi yana kallon ta kafin ya nisa yace "I will do it for your sake, zan bada kudin da za'a kaishi hospital din if that will make you happy", da sauri ta tashi taje ta rungumeshi tana cewa "Thank you Dada, you are the best", nan take ya rubuta mata cheque din 10million ya bata ta karba tana jin dadi sannan ta mishi godiya ta fice, tana zama a mota ta kira Jarood dan dama bata goge number dinshi ba ya dauka yace "hello Jawahir ya akayi?", tace "where are you", yace "I'm at home", tace "ok, I'm on my way", bata jira jin me zaice ba ta kashe wayan sannan ta dauki hanyar gidansu Jarood

UWA TA GARI - 49 - Page 3 - Wattpad
A gaban gidansu Jarood tayi parking sannan ta fito ta kwankwasa gate din, ba jimawa aka bude mata ta shiga, a bakin kofa ta tsaya tana sallama mahaifiyar Jarood Hajiya Turai na zaune tana kallon news tace "waye? shigo", Jawahir ta karasa shiga ta tsugunna ta gaisheta tareda gaishe da Alhaji El Mu'az dake zaune kan wheelchair gefe daya ya zabga uban tagumi, cike da farin ciki tace "Jawahir kice kika zama haka, ai rabon dana ganki har na manta", Jawahir tayi dariya ta zauna kusa da ita tace "wallahi Hajiya karatu ne ya boye ni", tace "madallah Allah ya taimaka, nasan an kusa gamawa yanzu koh", tace "yanzu nake third year dina", Hajiya tace "da kin kare se aure", Jawahir tayi dariya tana rufe fuska
Gaishe da Alhaji tayi ya amsa ta mishi ya jiki yace "da sauki", tareda dauke kai dan bayaso ana mishi ya jikin nan gani yake kaman kowa ya gama ganin weakness dinshi ba'a mishi kallon girman da ake mishi ada saboda yanzu bashi da komai, Hajiya Turai ce ta katse musu shirun da sukayi da cewa "bari na kira Jarood", tareda tashi ta shige ciki, bata dade ba suka dawo tareda Jarood dake kokarin sa riga dan yana jin Jawahir tazo ya tashi tareda rigarshi a hannu ya fito, a palor ya ganta yace "Jawahir hope all is well, naga bamu dade da rabuwa ba?", tace "nazo wurin ka", yace "ok, muje waje", ta mike tayiwa su Hajiya sallama gaba-daya sannan suka fice, a compound ta ciro cheque dinda Dada ya bata ta mika mishi ya amsa yana cewa "me wannan?", tace "bude ka gani", budewa yayi amma se ya kasa magana ganin cheque din 10million da suke nema ido rufe saboda kai Alhajin su kasar waje a mishi aiki, sedai baze iya amsar kudin daga hannun Jawahir ba dan wannan harkar karanta ce, maida mata cheque din yayi yace "I'm sorry bazan amsa ba", tace "Jarood why not, you need it", yace "You are right I need it amma bazan karbi makudan kudade haka daga wurin ki ba, don't worry zan samu koh a bank ne zanje na nema rance", tace "why bank bacin ga kudin nan a hannunka kaje ka karba, don't make this difficult, taimako nayi niyar yi karka ki karba please", yace "indai taimako na zakiyi toh ki ranta mun amma karki bani kyauta dan bazan karba ba, ki ranta min da kadan kadan zan biyaki har na gama", tace "ba matsala, you can pay back idan ka samu but for now have the money", ta mishi hakan ne dan ya karba bawai da gaske ranta mishin tayi ba ita kyauta ta bashi, da kyar ta samu ya karba ya mata godiya tareda alkawarin biyanta idan Allah ya bashi iko
Jarood ya nunawa iyayenshi kudin tareda fada musu yanda sukayi da Jawahir suka dinga sa mata albarka inda Alhaji da kanshi yace "yana dawowa kan kafafunshi ze biya ta kudin ta dan kuwa idan Allah ya bashi lafiya se ya maido duka abinda suka salwanta sakamakon fashin da aka musu danshi yafi zargin aiko su akayi, nan Jarood ya kira doctor dinsu wanda ze hadasu da me aikin afan yace sun samu kudin, cikin sati daya sukayi duk wani abinda ya dace sukabi duk wani process daya dace subi jirgin su ya aga daga nan gida Nigeria se Mexico dan nemawa Alhaji lafiya, (Allah yasa a dace)
Farida ce gaban malaminta tana cewa "malam ni na rasa abinda yasa aikin nan bayaci, kace zezo har yanzu bezo ba going to two months kenan ana abu daya gashi kudade na duk sun kare ba biyan bukata wai me kake ciki ne malam",  Malam ya sauke ajiyar zuciya yace "bincike na ya nuna min aiki ne ya mishi yawa dan be dade da dawowa garin ba ma amma yanzu zan miki aikin da duk yawan aikinshi dole ya samu lokaci yazo gareki", tace "malam dan Allah ka taimaka, banso na gama idda bezo ya maida ni ba, gashi saura na wata daya da en kwanaki", yace "karki damu zezo", sannan ya janyo tray din gabanshi wanda kasa ne ciki yayi en rubuce rubucen shi yace "zamuyi sadaka, kuma Inshallah da anyi sadakar nan an gama aiki", tace "Allah dai yasa baza'a bukaci kudi dayawa dan duk kudade na sun kare", yayi wani makirin murmushi yace "wannan karon  ba kudi ake bukata ba, aljani na  yace maniyyi yake bukata", gabanta ya fadi tace "subhanallah, maniyyi kuma, ina nasan zan samo shi", ya kalleta yana lashe baki yace "abu me sauki, tarawa dake zanyi idan kika kawo se mu zuba maniyyin ki a wannan kwaryar shikenan an gama aiki", ta zuba mishi wata irin harara tace "meka dauke ni, kawura ko me, ina budurwa ma banyi zina ba se yanzu, duk iskanci na bana zina, kuma idan zanyi ma bazanyi da kazamin mutum irinka ba, duk ka jera Qur'anai a daki kaman wani na Allah ashe nan dan iska ne kai, tur da hali irin naka", ta mike zata wuce yace "ai dani dake ba banbanci idan na nemi na tara dake sai me, ba gwanda ni a kan ke da kike shige shigen malamai kina kauce hanyar Allah ba, yanzu kin zo kina wani tur da halina, ke ba'ayi tur da halinki ba kinayi da na wani", batada abinda zatace mishi dan gani take kaman tsayawa mishi magana bata lokaci ne, dan haka taja tsaki tayi ficewar ta tana Allah wadar da masu hali irin nashi, se yanzu take dana sanin zuwa wurin shi da takeyi har take karanto mishi matsalolin ta tana gani kaman ze iya mata magani, ta manta cewar Allah ne wanda ya kamata ta koma gareshi ko al'amuran ta zasu warware
Tana komawa gida ta shiga karantowa su Zulaika yanda sukayi da sabon malamin ta Nafisa tace "dama kinsamu sabon malami shine bamu da labari", taja tsaki tace "ina ce miki ga abinda yace min ke kina maganan baku da labarin shi ai gani nayi komai ma na bukatar sirri tinda malamin da kika kaini wurinshi sanda nake gidan Osama ba abinda ya tsinana mun tunda aikinshi be hana Osama sallamo ni ba", Nafisa ta fusata tace "ni kike yiwa magana haka kaman wata tsarar ki, kar ki ga ina sake miki ina miki dariya ki nemi ki raina ni, yanzu shi wannan malamin da kika je wurinshi me ya tsinana miki", Farida tace "raini na yaushe kuma, tunda za'a zauna ayi wasa da dariya ayi shewa, ai babu wani mutumci daya rage tsakani na dake balle kice na raina ki",  nan fa abu ya zame musu fada banda tune tune na sirrikan junansu ba abinda sukeyi inda Farida ke blaming Zulaika da Nafisa akan bata gurbatattun shawara wanda ita take dauka har yayi sanadiyar mutuwar aurenta kuma ba komai yasa sukayi haka sedan sunga su ko mashinshini basu da shi, sosai fada ya kaure tsakaninsu har dambe, Salma ganin abun ba sauke ta wuce daki ta dauki wayarta ta fara kiran iyayensu, mahaifiyar Farida ce ta fara zuwa, duk yadda taso raba su abu ya gagara dan muryar su har makota ga unguwa estate ba hayaniya shiyasa muryarsu ke tashi sosai, gabadayansu iyayensu mata sunzo inda mahaifiyar Farida ta kira mijinta take fada mishi abinda ke faruwa, ba jimawa yazo ya shigo da sallama amma babu wanda ya amsa shi, tsawa ya daka musu wanda yasa  ko waccensu ta tsorota, Farida na ganin babanta tasha jinin jikinta danshi mutun ne da baya daukar nonsense yace "kowa ya nemi wuri ya zauna", duk suka zauna kasa iyayensu suka zauna kan kujera yace "meya faru", Salma ce ta koro musu abinda ya faru tun farko mahaifiyar Farida tasa salati tareda cewa "Farida dama aurenki ya mutu wurin wata biyu kenan amma bamu da labari, dan uwarki baki da gidan zuwa ne kikazo kika tare a nan, baki fada mana ba balle ayi sulhu shine zaki fara shigan malamai, nida nake mahaifiyarki ban bata sanin gidan malami ba balle ace a wurina kika koya shine ke dan rashin a'a zaki daga kafa kije gidan malami wai ke isassa koh, toh mema ya raba auren", Babanta yace "bari muje gidan zamuyi maganan a can, amma abinda nakeso shine daga yanzu an daina zaman gidan na dan banga dalilin da zesa kuzo ku tare a gida ku kadai ba kaman baku da mafadi, ada mun kyaleku ne dan muna gani kaman kuna da hankali ashe dai baku dashi dan haka duk ku tattare ku koma gaban iyayenku, ke kuma", ya fada yana nuna Farida yace "karki bari na riga ki kaiwa gida", yana fadar haka ya fice inda mahaifiyarta ma tabi bayan shi ko wannensu ya shiga motarsa suka tayar suka bar gidan itama Farida ta fito tana turo baki tabi bayansu
Sosai ran mahaifin Farida ya aci ya karasa gida yana huci, yana shiga matarshi ta biyo bayanshi tareda kawo mishi ruwan sanyi ya karba yasha ya zauna yana karkaa kafa yana jiran shigowar Farida dan yasan tana hanya, a tsorace ta shigo gidan tayi parking sannan ta iso parlorn muryarta na rawa tayi sallama mahaifinta yace "shigo marar kunya", a tsorace ta shiga ta nemi wuri jikin kujera ta zauna a takure tana jiran abinda za ai mata dan mahaifinta duk da yanason yara yana kuma shagwaba su bayason raini, ta tabbata da ace ita da kanta tazo ta fada mutuwar auren ta tun sanda abin ya faru bazeyi fushi haka ba, kallonta yayi zuciyarshi na kuna yace "meya fito dake gidan mijinki?", jikinta ya fara rawa ta rasa abinda zata ce dan kuwa harga Allah bazata iya bude baki tace mishi ciki ta zubar ba, maimaita tambayar yayi tayi shiru tana kallon carpet dinda ke shimfide a tsakiyar parlorn mahaifiyarta tace "Farida bada ke ake bane kin mana shiru kaman wasu sa'annin wasanki, kodan ana sake miki fuska, zaki fadi abinda kikayi mijinki ya sake ki ko kuwa dan na tabbata haka kurum Osama bazece ya sake ki ba", Farida taja baya ganin mahaifiyarta na neman kai mata duka tace "Mama kiyi hakuri amma wallahi bazan iya fada muku ba, sedai idan ku kirashi kuji ta bakinshi", mamanta tace "ya za'ayi mu kira mutum bamusan laifin da kikayi ba, ko shine da laifin?", ta tambaya Farida ta girgiza kai alamar "a'a", mamanta zatayi magana mahaifinta ya daga musu hannu alamar duk suyi shiru sannan ya kalli Farida yace "tashi ki shiga ciki, zan nemi shi mijin naki", cikin sanyin jiki ta tashi ta wuce ciki shi kuma ya ciro wayarshi ya lalubo numbar Osama ya danna mishi kira, ringing biyu ya daga tareda sallama mahaifin Farida ya amsa tareda cewa "dan Allah idan bazan takura ka ba inason ganin ka", Osama yace "Inshallah zanzo bayan magrib", Babanta yace "Allah ya kai mu", sannan duk suka kashe waya suka ajiye kowa da sake saken da yakeyi a zuciyarshi
Bayan magrib Dada yayi sallama a gidan sannan ya fadawa me gadinsu a cewa Alhaji ya karaso, ba dadewa me gadin ya dawo tareda mishi iso cikin gidan, a parlorn saukar baki ya zauna aka kawo mishi ruwa da kayan motsa baki shi duk ya kagu Babanta ya fito yaji kiran me ya mishi, ba dadewa ya shigo da sallama yana cewa "yi hakuri na barka zauna", Osama ya gyara zama yace "ba komai alhaji, na sameku lafiya", yace "lafiya lau", nan suka gaisa sannan Babanta ya mishi bayan halin da yaje ya riski su Farida da yanda yaji labarin sakinta ba tareda tazo gida ita ta fada musu ba, yanzu kuma ta fada lafin da tayi taki magana, Dada yace "ai wannan tsohon labari ne dan idan lassifa na daidai ne ta kusa wata biyu bata gida na", Babanta ya nisa yace "wani laifi ta maka har ka sake ta", Dada ya kalleshi sannan yayi murmushi yace "ita tana ina, dan bazan yi magana ba se'a gabanta dan kar tazo tace ba haka bane, saboda na tabbata Farida babu abinda bazata iya ba", Babanta yace "ok", sannan ya dauki waya ya kira Farida yace tazo ta sameshi a parlorn baki, duk da bataso ba haka ta zari hijabi taje, da sallama ta shiga suka amsa mata ta nemi wuri ta zauna tana kallon Osama Wanda ya kara haske da fresh amma ya danyi rama mahaifinta yace "gata tazo, bismilla ina jinku kumin bayani", Osama ya gyara zama yace "wato Alhaji Farida ta min gagarumin laifi wanda bajin zan iya yafe mata", Alhajin yace "subhanallah", yayin da zuciyar Farida ke dukan uku uku Osama yace "Alhaji ba komai bane dalilin da yasa na saki Farida ba illa cikina data zubar bada izini na ba kuma baso daya ba har so biyu", Babanta ya kalleta da sauri yace "zubar da ciki a zuri'a ta", Osama yayi murmushin rainin hankali sannan ya bashi labarin yadda akayi tiryan tiryan, banda salati da mamaki ba abinda Babanta keyi ya kalleta yace "Farida abinda ya fada da gaske ne", tayi shiru ta kasa karya tawa sema hawaye da takeyi dan tasan kashinta ya bushe Babanta yace "me dalilin ki na zubar da ciki", tayi shiru, ya kai mata duka tareda cewa "bada ke nake ba", cikin muryar kuka tace "wallahi Baba su Zulaika ne sukace wai idan na yarda na haihu zan tsufah da wuri kuma Osama ze daina sona ya auro wata banga haka yayiwa tsuhowar matarshi ba daga haihuwa se saki saboda ya daina sonta, wai nima idan na haihu haka zemin shiyasa nake zubar wa duk sanda na gane inada ciki", Babanta ya fara salallami, cikin fusata ya tashi ya fara jibgarta tana zillewa yana kamo ta da kyar Osama ya samu ya janye ta hannun Babanta sannan yace "Alhaji ayi hakura, adai mata fada saboda karta sake amma banda duka", ya koma ya zauna yana huci yace "yanzu wannan 'yar banzar yarinyar harta san ta zubar ciki, ta kashe rai, rai ne fa da Allah ya halitta ta tsatson ta wanda ba kowa Allah yakewa wannan baiwar ba shine ita zata samu kuma ta zubar", Dada dai hakuri yake bashi Babanta ya kalleta yace "da nayi niyyar bawa mijinki hakuri dan banyi tunanin laifi yayi girman wannan ba amma yanzu kam banda bakin nema miki afuwa a wurinshi", da fadar haka ya tashi ya buga babbar rigarshi ya shige gida ya barta wurin, ya shigewa Osama ma ya tashi ze fice tayi saurin riko kansan wandon shi tace "dan Allah Osama karka mun haka, wallahi banida gidan da yafi gidanka, ka taimaka kayi hakuri ka yafe mun ka maida ni gidan ka wallahi na tuba, kuma nayi alkawarin bazan sake ba dan Allah kayi hakuri", Dada ya kalleta cike da tausayawa dan in so ne yana son Faridar sa sedai laifin da ta mishi baya tunanin ze iya yafe mata balle har ya manta yacigaba da zaman aure da ita, girgiza kai yayi yana kawar da tunanin dake bijiro mishi ya janye kafarshi ya fice ya barta wurin tana kuka tareda dana sanin jin maganar su Zulaika da Nafisa, se yanzu ta gane Salma ce me sonta dukda kuwa itace karamar su amma tafi su hankali dan da tabi shawarar Salma da kila har yanzu tana gidan mijin ta, seda tayi kukanta me isarta sannan ta tashi ta shige cikin gida inda ta tarar da babban yayanta zaune kusa da Babansu yana karkaa kafa yayinda Mamanta ke zaune gefe tana hawaye, ko ba'a fada mata tasan Babanta ya riga ya fada musu komai, take jikinta ya fara rawa saboda tunkaro ta da yayanta keyi, beyi wata wata ba ya fara kai mata duka, ba wanda ya hanashi har seda sukaga ta kusa shidewa sannan mamanta tazo tana janyeshi amma ina wannan ma be mishi ba seda ya bita ya tattaka ta  ya kara mata da ashar sannan ya fice ya bar musu gidan, jiki na ciwo tana kuka haka ta tashi ta shige dakin ta, cikin dare jikinta ya kiya ciwo ya kamata farat daya har karkarwa jikinta keyi Allah yasa mamanta ta leka ta da niyyar gasa mata jiki da tarar da ita a wannan yanayin, dole suka kaita asibiti a wannan daren inda aka kwantar da ita tareda mata allurai ta samu bacci
Mamah na zaune a daki bayan sallar magrib ta rasa inda zatasa kanta saboda ciwon baya daya rie ta se safa da marwa takeyi a dakin ita kadai ta rasa inda zatasa kanta taji dadi, Sabreena ce ta shigo tana cewa "Mamah food is ready, kizo mu
", bata karasa ba tayi turus tana kallon Mamah da gaba-daya bata cikin hayyacin ta, maimakon ta bata taimakon gaggawa seta makale bakin kofa tana bin Mamah da kallo, idan tayi gabas ta bita da kallo idan tayi yamma ta bita kallo dan ita kanta a rude take, Jawahir ce jin shiru shiru ta biyo bayansu, tana ganin halin da ake ciki ta kaiwa Sabreena duka a baya tuni ta dawo hayyacinta, Jawahir tace "sa mata hijab ina zuwa", da sauri Sabreena ta sawa Mamah hajib ta kamo ta suka fito waje inda Jawahir kuma ta dauko key din motar ta tareda karamin jakar da suka sa kayan da za'a bukata ta kai mota sannan ta dawo ta taimaka musu suka sata mota, gate man na ganinsu ya bude gate din suka fice yana musu addu'ar Allah ya raba lafiya, a hanya Sabreena ta kira Abbanta ta fada mishi suna hanyar asibiti yace ze samesu a chan, basuyi wani tafiya me tsayi ba suka isa asibitin, nurses suka karbeta akayi labour room da ita, suna nan corridor din wuri suna duk wata addu'a da tazo bakinsu na Allah ya sauke ta lafiya, suna tsaye Abba yazo shima ya nemi wuri ya zauna yana cewa "Jawahir zoki zauna kema", ta matso ta zauna kusa da Sabreena hankali tashi dan kusan 30mins kenan amma har yanzu shiru ba labari, seda sukayi kusan 1hour sannan nurse ta fito da murmushi suka nufota da sauri Sabreena tace "nurse ya Mamah, me ta haifa?", nurse din tayi murmushi tace "ku kwantar da hankalinku ta sauka lafiya kuma an samu en biyu namiji dana mace", tsalle su Jawahir sukayi suna murna yayinda Abba keta hamdala yana mika godiyar shi ga  Allah me kowa me komai, cikin kankanin lokaci aka gyara Mamah da Babies dinta aka kawosu private room aka shimfide, Abba yazo ya mara yaran huduba yasa musu suna Nabil da Nabila su Jawahir dadi kaman zasuyi me, sun kira Yaya Aysha suka fada Jawahir ta kira Najib ta fada mishi good news din inda Sabreena ta dinga kira Hajiya kakarta ta fada mata, haka suka dinga kiraye kiraye cikin lokaci kankani labari ya kai har kogi inda ake ta tayasu murna wasu na alkawarin zuwa suna, Mamah dai se baccin gajiya takeyi batasan wainar da take toyawa ba

UWA TA GARI - 50 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Se tsakiyar dare Mamah ta tashi daga baccin gajiyar da takeyi wanda yayi daidai dasa kukan yaran, Sabreena da Jawahir basu tafi gida ba, su suka zauna da ita dan haka suka dinga lallashin yaran, ganin alamar ta tashi suka karasa gabanta da murmushi suna mata sannu, ta amsa musu tana mika hannu alamar su bata yaran, Jawahir ce ta fara mika mata maccen inda Mamah ta kare mata kallo taga da mahaifinta take kama, hamdala tayi tana godewa Allah daya mata wannan gagarumin kyautar ya sauya mata rayuwa lokaci daya ya dawo mata da farin cikinta, ya bata miji na nunawa sa'a, ya dawo mata da 'yarta sannan kuma ya kara mata da kyautar en biyu, lallai hausawa sunyi gaskiya da sukace "mahakurci mawadaci", nono taba yaran suka koma bacci sannan ta kalli su Jawahir tace "meyasa baku koma gida ba, kusan akwai makaranta gobe ai", Sabreena tace "bamason barin ki ke kadai ne, Yaya Aysha zatazo da safe mu kuma se mu wuce", ta kaa kai sannan tace "Abban ku fah?", Jawahir tace "ya koma gida dayaga baki tashi ba, ya sa musu suna Nabil da Nabila", Mamah tayi murmushi dan ita ta nemi alfarman yasa wannan sunan saboda tana son sunan
Washegari da safe Yaya Aysha tazo da kayan tea tareda duk wani abu da Mamah zata bukata su Jawahir kuma suka koma gida saboda zasuje school, da yamma aka sallami su Mamah dan daga ita har yaran duk lafiyarsu kalau, sosai en uwa da abokan arziki ke tururuwar zuwa barka harda makotan ta dama wa'anda bata sani ba, hidiman jego be hana su Jawahir zuwa school ba, weekend Najib da Salim sukazo ganin babies wanda albarkacin yaran Najib ya samu Sabreena ta mishi magana har take cewa ita ta dade da yafe mishi kawai dai bata ganin zata iya sakin jikinta dashi kamar da ne shiyasa bata daukar wayar shi dan bata ga dalilin daukar ba ma kwata kwata, beyi fushi ba yace shi ya gode mata ma da har ta iya ta yafe mishi, duk wannan hirar da sukeyi Salim na jinsu amma besa baki ba, seda ya bari suka gama sannan yace wa Najib "guy nima bani aron 5mins", Najib yayi dariya tareda tashi yace "take your time", kitchen ya wuce inda Jawahir ke kokarin dora ruwa yace "matar Najib", ta saki murmushi tareda juyowa ta kalleshi tace "angon Jawahir", ya karasa cikin kitchen din tareda zama kan stool tace "Ina ka baro Salim din?", yace "yana waje tareda Sabreena", cike da mamaki tace "Sabreena kuma?", yace "yes, shima ita ya kyallaro wa kanshi", ta kaa kai tareda cewa "ashe dai duk na gida za'ayi", yace "I can't wait", ta zauna kusa dashi sannan tace "you have to, na fada maka sena gama karatu na zamuyi aure dan bazan yarda ka ajiyeni a Kebbi ka tafi Abuja aiki ba", ya marairaice mata yace "Jawahir soyayyar ki na wahalar dani, idan bamuyi aure soon ba ina mai tabbatar miki da zan lalace in zama wani iri dan ni kadai nasan abinda nakeji tattare dake, shekara daya ya rage miki, cikin shekara dayan nan zan dinga zuwa ina duba ki, kema idan kin samu hutu se kizo Abuja inda nake, inyaso zan nema miki alfarma a kaiki Abuja youth service", ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tace "you know I love you too and I also want to be with you amma banson nayi distracting kaina, ga aure ga karatu, gashi zan shiga final year, and you know dole na kara himma yanzu, I want to graduate with first class", yace "Inshallah you will graduate with first class kuma auren mu baze hanaki karatu ba, ki duba ki gani pls", ta cire tagumin da tayi tana kallonshi tace "Dada baze yarda ba", yace "ze yarda, I'm sure ze yarda saboda abinda kikeso shi yake so", ta sake sauke ajiyar zuciya dan ta rasa yadda zatayi da Najib tace "I will think about it", yace "pls do and don't take time", tayi murmushi tace "I won't"
angaren Sabreena kuwa Salim ya sata gaba se magiya yake mata kan ta amince da soyayyar sa tana cewa a'a saboda shi abokin Najib ne, bazeyu su maida ita kaman rigar sawa ba, wannan ya cire wannan ya dauka yasa, ba yanda beyi da ita ba taki ta saurare shi, idanunshi har yayi ja ganin yana nema ya rasa ta yace "Sabreena ni daban, Najib daban, dan kinyi soyayya da Najib does not mean bazaki iya soyayya dani ba, look at you for example ada kince you don't mind dating Najib koda kuwa yana son Jawahir who happens to be your step sister, kinga nima that is my own case, soyayyar ki daga Allah ne Sabreena, i don't mind, I don't care ko kin taba soyayya da abokina ko baki taba ba all I want is you, consider my love for you and give us a chance pls", ta kalleshi tareda sauke idanunta kasa ganin kallon da yake mata wanda ke kashe mata jiki, tabbas tasan she feels something for him sedai ta kasa ganewa so ne take mishi ko kuwa makamancin hakan, bata so ta sake jefa kanta cikin soyayyar da daga baya zata wahala a cikin ta, ganin shirun da tayi yayi yawa ne yasa Salim cewa "Sabreena
", yanda ya kira sunanta yasata kallonshi, setaji ya bata tausayi ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tace "shikenan Salim na amince Allah yasa hakan shine mafi alkhairi", dadi yaji sosai kaman yayi tsalle ya rungume ta se kuma yayi restraining kanshi daga yin hakan yace "Nagode Sabreena Inshallah you won't regret making this decision, I promise", tayi murmushi ganin yadda yake murna kaman karamin yaron da aka ba biscuit, a hankali tace "ni zan shiga ciki, na bar Jawahir ita kadai tana aiki", yace "I will call you later", ta sake murmushi tareda girgiza kai ta shige ciki tana mamakin yadda yakejin dadi dan kawai tace ta amince, tana zuwa kitchen Najib ya fito ya koma wurin Salim suka wuce ita kuma Sabreena ta fara ba Jawahir labarin yadda sukayi da Salim Jawahir ta mata murna tareda cewa "Allah ya tabbatar mana da alkhairi", Sabreena ta amsa da "ameen"
Kwanan Farida biyar a hospital aka sallameta, da komawarta gida mahaifinta ya sallami masu aikin gidan yace aiki ya dawo hannunta tinda batajin magana, tayi kuka kaman ranta ze fita tareda dana sanin halin da ta jefa kanta, gashi yanzu ta dawo square one, ba mijin ba haihuwa ga wahalan aikin gida, tana zaune bayan ta gama goge kayan ta wayarta ya fara ringing, tana dubawa taga Salma ce ke kiranta, dauka tayi tareda mata sallama Salma ta amsa sannan tace "Farida Zulaika ta kira ki?", tace "a'a bata kira ba, ya akayi", Salma tace "wai aure zatayi, babanta yace ta fito da miji tace bata dashi aka bata cousin dinta, nan da two weeks ne auren", Farida ta tae baki tace "Allah ya basu zaman lafiya", Salma ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tace "Farida ya kamata ku zauna kuyi settling differences dinku, bazeyu ku rabu akan abinda bekai ya kawo ba, itama Nafisa na kirata take cemin ita an bata one month ta fito da miji wai zaman nata hakan bazeyu ba, nasan basu miki adalci ba sedai kema da naki a ciki, yanzu hakuri zakiyi ku hadu ku gyara abinda kuka bata", Farida tace "in kin gama inada aikin yi se an jima", Salma tayi mamakin abinda Farida tace sedai itama batada wani abin cewar dan haka tace "ki gaishe da mama", daga haka duk suka kashe wayan Farida tasa kuka a ranta tace "wato ita sunyi sanadiyar mutuwar aurenta shine su zasuyi bayan sun maida ta bazawara", seda tayi me isarta bame lallashi sannan tayi shiru ta dauki wayarta ta dannawa Osama kira, har wayar ta gama ringing be dauka ba ta sake kira still be dauka ba, seda tayi kira ya kai so biyar sannan ana shida ne ya dauka ganin batada niyyar dena kira, yana dauka tasa mai kuka tareda bashi hakuri kan yayi hakuri yazo ya maida ita gidanta tayi alkawarin bazata sake aikata abinda ta aikata ba, sosai ta bashi tausayi cikin sanyin murya ya shiga kwantar mata da hankali sannan yace zeyi tunani akai idan har yaji ze iya dawo da ita zezo ya maida ita kafin ta gama idda, godiya ta dinga jero mishi shikuwa banda mamakin ta ba abinda yakeyi
Anyi taron suna lafiya an watse wa'anda sukazo daga nisa da kusa duk sun tafi se Baba Salamatu da tace zata zauna da Mamah har tayi arba'in wanda Mamah taji dadin hakan ta shaku da Baba Salamatu sosai kwata kwata bataso rabuwar su ba, ta samu kaya sosai daga ita har babies dinta wa'anda suke kara kyau da girma, Nabil yafi Nabila rigima dan idan yanajin yunwa ya dinga kuka kenan bejin lallashi harse an kulashi, ita kuwa Nabila idan tanajin yunwa zatasa babbar yatsar ta a baki tayi ta tsotsa abinta bata cika kuka ba shiyasa ma Jawahir tafi sonta dan ita bame son hayaniya bace amma kullum setace Nabil ya cika son hayaniya a koda yaushe kukanshi akeji
Kafin Najib ya koma bakin aikinshi a kullum seyasa Jawahir gaba yana mata magiya kan ta amince ya fito akai kudi gidansu tace "a'a", tun tana kiyawa har dai ta gaji tace mishi taji zasuyi shawara da Mamah duk abinda tace zata bari ya sani, da wannan ta samu ya shafa mata lafiya inda soyayyar Sabreena da Salim kuwa se abinda yayi gaba dan tun bata sakin jikin ta dashi har tazo ta saki jikinta dan Salim mutum ne me faran faran da wasa ga zolaya
Suna zaune a parlorn Baba Salamatu hankalinta na kan tv inda Mamah ke bawa Nabil nono tana hira da Baba Salamatu sama sama Sabreena na chatting a wayarta wanda ga dukkan alamu da Salim take chatting Jawahir kuma na zaune gefe da Nabila a hannunta tana mata wasa, kallo daya zaka musu ka tabbatar da kwanciyar hankalin dake wanzuwa a wannan family din, wayar Jawahir ce ya dauki ruri alamar kika ta duba taga an rubuta LOML dauka tayi tareda tashi tabi hanyar dakinsu Mamah ta bita kallo, a daki ta zauna tace "Ya Najib", yace "babyna na kasa sukuni, gani a wurin aiki amma na kasa tabka komai, dan Allah do something kiyiwa Mamah magana", Jawahir ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tana kallon Nabila dake gyangyadi tace "ya zanyi dakai tinda ina son ka, ka kwantar da hankalinka zan mata magana duk yadda ake ciki I will let you know", yayi kayataccen murmushi yace "shiyasa kullum nake kara sonki, ba kyason ganina cikin damuwa", tace "inka shiga damuwa nima hankali na baze kwanta ba", haka sukaci gaba da hirar su cike da nishadi kafin ya mata sallama yace ze kira anjima yaji abinda suka yanke
Parlor ta koma inda ta zauna kusa da Mamah tareda mika mata Nabila tace "tayi bacci", Mamah tace "kedai da Nabila indai kina gida toh tana makale dake, karki sabar mata da hannu fah", Jawahir tayi murmushi tareda cewa "Mamah akwai maganar da nakeso muyi", Mamah ta kalleta tace "do you need privacy", ta girgiza kai tace "no need, dama Ya Najib ne ya dameni wai ze turo manyansa", Mamah ta girgiza kai tace "dadi na dashi gajen hakuri, yanzu ke me kika ce mai?", "nace zan miki magana duk abinda kika ce I will let him know", Mamah tace "shikenan, bari Abbanku ya dawo zan fada mishi inyaso se yaje ya samu Dadanki, ki daiyi addu'a Allah yasa kar Dadanki yace a'a", Jawahir tace "shikenan Allah yasa muji alkhairi", kowa ya amsa da "ameen", Sabreena tace "su sister an kusa zama amarya, daga yanzu Anty amarya zan dinga ce miki", tayi dariya tareda cewa "banson zolaya, waya sani ma koh tare dake za'a haamu", Baba Salamatu tace "ai kuwa da yafi", Mamah tace "kun kawo shawara, indai Dadanki ya yarda Najib ya fito shima Salim zamuce ya fito", Sabreena tace "Allah Mamah ban shirya ba", Mamah tace "ai dama base kin shirya ba indai mu a shirye muke ai shikenan", duk suka sa mata dariya Jawahir na mata gwalo

UWA TA GARI - 51 - Page 4 - Wattpad
Bayan Abba ya dawo yayi wanka yaci abinci ya huta Mamah ta dauko mishi maganar Najib na yanason ya turo magabatan shi dan haka idan bazai takura ba ya taimaka yaje suyi maganar da Dada, Abba yace "haba kekuwa ai ba maganar takura a nan tinda Jawahir 'yata ce, in Allah ya kai mu gobe zanje tareda abokina Alhaji Abbas mu mishi maganar", Mamah taji dadi tace "nagode, Allah ya saka da alkhairi", yayi murmushi tareda cewa "ameen", nan Mamah tace "se kuma maganar Sabreena", yace "uhm inaji", ta gyara zama tace "dama so nake idan mahaifin Jawahir ya amince Najib ya fito itama a bari wannan yaron Salim ya fito kaga se a haa auren a musu tare", ya kalleta yace "wannan ma shawara ce amma a iya sanina ai basu dade dashi Salim din ba", tace "eh basu dade ba amma ai yaron kirki ne, ga girmama na gaba dashi", Abba yayi shiru yana tunani sannan yace "shikenan zan sa ayi bincike kan yaron dan banso azo a samu matsala nan gaba", Mamah tace "Inshallah baza'a samu matsala ba, amma kasa ayi binciken a kanshi naji kaman Najib yace dan Katsina ne", Abba ya kaa kai yace "zan bari a bincika mun", nan suka tsaida magana kan cewar washegari zeje yaga Dada
Washegari se yamma Abba ya samu abokinshi Alhaji Abbas suka je wurin Dada kuma cikin ikon Allah suka sameshi zaune a harabar gidanshi yana karanta jarida, suna shigowa ya dago ya kallesu yanaso yasan inda ya sansu amma babu alamar ya sansu a wani wuri, mikewa yayi bayan sun karaso suka mika mishi hannu sukayi musabaha sannan yace "sedai ban gane fuskokin ba", Abba yayi murmushi sannan yace "mu samu wuri mu zauna tukun", Dada yace "toh mu shiga daga ciki", Alhaji Abba yace "a'a nan ma yayi, gwara mu zauna iskar Allah na kada mu", duk suka dara sannan Dada ya karo musu kujera biyu ya ajiye duk suka zauna yace "ina zuwa bari na kawo muku ruwa", Abba yace "daka barshi wallahi dan daga gida muke", Dada ya dawo ya zauna yana jira su fara magana, Abba ya gyara zama yace "sunana Harun miji ga mahaifiyar Jawahir wato Hindu tsohuwar matarka", duk da yaji ba dadi a ranshi amma ko a fuska be nuna ba yace "Masha Allah, Ashe da rabon zamu gana", Abba yace "Jawahir ta haa fuskokin mu", Dada yace "ai kuwa", basu tsaya dogon zance ba Abba yace "nazo ne akan Jawahir, wato ta samu ma nemi wanda yake sonta da aure shine yakeso ya turo magabatanshi, kasancewar ka mahaifinta mukaga kai ka dace daka bada go ahead shiyasa mukayi tattaki mukazo gareka", Dada yayi murmushi dan beda burin da ya wuce yaga ya aurar da Jawahir hannun na gari, nan yace "alhamdulillah, alhamdulillah alhamdulillah, gaskiya naji dadin wannan maganar dan duk wani uba dake da yarinyar da takai munzalin aure a gabanshi zaka tarar beda kwanciyar hankali harse ya aurar da ita", Alhaji Abbas yace "wannan haka yake", Dada yacigaba da cewa "toh waye yaron da yaga Jawahir yakeso, dan yana da kyau muyi bincike kafin mu bashi 'yarmu?", Abba yayi murmushi yace "ai na gida za'ayi, tuwo na mai na ne", Dada yace "waye kenan toh", Abba yace "danka ne Najib, dan wurin yayar Hindu Aysha", nan take annurin fuskar Dada ya dauke dan baze manta warning din da Najib yazo ya mishi a hospital ba lokacin da Jawahir ta fado daga kan dutse aka kwantar da ita yayi blaming din Mamah, kallon su Abba yayi yace "I'm sorry bazan bawa Najib Jawahir ba dan baya ganin girman na gaba dashi", kallonshi sukayi da mamaki Alhaji Abbas yace "laifi ya maka wani abun ne?", Dada ya kallesu ya basu labarin abinda yazo ya mishi a hospital, basuga laifin Najib ba, haka kuma su a wurinsu ba rashin kunya yayi ba dan idan babba ya kauce hanya yaro na iya dawo dashi ya dora shi hanya madaidaiciya, nema suka su fahimtar da Dada amma yaki kulasu yace shi besan zancen ba, Abba ne ya nisa yace "shikenan tinda ka nuna bakaso zamu sanar dashi amma dai ina ga ka sake tunani akan hakan, farin cikin Jawahir zaka duba", Dada yace "ai ba maganan tunani a nan, yaron be kwanta mun bane dan haka bazan bashi ita ba", Abba yace "shikenan", nan ya mike dan beji dadin hukuncin da Dada ya yanke ba shima Alhaji Abbas ya mike sukawa Dada sallama suka wuce ba tareda sun jira rakiyar sa ba
Abba be koma gida ba masallaci ya wuce, seda akayi magrib ya zauna har akayi isha aka idar sannan ya koma gida, cike da dauki Jawahir ta bude mishi kofa dan tanada tabbacin zataji good news, sedai mood dinshi kawai ta kalla ta tabbatar labari yasha bamban, sannu da zuwa suka mishi ya amsa yana zama inda Mamah ta tashi ta kawo mishi ruwa ya karba yasha ya ajiye cup din sannan ta kalleshi tace "abinci koh wanka?", yace "abinci, na kwaso yunwa da gajiya, I am famished", tayi murmushi sannan taje ta haa mishi abincinshi kan dinning table ta dawo ta fada mishi ya tashi yaje ya zauna tayi serving dinshi yanaci yana tunanin yanda ze fada mata abinda Dada yace dan kallo daya yawa Jawahir ya dauke kai ganin yadda take kallonshi cike da zumudin jin labari me dadi, seda ya gama Mamah ta haa mishi ruwan wanka yayi wanka yasa jallabiya sannan ya zauna kan gado yana sauke ajiyar zuciya Mamah ta zauna gefenshi tana cewa "ya akayi", Abba ya kalleta ya girgiza kai sannan yace "wai baze ba Najib Jawahir ba saboda ya mishi rashin kunya", Mamah da ta cika da mamaki tace "rashin kunya kuma?", Abba ya kaa kai ya bata labarin yadda sukayi da Dada ranta ya aci tace "shidai baze taba canzawa ba, yana girma amma baya hankali", Abba yace "uhm uhm, kar na sake jin haka", ta turo baki tana cewa "al'amarin shi da ban haushi ne wallahi, yanzu ni me nasan zan cewa Jawahir, ga irin wahalar da suka sha kan soyayyar nan har seda ya shafi Sabreena yanzu kuma se ace akan wani dalilin shi da bekai ya kawo ba zece baze bada aurenta ba, wannan ai ba yi bane", Abba yace "toh ya zamuyi, shine mahaifinta shi keda ikon bada ita", Mamah tace "inada yadda zanyi, dan wannan karon dai bazan zuba mishi ido ba", shidai Abba beja maganar ba yace "Allah ya bada sa'a"
Da Mamah taje yiwa su Sabreena seda safe basu bari ta tafi ba suka tambaye ta yadda akayi, cike da tausayawa ta fada musu Jawahir tace "na shiga uku", Mamah ta kalleta tace "karki damu, aure kaman anyi an gama ne dan inda raina wannan karon bazanyi shiru ba", seda ta lallashi Jawahir sannan ta fice ta bar musu dakin Sabreena taci gaba da lallashin ta, koda Najib ya kira Jawahir kasa dauka tayi dan batasan me zatace mishi ba, washegari Mamah ta nemi izinin zuwa wurin Hajja Abba yace "base anyi arba'in ake fita ba?", tace "eh, amma uziri zaka mun, dole inje saboda asan abinyi kan lamarin yaran nan", Abba yace "shikenan shirya na kaiki" nan ta shirya tace su Sabreena ma su shirya duk suje tare, a gaban gidan Abba ya sauke su ba tareda ya shiga ba ya juya, sosai Hajja taji dadin ganinsu tace "en jikokina ne a gidan yau", Jawahir tayi murmushi wanda iyakar shi labba, Mamah ce ta tsugunna ta gaisheta sannan su Jawahir ma suka gaisheta ta amsa tana me farin cikin ganinsu, ta karbi Nabil da Nabila tana sa musu albarka sannan ta kalli Mamah tace "gaskiya naji dadin ganinku yau din nan", Mamah tayi murmushi tace "Hajja a mana afuwa bama zuwa ziyara", Hajja tace "ayyah ai kuna kokarin kam", me aikinta ta kira ta kawo musu ruwa da kayan abinci sukaci suka sha sukayi hira, seda duk suka shige sallah sannan Mamah ke labatarwa Hajja abinda Dada yace kan auren Najib da Jawahir, Hajja taja tsaki tace "zancen banza kenan, dan yayi ba daidai ba Najib ya gyara mishi shine rashin kunya, shi Osama har yau na kasa gane wani irin mutum ne shi me tsatsauran ra'ayi", Mamah ta numfasa tace "wallahi Hajja yaran nan suna son junansu, kisa baki ko ze yarda ayi abin nan lafiya", Hajja tace "kwantar da hankalinki, daga Jawahir har Najib din duk nawa ne, banga dalilin da zesa yace baza'ayi ba, zan kirashi in mishi magana, karki damu, sannan ki kwantar wa Jawahir da hankali itama", Mamah taji dadi tace "Nagode Hajja, Allah ya kara nisan kwana", Hajja ta amsa da "ameen", se yamma lis sannan Abba ya dawo daukansu inda ya shiga suka gaisa da Hajja ya mata alkhairi me tarin yawa sannan ya kwashi iyalinshi suka bar gidan a hanya Mamah tace su tsaya suyiwa Baba Salamatu tsaraba tinda an barta a gida ita kadai tun safe
Suna barin gidan Hajja ta dau waya ta kira Dada ya dauka tareda sallama ta amsa mishi sannan tace "Osama zan samu ganinka yau?", yace "Ummi bayan Isha zan leko, da fatan dai lafiya?", tace "lafiya lau, se kazo", yace "toh", sannan ya kashe wayar yana tunanin kiran me take mishi, yana ajiye wayar Farida na kira ya tsuke fuska tareda cewa "wai ita Farida bata gajiya da kira ne, se kace bani nace zan neme ta ba, ni kaina na gaji da zaman haka inason dawo da ita amma so nake tayi hankali kafin ta dawo", shi kadai yake wannan maganar wata zuciyar tace mishi "ai yanzu ta shiga hankalinta tinda kaga tana takura maka da kira", tsaki yayi ya tashi daga inda yake zaune a gaban gidanshi ya shige ciki dan kimtsawa ya tafi masallaci ba tareda ya amsa kiran da Faridar ke damunshi dashi ba
Seda yayi sallar magrib yayi isha sannan ya dau motarshi ya kama hanyar gidan Hajja, a compound yayi parking sannan ya shiga parlorn ta da sallama me aikinta ta amsa mishi ya shiga ya zauna, seda ta kawo mishi ruwa yace idan akwai abinci ta kawo mishi taje ta zubo mishi rafar shinkafa da miyan ganye wanda yaki kifi tazo ya ajiye mishi sannan ta shiga dan ta kira mishi Hajja, a daddafe Hajja ta fito dan tana fama da ciwon kafa duk da bawai ta wani tsufa sosai bane dan shekarunta bazasu wuce 65 bah, zama tayi tana cewa "yau kuma abincin gidana ake ci, kai kenan ka kasa zama da mace da ka aura ka sallama", ya hae girar sama data kasa yace "Ummi mata nawa na sallama, Hindu dai Allah ya riga ya rubuta babu zama ne shiyasa, ita kuma Farida laifin daga wurinta ne kuma a halin yanzu ma inaso na dawo da ita dan ta nuna tayi nadama se neman hakuri takeyi a wurina", Hajja ta zauna tace "da dai yafi, da ace baka maida kanka agogo sarkin aikin ba ai da zaka san halin da matarka ke ciki amma kai kenan, yau kana wannan garin gobe baka wancan garin, ba dole ta zubar da ciki ba tareda sanin ka ba", bece mata komai ba ta cigaba da cewa "dama akan zancen Najib na kira ka", ajiye abincin hannun shi yayi tace "akan wani dalili zakace bazaka bashi mata ba", yace "Ummi laifi yayi mun", ta hararashi tareda cewa "wani irin laifi", yayi shiru tace "inaso ka bashi go ahead ya turo magabatanshi dan ban so aja maganar nan", ya girgiza kai yace "yi hakuri Ummi amma bazan iya bawa Jawahir wanda ni banason tarayyar ta dashi ba, ita kadai ce gareni, shiyasa zan bada ita ga wanda ya dace ba wanda yake ganin shi a komai he's perfect ba", Hajja ta saki baki tana kallonshi kafin tace "ban isa ba kenan?", yace "ba haka bane Ummi, wallahi kin isa amma akan zancen Jawahir kar kisa baki kawai", tace "shikenan, tinda ka nuna min iyaka ta", zeyi magana ta daga mishi hannu tareda maida hankalinta kan tv alamar batamason jin abinda zece, beji dadi ba sedai baya ganin se iya bawa Najib Jawahir, ganin zaman shirun ya ishe shi ya mata sallama ya fito, yana fita ta dauki waya ta Mamah tareda shaida mata yadda sukayi dashi amma ta bata assurance din zata kara mishi magana
Dada na barin gidan ya wuce gidansu Farida inda ya kirata a waya yace mata yana waje ta fito, cike da jin dadi ta feshe jikinta da turare sannan ta dauki mayafi ta yafa ta leka dakin mahaifiyarta ta fada mata Osama na waje yana jiranta, duk da basusan dalilin zuwan nashi ba amma sunji dadi, a kofar gidan ta sameshi zaune cikin mota ta bude ta shiga tareda gaisheshi ya amsa sannan yace "sauri nakeyi, na biyo ne in fada miki ki shirya next week zanzo na maida ke gida", dadi kamar tayi yaya, godiya ta dinga mishi tana hawaye ya kalleta cike da tausayawa yace "toh kukan na menene?", ta goge hawayenta tace "I'm just happy, nagode kuma Inshallah you won't regret it, wallahi I've changed now", yayi murmushi sannan yace "I'm looking forward to having a happy home from now onwards", sannan ya bude dashboard dinshi ya ciro kudi masu yawa ya mika mata yace "you might need it for something", ta karba tana mishi godiya, sallama sukayi ta shiga gida tana murna inda ta shaidawa iyayen ta abinda sukace mahaifiyarta ta tayata murna mahaifinta kuma ya shiga mata fada yana kara mata nasiha kan zaman aure da hakkin miji akan matarsa da kuma hakkin mata akan mijinta
Najib ya shiga tashin hankali ganin Jawahir taki ta dauki wayarshi, wannan dalilin yasa ya kira Sabreena yaji ko lafiya tace mishi lafiya lau sannan ta fada mishi dalilin da yasa Jawahir ta kasa daukar wayarshi wanda ya daga mishi hankali sosai, shi yama manta cewar ya taba zuwa hospital yajawa Dada kunne akan Mamah, tirkashi!!! wannan shi ake cewa ga koshi ga kwanan yunwa, sallama yama Sabreena bayan yace tacewa Jawahir ta dau wayar ta, kiran Jawahir din yayi, duk da bataso dauka ba haka Sabreena ta tursasata ta dauka inda Sabreena ta bar dakin dan ta basu privacy, sallama ya mata ta amsa sannan yace "babyna kin sani cikin damuwa, ai da kin fada mun halin da ake ciki se in san abinyi", ta sakar mishi kuka tace "ince maka me? Dada yace baze baka aure na ba, I can't Ya Najib, I don't want to lose you", ya runtse ido yanajin sautin kukanta har cikin kanshi yace "stop crying Jawahir, you won't lose me I promise, we will pass this trying time together, zanzo weekend dinnan I will go to your father and ask for forgiveness, nasan idan na nemi yafiya ze sauko", ta share hawayenta tace "I hope so", a hankali yace "pray for me kinji, keep praying Inshallah everything will be solved, ki daina kuka, banason jin kukan ki yana daga mun hankali", tace "na daina, kuma zan mana addu'a", yayi murmushi yace "that's my baby, Allah ya bar mun ke muyi auren mu ta tafi kasashe honeymoon, ki haifa mun yara kyawawa kaman ki", tayi murmushi tana rufe fuska se kace yana gabanta, hira suka danyi sannan ya mata sallama badan ya gaji ba sedan yanaso yayi aiki
Tinda Najib yace zezo weekend Jawahir kesa idon ganinshi, ranar friday da dare ya diro Kebbi wanda tareda Salim sukazo dan shima yanaso yaga Sabreenar shi, basuje gidan ba se washegari inda bayan Najib yaga Jawahir sun gaisa da Mamah yace zeje yaga Dada inda Jawahir tace zata bishi yace a'a ta zauna yaje ya dawo, he needs to do this alone, badan taso ba ta zauna tareda mishi addu'an samun nasara, Salim ma yaso rakashi amma yace a'a su bari yaje ya dawo, haka ya shiga mota ya wuce gabanshi na dukan uku uku dan be sani ba koh ze samu nasara, a gaban gidan yayi parking sannan yayi knock gate din Malam Gado yazo ya bude mishi, sosai suka gaisa dan ya gane shi sannan yace "shigo bari na kira maka me gidan, kasan matar gidan ta dawo jiya dan haka yau koh lekowa waje beyi ba", Najib yayi murmushi at the same time yana tunanin dama Farida tayi tafiya ne, be dade ba sega Malam Gado ya dawo tareda cewa "wai yana zuwa", Najib yace "toh nagode", yana nan tsaye Dada ya fito sanye da Jallabiya yazo yace "kai ne?", Najib ya tsugunna har kasa ya gaisheshi Dada ya amsa yana kare mishi kallo, a tsugunnen da yake yace "dama nazo ne in nema gafara kan zuwan da nayi na sameka a asibiti da dadewa", Dada yace "tashi daga tsugunne", tashi Najib yayi sannan Dada yace "toh yanzu me kakeso nayi?", Najib kanshi kasa yace "gafara nazo nema, ka yafe mun, a lokacin zuciya ce ta debe ni na aikata abinda nayi dan Allah karka hukunta ni ta hanyar hanani auren Jawahir, ina sonta, wallahi idan ban aureta za'a samu matsala dan bansan ya rayuwata zata kasance ba", Dada ya kalleshi a zuciyarshi yace "toh idan ma na hanashi aurenta what will I gain from it, gashi yanzu Ummi ta daina mun magana ta daina kulani duk akan wannan zancen", ganin Dada ya shiru Najib ya sake cewa "kayi hakuri dan Allah, ka hukunta ni ta ko wani hanya amma karka hanani auren Jawahir", kallonshi Dada yayi inda ya hango tsantsar tashin hankali a idanunshi yace "shikenan ya wuce, idan kaje ka turo magabanta ayi maganar auren", dadi sosai Najib yaji ya sake tsugunnawa yana godiya Dada yace "you don't have to thank me", seda yayiwa Dada godiya sosai sannan ya mishi sallama ya wuce bayan yayi alawarin zuwan magabatanshi next weekend, yana fita Dada ya bishi da kallo tareda cewa "Allah yasa ka kular mun da Jawahir sosai", komawa cikin gida yayi yana tunanin Farida da yaje ya dauko a jiya wacce yaga duk ta canza mai dan yanzu ta nutsu ga wani respect da yake bashi wanda ada babu shi
Najib gidan Mamah ya koma inda ya shaida musu yadda sukayi da Dada, duk sun tayashi murna dan Jawahir kasa boye farin cikin ta ma tayi, Abba najin wannan zancen yace Salim ma ya turo dan tuni ya bari an mishi bincike kuma alhamdulillah bashi da wani matsala sema yabon shi da mutane keyi, Najib na zuwa gida ya fadawa Abbanshi inda shima ya tayashi murna yace sabon sati zasuje kuma idan sunje za'ayi komai ne har da sa rana dan bazasu tsaya bata lokaci ba, dadi Najib yaji dan ji yake kaman har an riga an daura auren, Salim kuwa da yammacin ranan ya hau jirgi ya wuce Katsina dan ya shaidawa iyayenshi ya samu mata kuma ance ya turo, alhamdulillah shima ta bangarenshi be samu matsala ba dan mahaifiyarshi ma dadi taji inda mahaifinshi yace yaba Abban Najib wuka da nama yayi komai tinda shi yana a garin Kebbi din dan tuni mahaifin Salim da mahaifin Najib sun zama abokan juna tun wani seminar da sukaje wanda aka gayyace su wurin aikin yaran nasu inda suka hadu yaran sukayi introducing dinsu ga junansu

UWA TA GARI - 52 - Wattpad
NOT EDITED
Kaman yadda suka tsara hakan ce ta kasance, sati na zagayowa duk a hadu aka kai kudin Jawahir at the same time aka karbi na Sabreena inda a nan mazajen suka yanke hukuncin sa rana gaba-daya base sun tsaya batawa kansu lokaci ba, in the next 7 months zasu gama semester dinsu na wannan shekaran dan haka aka sa biki wata takwas, Najib da Salim ji suke kaman su zuba ruwa a kasa su sha dan murna, ba kaman Najib da yake gani kaman yafi kowa dace a duniya, tinda aka sa rana suka fara shiri ta ko wani angare inda Abba mahaifin Najib ya basu gida nan kebbi din cikin gidajen da yake bayarwa haya, two flats be a gidan suna kallon juna koh wannan two bedroom ne da bathroom a ciki se kuma visitors toilet a waje wurin balcony, parlor da kitchen kuwa a wadace inda compound din gidan aka zuba interlock ciki kuma koh ina yaji tiles masu tsada da sheki, tinda Abba ya musu kyautar wannan gidan suka fara gyara inda ya dace a gyara, amma sukace bazasuyi paint ba se biki ya matso
Ta bangaren amare Jawahir da Sabreena kuwa tuni Mamah ta fara musu gyara duk da kakar Sabreena ta bangaren uwa tayi alkawarin aiko musu da mai gyara daga Libya amma still Mamah bata zauna haka ba tace gwara ta musu irin nasu na nan gida kafin ita waccan tazo, Jawahir da Sabreena dai ido suka samata ba tareda sunsan me ake ciki ba dan kuwa ce musu tayi maganin basir ne dana sanyi kuma ba karya a ciki dan maganin maganin sanyi dana basir take basu saboda ya fara wanke musu dattin ciki kafin ta fara basu na gyara
Dada seda ya shaidawa Abban Sabreena ya dauki nauyin Sabreena kawai tinda shima yana raye ze dauki nauyin 'yarshi wato Jawahir, tuni ya bada order din kayan furnitures wanda daga Dubai wanda Jawahir da kanta ya kira tazo ta zaba wanda takeso online lokaci suke hira a kawo mata, kayan kitchen kuma Mamah tace ita zata musu dan haka iyayensu maza su musu furnitures
Wannan kenan
Farida ce zaune gaban Dada yana cin abinci ya dago ya kalleta ta saki murmushi tareda cewa "dama inaso in tambayeka izini zanje wurin Jawahir dan neman yafiya saboda abubuwan da na aikata mata sun tsaya mun rai, badan Allah ya bata UWA TA GARI ba na tabbata da a halin yanzu labari yasha bamban dan da ta salwantar da rayuwarta ga shaye shaye da yawon banza", ta karashe tana goge kwallar daya zubo mata sannan tacigaba da cewa "my dear wallahi harga Allah nayi nadaman abubuwan da na aikata saboda sunkai da son zuciya", duk da Dada yaji ba dadi amma ya iya, shi haka nashi kaddarar yake kuma Allah yasa ma yanzu tayi nadama kuma tana kokarin gyara kurakuranta dan haka baze hanata ba, hannunta ya riko cike da tausayawa yana murza su yace "karki damu, idan na dawo aiki da daddare zan kaiki da kaina kije ki nemi yafiyarsu, na tabbata zasu yafe miki tun da dama haka ake mutumin da yayi kuskure kuma ya gane kuskurenshi seya nemi yafiya ya gyara, ki kwantar da hankali komai se wuce", ya sakar mai murmushi duk da hawayen da ya bata mata fuska tace "Allah yasa Jawahir ta kulani, dan bata sona", yace "always think positive, na tabbata zata yafe miki", nan tace mishi "Allah yasa", ya amsa da "ameen", sannan ya mike bayan ya gama cin abinci ta rakashi har bakin mota sannan sukayi sallama ya wuce wurin aiki ita kuma ta koma cikin gida
Jawahir, Sabreena da Mamah ne zaune suna kallon styles na bridal gowns a Instagram mai gadinsu yayi sallama suka amsa mishi ya shiga ya tsugunna yana gaishe da Mamah ta amsa da fara'ar ta yace "ga wani nan a waje wai a mishi sallama da Alhaji shida matarshi sukazo wai ace Osama ne", ko kadan Mamah bataji ko dar a zuciyar ta ba duk da ta gane me sallaman, kallon Sabreena tayi tace "je kice wa Abbanki ana sallama dashi a kofar gida", mikewa Sabreena tayi ta wuce parlorn Abbanta inda Jawahir ta kalli Mamah tace "ba Dada bane yazo ba?", Mamah tace "shine, koh zakije ku gaisa ne?", Jawahir ta gyara zama tace "eh, amma bari ya gama da Abba tukunnan", suna zaune Sabreena ta fito tace "Mamah yace a shigo dasu gashi nan zuwa", tashi Mamah tayi ta mikawa Sabreena Nabil wanda ya riga yayi bacci tace "jeki kwantar dashi, kiyi hankali karki tashi Nabila", tace "toh", sannan ta wuce ciki, Mamah da Jawahir kuwa seda suka dan gyagyara wurin sannan Mamah ta shige daki ta sako hijabi ta fito tace "Jawahir jeki shigo dasu", fita Jawahir tayi ta karasa inda sukayi parking ta wuce ta side din Dada tace "Dada bismilla wai ku shigo", yayi murmushi ya fito tareda cewa "my princess ba gaisuwa", ta rufe fuskar ta da tafukan hannayenta tace "mantawa nayi, ina wuni Dada", yace "lafiya lau princess, ya kike ya gida", ta amsa da "lafiyar lau", yana jira yaji ta gaishe da Farida amma yaji shiru dan ko kallon inda take batayi ba tace "bismilla mu shiga ciki", bayanta suka bi ta musu jagora har cikin parlour inda ta nuna musu wuri suka zauna sannan ta shige kitchen inda taga Sabreena na kokarin hada musu kayan motsa baki akan tray ta taimaka mata suka fito dashi Sabreena ta gaishe su sannan duk suka koma ciki kasancewar Abba ya fito
Da sallama ya shigo parlorn ya mikawa Dada hannu sukayi musabaha sannan ya nemi wuri ya zauna Farida ta gaishe shi ya amsa fuska a sake, Dada ne ya mishi bayanin zuwansu Abba yace "ah toh da kyau, bari na muku kiranta", Dada yayi saurin cewa "idan Hindu ma na kusa tazo dan Allah", Abba yace bari ya kirasu sannan ya shige ciki, ba dadewa Jawahir da Mamah suka fito Abba da Sabreena basu biyo su ba dan su basu privacy, Farida na ganin Jawahir ta mike ta karasa inda Jawahir ke zaune zata tsugunna Mamah tace "a'a ai baza'ayi haka ba, ke uwa ce a gareta dan haka be dace ki tsugunna gabanta ba", Farida ta sunkuyar da kai kasa ta rasa ta ina ma zata fara, ganin haka yasa Dada sa baki yace "princess Farida tazo neman yafiya wurinki ne akan abubuwan da ta aikata miki na ba daidai ba", Jawahir ta kalli Dadanta tace "Dada bata mun komai ba, kuma idan ma tayi ni harga Allah na yafe mata", sosai Farida taji dadin abinda Jawahir tace ta goge kwallarta tace "Nagode Jawahir, Nagode Allah yayi miki albarka", ta amsa da "ameen", sannan ya Dada ya juya ya kalli Mamah yace "nima nasan ni mai laifi ne, nima ina neman gafara dan nasan na kuntata miki a rayuwa, bakiji dadin zama dani ba ko kadan kuma ban baki goyon baya wurin ganin mun bawa yarinyar mu tarbiyya me kyau ba", Mamah ta girgiza kai tace "ai ni na dade da yafe ma, ban rike ka a rai ba, duk abinda ya faru a baya kaddarar mu ce kuma na karbeta da hannu bibbiyu", yayi murmushin takaici dan yasan yayi rashin mata me hakuri da nutsuwa yace "Nagode, Allah ya bar zumunci", ta amsa da "ameen", yace su zasu wuce dan dama abinda ya kawo kenan tace bari ta kira mishi Abban Sabreena suyi sallama, Abba da Sabreena suka fito sukayi musu sallama har bakin mota suka rakasu sannan suka koma cikin gida Mamah a ranta tace "rayuwa kenan, idan ka rungumi kaddarar ka me kyau da mara kyau se kaga Allah ya sauya maka da mafificin sa", duk da ada taso Osama amma kam Abban Sabreena yafiye mata shi so dubu dan kuwa yafishi nutsuwa, hakuri, tattali da sanin ya kamata
FEW MONTHS LATER
Jawahir ce zaune a parlor tana chatting, yau ita kadai ce a gidan dan Mamah da Sabreena sun tafi wurin aikin Mamah dan tuni ta koma bakin aikinta, Baba Salamatu ma ta koma gida yanzu daga su se su, koda Mamah tace su mata rakiya Jawahir cewa batajin dadi dan bason fitar takeyi ba saboda yadda skin dinta ke shan gyara yake glowing yanzu batason shiga rana tafison zaman gida zaman hutu, wayar hannunta ne ya fara ringing ta dauka ganin Jarood ne ke kira, sallama ta mishi ya amsa mata yana cewa "Jawahir thanks to you my Dad is back on his feet, nagode ya taimakon da kika mun kuma ban manta alkawarin mu ba idan na samu kudin zan maido miki dashi", tayi murmushi tace "since your dad is back on his feet toh alhamdulillah, that's all that matters now, maganan kudi ka ajiye shi gefe I gave it to you, ba bashi bane", yace mata "naji", badan ya gamsu ba amma saboda bayason yaja zancen sedai ya kudiri maida mata da kudinta duk ranar da ya samu, hira suka danyi kadan tace "idan na samu lokaci da yamma zanzo na duba Dad dinka", yayi murmushi yace "ai Dad dina baya gari, yana Abuja tinda yanzu an samu kafa ai ba zama, yace he wants to get everything back real quick", tace "toh Allah yasa a dace, nasan baza'a rasa na Allahn da zasu mara mishi baya yaci gaba da siyasar sa", yace "ameen", ganin call din Najib na shigowa ta mishi sallama ya kashe sannan ta dauki Najib, seda suka gaisa ya zolayeta kadan sannan yace "baby na jallabiya me size dinki?", tayi murmushi dan Najib ya dage se hada lefe yakeyi tace "length dina 56 ne", yace "ashe matar tawa doguwa ce", tayi murmushi yace "size dinki na takalmi fah", tace "38", yace "okay, Ina cikin mall Ina miki siyayya, kuma nasan you will like everything", tace "is that so?", yace "Yes princess, sannan idan nazo Kebbi zamuje ki siya sauran abunda babu", tace "Allah ya kawo ka lafiya", ya amsa da "ameen", sannan ya mata sallama ya kashe wayarta ya barta zauna tana tunanin rayuwar auren da zatayi da Najib dan yadda Najib ke zumudi abin har tsoro yake bata
