UWA TA GARI - 53 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Wasa wasa fah biki ya matso dan yanzu saura two months da en kwanaki, su Jawahir kansu ya dau zafi dan sun kusa fara exam a school, wannan dalilin ne yasa basu da lokacin kansu dan in sun tafi tun safe se yamma suke dawowa saboda za suyi lectures, suyi tutorials, su shiga library duk dan kada su fadi exam, kosu Najib ma sun shafa musu lafiya wannan karon kam dan sun ga cewar en matan nasu batasu suke ba, sedai wannan dalilin be hana Mamah cigaba da gyaran da take musu ba dan tuni wacce aka ce musu za tazo daga Libya tazo kuma ta fara aikinta, Mamah kiran Baba Salamatu tayi ta nemi alfarma kan ta dawo saboda yanzu aikin gidan ya mata yawa dansu Jawahir basa zama ga renon Nabil da Nabila, ga aikin gida ga zuwa ma'aikatar ta dan kuwa aikinta se bunkasa yakeyi har ya kai ya kawo tana distribute wa mutane kuma still tana siyar da daddaya idan ana so sannan idan profit ya fito tana cirewa su Jawahir nashi tasa kowa nashi a account
Ta fannin shirye shiryen biki ba abinda ya tsaya dan angwanan ma kusan sun gama hada lefen su inda Mamah ma tuni ta gama musu siyayyar kayan kitchen, ko waccensu abinda take aka siya mata inda Farida ta bada nata gudunmawar na daukar nauyin event din Mother's Eve dan tuni sun dinke da Mamah kaman ba abinda ya taa faruwa, ita dasu Zulaika da Nafisa ma alhamdulillah da taimakon Salma duk suka hadu sukayi settling differences dinsu inda suka yafewa junansu suka maida komai ba komai ba sukaci gaba da rayuwarsu dan Zulaika har an aurar da ita ga cousin dinta inda Nafisa kuma ansa rana, Salma kuma ta samu wani dan minister of education suna shan soyayyar su kuma har a gida an san dashi
Satin exam dinsu Jawahir ya matso, wannan yasa suke zaman gida dan a rana befi suyi paper daya ba kuma suna gamawa suke dawowa, three weeks suka dauka suna zana jarabawa wanda a ranar da sukayi last paper dinsu suka dinga raba wedding IV dinsu ga course mates dinsu da abokan arziki harma da wa'anda suke mutunci dasu, a Islamiyya ma haka suka rarraba IV Khadija nata jin dadi zatayi awance dan koda ta fadawa mijinta be hanata ba saboda a ganinshi abubuwan da bata samu yinsu a kuriciyarta ba baze hanata yinsu a yanzu ba, kasancewar Jawahir ba wasu kawaye ne da ita ba haka Sabreena ma yasa Rumana da Zahra basu shawaran suyi friends in general, duk wanda keda sha'awan yin awance toh she's free to buy the anko sedai fah aljihun su ne zeyi kuka, ai kuwa koda suka fadawa coursmates dinsu sun samu masu siya sosai harda ma wa'anda batayi tunanin zasuyi ba, ko a Islamiyyan su ma mutane biyar sun musu anko wanda yasa sukaji dadi sosai dan alamu sun nuna koda ace batada sakewa mutane na sonta
Biki fah saura two weeks, Baba Salamatu ta bari autar ta tazo wacce a alla zatayi 15yrs tace idan an gama biki ita yarinyar zata zauna dasu ita kuma Baba Salamatu zata koma kauyen su, kallon yarinyar Mamah tayi kyakyawa da ita daidai gwargwado Mamah tace "ya sunan ki", tace "Halima" Mamah tace "suna me kyau da fatan dai ba'a takura ki ba idan akace ki zauna nan kina tayani aiki?", ta girgiza kai tace "ko kadan", Mamah tace "toh alhamdulillah, seki kai kayanki dakin Baba Salamatu, zata fada miki komai aikin ba wasu masu yawa bane", tace "toh, nagode", sannan ta mike ta wuce dakin da akace mata
Sosai Halima ke tayasu da duk wasu ayyuka da aka sata dan ko kadan batasa son jiki ba shiyasa Mamah kejin dadin aiki da ita
Gida ya fara cika dan dagin Jawahir ta bangaren mahaifiyarta sun fara zuwa daga kogi da kuma Maiduguri dan mahaifin Hindu dan kogi ne mahaifiyarta kuma yar Maiduguri wanda yawancin a wurin Mamah suka sauka wasu kuma wurin Yaya Aysha inda itama Sabreena dangin mahaifiyarta sunzo daga Libya dangin mahaifinta kuma daga kano, haka ta bangaren Osama dangin mahaifiyarshi sunzo daga Kaduna dan dashi dasu Hindu duk en gari daya ne wato kogi, shiyasa koda sukazo basu sauka wurinshi dan sunji takaicin sakin Hindu da yayi amma en Kaduna da sukazo a gidanshi matasan suka sauka inda iyaye iyayen suka sauka wurin Hajja, Jawahir har kwalla tayi dan farin ciki dan bata taa tunanin zatayi kai haka ba saboda yanda akazo bikinta, tasan ita bame shiga mutane bace sannan batada zumunci dan yawancinsu ma koh number wayarsu bata dashi shiyasa kwata kwata batasa a ranta za'azo bikinta ba se gashi sun bata mamaki dan kuwa ko wani gida kaje a cike yake da dangi da abokan arziki har gidan Yaya Aysha kuwa itama en uwan Najib ta bangaren mahaifinsa duk sunzo, en samarin ma wasun su hotel suka sauka
A satin bikin aka kawo lefen Jawahir amma banda na Sabreena dan mahaifiyar Salim tace a bari yayyenshi suzo suga abinda yasa a lefen ko yayi ko kuma da abinda za'a kara, lefen Jawahir akwati shadaya da kit making it twelve sheke da kaya na gani na fada dan kuwa bana zubarwa, gua kawai ke tashi gidan Mamah dan kowa yaga lefen nan seya yaba koda kuwa makiyinta ne, shadda, lace, atampha, jallabiya, materials, kananan kaya, undies, kayan makeup, bags, jewelries, veils da hijab duk babu na banza dan kuwa babu na yarwa, wata Aunty din Jawahir ce tayi gua wanda seda gidan ya dauka tace "amma fah 'yar tamu tayi kai, irin wannan kaya ai se tayi shekaru tana sawa basu kare ba, gaskiya Najib yayi mugun kokari wurin hada kayan nan", wacce ke gefenta tana rike da jaka a hannunta tace "kuma wai harda kudin inki Naira dubu dari", wata kuma tace "kayan kam sunyi kyau, Allah yasa musu albarka yasa rai ya mora", duk suka amsa da "ameen", suna maida kayan cikin akwati
Duk wannan bidirin da akeyi basu Jawahir a gidan dan sun tattara ne sun koma gidansu Rumana suna meeting kan events din da zasuyi, Jawahir ta kallesu tace "nifa nace muku bama son wani hayaniya, kawai Thursday zamuyi party iya mu dinnan, friday ayi mother's Eve, Saturday biki Sunday daurin aure bayan daurin aure ayi walima wanda malam yace za'a mana nida Sabreena se kuma wa'azi tunda dinner se dare", Khadija tace "gaskiya kam hakan yayi, yawan events dinnan bashi bane amma bari muji ta bakin Sabreena ko hakan ya mata", Sabreena tayi murmushi tace "hakan yayi, ai tare muka yanke wannan shawarar, kuma mun riga mun fada muku kowa yasa kayan da Allah ya hore mishi, dama anko na ranar Mother's Eve ne se biki da kuma dinner, anko uku ba yawa, kuma alhamdulillah kowa ya riga ya siya a nan, har ma da wa'anda basa nan din", Rumana tace "wasu ma na kan siya, dan anjima ma dole in koma kasuwa nida Zahra, sedai na fada musu duk wanda keson anko ya kawo kudinshi kafin la'asar dan daga yau bazan koma ba, biki saura sati nima ina bukatar hutu", duk sukace "hakan yayi", nan suka tsaida zance sannan suka watse
Koda su Jawahir suka koma gida an ragu dan anje musu jere, wannan ne ya basu daman kallon lefen da aka kawo dan wata cousin dinsu me suna Walida ce ta jasu dakin da aka ajiye lefen Jawahir tayi farin cikin abubuwan da ke ciki inda Sabreena keta santin su suna mata dariya Jawahir tace "na tabbata abinda ke nan shine cikin naki tunda kusan tare suke siyan kayan", Sabreena tace "Allah yasa", mikewa Jawahir tayi ta bar dakin ta shige dakinsu ganin ba kowa ciki tasa key saboda batason takura sannan ta dauki wayarta ta kira Najib, ringing biyu ya dauka duk da yayi busy amma wannan be hanashi daukar wayanta ba yace "baby na ya akayi?", a hankali tace "naga kaya, sunyi kyau sosai na gode", yayi murmushi yace "I told you that you will like it, nasan abinda kikeso and you don't have to thank me, you deserve it", tace "me zanyi danna faranta ma kaman yadda kake faranta mun rai", yayi ajiyar zuciya yace "baby na you don't have to do anything, just take care of yourself for me and be happy because seeing you happy makes me happy as well", tayi murmushi me kayatarwa tace "I will do that", yace "promise?", tace "I promise", hira suka danyi sannan suka ma junansu sallama ta kashe wayar tareda kwanciya kan gado ta lumshe idanu tana murmushi ita kadai
Se yamma lis masu jere suka dawo duk a gajiya suna fadin irin kyawun da gidajen sukayi dan tsakanin na Jawahir da na Sabreena baka isa kace ga wanda yafi kyau ba saboda ko wanne an kashe kudi kuma Dada da Abba ma sun kokari wurin kayan furnitures dan ko Sabreena ma a kasar waje aka siyo mata nata kuma itama ita ta zabi wanda takeso, ko wanne idan mutum ya kalla sedai yace "Masha Allah", dan kuwa naira tayi kuka
Nan suke fadawa Mamah yayyen Salim da cousins dinshi sunzo sun sauka gidan Yaya Aysha harda kakarshi kuma sunce washegari zasu kawo lefen Sabreena, da kayan sa lalle tace Allah ya kai su goben, tuni Abba yayi kaura ya bar musu gidan saboda yadda mata suka cike gidan
Washegari kuwa se gashi an kawo lefen Sabreena itama dai irin na Jawahir dinne kumai daya sedai color ne ya bambanta su dan akwatin Jawahir silver ne na Sabreena kuma gold, nan daya daga cikin yayyenshi tace "idan ba damuwa mahaifiyar Salim tace idan anyi dinner ranar Sunday ran Monday akawo Sabreena Katsina akwai bikin da akeso ayi saboda mutanen mu na chan kuma wannan dama ne da zatasan en uwan mijinta muma mu santa", aka kira Mamah ta fito aka fada mata dan a halin yanzu itace uwar Sabreena Mamah tace "ai ba komai hakan ma daidai ne, abinda ya kamata ayi kenan tuntuni amma koh yanzu ma bata aci ba seku tafi da ita, da fatan dai Salim din ya sani?, sukace "ya sani", Mamah tace "ai shikenan", sosai suka yaba da karamci irin na Mamah ga son mutune da haba haba dasu wata cousin dinsa tace "Ina amaryar tamu mu ganta, ko rowar ta ake mana", duk sukayi dariya sannan aka kira musu Sabreena ta fito kanta kasa ta gaishe su suka amsa suna jin dadi dan sun yaba da nutsuwar ta gata kyakyawa cousin din da tace a fito musu da Sabreena tace "ashe dai Salim ya iya zabe, irin wannan zankaediyar budurwa haka, ga kyau Masha Allah", Sabreena tayi murmushi tana sunkuyar da kai wata cikinsu tace "gaskiya kam Salim yayi zabe me kyau, Allah ya basu zaman lafiya ya kawo zuri'a na gari", duk aka amsa da "ameen", basu bata lokaci sosai ba suka koma gidan Yaya Aysha, nan aka nunawa Sabreena lefenta tanata sunne kai kasa Jawahir tace "ki dago kai ki kalla mana", Sabreena ta girgiza kai wai ita kunya, ranar haka suka wuni ana hira gidan amare da lefen da aka kawo wa amaren, inda su Jawahir da cousins dinsu ke daki suna nasu hiran na rayuwar aure

UWA TA GARI - 54 - Page 2 - Wattpad
Yau Thursday kuma yau ne su Jawahir zasuyi party dinsu na en mata kawai a gidan su Rumana dan sauran gidajen duk da hayaniya, sunyi decorating wurin da blue and white wanda ya kayata wurin yayi kyau sosai, Sabreena tayi kwalliya cikin blue gown wanda aka kawata shi da white stones, sosai yayi kyau ya amshi jikinta, kwalliyan fuskarta ba wani me yawa bane nude make up tayi dan batason hayaniya a fuskar, Jawahir kuma white gown tasa me adon blue stones itama kwalliyan ta nude ne duk da bame makeup daya ta musu ba, sunyi kyau sosai se daukansu hoto akeyi ana post a watsapp status da Snapchat wanda tuni su Najib sun fara ganin yadda amaren nasu sukayi kyau, kawayen amarya sunsa white top me sunan amare da angwanan su a gaba se baya kuma aka musu customize din sunan su suka hada da blue jeans wasu kuma skirt dan koh Khadijah skirt tasa, sunyi rawa sosai Jawahir da Sabreena baka ce sun iya rawa haka ba saboda kowaccensu da kalar nata miskilancin sedai yau sun ajiye wannan gefe sunyi rawa har sun gaji, kayan snacks da juices kuwa sedai ka gaji daci ka barshi ba dai kace baka samu ba dan komai sunyi shine a wadace
Se bayan Isha suka koma gida duk a gajiye, hiran party suka dingayi har sukayi bacci bayan sun gama waya dasu Najib danshi cewa ma yayi kar ta cire kayan ta bari yazo ya gani tace bazata iya zama da kayan nauyi ba cirewa zatayi, washegari da safe Hajja ta sasu lalle sannan wacce zata zana musu henna ta musu da red henna, sosai sukayi kyau kaman ka sace su ka gudu, se kyalli da sheki sukeyi jikinsu na glowing, Jawahir ganin fah da gaske aure zatayi se jikinta ya fara sanyi, yanzu shikenan tafiya zatayi ta bar Mamah ba tareda sunyi spending wani quality time ba, kuruciyarta da ya kamata ace tana tareda mahaifiyarta su saba su shaku amma ina tana chan tana shashancin a tunaninta rayuwar da Dada ya dora ta akai shine rayuwa me orawa, yanzu da Allah yasa ta gane ya dawo kan hanya ta dawo wurin Mamah kuma koh shekara uku kwakwara basuyi ba se aure, tana wannan tunanin ta fashe musu da kuka, gaba-daya en matan dake dakin kallonta suke suna tambayan lafiya amma Jawahir ba bakin magana, sunyi lallashin har sun gaji taki tayi shiru, Sabreena ganin kukan da gaske take yinshi itama se ta shiga tayata duk da batasan dalilin kukan Jawahir din ba, ganin abin nasu basajin lallashi yasa Zahra fita ta kirawo Mamah wacce take hada musu kayan da zasu sa cikin akwati dan yanzu za'a wuce dasu gidan Dada dan daga chan zasu wuce inda za'ayi Mother's Eve wanda Farida ta dau nauyin shi, kallon Zahra Mamah tayi tace "Zahra ya dai?", "su Jawahir ne suka hada kai suke ta kuka wanda bamu san dalilin kukan nasu ba", cewar Zahra, kallonta Mamah tayi tana kokarin mikewa tace "lafiyar su suke kuka?", Zahra tayi gaba Mamah ta bita a baya bayan ta rufo dakin ta da mukulli saboda tsaro sannan tayi dakin su Jawahir, ganin da gaske kukan sukeyi ta zauna gefen su tace "en matan Mamah ya da kuka kuma, wani abun ya faru ne?", Jawahir ta kwanta jikin Mamah tana cewa "Mamah ki yafe mun akan abubuwan da na miki a baya, nayi nadama kuma na gane kure na, ki yafe mun kinji Mamah", Mamah ta maida kwallar ta tace "Jawahir me yasa kike dawo da hannun agogo baya, i thought mun gama maganar nan, ke kanki kinsan komai ya riga da ya wuce, toh yanzu mena dawo da wannan zancen", Jawahir ta girgiza kai amma batace komai ba ta kara lafewa jikin Mamah, Mamah maida kallonta tayi ga Sabreena wacce ke hawaye tace "kema kukan me kike yi?", Sabreena ta girgiza kai dan ita kanta batasan kukan me takeyi ba, sedai a yanzu ganin Jawahir jikin Mamah yasa ta tuna da nata mahaifiyar se gaba-daya jikinta yayi sanyi, girgiza wa Mamah kai tayi Mamah tayi murmushi ta janyo ta jikinta tana goge mata hawaye tace "ku daina kuka, ku gaku amare kuma kuna kuka ai se kwalliyar da za'ayi yaki yin kyau, ku tashi kuje ku wanke fuskokin ku auntyn ku ta kira wai wacce zata muku make up ta zo, na kira Najib sunce zasu aiko da mota wanda ze kwashi ku da kawayen ku, yanzu ba lokacin kuka bane kunji", suka mike suna share hawayen su ta tashi ta fice tana cewa "kuyi sauri kar suzo suna jira"
Shiryawa sukayi Mamah ta mika musu akwatin kayansu dasu da kawayen su suka fito aka kaisu gidan Dada, Farida taji dadin ganinsu inda Jawahir taje tsohon dakin ta Sabreena kuma guest room dan ko wannensu da me makeup dinta, sun dau wurin two hours suna shiryawa kafin su gama, inda amare suka sa buba da zani da head tie wanda aka dinka da aso oke peach color, kaya iri daya suka sa inda suka sa talkami da purse da jewelries silver color inda kawaye kuma sukayi anko na swiss atampha, kyau de kam sunyi kyau, mota aka ajiye musu ana kwasan su ana kaisu Madonna Guest Inn Hall inda za'ayi event din, koda suka je su Mamah na wurin, nan angwanai sukayi kamu da yake abin duk na gida ne, event din sosai ya kayatarwa, angwanai sunzo sunyi liki akayi hotuna suma anko sukayi shida Salim, sunyi kyau kam ba laifi, tun wurin 4pm suka fara har kusan Isha sannan aka tashi daga nan aka maida su gidan Mamah, washegari zasuyi biki inda za'ayi a Kakale Crown Hall, tun wurin 2 na rana suka fara biki inda amare sukayi kyau cikin pink swiss lace wanda aka mishi ado da Black and gold stones, head dinsu ma pink ne se takalmi, purse da jewelries gold, kawaye kuma suka sa cord lace sea blue da head silver, abokan ango ma anko sukayi na sea blue getzna, wurin ya kawatu da decoration me kyau ga caterers se yawo sukayi table table suna tambayan abinda zakaci, duk abinda ke ranka shi za'a kawo maka, biki ne akayi shi na ece raini, naira tayi kuka dan kuwa zubasu ake ana liki kaman ba'asan zafin su, amare da angwanan su sunsha rawa sun kuma sha yabo wurin mutane tareda sanya albarka, gaba-daya fans din hayaniya ba, Salim da Najib dadi sukeji gobe daurin aurensu har ji suke kaman su janyo gobe ya dawo yau sedai dole suci gaba da hakurin da sukeyi tinda da yau da gobe duk daya ne
Su Jawahir sun koma gida agajiye suka rage kayan jikinsu sukayi wanka suka dawo suka kwanta ko wacce da sake saken da takeyi a zuciyar ta akan gobe, yanzu fah daga gobe shikenan sun zama matan aure, zasu tashi daga karkashin Mamah, Dada da Abba su koma karkashin mazajen su, rayuwa kenan! tin kafin kazo duniya komai na rayuwarka na rubuce cikin allon kaddarar ka wanda baka isa ka kauce masa ba, lokacin zuwan ka duniya, lokacin auren ka, lokacin mutuwar ka komai na arubuce wanda komin guje mishi da zakayi seya dawo ya same ka
Washegari tun wuraren karfe tara na safe su Jawahir sukayi wanka suka shirya cikin atampha super na Jawahir red na Sabreena green sedai design din atamphar duk daya ne, a masallacin unguwar su za'a daura auren, shiyasa duk abinda akeyi suna ji, wuraren goma da rabi aka daura auren Jawahir da Najib akan sadaki dubu dari biyu sannan aka daura na Sabreena da Salim itama akan sadaki dubu ari biyu, Najib da Salim daka kalli fuskokin su kasan suna cikin farin ciki, ko wannensu murna kawai yakeyi yana washe baki, mabarata da marokata sun zagaye su se kirari ake musu inda su kuma suke fitar da kudi suna kyautar shi kaman suna kyautar pure water (nace ba laifinsu bane, suna daukan 5million albashi ne shiyasa), seda suka gama da en daurin aure suka gaggaisa da abokan mahaifansu dan mahaifin Salim da abokanshi ma sunzo, Jarood ma yazo da abokan shi biyu saboda Jawahir kuma har gaisawa sukayi da Najib inda ya tayashi murna Najib yayi godiya sannan duk suka dau hanyar gidan amare da kafa tinda ba nisa harda Jarood da abokanshi dan Najib cewa yayi suje gaba-daya saboda tarihi
A gida kuwa su Sabreena najin an daura idanunsu ya soma rena fata inda aka fara musu gua ana sama auren albarka, wata babbar mace ce ta bada umarnin a bari suyi sallah raka'a biyu suyiwa Allah godiya tareda rokawa kansu zaman lafiya a gidan mazajen su, hakan kuwa akayi suka tashi sukayi nafila kaman yadda tace sannan aka musu wanka da turare se kamshi suke zubawa suka fita compound inda angwanai keta hotuna da iyaye mata, ko wannensu jan matarshi yayi gefe ana musu hoto seda aka bari suka gama sannan Hajja tayi kiransu ta hadasu duka tayi musu nasiha me ratsa jiki wanda yasa su Jawahir zubar da kwalla, bayan ta gama sun tashi zasu wuce Najib yaje daidai saitin kunnen Jawahir yace "banso kiyi kuka babyna, ki adana mun hawayenki se kinzo gidana I promise you will have the most memorable night ever", babban mayafin ta taja ta rufe fuskarta saboda kunya Hajja tace "me kace mata da take kunya haka?", yayi murmushi yace "Hajja tsakanin mata da miji ne, base kinji ba", tayi kwafa tace "idan kayi wasa semu hanaka matar ma yau dinnan", ya waro ido waje yace "indai baso kike inyi kwanan asibiti ba wallahi ku kawo mun matata", en wurin suka kwashe da dariya Mamah da tun dama ba kunya tsakanin ta da Najib dan koh na sirika ma bataji ba tace "fita ka bamu wuri, ai ko kunyar ido na kaji amma ka tsaya kana mana tabara", yayi dariya yace "haba Aunty na, ai tsakanina dake babu wannan", haka suka lallaa suka tasa keyarshi waje, Salim kam duk kunyar mutanen wurin yakeyi shiyasa ya kame wuri aya yanama sahibarsa murmushi
Wurin sha biyu wata malam tazo tayi wa'azi kan zamantakewar aure, kowa ya nutsu yana jin jawabin ta, masu tuba na tuba masu dana sani nayi masu hawaye nayi irinsu Sabreena da Jawahir, sosai ta kashe musu jiki da wa'azin ta kafin tayi sallama ta tashi ganin azahar tayi, suma sauran nan sukayi sallah sannan suka canza kaya zuwa shadda wanda yasha bead work suka dora bakin alkyabba akai malaman Islamiyyan su guda uku sukazo suka musu walima harda basu allo, Jawahir da Sabreena sunyi kuka sosai ganin da gaske sun tashi daga en mata sun koma matan gida wato matan aure, se wuraren biyar na yamma aka fara shirin dinner inda su Jawahir sukasa white and royal blue material wanda aka mishi dinkin pencil gown da veil wanda ze sauka har kasa, kawayen su kuma sukasa lace lilac, se bayan isha aka fara dinner kuma ya kawatar sosai, anyi komai cikin kwanciyar hankali ba wani hayaniya, se wuraren 10 aka tashi dan basu dau lokaci ba saboda sunyi komai a tsare, daga nan aka wuce da amare gida inda cikin lokaci kankani aka shirya su aka kara musu nasiha sannan masu daukan amare sukazo suka dauke su dan ba lokaci, koda aka kai su ba'a wani zauna ba aka wuce dan koh kawaye kin zama sukayi, suna wucewa koh minti biyar ba'ayi ba sega angwanai inda suka fara raka Salim dan acewarsu shine karami sannan suka raka Najib, duk inda suka shiga se sunyi nasu nasihar sannan su bar wurin, bayan Najib ya rakosu ya rufe kofar gidan ya koma ciki yana sakin murmushi

UWA TA GARI - 55 - Page 3 - Wattpad
Da sallama Najib ya shiga dakin Jawahir bayan ya rufe ko ina ta amsa mishi cikin zazzakar muryarta tana zaune tsakiyar gado jikinta da fuskarta lullube cikin farin mayafi me adon stones ta tankwashe kafafuwanta se shessheka takeyi alamar tayi kuka sosai, murmushi yayi tareda karasawa kan gadon ya zaune gefenta ya cire hular kanshi ya ajiye kan bedside drawer sannan ya juyo kanta tareda janyota jikinshi ya rungume ta suka sauke ajiyar zuciya a tare ya budi baki cikin tsananin farin ciki yace "alhamdulillah!! dukkan godiya ya tabbata ga Allah Ubangijin talikai wanda cikin isansa da ikon sa ya nuna min wannan rana, ya cika mun burina, ya mallaka mun abar sona abar kaunata", murmushi kawai takeyi tana sauraronshi tareda kara shigewa jikinshi ta lafe yaci gaba da gaya mata kalamai masu kayatarwa da kwantar da hankalin mai saurare da kuma kara yiwa Allah godiya daya nuna musu wannan rana, ganin tana nema ta fara gyangyadi ya dagota ta bude ido yaja hancinta yace "ki tashi dan yau bacci be ganki ba", ta sunkuyar da kanta kasa tace "kai Ya Najib", yace "ai na tashi daga wannan sunan, na tashi daga Yaya na koma miji dan haka a canza mun suna amma for now tashi zakiyi kije ki rage kayan jikinki kiyi alwallah kizo muyi nafila na nuna godiyar mu ga Allah da kuma samun zaman lafiya", ta turo baki cike da shagwaba tace "Ya Najib bacci fah nakeji kuma na gaji dayawa", ya mike dan besan zancen ba ya bude trolley din da aka kawo ta dashi ya ciro mata rigar baccin da yasan bazataji kunyar sawa a gabanshi ba sannan ya riko hannunta ya tada ta ya raka ta har kofar bathroom sannan yace "15mins na baki, nima zanje nayi alwallah", karbar kayan da yake mika mata tayi ta shige bathroom din gaban ta na faduwa dan taga alamu Najib ba sarara mata zeyi ba, seda yaga ta shige sannan shima ya fice daga dakin ya wuce nashi dakin
Cikin 15mins se gashi ya dawo hannunshi dauke da leda da kuma plate da cup ya ajiye gefe sannan ya kalleta yaga harta shirya tasa hijab ya dauko sallaya ya shimfida musu sannan yace "bismilla", ba musu ta tashi ta tsaya bayanshi kadan ya tada sallah, raka'a hudu sukayi suna nunawa Allah godiyarsu ya daga hannu sama yana kwararo addu'a tana amsa masa da "ameen", seda ya gama suka shafa sannan ya juyo ya kama kanta yayi mata addu'a sannan ya fara mata tambayoyi kan addinin Islama tana bashi amsa daidai gwargwado sedai abubuwan da baza'a rasa ba da kuma wanda ya gyara mata sedai kuma alhamdulillah dan yayi alfahari da ita kuma yasan be auro jahila ba dan daidai gwargwado kam tana da abinda zata tarbiyyantar mishi da yara, tashi yayi ya janyo ledan da ya shigo dashi ya juye mata gasasshiyar kaza a plate ya tura mata gabanta sannan ya bude hollandia yogurt ya zuba mata a cup shima ya tura mata a gaba sannan yace "bismilla, ci ki koshi", ta dago ta kalleshi yace "ko na baki da kaina", tayi murmushi ta maida kanta kasa ya matso kusa da ita ya shiga bata a baki tana karba hartaga ta koshi tace "Ya Najib na koshi", ya kai hannu ya taba cikinta sannan ya janye plate din gefe ya mika mata cup ta karba tana sha tana kallonshi shima yana ci, seda suka gama ya mike ya tattare wurin da kanshi sannan ya dawo ya kashe fitilun dakin ya koma kan gado ya zauna gefen ta tareda riko hannunta, nan da nan zuciyar ta ya fara lugudi yana dukan uku yace "babyna let's sleep", cikin sanyi jiki ta kwanta ya kwanta gefenta tareda ja musu bargo ya rungumota jikinshi yana mata tafiyan tsutsa a jiki tace "Ya Naj
", yayi sauri rufe mata baki ta hanyar dora lips dinshi kan nata ya fara kissing dinta, ganin haka yasa ni Mhizzdaddy na fice tareda janyo musu kofa saboda a halin yanzu suna bukatar privacy
A bangaren Sabreena kuwa da sallama Salim ya shiga ta amsa mishi cikin sanyin murya ya karasa gareta tareda zama gefenta yasa hannu ya yaye mayafin kanta ta dago ta kalleshi yayi murmushi yace "Masha Allah", ta sauke idanunta kasa tana wasa da en yatsun ta ya riko hannun tareda sumbatar yatsun ta yace "alhamdulillah angel, yau nayi farin ciki da Allah ya nuna mun wannan ranan, da fatan kema kinyi farin ciki?", ta dago idanunta cike da hawaye tace "sosai Ya Salim, nayi farin ciki saboda Allah ya dubi zuciyata yayi mun musaya wanda yafi alkhairi a gareni, tabbas da ace ban saurare ka ba na rasa ka na tabbata da nayi rashi mai girma dan a kullum ina ganin irin son da kake mun cikin idanunka", ya goge mata kwallar da ya zubo da hannunshi yace "tabbas ina sonki sosai Sabreena, soyayyar da nake miki biro ko baki basu isa su fadi ko su rubuta irin son da nake miki ba dan koni banzan iya ce miki ga yanda nake son ki ba, sedai abinda na sani shine rasaki a rayuwata daidai yake da rasa numfashi na dan haka nake addu'a Allah ya barmu tare har karshen rayuwar mu", ta kwantar da kanta kan kirjin shi tace "nima ina sonka sosai Ya Salim", besan sanda murmushi ya kubce mai ba dan ya dade yana jiran jin wannan kalamai daga bakinta amma bata taa furta mishi ba se yau, shafa kanta yayi cikin sanyin murya yace "thank you angel", ta kara rungume shi jikinta yace "tashi muyi sallah", ba musu ta tashi sukayi alwallah suka canza kaya sannan yaja su sallah, suna idarwa yayi musu addu'o'i ta amsa da "ameen", ya kama kanta ya mata addu'a sannan ya mata tambayoyi ta bashi amsa itama dai ba laifi kuma yaji dadi, nan ya kawo mata gasasshiyar kazar ta tace "Ya Salim na koshi", yayi murmushi yace "ai wallahi gwanda kice dan ko kinci ko baki ci ba dole ki biya", bata gane inda zancen nashi ya dosa ba ta marairaice tace "Allah na koshi", yace "ban yarda ba", dole ta hakura ya dinga bata tana karba har yaga alamun ta koshi sannan ya tattare wurin yace "toh angel taho mu kwanta", ba musu ta bishi kan gado dan duk a tunaninta ba abinda ze mata tinda akwai tafiya gabansu gobe sedai ga mamakin ta taga ya kashe fitilu ya biyo ta kan gadon yana neman lalubar ta tayi saurin rike mishi hannu tace "Ya Salim dan Allah kayi hakuri ka bari muje katsina mu dawo tukunna, banso a samu matsala gobe inzo inajin kunyar sisters dinka", yayi murmushi tareda pecking din goshinta yace "don't worry, babu matsalar da za'a samu, I will take it slow", magiya ta fara mishi da bashi hakuri amma ina Salim kam bayama jin ta dan tuni yayi nisa, fita nayi na basu wuri ina me tausayawa Sabreena da ganin wautar ta na cewar tayi tunanin ze hakura saboda tafiyan su gobe
Washegari da asuba Najib ya riga Jawahir farkawa, da addu'a ya tashi ya zauna yana stretching jikinshi sannan ya kalli gefenshi yaga Jawahir kwance tana bacci peacefully se sauke nannauyar ajiyar zuciya takeyi da gani kasan tasha kuka yayi murmushi tareda kai fuskarshi daidai saitin fuskarta ya sumbaci bakin ta sannan yace "Allah ya miki albarka Qurratul aiyn", duk motsin shi tana ji dan tunda ya fara addu'a ta farka sedai tayi lamo dan bataso ya gane ba bacci takeyi ba dan kuwa wata muguwar kunyarshi takeji har batajin zata iya hada ido dashi, tashi yayi ya shiga bathroom yayi wanka sannan ya haawa Jawahir ruwan dumi cikin bathtub ya fito kugunshi daure da towel, gefen gadon yaje ya zauna ya tashe ta yana cewa "babyna, babyna tashi kiyi wanka muyi sallah kar lokaci ya kure mana", tana jinshi tayi banza dashi yace "ko in dagaki in miki wankan da kain
", ai bata bari ya karasa ba ta bude idanunta ta sauke su kanshi tayi saurin mayar da idanunta kasa tace "idan kanaso in tashi toh ka tafi dakin ka", yace "ina, ai bazan tafi in barki haka ba, dole in kula dake in nuna miki kulawa saboda farin cikin da kika sani ciki a daren jiya banajin zan iya tafiya in bar ki, Allah ya miki albarka babyta, tabbas na tsinci kaina cikin farin ciki da nishadi kasancewar na sameki a yadda nakeso, dan Allah ki tashi in taimaka miki ki gyara jikin ki", bata kulashi taci gaba da kwanciyar ta saboda koh kaya babu a jikinta, ganin batada niyyar tashi ya mike tsaye tareda daukar ta a hannu tayi saurin sa hannu tana kare kirjin ta cikin shagwaba tace "nika saukeni", be kulata ba dan yasan idan yace ze biye mata haka zasu saura har lokacin sallah ya wuce, da kyar ya samu ya sata a bathtub din da kuka da cizo da yakushi haka sukayi wankan, ita kanta taji dadin wankan amma haushin tilasta ta da Najib yayi yasa tayi kicin kicin da fuska, pant and bra ya miko mata ta karba tasa sannan ya dauko mata jallabiya ya taimaka mata tasa shima yasa nashi jallabiyan yajasu sallah, suna idarwa sukayi addu'o'in su ta koma ta kwanta shikuma ya tashi ya fita daga dakin, ba jimawa ya dawo da tea me kauri yazo ya zauna kusa da ita yace "babyna tashi kisha", bata musa mishi ba dan kuwa ita kanta tanajin yunwa duk da ta koshi kafin su kwanta, da kanshi ya dinga bata tana sha harta kusa shanyewa sannan tace "na koshi", be matsa mata ba dan ya lura tanaji da rigima idan yace ze matsa mata zata iya sa mai kuka dan muryarta ma rawa yakeyi, magani ya dauko ya balla mata ba musu ta karba tasha yace "ze rage miki zafin da wurin yake miki da kuma ciwon jiki", ta maka mishi harara yayi murmushi yace "kwanta ki huta", kwanciya tayi shikuma ya fita da cup din sannan ya dawo ya kwanta gefenta tareda janyota jikinshi ta kara shige mishi suka koma bacci
A bangaren Sabreena itama ta samu kulawa sosai dan tun gabanin asuba Salim ya tabbata ta gyara jikinta tasha pain killer dan bayaso yayyenshi suzo daukarta da safe suka tana tafiya ba daidai ba, seda sukayi sallah sannan suka koma acci, karfe tara ya tashi ya sake hada mata ruwan dumi ya tasheta ta sake shiga ta gasa jikinta sannan tayi wanka gaba-daya ta fito, atampha super Holland tasa tayi er kwalliyar ta bame yawa ba ta fito parlor inda ta ganshi da basket a hannu alaman abinci aka kawo yace "angel kin fito, zokici abinci daga gidansu Najib Ummi ta aiko wai saboda ki samu kici kafin a wuce Katsina", kanta kasa taje ta zauna kam dinning ya zuba mata soyayyar dankali da kwai da kuma romon catfish sannan ya hada mata tea me kauri yace "kici sosai kinji angel, zanje nayi wanka na dawo", daga mishi kai tayi yayi pecking kumatun ta sannan yayi ciki, harta gama cin abinci tana kokarin tattare wurin ya fito, serving nashi tayi sannan ta kwashe sauran ta kai kitchen, yana cikin cin abinci aka fara knock, yasan sisters dinshi ne dan haka ya tashi yaje ya bue musu suka shigo babbar yayarshi na cewa "a'a kunga ango har ya fara wani kyalli yana sheki saboda amarci", sukayi dariya Sabreena dake tsaye gefen kujera tayi murmushi ta duka har kasa ta gaishe su suka amsa mata cikin fara'a, Salim yace "da wuri haka zaku wuce?", cousin dinshi tace "goma da rabi yanzu fah, kuma kasan jirgin 11:30 zamu bi", yace "zakuje kuga Najib da amaryar sa ne kafin ku wuce?", Babbar yayarshi tace "hanya mayi hakan, mutane na amarcin su muje musu da sanyin safiya kila ma basu tashi ba, ai ku ma badan da tafiya gabanmu ba dase yamma zaku ganmu", Salim yace "shikenan, bari mu shirya se in rakaku airport danni se yamma", sister dinshi tace "Hajiya tace kar amarya tazo da komai, akwai kayan da zatasa a chan, dama yinin biki kawai za'ayi yau dan en uwa da abokan arziki su ganta, gobe kuma zakuje wurin inna itama ta ganta da yamma ku juyo abinku dan tace bataso ta shiga hakkin ku dayawa", Salim ya kaa kai ba kunya yace "ai kuwa ta kyauta, ina zuwa, bari na shirya matata inzo in kaiku", kallonshi kawai sukeyi yaja Sabreena suka shige dakin ta yana rufo kofa ya rungume ta jikinshi cikin rada yace mata "take care of yourself when you get there, inshallah da yamma zaki ganni kinji, I'm going to miss your lovely smile", ta kaa mishi kai dan ba bakin magana tana kokarin haiye kukan ta dan batasan ya zatayi a chan ba, babu wanda ta sani se shi, mayafi ya dauko da kanshi ya yafa mata sannan ya dauko purse ya zuba kudi ba tareda ta sani ba yaja hannunta suka fito
Shi ya sauke su airport dansu uku ne da Sabreena hudu, sauran tuni sunyi gaba duk zasu hadu acan, seda taga sun kusa tafiya tace "kai ma ka kular mun da kanka, sannan kazo akan lokaci kaji, kasan na manta wayana a gida balle mu dinga waya", ya shafa gefen fuskarta yace "karki damu ina nan zuwa kuma wayarki zan bari akawo mun in zo miki dashi", murmushi tayi sannan ta juya ta shige ciki tana daga mishi shima yana daga mata, seda yaji tashin jirgin sannan ya koma gida jiki a sanyaya, yazo ze shiga gida ya hango basket bakin kofan su Najib yayi murmushi yace "wato shegen be tashi ba kenan har yanzu tinda besan an kawo abinci ba", cike da mugunta ya zaro wayarshi ya dannawa Najib kira, dayake wayan na kusa da pillow dinshi yasa yayi saurin jin ringing din, daukar wayar yayi ba tareda ya duba suna ba yasa a kunne cikin muryar bacci yace "hello", Salim yayi dariya yace "kana gauro baka makara ba se yanzu da kayi mata, dalla malam ka tashi hakanan lada ya isa, ga abinci an kawo muku gaban kofar ka", tsaki Najib yayi yace "mood spoiler, kai ina naka matar kazo kana damuwa da sassafen nan", Salim yace "duba time, se kasan gari ya waye ba sassafe bane", kashe wayar Salim yayi Najib ya kalli agogo yaga daya saura ya kalli gefenshi yaga har yanzu Jawahir bacci takeyi, yasan ta gaji, ga gajiyan biki ga kuma gajiyan da ya tara mata jiya, dan haka be tashe ta ba ya tashi ya wuce dakin shi dan yayi wanka ya shirya
Koda Jawahir ta tashi Najib baya dakin, hamdala tayi da bata ganshi ba ta tashi tsaye dan tafiya bathroom, sosai taji dama dama ta shiga ta kara gasa jikinta tayi wanka sannan ta fito daure da towel ta wuce gaban dressing mirror dinta, tayi shafe shafenta ta dauko atampha vilisco inkin riga da skirt ta saka ya zauna mata das a jiki, gaban mirror ta dawo tana kokarin daura dankwalli ya shigo da sallama ta amsa mishi, beji amsa sallamar ta ba amma yasan ta amsa saboda ya hango yadda bakinta ya motsa ta cikin mirror ya karaso ya tsaya bayanta yana kallonta ta cikin mirror yace "Qurratul aiyn kin tashi", tace "uhmm na tashi, yaushe kuma sunana ya tashi daga babyna ya koma Qurratul aiyn?", yayi murmushi me kayatarwa sannan yaje daidai saitin kunnenta yace "daga daren jiya zuwa yau", da sauri da sauke idanunta kasa tana regretting tambayar shi da tayi dan ta lura Najib ya daina kunyar gaya mata magana kwata kwata ya taba cikinshi yace "taso muje muci abinci yunwa nakeji", tashi tayi ya kama hannunta suka fice daga dakin, kan dinning suka zauna dan tuni ya shigo da abincin ta bude ta zuzzuba musu irin abincin da aka kaiwa Sabreena ne soyayyiyar dankali da kwai da kuma romon catfish, sosai suka ci sukayi nak sannan sukayi sallar azahar jin an kira, wuni sukayi a ranar makale da juna suna wasannin tun Jawahir bata sake jikinta dashi ba har tazo ta sake dan Najib namiji ne daya iya siye zuciyar mace da nashi salon soyayyar
Da yamma mutanen da suka zo biki suka kawowa Jawahir lefenta gida sukace na Sabreena se ta dawo sannan sukayi sallama dan washegari zasu fara tafiya inda suka fito, sosai Jawahir ta musu godiya harta karba numbers din wasu daga cikinsu dan ta gane zumunci shine komai ta kuma musu sha tara ta arziki ta musu kyaututtuka Najib ma ya kara musu da kyautar kudi sukayi sallama, har bakin gate Jawahir ta rakasu danji take kaman ta bisu saboda ananin lokacin da sukayi dasu ta shaku dasu ba laifi, yinin ranar ba inda Najib yaje yana gida se da yamma wuraren shida Salim ya kirashi kan cewar ze tafi Katsina Najib ya rakashi bakin mota ya dawo wurin amarshi, da daddare tace mishi balango zataci yace ta canza kaya suje su siyo ta dora after dress kan riga da wandon da tasa ta yafa mayafi suka fita a mota, seda suka zaga gari sannan suka siyo balangon da yogurt suka dawo gida
Hajiya Hadiza itace mahaifiyar Salim, mahaifinsa kuma Alhaji Muhammad duk en garin Katsina ne, iyayen Alhaji Muhammad duk sun rasu inda ta bangaren mahaifiyarshi kuma Innar ta nada rai amma ta tsufa sosai tana zauna gidan yayar Hajiya Hadiza wacce suke kira da Nana, yayyanenshi biyu mata Zaliha itace babba se Iklima me bin mata se shi Salim din sannan kanwarshi Fauziya, yana da cousins dayawa dan gidan family house ne saboda mahaifinshi yayyenshi uku duka maza shine auta kuma duk a gida daya suke zaune, sannan ta bangaren mahaifiyarshi ma suna dayawa, basa lissafuwa
Wannan kenan
Mahaifiyar Salim sosai tayi muryar ganin Sabreena dan ta dade tana burin ganin auren danta namiji kwaya daya da Allah ya bata saboda duka yayyanenshi da kanwarshi sunyi aure, gashi cousins dinshi ma suna kanyi duk da ba wani shekaru ne dashi ba, ta yaba da hankali da nutsuwar Sabreena, cikin lokaci kankani parlorn Hajiya Hadiza ya cika da en uwa wa'anda basu samu zuwa biki ba anzo ganin amaryar Salim duk da wasu nasu na gulma ne, Sabreena tasha yabo sosai kuma cikin lokaci kankani suka bari ta sake dasu dan sun nuna mata ta zama 'yar uwar su ta ajiye maganan sukurtaka gefe, yinin ranan sukasha shagali nasu na angwanai wanda Sabreena tayi mamakin yadda akayi suka san size dinta dan kayan da tasa sun amshe ta sun zauna cif cif a jikinta, se dare ta samu kanta kuma se lokaci ta samu ganin Salim inda Hajiya Hadiza da Alhaji Muhammad suka sasu gaba da nasiha, seda suka gama Alhaji ya wuce bangarenshi Hajiya ta zubo musu jollof din shinkafa da hadin coslow da kaza hade da lemun wawa tace "gashi kuci, idan kun gama Sabreena kizo dakina ki kwanta kai kuma kasan makwancin ka", ya marairaice fuska yace "Hajiya", tace "banson dogon zance, yi sauri kuci abinci", da fadar hakan ta shige ciki abinta Salim ya kalli Sabreena tasa mishi dariya yace "ba dariya kikeyi yanzu ba, zan kamaki ne ai", ta mai gwalo sannan ta maida hankalinta kan abinci ya mike ze fice tace "bakaci abincin ba", kaman karamin yaro yace "ba gwalo kike mun ba", tayi murmushi tace "haba nawan, yi hakuri kazo muci bazanso mijina ya kwana da yunwa ba bayan nasan ka kwaso gajiyar tafiya", ya make kafada yace "ni bazanci ba sedai idan zaki bani a baki", a zuciyarta tace "na shiga uku, dama haka Ya Salim yake", ganin tayi shiru ya juya ze fice tayi saurin cewa "zoka zauna in baka toh", yayi murmushi ya dawo ya zauna ta dinga bashi yana amsa yayin da shikuma ya zuba mata ido yana sakeyiwa Allah godiya daya bashi Sabreena a matsayin mata, koda suka gama be bari ta tafi haka kawai ba seda yayi kissing dinta ya rungumeta yana fada mata yadda zeyi missing dinta sannan da kyar da lallaa wa ya barta ta tafi dakin Hajiya tana me kewan mijinta
Washegari bayan Sabreena ta shirya tayi breakfast Hajiya tace "Salim ka kaita wurin Inna ta ganta, se ku dawo kuci abincin rana sannan ku tafi", yace "toh hajiya bari mu tashi", nan Sabreena ta tashi tabi bayanshi suka fice, motan wani cousin dinshi ya karba ya kaita gidan Nana dan Inna ta ganta, sunji dadin zuwan su ba kaman inna da duk da ba wani gane mutane takeyi ba amma tana gane muryar Salim, sanda akace mata matar dake zaune kusa dashi itace wacce ya aura kuwa tayi farin ciki sosai har da hawayen ta, nan Salim ya barta yaje ya zaga gari ga leka abokan shi wa'anda basu samu zuwa daurin auren shi ba sunata tayashi murna da mishi addu'an zaman lafiya da zuri'a na gari, seda yayi azahar a masallaci sannan ya koma ya dauko Sabreena bayan Nana ta bata turaren humra na jiki da kuma turaren daki na tsinke da turmin atampha, sosai Sabreena tayi mata godiya suka musu sallama suka koma gida, suna gama cin abincin rana Hajiya tace suje dakunan sauran mutanen gidan su musu sallama sannan suzo su wuce, ko wani daki sun shiga kuma duk inda sukaje se an hado Sabreena da kaya, godiya kawai take musu tana yiwa Allah godiya ganin dangin mijinta na sonta, Hajiya kuwa atampha kala uku, mayafi kala biyu, takalmi kala biyu, turare arbi'an oud me tsadan, da kuma jallabiya me kyau na saudiya ta bata tace jallabiyan ta dinga sallah dashi, sannan ta kara hada mata kayan kuka dasu kubewa harda daddawa tace koh Salim yace bayacin tuwo ta tuka ta ajiye mishi zeci, godiya sosai Sabreena tayi taje tayiwa Alhaji Muhammad sallama ya bata dubu hamsin taki karba yace ai bata isa ba seta karba, da kyar ta karbi kudin dan batasan ya zatayi dasu ba ga sadakin ta ga wanda Salim yasa mata a purse bata sani ba, ga wannan da Alhaji ya bata sannan kuma ga na company din Mamah dan yanzu company za'a ce mai tinda kara habbaka yake yi, Sabreena tayi godiya sosai aka kaisu airport suka hau jirgi suka dawo Kebbi inda ta raba abubuwan da ta samo biyu ta kaiwa Jawahir rabi itama ta rike rabi sukaci gaba da cin amarcin su hankali kwance ba kaman Najib da Jawahir da basa bawa kansu breathing space, kusan ko wani lokaci suka makale da juna
Na kusa karshe Inshallah, karku gaji dani

Sati daya kenan su Najib suna gida suna kwasan amarci babu inda suke zuwa, Najib da Jawahir wata irin shakuwa ce ta shiga tsakaninsu me wuyar fassara, kullum suna tare, suyi wanka tare, suci abinci tare, suyi kallo tare, suyi bacci rungume da junansu kaman ance za'a rabasu, ya sabar mata da zama a jikinshi a koda yaushe dan muddin yana wuri batada wurin zama koh kwanciya se jikinshi, wannan dalilin ne yasa sanda yazo mata da maganar komawarsu wurin aiki shida Salim taji hankalin ta ya tashi, kuka tasa mishi sosai tana cewa zata bishi yace "bani da inda zan ajiye ki a Abuja babyna, apartment din da nake nida Salim muke sharing dinshi amma karki damu, idan naje I will find a solution, ko hayane zan kama sekizo ki zauna wurina kafin lokacin komawarku school yayi", da wannan ya samu ya lallashe ta sannan yace ta shirya ya kaita wurin Mamah ze musu sallama, cikin murnar ganin Mamah ta tashi taje wanke fuskarta sannan tazo tasa shadda maroon color dinkin doguwar riga ta gyara fuskarta tasa farin mayafi da takalmi tace mishi ta gama, a tare suka fito sun jero gwanin sha'awa dan ba karamin kyau sukayi bah, shi ya tukasu suka fara zuwa gidan Yaya Aysha, sosai taji dadin ganinsu ta kumayi farin ciki ganin suma suna cikin farin ciki da kwanciyar hankali dan har er kiba Najib yayi cikin sati daya, itama Jawahir tayi fresh tayi kyau jikinta duk ya ciko yayi bul bul ga fatarta se sheki yakeyi, sun jima suna hira wurin Yaya Aysha kafin su mata sallama su tafi gidan Mamah
Mamah na zaune tana haawa su Nabil madara dan taga alamun nono kadai baya isansu su Jawahir suka shigo da sallama, dagowa tayi ta kallesu fuskarta dauke da murmushi tace "a'a kaga amarya da angon ta", Jawahir ta dukar da kai Mamah tayi dariya suka samu wuri suka zauna Najib ya gaisheta ta amsa sannan Jawahir ma ta gaisheta ta amsa tana kallon yadda ta canza sannan ta kalli Najib tace "ashe dai ka iya kiwo, ji yadda ka mayar mun da yarinya kaman balarabiya cikin sati daya", Najib yayi murmushi yana sosa kanshi yace "Aunty na kenan, ai abinda kakeso dole ka kula dashi", tace "hakane", sannan ta kwalawa Halima kira ta fito daga kitchen da saurinta Mamah tace "kawo musu abinsha", Jawahir ta kalli Mamah tace "kai Mamah se kace wasu baki", Mamah tace "Jawahir ai kun zama baki yanzu tinda tsakani na daku yanzu se ziyara", Halima tazo ta ajiye musu Chi exotic Mamah ta kalli Jawahir tace "taso ki zubawa mijinki", ba musu ta tashi ta zuba mishi a cup ta mika mishi ya haa da hannunta ya amsa Mamah ta girgiza kai a zuciyarta tace "yaran zamani sedai a barsu", bayan Jawahir tayi nasarar cire hannunta daga na Najib ta koma kusa da Mamah ta zauna tareda dora kanta kan kafadar Mamah tace "Mamah inasu Nabila, ban gansu ba", Mamah tace "suna bacci amma nasan Nabil ya kusa tashi dan besha nono ba ya kwanta kuma daya fara jin yunwa tashi zeyi", ai tana rufe baki suka ji kukan shi Mamah ta kallesu tace "ai na gaya muku", Jawahir na murmushi tace "bari in dauko shi", tashi tayi taje dauko shi inda taga Nabila ma ta tashi amma hannu kawai tasa a baki tana tsotsa abinta Jawahir ta dauki Nabil ta kaishi wurin Mamah tana cewa "bari na dauko Nabila, itama ta tashi se shan hannu takeyi", Mamah ta karbi Nabil tana cewa "ai idan kika bibiya ma ta rigashi tashi, ita kwatakwata batada rigima, da wuya kiji kukan ta ba kaman wannan jarababben ba", dauko Nabila tayi tazo ta zauna kusa da Najib ya mika hannu alamar ta bashi ta mika ta wurin Najib ya karbeta ya kalli Mamah yaga hankalinta nakan Nabil dake karban nono yazo saitin kunnen Jawahir yace "irin wannan yaran zaki bani nan da nine months", ta zaro ido tana kokarin matsawa ya riko hannunta sukaji muryar Mamah na cewa "ku tashi ku tafi gidanku, baza kumin tabara a nan ba", Najib ya saki dariya yana sosa keya yace "Aunty na korar mu kikeyi", tace "gani nayi baka kunyar idona", yayi murmushi yace "na isa Aunty na", bata kulashi ba tace "a zubo muku abinci, tuwo nayi miyar busasshiyar kubewa", Najib yace "a zubo", Jawahir ta mike tana cewa "bari in zubo muci", taje ta zubo musu daidai wanda tasan zasu iya cinyewa ta ajiye can dinning ta koma ta kawo ruwan wanke hannu sannan ta kirashi yazo ya zauna hannunshi rike da Nabila suka fara cin abincin, seda suka gama Jawahir ta tattare wurin sannan ta karbi Nabila ta mikawa Mamah ta kira Halima wacce ke wanke wanke a kitchen tazo ta goya Nabil sannan sukace zasu wuce, har bakin mota Mamah ta rakasu taja Jawahir gefe tana bata shawarwari da kuma yadda zata kula da kanta da mijinta sannan ta musu sallama suka wuce, gidan Dada suka je daga nan suka gaida Farida basu dade ba suka koma gida
Washegari Sabreena da Salim sukaje sukayi nasu ziyaran tareda sallaman mutane, Sunday na zuwa Najib da Salim suka fito zasu wuce, kowa ya kalli idanun Jawahir yasan tayi kuka dan dakyar Najib ya samu ya lallabata, Sabreena ma idanun ta sun kada sedai tana kokarin boye damuwarta, a bakin mota Najib ya kalli Jawahir yace "Babyna idan na tafi karkiyi kuka dan Allah, zamu dinga waya kuma ranar friday zan dawo kinji", cikin sanyin murya tace "toh bazanyi ba", yayi murmushi yayi pecking lips dinta sannan ya shige motar, Salim ya kalli Jawahir yace "ga sister dinki nan, pls take care of her on my behalf", Jawahir tayi murmushi tace "I will", Sabreena ta harare shi tace "cikin ni da ita waye ze kula da wani, koh bakaga ita kuka takeyi ba ana lallashin ta kaman jaririya, ni kuwa kaga nayi kuka", ya rungumota jikinshi yace "nasan zakiyi ne, nasanki da boye damuwa, bakyaso naganki cikin damuwa shiyasa kike kokarin dannewa amma dana tafi nasan zakiyi", hawaye ya zubo mata dan tasan gaskiya ya fada ya goge mata hawayenta yayi pecking goshinta yace "take care", tace "you too", haka ya shiga mota Najib ya jasu suka fita suka dau hanyar Abuja, Sabreena bata shige dakin ta ba tabi Jawahir suka shiga bangarenta suka zauna a parlor Jawahir tace "I can't believe being married is as percious as what I'm feeling right now, I only spent a week with him but I'm already feeling lonely", Sabreena tayi murmushi tace "same here sis, but we need to learn how to live without them, mazajenmu ba nan suke aiki ba, dole mu koyi zama ba tare dasu ba ako da yaushe", Jawahir tace "hakane, are you hungry, mu dafa abinda zamu ci", Sabreena tace "nayi girki, in kawo nan koh zaki zo", Jawahir tace "bari nayi wanka ina zuwa", da haka Sabreena ta fice Jawahir kuma ta shige dakin ta tanajin gidan ya zama mata babba saboda babu Najib a ciki
Wasa wasa lokaci ya tafi dan wata shida kenan da aurensu Jawahir, duk weekend su Najib suna gida wurin iyalinsu inda weekdays kuma suna Abuja wurin aikinsu, Najib yaso kama gida amma Abbanshi yace a'a suyi hakuri tinda zata koma school idan ta koma kudin hayan zeyi waste dan haka yayi hakuri idan ta gama final year dinta zasu nemi alfarma a turata Abuja service that way ze iya kama gida koma ya siya, badan ransu yaso ba haka suka hakura suka zauna, auren da wata uku dukkansu suka fara laulauyin ciki kusan lokaci daya sedai na Sabreena na wahalar da ita sosai, dole Mamah tace ta dawo gida tinda mijinta ba zama yakeyi ba, ganin haka Jawahir ma tasa rigima itama zata koma gida Najib yace besan zancen ba tayi zamanta, har fushi tayi dashi na sati daya bata daukar wayarshi wai koh ze yarda taje amma be canza ra'ayin shi ba sema canza mata tunani da yayi da yazo weekend ta daina maganan komawa gida, a halin yanzu sun dade da komawa school inda Dada ya canza musu mota wannan karon harda Sabreena aka siyawa ta koyi driving ko wannensu da motar ta take zuwa makaranta dan lokacin lectures dinsu ya bambanta, sosai Jawahir take maida hankali kuma Najib yana iya kokarin wurin ganin ya bata full support dan tace ita da first class takeso ta fita, wasa wasa cikinsu ya fara tsufa har ya fito kowa na gani ita Sabreena har kunya takeji wai za'ace karama da ita sa ciki, Jawahir kuwa har wani yanga takeyi da nata ganin ya karbi jikinta besata muni ba
Cikin Jawahir na wata bakwai suka fara final exams dinsu, karatu kam tanayi sosai wannan dalilin yasa exams din suka dinga zuwa mata da sauki, ranar da suka gama exams dinsu sukayi sign out a gaban department dinsu, Jawahir na zaune tana kallonsu suna hotuna suna rubuta suna jikin white shirt dinda suka sa, Rumana da Zahra ne suka zo wurin tareda janta Zahra na cewa "matar Najib dan Allah taso today is your day kinje kin zauna", haka ta shiga cikinsu tana hotuna har yamma sannan ya musu sallama ta wuce gida, a waya Najib ya kirata yana congratulating dinta, tana ajiye waya Sabreena ta shigo hannunta rike da cake tace "congrats sis, come let's celebrate", murmushi Jawahir tayi suka zauna suna hotuna da Snapchat suna turawa mazajensu Jawahir harda emoji din gwalo ta turawa Najib yace ze kamata, Salim kuma yace Inshallah lokacin da Sabreena zata gama yana nan dan haka tare zasuyi celebrate ita ma sauranta shekara daya
Kwana biyu da gama exam din Jawahir ta tattara tabi mijinta Abuja dan tuni ya kama hayar two bedroom flat, sosai yaji dadin ganinta kuma yayi farin ciki, tinda ta koma ya dena zuwa Kebbi weekend se Salim ne ke jigilar zuwa saboda Sabreena wacce itama sun fara exam, itama tana gama exam dinta ta bishi Abuja sukaci gaba da zamansu suna rainon cikinsu, cikinsu na shiga wata tara Mamah tace su dawo gida, badan mazajensu sun so ba suka dawo dasu inda suka kaisu gidan Mamah, dawowarsu da sati biyu Jawahir ta tashi da nakuda cikin dare, tun tana daurewa har abun ya gagara ta fara kiran Mamah, a daren suka kaita asibiti sedai har wayewar gari Jawahir ta gagara haihuwa, sun shiga tashin hankali marar misaltuwa ba kaman Dada da yake ganin Jawahir kadai Allah ya mallaka mai gashi tana kwance kafa daya duniya daya lahira, basu so kiran Najib ba amma tunda likita yace se an mata cs suka kirashi dan su sanar dashi, iya tashin hankali ya shiga yace yana zuwa, airport ya wuce cikin ikon Allah ya samu jirgin da zeje Kebbi, yana zuwa aka kaishi dakin da Jawahir take ana mata arin ruwa ya zauna gefen gadon ta kalleshi cikin zafin nakuda tace "karka bari ayi mun cs, a kira mun Mamah na tabbata idan tana tare dani zan iya haihuwa da kaina", hakan kuwa akayi aka kira mata Mamah wacce ke hawaye Jawahir ta rike hannunta tana cewa "don't leave me Mamah, I need you by my side", dole Mamah ta tsaya har nakudar ya sake tashi suka kira likita aka kaita labour room suka bari Mamah ta shiga tinda abinda Jawahir keso kenan, cikin lokaci kankani se gashi santalelen danta ya fito dan wannan karon kam da karfinshi yazo, murna Mamah keyi ta fito tana fada musu an samu baby boy duk suka dinga hamdala banda Sabreena data gama tsurewa ganin irin wahalar da Jawahir tasha, an gyara Jawahir da babynta aka kaisu ward inda aka basu private room Najib cikin farin ciki yazo yana sumbatar fuskar Jawahir yanasa mata albarka tareda mata sannu, kowa ya shigo sannu yake mata ita kuma tana murmushi dan Allah kadai yasan farin cikin da takeji da kudirin da ta dauka na zame ma danta UWA TA GARI saboda gudun kar ya shiga halin rudin duniya, Najib yayiwa danshi kiran sallah a kunne ya mishi khutuba da suna Yusuf sunan mahaifinsa Jawahir tace tanaso a dinga kiranshi da Khalifa, da yamma aka sallamesu suka koma gida, sati na zagayowa akayi suna wanda ya tara en uwa da abokan arziki wannan karon Adil ma yazo kanin Najib dan be samu zuwa bikinsu ba saboda exam da yakeyi lokacin amma wannan karon kasancewar suna hutu yazo, sosai Khalifa ya shiga ran mutane saboda kyawunshi, ya samu kaya sosai dashi da mahaifiyarshi
Anyi suna da kwana uku itama Sabreena ta fara nakuda, haka suka kwashe ta akayi hospital da ita inda cikin mintunan da basu fi talatin ba ta haifi danta shima kyakyawa me kamada mahaifinsa, kasancewar Salim be koma Kebbi ba yana nan ta haihu yazo asibitin bayan Mamah ta kirashi, yayi murna sosai jin Sabreena ta haihu lafiya, nan ya dinga sa mata albarka tareda mata sannu inda yawa yaron khutuba da Muhammad sunan mahaifinshi, suna kiranshi da Al ameen, ranar suna an cika sosai dan en uwan shi na Katsina sunzo harda gudummawar su, lokacin da Jawahir tayi arba'in Najib ya shaida mata ya siya gida a Abuja a maitama nan zasu koma, ta mishi fada sosai ganin yaushe yaushe ya kama gida amma har ya sake dakin ya siya musu gida, sanda taje taga gidan da ya siya seta kama bakinta tayi shiru ganin ba karamin gida bane, gidane lafiyayye duplex me dauke da dakuna shida, komai na gidan yayi inda ya nuna mata gidan dake kusa dasu yace na Salim ne wan nan shima ya siya, ta tayashi murna amma yace karta fadawa Sabreena tukunna surprise ze mata, kafin Sabreena tayi arba'in sun koma school inda Jawahir kuma ke service dinta a Abuja a wani public secondary school tana koya musu English language, bata samun matsala da yaran kasancewar suna sonta kuma all girls school ne, ta samarwa Khalifa nanny wacce ke kula dashi idan ta tafi karantarwa zuwa biyu kuma idan ta dawo gida ta karbeshi nanny kuma ta wuce
Haka sukaci gaba rayuwarsu har Jawahir ta gama service dinta Sabreena kuma ta gama exams dinta ta dawo Abuja gidan mijinta da zama inda itama ake neman mata alfarman ta samu tayi service dinta nan Abuja din
Business din Mamah ya bunkasa sosai wanda ganin haka su Jawahir suka bata shawaran ta bude branch a Abuja se su dinga kula mata dashi, hakan kuwa akayi cikin kankanin lokaci suka bude branch Jawahir na zama ciki tinda Sabreena na service dinta a wani oil company, Mamah ta yaye su Nabil dan yanzu shekarar su biyu kenan, sunyi baki magana kaman sunci shirwa ba kaman Nabil dan Nabila halin Sabreena ne da ita bata cika magana ba sedai ta barwa cikin ta, an sasu school sun fara da play group inda Mamah ta maida hankalinta kan business dinta Halima kuma na kular mata dasu Nabil, Khalifa da Al ameen shekarar su daya kenan yanzu sun yi jiki gwanin sha'awa dan suna samun kulawa daga wurin iyayensu harma da kakannin su
Farida tasha kuka lokacin da taje asibiti gwaji jin shiru har yanzu ba maganan ciki likitan da ya gwadata ya shaida mata ai mahaifarta ta lalace tayi hakuri, ta dawo gida cikin kuka Dada ya dawo ya sameta a wannan halin ya tambayi lafiya take shaida mishi abinda likita yace sannan ta bashi shawaran ya kara aure dan dai ita bazata iya producing mishi yara ba, hakuri ya bata ya lallashe ta sannan yace babu auren da ze kara kaddarar suce tazo a haka kuma shi ya karbeta hannu bibbiyu, haka sukaci gaba da zama cike da kuncin rashin haihuwa
Alhamdulillah mahaifin Jarood ya dawo kan harkokinshi na siyasa kuma se abun ya kara bunkasa fiyeda da, yayi depositing 10million account din Jarood yace ya maidawa Jawahir kudinta sannan ya mata godiya, har Abuja Jarood yaje, seda ya biya bank yayi withdraw din kudin sannan yaje gidan Jawahir wanda ta bashi address, cikin sa'a kuwa tana gida har da Najib, da sallama ya shiga parlorn Najib ya amsa mishi yana cewa "a'a Jarood yau kaine a gidan, daga ina haka", Jarood ya zauna yace "wallahi daga Kebbi nake", gaisawa sukayi Najib ya kira Jawahir ta fito rike da Khalifa wanda keta rigima, tayi farin cikin ganin Jarood inda ta zauna suka gaisa ya karbi Khalifa yana mishi wasa ta shige kitchen ta hado mishi kayan snacks da drink tazo ta ajiye gabanshi sannan ta koma kusa da Najib ta zauna Jarood ya dago ya kalleta yace "Jawahir ga kudin ki nan, na dawo miki dashi kaman yadda nayi alkawari", Jawahir ta girgiza kai tace "ai cewa nayi na baka, dan Allah Jarood ka barshi, what are friends for", Najib ya kalleta yace "wani kudi ne?", nan ta mishi bayani ya kalli Jarood yace "bro tinda tace ka barshi taimako tayi ka barshi kawai, ai wannan shine abotan, na tabbata da itace a situation dinda ka shiga zaka taimaka mata", Jarood yayi ajiyar zuciya ganin anfi karfinshi yace "shikenan toh zan dauki 5million in bar mata 5million", da kyar Jawahir ta yarda da wannan tsarin nashi ya bata 5million ya rike 5 ya sake mata godiya sannan ya bata iv din aurenshi yace "wata me zuwa", ta tayashi murna sosai tace Inshallah zatazo, har bakin mota suka rakashi ya wuce ita kuma ta dawo cikin gida ta zauna gefen Najib tace "habibi", yace "ya akayi Qurratul aiyn", ta kwantar da kanta kafadarshi tace "ya zanyi da wannan kudaden", yace "ki kara hannun jari", ta dago tace "toh ka cire wani abu a ciki", ya girgiza kai yace "ban zan iya karba ba Jawahir, kinsan I'm worth more than that, idan na karba kaman karawa me karfi karfi ne, think wisely and use the money wisely kinji", ta kaa mishi kai tace "ok"
Tuni Jawahir ta zuba kudinta ta kara hannun jari sun kara bude wani branch din a nan Abuja inda suka sa Sabreena as manager, cikin lokaci kankani abubuwa suka bunkasa suka zama masu kudi daga su har Mamah wacce ta dade a harkar, Najib ya biyawa kanshi da Jawahir kudin hajji inda Salim ya biyawa shida Sabreena, su Jawahir ganin haka suka hada kudi suka biyawa Mamah, Salim da Najib ganin an biyawa Mamah sukayi shawara Najib ya biyawa Yaya Aysha Salim kuma ya biyawa Hajiyar sa, su Dada da Abba sukace an ware su, Mamah ce tayiwa su Jawahir magana kan cewa zata bawa Farida kujerar ta tinda ita ta taba zuwa sukace baza'ayi haka zasu biyawa Farida, sanda taji sun biya mata hajji tayi murna harda kwallarta tana dana sanin abinda tayiwa Jawahir a baya gashi yau ta mata rana, cikin ikon Allah dasu akayi hajji a wannan shekarar inda suka kaiwa Hajja renon yaransu
Alhamdulillah anan ba kawo karshen litattafin UWA TA GARI, kuskuren da nayi da abinda na fada ba daidai ba Allah ya yafe, fadakarwar dake ciki kuma Allah yasa ayi amfani dashi a kuma kiyaye da muzguna UWA da ata mata rai dan UWA ba abar wasa bace
